
<p>
[p. 1]<br/>
[śrīḥ<br/>
pampakavi viracitaṁ<br/>
vikramārjuna vijayaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[prathamāśvāsaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
śrīyanarātisādhana payōnidhiyoḷ paḍeduṁ dharitriyaṁ<br/>
jīyene bēḍikoḷḷade virōdhi narēndraranottikoṇḍumā<br/>
tmīyasupuṣpavr̥ṣṭiyanoḍambaḍe tāḷdiyumintudāttanā<br/>
rāyaṇanāda dēvanemagīgarikēsari saukhya kōṭiyaṁ // ViVi.1.1 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
muḷisu lalāṭanētraśikhi mecce vinūtarasaprasādamu<br/>
jjaḷa jasamaṅga saṅgata lasadbhasitaṁ prabhuśakti śakti ni<br/>
rmaḷamaṇibhūṣaṇaṁ phaṇivibhūṣaṇamāge negaḻteyaṁ puduṁ<br/>
goḷisidanīśvaraṁ negaḻdudāra mahēśvaranīgebhōgamaṁ // ViVi.1.2 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
caṇḍavirōdhisādhana tamastamamōḍe viśiṣṭa padmanī<br/>
ṣaṇḍamaraldu rāgadinoṟaldire yācaka bhaṅgakōṭi kai<br/>
koṇḍu nirantaraṁ taguḷdu kīrtise mikkeseva pracaṇḍamā<br/>
rtāṇḍanalarcugenna hr̥dayāmbujamaṁ nija vāṅmarīciyiṁ // ViVi.1.3 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
sahajada celvinoḷ ratiya sōlada kēḷiyoḷ podaḻdu sa<br/>
nnahitavenippapūrva śubha lakṣaṇa dēhadoḷoḷpanāḷdu saṁ<br/>
dahikaṭaka prasādade manōjanumaṁ gelevandanāgaḷuṁ<br/>
sahajamanōjanōjanemagīge vicitra ratōtsavaṅgaḷaṁ // ViVi.1.4 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 2]<br/>
kṣayamaṇamillakēḷdu kaḍegaṇḍavanāvanumillenal tada<br/>
kṣayanidhi tāne tannanosedōlagipaṅgaridillenippa vā<br/>
ṅmayamanitarkamambi[ke]sarasvati manmukhapadmaraṅgadē<br/>
ḻgeyaneḍegoṇḍu koṇḍukonedīgarigaṅge viśuddhabuddhiyaṁ // ViVi.1.5 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
tisuḷadoḷuccaḷippa posa nettare kendaḷirāgekaṇgagu<br/>
rvisuvinamokku nēlva karuḷōḷiye bāḷa mr̥ṇāḷamāge mi<br/>
kkasurara meyyoḷāda virahāgniyanāṟisutintetanna kū<br/>
rasiyoḷaḍurtu kondasiyaḷi[rka]siyoḷ paḍemeccegaṇḍanā // ViVi.1.6 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
enna dānamidāgaḷuṁ madhupāśrayaṁ dharegavyava<br/>
cchinna dānamidāgaḷuṁ vibudhāśrayaṁ gelevandane<br/>
nnannijōnnatiyindamī patiyendu mecci vināyakaṁ<br/>
tānnimircuge kabbamaṁ nayadiṁ guṇārṇava bhūpanā // ViVi.1.7 [mallikāmāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
bage posatappudāgi mr̥du bandhadoḷonduvudondi dēsiyoḷ<br/>
puguvudu pokka mārgadoḷe taḷvudu taḷtoḍe kāvyabandhamo<br/>
ppugumeḷamāvu kendaḷira pūvina biṇpoṟeyiṁ baḻaldu tuṁ<br/>
bigaḷine tumbi kōgileye baggise suggiyoḷoppuvantevōl // ViVi.1.8 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
ā sakaḷārtha saṁyutamaḷaṅkr̥tiyuktamudātta[vr̥tti]vi<br/>
nyāsamanēka lakṣaṇa guṇa prabhavaṁ mr̥du pādamāda vā<br/>
kśrī subhagaṁ kaḷākaḷitamemba negaḻteyanāḷda kabbamaṁ<br/>
kūsumanīvudīvudarikēsarigalladavastugīvudē // ViVi.1.9 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
kavigaḷa nāmadhāraka narādhiparōḷiyoḷītanoḷḷidaṁ<br/>
kavi nr̥panītanoḷḷidanenal doreyaltu negaḻtevetta sa<br/>
tkavigaḷa ṣōḍaśāvaniparōḷiyoḷaṁkavitāguṇārṇavaṁ<br/>
kaviteyoḷaggaḷam guṇadoḷaggaḷamelliyumā guṇārṇavaṁ // ViVi.1.10 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
kate piridādoḍaṁ kateyameygiḍalīyade muṁ samasta bhā<br/>
ratamanapūrvamāge sale pēḻda[kavīśvarari]lla varṇakaṁ<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 3]<br/>
kateyoḷoḍambaḍaṁ paḍeye pēḻvoḍe pampane pēḻgumendu paṁ<br/>
ḍitare taguḷdu biccaḻise pēḻaloḍarcidenī prabandhamaṁ // ViVi.1.11 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
lalitapadaṁ prasanna kavitāguṇamillade pūṇdu pēḻda be<br/>
ḷgaḷa kr̥tibandhamuṁ barepakāṟara kaigaḷa kēḍu nuṇṇana<br/>
ppaḷakada kēḍu pēḻisidoḍarthadakēḍene pēḻdu bīgi po<br/>
ṭṭaḷisi negaḻtegāṭisuva duṣkaviyuṁ kaviyemba lekkamē // ViVi.1.12 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
vyāsamunīndra rundra vacanāmr̥tavārdhiyanīsuveṁ kavi<br/>
vyāsanenemba garvamenagilla guṇārṇavanoḷpu manmanō<br/>
vāsamaneydepēḻdapenadalladegarvamedōṣamaḻtigaṁ<br/>
dōṣame kāṇenennaṟiva māḻkeye pēḻvenidāva dōṣamō // ViVi.1.13 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
vipuḷa yaśō vitāna guṇamilladanaṁ prabhu māḍi pūrva bhū<br/>
mipara padaṅgaḷaṁ pugisipōlipoḍītanudātta pūrva bhū<br/>
miparumanoḷpinoḷ taguḷevandoḍeyī katheyoḷ taguḷci pō<br/>
lipoḍenagaḻtiyādudu guṇārṇava bhūbhujanaṁ kirīṭiyoḷ // ViVi.1.14 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
śrīmaccaḷukya vaṁśa<br/>
vyōmāmr̥takiraṇanenipa kāntiyanoḷakoṁ<br/>
ḍī mahiyoḷātmavaṁśa śi<br/>
khāmaṇi jasameseyeyuddhamallaṁnegaḻdaṁ // ViVi.1.15 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
ātaṁ nija bhujavijaya<br/>
khyātiyanāḷdāḷdanadhikabalanavanipati<br/>
vrāta maṇimakuṭa kiraṇa<br/>
dyōtitapādaṁ sapādalakṣa kṣitiyaṁ // ViVi.1.16 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 4]<br/>
ēnaṁ pēḻvudo siriyu<br/>
ddāniyaneṇṇeyoḷe tīvi dīrghikegaḷanaṁ<br/>
tā nr̥pati niccalaynū<br/>
ṟāneyanavagāhamirisuvambōdanadoḷ // ViVi.1.17 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
śrīpatigeyuddhamallama<br/>
hīpatige negaḻte puṭṭe puṭṭidanakhiḷa<br/>
kṣmāpāla mauḷi maṇi kira<br/>
ṇāpāḷitanakhamayūkharañjita caraṇaṁ // ViVi.1.18 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
arikēsariyembaṁ suṁ<br/>
darāṅganatyanta vastuvaṁ madakariyaṁ<br/>
hariyaṁpaḍivaḍegurcida<br/>
karavāḷane tōṟi nr̥pati gellaṅgoṇḍaṁ // ViVi.1.19 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
nirupama dēvana rājyado<br/>
ḷarikēsariveṅgiviṣayamaṁ tri[kaḷiṅgaṁ]<br/>
berasottikoṇḍu garvade<br/>
bareyisidaṁ pesaranakhiḷa digbhattigaḷoḷ // ViVi.1.20 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
kṣatraṁ tējōguṇamā<br/>
kṣatriyaroḷ nelasi nindudā negaḻdādi<br/>
kṣatriyaroḷamillenisidu<br/>
dī trijagadoḷesagidesakamarikēsariyā // ViVi.1.21 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
arikēsarigātmajarari<br/>
narapa śirōdaḷana pariṇatōgrāsi bhayaṁ<br/>
karakararāyirvaroḷār<br/>
doreyene narasiṁha bhadradēvar negaḻdar // ViVi.1.22 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 5]<br/>
avaroḷ narasiṅgaṅgati<br/>
dhavaḷayaśaṁyuddhamallanagrasutaṁ ta<br/>
dbhuvanapradīpanāgi<br/>
rdavārya vīryaṅgebaddegaṁ piriya magaṁ // ViVi.1.23 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
puṭṭidoḍātanoḷaṟivoḍa<br/>
vuṭṭidudaṟiviṅge pempu pempinoḷāyaṁ<br/>
kaṭṭāyadoḷaḷavaḷavino<br/>
ḷoṭṭaje puṭṭidudu pōlvarār baddeganaṁ // ViVi.1.24 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
balvarikeyoḷari nr̥para pa<br/>
ḍalvaḍe taḷtiṟidu raṇadoḷā vikramamaṁ<br/>
solvinamāvarjisidaṁ<br/>
nālvatteraḍaṟikegāḷegaṅgaḷoḷītaṁ // ViVi.1.25 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
vanadhi parīta bhūtaḷadoḷītane sōlada gaṇḍanemba peṁ<br/>
pinapesaraṁnimircidudumallade vikramadinde nindagu<br/>
rvenaliṟidāntaraṁmosaḷeyaṁ piḍivantire nīroḷotti bhī<br/>
mananatigarvadiṁ piḍiyemeygali baddeganannanāvanō // ViVi.1.26 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
mugilaṁ muṭṭida pempu pempanoḷakoṇḍudyōgamudyōgadoḷ<br/>
negaḻdājñāphalamājñeyoḷ toḍardagurvondondagurvindagu<br/>
rvugoḷuttirparimaṇḍaḷaṁ jasakaḍarpappannegaṁ sandanī<br/>
jagadoḷ baddeganannanāvaniḻikuṁbhrūkōṭiyiṁkōṭiyaṁ // ViVi.1.27 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
mēruvapon kalpāṅghripa<br/>
dārave rasadoṟavuparusavēdiyakaṇi bhaṁ<br/>
ḍāradoḷuṇṭene kuḍuvani<br/>
vārita dānakke pōlvarār baddeganaṁ // ViVi.1.28 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 6]<br/>
surabhi dēvateyembakāpinemāṇdudēṟuvudondadeṁ<br/>
dirade māṇdududēva vāraṇavēḻeuṇṭavu pōdoḍā<br/>
kharakaraṅgaridendemāṇdi[re]māṇduvā hari nīne pē<br/>
ḻariyavendivu bhadradēvara cāgadoḷpoṟagāduvē // ViVi.1.29 [taraḷaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
ā baddegaṅge vairi ta<br/>
mōbaḷa daśaśatakaraṁ virājita vijaya<br/>
śrī bāhuyuddhamallani<br/>
ḷābahuvidharakṣaṇa pravīṇakr̥pāṇaṁ // ViVi.1.30 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
ātmabhavanā narādhipa<br/>
nātmajanānahuṣa pr̥thu bhagīratha naḷa mā<br/>
hātmaraniḻisi negaḻda ma<br/>
hātmaṁ narasiṁhanaṟivinoḷ paramātmaṁ> // ViVi.1.31 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
māṅkarisadaṟivu guru vaca<br/>
nāṅkuśamaṁ pāḻiyeḍege poṇardaribalamaṁ<br/>
kiṅkoḷemāḻpeḍegaṇameni<br/>
raṅkuśamenisidudu munisu bhadrāṅkuśanā // ViVi.1.32 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 7]<br/>
taṟisandu lāḻaroḷta<br/>
[ḷti]ṟidēṟaṁ pēḻe kēḷdumaṇḍalaminnuṁ<br/>
tiṟunīrikkuvudenisida<br/>
taṟisalavina calada balada kali narasiṁhaṁ // ViVi.1.33 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
siṅgaṁ masagidavōl nara<br/>
siṅgaṁ taḷtiṟiyenegaḻdanettar nabhadoḷ<br/>
keṅguḍi kavidantādudi<br/>
dēṁ garvada pemposakalalōkāśrayanā // ViVi.1.34 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
ēḻuṁ māḷamumaṁ pā<br/>
ṟēḻetaguḷdiṟidu naraganuripidoḍe kariṁ<br/>
kēḻisidātana tējada<br/>
bīḻalananukaripuvāduvogedurivurigaḷ // ViVi.1.35 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
vijayārambha purassara<br/>
vijaya gajaṅgaḷane piḍidu ghūrjara rāja<br/>
dhvajiniyaniṟidōḍisi bhuja<br/>
vijayade vijayanumaniḻisidaṁ narasiṁhaṁ // ViVi.1.36 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
siḍilavoleṟaguva naragana<br/>
paḍegagidummaḷadinuṇḍeḍeyoḷuṇṇadeyuṁ<br/>
keḍedeḍeyoḷkeḍeyade niṁ<br/>
deḍeyoḷ nilladeyumōḍidaṁ mahipālaṁ // ViVi.1.37 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
gaṅgāvārdhiyoḷātma tu<br/>
raṅgamumaṁ misisi negaḻdakāḷapriyanoḷ<br/>
saṅgata guṇanasilateyana<br/>
suṅgoḷe bhujavijaya garvadiṁ sthāpisidaṁ // ViVi.1.38 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 8]<br/>
ā narasiṁha mahīśa ma<br/>
nōnayana priye viḷōḷa nīḷāḷake caṁ<br/>
drānane jākavve dalā<br/>
jānakigaggaḷamekuladoḷaṁ śīladoḷaṁ // ViVi.1.39 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
posatalarda biḷiya tāvare<br/>
yesaḻgaḷa naḍuvirpa siriyumākeya keladoḷ<br/>
nasu masuḷdutōrpaḷenepō<br/>
lisuvoḍejākavveguḻida peṇḍir doreyē // ViVi.1.40 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
ā jākavvegamā vasu<br/>
dhājaya sadvallabhaṅgamati viśada yaśō<br/>
rājitaneniparikēsari<br/>
rājaṁ tējōgnimagnaripu nr̥paśalabhaṁ // ViVi.1.41 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
maganādanāgi cāgada<br/>
negaḻteyoḷ bīradēḻgeyoḷ negaḻe magaṁ<br/>
maganene puṭṭaloḍaṁkō<br/>
ḻmogagoṇḍudu bhuvana bhavanamarikēsariyoḷ // ViVi.1.42 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
madada nīroḷe lōkavārtege beccunīrdaḷidāgaḷā<br/>
madagajāṅkuśadinde percisi nābhiyaṁ madadanti daṁ<br/>
tadoḷe kaṭṭida toṭṭilaṁ nayadindamēṟisebāḷakā<br/>
ladoḷe toṭṭiligaṁ gajapriyanappudaṁ sale tōṟidaṁ // ViVi.1.43 [taraḷaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
rundrāmbhōdhi parīta ma<br/>
hīndraradārinnarī narēndraṁ sākṣā<br/>
dindraṁ tānene sale nega<br/>
ḻdindrēndrana tōḷe toṭṭilāgire baḷedaṁ // ViVi.1.44 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 9]<br/>
amita matiguṇadinati vi<br/>
krama guṇadiṁśāstrapāramuṁ ripubaḷapā<br/>
ramumoḍane sanduvenisida<br/>
namēya balaśālimanujamārtāṇḍa nr̥paṁ // ViVi.1.45 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
uḍevaṇipaṟiyada munname<br/>
toḍagi calaṁ negaḻe ripu balaṅgaḷane paḍa<br/>
lvaḍisi parabalada nettara<br/>
kaḍaloḷagaṇa jiguḷe baḷeva teṟadoḷe baḷedaṁ // ViVi.1.46 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
mēleḻdabalaṁkōṭige<br/>
mēlappoḍamanya vanite negaḻdūrvaśigaṁ<br/>
mēlappoḍamakkenduṁ<br/>
sōlavu kaṇ para balābdhigaṁ para vadhugaṁ // ViVi.1.47 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
dhuradoḷ mūṟuṁ lōkaṁ<br/>
neredireyuṁ kuḍuvapo[ḻta]ṟoḷmēruve muṁ<br/>
direyuṁ bīrada biyadaṁ<br/>
tarakke kiṟidendu cintipaṁ priyagaḷḷaṁ // ViVi.1.48 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
samanenisuva[r]praśasti<br/>
kramadoḷ svasti samadhigata pañcamahāśa<br/>
bdamahāsāmantarenal<br/>
samanenipare guṇadoḷariganoḷ sāmantar // ViVi.1.49 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
cāgada kambamaṁ niṟisi bīrada śāsanamaṁ negaḻci kō<br/>
ḷpōgada maṇḍalaṅgaḷane koṇḍu jagattritayaṅgaḷoḷ jasa<br/>
kkāgaramāda baddeganinā narasiṁhaninatta nālveral<br/>
mēgupodaḻda cāgadoḷamondida bīradoḷaṁ guṇārṇavaṁ // ViVi.1.50 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 10]<br/>
ene sanduṁ vīra vairi kṣitipa gaja ghaṭāṭōpa kumbhasthaḷī bhē<br/>
dananugrō[dghā]si bhāsvadbhujaparighananārūḍhasarvajñanaṁ vai<br/>
rinarēndrōddāmadarpōddaḷanananekathānāyakaṁ māḍi sanda<br/>
rjunanoḷ pōlvī kathā bhittiyananunayadiṁ pēḻalendettikoṇḍeṁ // ViVi.1.51 [mahāsragdhare]<br/>
</p>

<p>
andentene – samunmiṣadvividharatnamālā prabhābhīlāruṇa<br/>
jalaplavāviḷa viḷōḷavīcīrayapradārita kuḷācalōdadhi parītamāgirda<br/>
jambūdvīpadoḷaguṇṭu nāḍu kurujāṅgaṇa nāmadiṁ antā kurujāṅgaṇa viṣayadoḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
jala jalanoḻkutirpa parikāl parikāloḷaḷurkegoṇḍa nai<br/>
dila posavū podaḻda posa naidila kampane bīṟe kāyta keṁ<br/>
goleyoḷe jōlva śāḷinavaśāḷige pāyva śukāḷi tōṟe ke<br/>
yvolagaḷinoppitōṟisiri nōḍugumā viṣayāntarāḷadoḷ // ViVi.1.52 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
beḷedeṟagirda keyvolane keyvolanaṁ baḷasirda pūta pū<br/>
goḷagaḷe pūtapūgoḷagaḷaṁ baḷasirda vicitra nandanā<br/>
vaḷigaḷe nandanāvaḷigaḷaṁ baḷasirda madāḷisaṅkulaṁ<br/>
gaḷe viṣayāṅganā luḷita kuntaḷadantevoloppi tōṟuguṁ // ViVi.1.53 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 11]<br/>
laḷita vicitra patra phala puṣpayutāṭavi sorkidāneyaṁ<br/>
beḷevududēvamātr̥kamenippa polaṁ nava gandha śāḷiyaṁ<br/>
beḷevudu ramya nandanavanāḷi viyōgi janakke bēṭamaṁ<br/>
baḷevudu nāḍa kāḍa beḷasimbeḷasā viṣayāntarāḷadoḷ // ViVi.1.54 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āvalaruṁ paṇṇuṁ bī<br/>
tōvavu gaḍa bīyavalli malligegaḷumi<br/>
mmāvugaḷumendoḍiṁpeṟa<br/>
tāvudu saṁsāra sāra sarvasva phalaṁ // ViVi.1.55 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
miḍidoḍe tanigarvurasaṁ<br/>
biḍuvuvu biridondu muguḷa kampinoḷe mogaṁ<br/>
giḍuvuvu tumbigaḷaḻkame<br/>
vaḍuvuvu kuḍidondu paṇṇa rasadoḷe giḷigaḷ // ViVi.1.56 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
suttiṟida rasada toṟegaḷe<br/>
muttina māṇikada palavumāgarame madō<br/>
nmatta madakari vanaṅgaḷe<br/>
suttalumā nelada siriyanēnaṁ pogaḻveṁ // ViVi.1.57 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu sogayisuva kurujāṅgaṇa viṣayakke rājadrājadhāniyāgirdu<br/>
hara jaṭājūṭakke candralēkheyirpantedikkarikaṭa taṭakkemadalēkheyirpante<br/>
kaiṭabhārātiya viśālōrasthaḷakke kaustubhamirpante sogayisutirdudu hastinapura<br/>
vembudu poḻalalli—<br/>
</p>

<p>
adaṟa poṟavoḻala viśāḷa kanaka kr̥taka girigaḷiṁ phaḷaprakīrṇatarugaḷiṁ<br/>
naneya koneya taḷira muguḷa vanalatānikuñjadiṁprasūna rajada puñjadiṁ<br/>
gaganataḷame paṟidu biḻdudenipa bahu taṭākadiṁ kukilva naliva kōkadiṁ<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 12]<br/>
suriva surayiyarala muguḷge mogasidaḷikuḷaṅgaḷiṁtoda[lva]śiśu śukaṅgaḷiṁ<br/>
tegeye bīra ravadamēlepariva madagajagaḷiṁ caḷatturaṅga maṅgaḷiṁ<br/>
lavaṇa jaḷadhi baḷasidante baḷasidagaḻa nīḷadindudagrakanaka śāḷadiṁ<br/>
doḷage kula nagaṅgaḷenipa dēvakulada bhōgadiṁ sarāgamāda rāgadiṁ<br/>
divamanēḷipantu miḷirva vividha kētanaṅgaḷiṁ sadānikētanaṅgaḷiṁ<br/>
dhanada bhavanamenipa siriya baccarāpaṇaṅgaḷiṁpodaḻda[kāva]ṇaṅgaḷiṁ<br/>
viṭajanakke toḍarva cāriyenipa sūḷegēriyiṁ vidagdha hr̥daya hāriyiṁ<br/>
kanaka gōpuraṅgaḷoḷagaṇeraḍu deseyaguṇaṇeyiṁ viḷāsiniyara gaḍaṇeyiṁ<br/>
suratasukhada baḷḷavaḷḷiyenipa baḷḷimāḍadiṁ mahāvinōda nīḍadiṁ<br/>
kanakaśailamenisi negaḻda bhūmipāla bhavanadiṁ samasta vastu bhuvanadiṁ // ViVi.1.58 [ragaḷe]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu mūṟu lōkada celvellamaṁ vidhātranondeḍege teraḷcidante samasta<br/>
vastu vistāra hāramāgirda hastinapurave nijavaṁśāvaḷambamāge negaḻda<br/>
bharatakulatilakara vaṁśāvatāramentādudendoḍe—<br/>
</p>

<p>
jaḷaruhanābhana nābhiya<br/>
jaḷa budbudadoḷage surabhi parimaḷa miḷitō<br/>
lluḷitāḷijala[ja]māytā<br/>
jaḷa[ja]doḷogedaṁhiraṇyagarbha brahmaṁ // ViVi.1.59 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
kamalōdbhavanamaḷina hr̥<br/>
tkamaladoḷogedar‌ surēndradhārakarāvā<br/>
gamaḷarnegaḻdirdarpula<br/>
hamarīcyatryaṅgiraḥ puḷastya kratugaḷ // ViVi.1.60 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 13]<br/>
antu hiraṇyagarbha brahma manassambhavadoḷ puṭṭidaṟuvarmakkaḷoḷage<br/>
marīciya magaṁ kaśyapananēka bhuvanōtpatti nāṭakakke sūtradhāranādanātana<br/>
maganavāryavīryaṁ sūryanātanindavyavacchinnamāgi banda vaṁśaṁ<br/>
sūryavaṁśamembudāytu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
atriya piriya magaṁ bhava<br/>
natraya saṅgītakīrti sōmaṁ sakala<br/>
kṣatrakulapūjyanamaḷa ca<br/>
ritraṁ prōddāma sōmavaṁśalalāmaṁ // ViVi.1.61 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
ā sōmavaṁśajar pala<br/>
rāsukaraṁ berasu negaḻda jasadiṁ jagamaṁ<br/>
bāsaṇisi pōdoḍadhika vi<br/>
ḷāsaṁ dauṣyanti bharatanembaṁ negaḻdaṁ // ViVi.1.62 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
cāru caritraṁ bharatana<br/>
pāraguṇaṁ tanna pesaroḷamardeseye yaśō<br/>
bhāraṁ kulamuṁ katheyuṁ<br/>
bhāratamene negaḻdanantu negaḻvudubhūpar // ViVi.1.63 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
bharatananēkādhvara bhara<br/>
nirataṁ jasamuḻiye kaḻiye bhūpar palarā<br/>
darisida dharaṇī bharamaṁ<br/>
dhariyisidaṁ pratimanembanapratima balaṁ // ViVi.1.64 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antā pratimaṅge sutar<br/>
śantanu bāhlika vinūta dēvāpigaḷō<br/>
rantedhare pogaḻe negaḻdara<br/>
nanta baḷa‌r parabaḷa prabhēdana śaurya‌r // ViVi.1.65 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 14]<br/>
avaroḷage dēvāpi nava yauvana prārambhadoḷe tapaścaraṇa parāyaṇanādaṁ<br/>
pratimanuṁpratāpa prasara prakaṭapaṭuvāgi palavu kālamarasugeydu saṁsārāsāratege<br/>
pēsi tapōvanakkabhimukhanāgalbagedu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
kantuśara bhava[na]nāpriya<br/>
kāntā bhrūvibhrama grahāgrahavaśadiṁ<br/>
bhrāntisadupaśānta manaṁ<br/>
śantanugittaṁ samasta rājyaśrīyaṁ // ViVi.1.66 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
śantanugamamaḷa gaṅgā<br/>
kāntegameṇṭaneya vasu vasiṣṭhana śāpa<br/>
bhrāntiyoḷe bandu nirjita<br/>
kantuvenalkantu puṭṭidaṁ gāṅgēyaṁ // ViVi.1.67 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu bhuvanakkellamāyamumaḷavumaṟimaṇmuṁ puṭṭuvante puṭṭi<br/>
navayauvanaṁ neṟeya neṟeye—<br/>
</p>

<p>
sālaprāṁśu viśālalōlanayanaṁ prōdyadvr̥ṣaskandhanu<br/>
nmīlatpaṅkajavaktranāyata samagrōrasthaḷaṁ dīrgha bā<br/>
hālambaṁ bhujavīrya vikramayutaṁgaṅgātmajanmaṁ jaya<br/>
śrīlōlaṁjamadagnirāmamuniyoḷ kaltaṁ dhanurvidyeyaṁ // ViVi.1.68 [śārdūlavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu kaltu munname cāpavidyeyoḷārindamītanebhārgavanenisida<br/>
bhārgavaṅge tāne bhārgavanāgi yuvarājakaṇṭhikā parikalita kaṇṭhaluṇṭhanumāgi<br/>
pramāṇa nija bhuja daṇḍadaṇḍitārāti maṇḍalanumāgi gāṅgēyaṁ<br/>
sukhadoḷarasugeyyuttirpannegamitta gaṅgādēśadoḷuparicaravasuvembarasaṁ puṭṭida<br/>
girijeyemba kanneyanātaṁ kaṇḍu kaṇbēṭaṅgoṇḍu maduveyaṁ nindondu divasa<br/>
mindranōlagakke pōgi r̥tukālaprāpteyāgirda nallaḷallige baral paḍeya<br/>
dākeyaṁ nenedindriya kṣaraṇeyādoḍadanondu kadaḷīpatradoḷ pudidu tanna<br/>
naḍapida giḷiya kaiyoḷōpaḷalligaṭṭidoḍadaṁ tarparagiḷiya nondu<br/>
[p. 15]<br/>
giḍuganeḍegoṇḍu jaguneyaṁ pāyvāgaḷugibagi māḍidāgaḷadaṟa kaiyiṁ barduṅki<br/>
toṟeyoḷage biḻdoḍadanondu bāḷemīnnuṅgi garbhamaṁ tāḷdidoḍondu<br/>
divasamā mīnanorva jālagāṟaṁ jāladoḷ piḍidalligarasappa dāśanalliguydu<br/>
tōṟidoḍadaṁ vidārisi nōḻpannegaṁ bāḷeya garbhadoḷirda bāḷeyaṁ bāḷanumaṁ<br/>
kaṇḍettikoṇḍu matsyagandhiyuṁ matsyagandhanumendu pesaraniṭṭu naḍapi<br/>
yamunānadītīradoḷirpannegamalligorme brahmara mommanappa vr̥dda<br/>
parāśara munīndranuttarāpathakke pōguttuṁ bandu toṟeya taḍiyoḷōḍamaṁ<br/>
naḍeyisuva matsyagandhiyaṁ kaṇḍemmanī toṟeyaṁ pāyisembuduṁ sāsirvarēṟi<br/>
doḍalladīyōḍaṁ naḍeyadembudamāmanibara biṇpumappemēṟisendoḍante<br/>
geyvenendōḍamēṟisi naḍeyisuvalli divya kanneyanaḻkartu nōḍi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
manadoḷ sōltu munīndranākeyoḍalī durgandhavōpanteyō<br/>
janagandhitvamanittu kāṇḍa paṭadantirpannegaṁ māḍi maṁ<br/>
janalampaḻkaṟanīye kūḍuveḍeyoḷ jñānasvarūpaṁ mahā<br/>
munipaṁ puṭṭidanantu divya munigaḷgēgeydoḍaṁ tīradē // ViVi.1.69 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu nīlāmbuda śyāmanuṁ kanakapiṅgaḷa jaṭābandhakaḷāpanuṁ daṇḍa<br/>
kapāḷahastanuṁ kr̥ṣṇa mr̥gatyakparidhānanumāgi vyāsabhaṭṭārakaṁ puṭṭuvudu<br/>
mātananoḍagoṇḍu satyavatige punaḥ kanyābhāvamaṁ dayegeydu parāśaraṁ<br/>
pōdanittal—<br/>
</p>

<p>
mr̥gayā vyājadinorme śantanu toḻaltarpaṁ paḷañcalke ta<br/>
nmr̥gaśābākṣiya kampu taṭṭi madhupambōlsōltu kaṇḍoldu na<br/>
lmege dibyambiḍivantevōl piḍidu nīn bā pōpamendaṅge me<br/>
llage tatkanyake nāṇci bēḍuvoḍe nīvemmayyanaṁ bēḍirē // ViVi.1.70 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 16]<br/>
embuduṁ śantanu poḻalge maguḻdu vandavarayyanappa dāśarājanallige<br/>
kūsaṁ bēḍa pergaḍegaḷanaṭṭidoḍe gāṅgēyaṁ doreya piriya maganuṁ<br/>
kramakramārhanumirdantenna magaḷaṁkuḍevemmamagaḷge puṭṭidātaṁ rājya<br/>
kkoḍeyanuṁ piriya maganuṁ kramakkarhanumappoḍe kuḍuvemene tadvr̥ttāntamaṁ<br/>
mantrigaḷiṁ śantanu kēḷdu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
kramamaṁ vikramadinde tāḷduva magaṁ gāṅgēyanirdante nō<br/>
ḍa maruḷ śantanu tannadondu savigaṁ sōlakkamittaṁ nija<br/>
kramamaṁ tannaya bēṭadākeya magaṅgembondapakhyāti lō<br/>
kamanāvartise biḻdoḍenna kulamuṁ takkūrmeyuṁ māsadē // ViVi.1.71 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu tanna nāṇgāpane bagedatanu paritāpitaśarīranumāgi śantanu<br/>
karaṅgerdegiḍe tadvr̥ttāntamellamaṁ gāṅgēyanaṟidu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
ennaya dūsaṟiṁ nr̥pati bēḍidudaṁ kuḍalolladaṅgajō<br/>
tpanna vimōhadindaḻidapaṁ pati sattoḍe satta pāpame<br/>
nnannarakaṅgaḷoḷ taḍeyadaḻdugumēvudu rājyalakṣmi pō<br/>
tannaya tandeyendudane koṭṭu vivāhamaninde māḍuveṁ // ViVi.1.72 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu niścayisi gāṅgēyaṁ dāśarājanallige vandātana manada toḍarpaṁ<br/>
piṅge nuḍidu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
nīḍiradīvudī nija tanūjeyanī vadhugāda putraroḷ<br/>
kūḍuge rājyalakṣmi moṟeyaltenagantadu peṇḍirembaroḷ<br/>
kūḍuvanallenindu modalāgire nikkuvamendu rāgadiṁ<br/>
kūḍidanuydu satyavatiyaṁsatiyaṁ patiyoḷnadīsutaṁ // ViVi.1.73 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu śantanuvuṁ satyavatiyumanyonyāsaktacittarāgikelavu kālamirpanne<br/>
gamavara bēṭadakandalgaḷante citrāṅgada vicitravīryaremba makkaḷ puṭṭi mahā<br/>
pracaṇḍaruṁ pratāpigaḷumāgi baḷeyuttirpannegaṁ śantanu paralōka prāptanādoḍe<br/>
gāṅgēyaṁ taducita paralōka kriyegaḷaṁ māḍi munne tanna nuḍida nuḍivaḷiyemba<br/>
[p. 17]<br/>
prāsādakkadhiṣṭhānaṅgaṭṭuvante citrāṅgadaṅge paṭṭamaṁ kaṭṭi rājyaṁgeyisuttu<br/>
mirpannegamorva gandharvanoḷe citrāṅgadaṁ dvandvayuddhamaṁ poṇarci<br/>
kurukṣētramaṁ kaḷambēḻdu kādi sattoḍe vicitravīryanaṁ gāṅgēyaṁ<br/>
dharābhāradhurandharanaṁ māḍi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
sakaḷa kṣatriya mōhadiṁ nijabhuja prārambhadiṁ pōgi tā<br/>
gikelar‌ nondoḍekādi rājasutaroḷtannaṅkadondugrasā<br/>
yakadiṁ nāyakaraṁ paḍalvaḍisutuṁ tāṁ tandanandambeyaṁ<br/>
bikeyambāleyaremba bāleyaranēṁbhīṣmaṁ yaśō bhāgiyō // ViVi.1.74 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu tandu tanna tammaṁ vicitravīryaṅgā mūvarkanneyaraṁ<br/>
pāṇigrahaṇaṅge yvāgaḷellariṁ piriyāke ninnanallade peṟaranollenendirdoḍe<br/>
mattinirvarumaṁ maduveyaṁ māḍi gāṅgēyanambeyanintendaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
atra surēśvarāvasathamitta mahītaḷamutta pannagō<br/>
dātta samasta lōkamaṟidantire pūṇdenagāgadaṅgajō<br/>
tpatti sukhakkesōlalaḻiguṁ puruṣavratamīgaḷabbeyeṁ<br/>
dattigeyemba mātanenagēnenalakkumo paṅkajānanē // ViVi.1.75 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu nuḍida gāṅgēyana nuḍiyoḷavasaramaṁ pasaramaṁ paḍeyade tanage<br/>
kiṟiyanduṅguraviṭṭasālvalanembarasanallige pōgi nīnennaṁ kaikoḷa<br/>
vēḻkumendoḍātanintendaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
baṇḍaṇadoḷennanōḍisi<br/>
koṇḍuydaṁ ninnanā saritsutanānuṁ<br/>
peṇḍatiyenādenadaṟiṁ<br/>
peṇḍir peṇḍiroḷadentu berasuvarabalē // ViVi.1.76 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu sālvalaṁ tanna paribhavadoḷāda siggaṁ sālvinamuṇṭu<br/>
māḍidoḍātana manamanoḍambaḍisalāṟade paraśurāmanallige pōgi bhīṣmanenna<br/>
[p. 18]<br/>
svayaṁvaradoḷ neredarasumakkaḷellarumanōḍisikoṇḍu bandenna[ṁ]maduveyaṁ<br/>
nilalolladaṭṭi kaḷedoḍenna devasamuṁ javvanamumaḍaviyoḷage pūta pūvinante<br/>
kiḍalīyadātananennaṁ pāṇigrahaṇaṁ geyvantu māḍu māḍalāṟadoḍe kiccaṁ<br/>
dayegeyvudendambe kaṇṇanīraṁ tumbe—<br/>
</p>

<p>
nayamaṁnambuvoḍenna pēḻva satiyaṁ kaikoṇḍanaṁtalladu<br/>
rṇayamaṁ naccuvoḍennanugra raṇadoḷ mēṇ mīṟi mārkoṇḍanā<br/>
raye kajjaṁ peṟatilla śantanu sutaṅgennaṁ karaṁ nambidaṁ<br/>
beyoḷennabevalaṁ vivāhavidhiyaṁ māḻpeṁ peṟar māḻparē // ViVi.1.77 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu nāgapurakke varpa paraśurāmana baravaṁ gāṅgēyaṁ kēḷdirvandu<br/>
kanaka rajata pātraṅgaḷoḷarghyamaṁ koṭṭu poḍamaṭṭu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
besanēnendoḍe pēḻvenenna besanaṁ kaikoḷvudī kanneyaṁ<br/>
pasurvandar paseyembivaṁ samedu nīṁ kaikoḷ koḷalkāgadeṁ<br/>
besakaṁ cittadoḷuḷḷoḍīgaḷivaremmācāryareṁdōvadē<br/>
rvesanaṁ māṇade kaidugoḷḷeraḍaṟoḷ meccittenēnendapay // ViVi.1.78 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu nuḍida paraśurāmana nuḍiyaṁ gāṅgēyaṁ kēḷdenage vīraśrīyuṁ<br/>
kīrtiśrīyumalladuḻida peṇḍir moṟeyalli nīvidanēkāgrahaṁ geyvireṁ<br/>
doḍentumemmoḷ kādalvēḻvudendu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
keḷardandugra raṇāgrahapraṇayadindāgaḷ kurukṣētamaṁ<br/>
kaḷavēḻdirvarumaindra vāruṇade vāyavyādi divyāstra saṁ<br/>
kuḷadindorvaranorvareccu nija pīṭhāmbhōjadiṁ brahmanu<br/>
ccaḷipannaṁ piridondu saṅkaṭamanī trailōkyadoḷ māḍidar // ViVi.1.79 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 19]<br/>
atarkyaṁ vikrāntaṁ bhujabalamasāmānyamadhikaṁ<br/>
pratāpaṁ pōgītaṅgeṇeye divijarvāyupathadoḷ<br/>
śitāstraṅgaḷpoṁ[ka]ṅgiḍisesugidaṁ bhārgavanidēṁ<br/>
pratijñāgāṅgēyaṅgadiradidirnilvannaroḷarē // ViVi.1.80 [śikhariṇi]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu gāṅgēyanoḷ paraśurāmaṁ kādi basavaḻidusiralappoḍamāṟade<br/>
mūrchevōgirdanaṁ kaṇḍambeyembadaṇḍurumbe ninage vadhārthamāgipuṭṭuve<br/>
nakkendukōpāgniyindamagniśarīreyāgi drupadana mahādēvige maganāgi puṭṭi<br/>
kāraṇāntaradoḷ śikhaṇḍiyāgirdaḷitta bhīṣmara bembaladoḷ vicitravīryanu<br/>
mavāryavīryanumāgi kelavu kālaṁ rājyalakṣiyaṁ tāḷdi rājayakṣmataptaśarīranātmaja vigatajīviyāgi paralōka prāptanādoḍe gāṅgēyanuṁ<br/>
satyavatiyumatyanta śōkānala dahyamāna mānasarkaḷāgi ātaṅge paralōkakriyegaḷaṁ<br/>
māḍi rājyaṁ naṣṭarājamādudarkemammalamaṟugi yōjanagandhi<br/>
sindhuputrananintendaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
maganembantu dharitri ninnanujaraṁ kaikoṇḍu muṁ pūṇda na<br/>
nnige bannaṁ baralīyadārtesagidī vikhyātiyuṁ kīrtiyuṁ<br/>
mugilaṁ muṭṭidudalte namma kuladoḷ makkaḷpeṟar nīnē ja<br/>
ṭṭiganai munninoraṇṭuvēḍa maganēkaikoḷ dharābhāramaṁ // ViVi.1.81 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu ninnanāninitaṁ kaiyoḍḍi bēḍidenenda satyavatigamarāpagā<br/>
nandananintendaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
kiḍugume rājyaṁ rājyada<br/>
toḍarpadēvāḻte nanniyanuḍiyaṁ<br/>
kiḍe negaḻe nānumeraḍaṁ<br/>
nuḍidoḍe hari hara hiraṇyagarbhar nagarē // ViVi.1.82 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 20]<br/>
himakaranātma śītaruciyaṁ dinanāyakanuṣṇa dīdhiti<br/>
kramamanagādhavāridhiyeguṇpaniḷāvadhu tanna tiṇpanu<br/>
ttamakulaśailamunnatiyanēḷidavāge bisuḻpoḍaṁ bisu<br/>
[ḻkema]bisuḍeṁmadīya puruṣavratamondumanīgaḷambikē // ViVi.1.83 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu tanna nuḍida pratijñeyanēgeyduṁ tappidanilla—<br/>
</p>

<p>
raṅgattaraṅga vārdhica<br/>
yaṅgaḷ tantammamēreyaṁ dāṇṭuvoḍaṁ<br/>
gāṅgēyanuṁ pratijñā<br/>
gāṅgēyanumorme nuḍidudaṁ tappuvarē // ViVi.1.84 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antacalita pratijñārūḍhanāda gāṅgēyananēgeydumoḍambaḍisalāṟade<br/>
satyavati tānumātanumāḷōcisi niścita mantrarāgi kr̥ṣṇadvaipāyananaṁ nenedu<br/>
barisidoḍe vyāsamunīndranēgeyvudēnaṁ tīrcuvudendoḍe satyavatiyintendaḷ<br/>
hiraṇyagarbha brahmariṁ taguḷdavyavacchinnamāgi banda sōmavaṁśamīgaḷemma<br/>
kulasantatigamārumilladeḍe vaṟidu kiḍuvantāgirdudadu kāraṇadiṁ nimma tammaṁ<br/>
vicitravīryana kṣētradoḷambikegamambālegaṁ putrarappantu varaprasādamaṁ<br/>
dayegeyvudene antegeyvenendu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
tridaśa narāsurōraga gaṇa prabhu niścita tattvayōgi yō<br/>
gada balamuṇmi poṇmi nile putra varārthigaḷāgi tanna ka<br/>
ṭṭidiroḷe nindaraṁ nayade nōḍe munīndrana divya dr̥ṣṭi maṁ<br/>
tradoḷe podaḻdudā satiyarirvaroḷaṁ nava garbha vibhramaṁ // ViVi.1.85 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu divya saṁyōgadoḷirvaruṁ garbhamaṁ tāḷdar mattorva maganaṁ<br/>
varamaṁ bēḍendambikege pēḻdoḍākeyuṁ vyāsabhaṭṭārakanallige pōgalalasi tanna<br/>
sūḻāyteyaṁtannavole kaygeydu baravaṁ bēḍalaṭṭidoḍākege varadanāgi<br/>
vyāsamunīndraṁ satyavatigaṁ bhīṣmaṅgamintendanenna vara prasāda kāladoḷennaṁ<br/>
[p. 21]<br/>
kaṇḍambike kaṇṇaṁ muccidaḷappudaṟindākege dhr̥tarāṣṭranemba maganatyanta<br/>
sundarāṅganāgiyuṁ jātyandhanakkumambāle madrūpamaṁ kaṇḍu mogamaṁ<br/>
pāṇḍuraṁ māḍidaḷappudaṟindākege pāṇḍurōga saṅgatanumanēka bhadra lakṣaṇa<br/>
lakṣitanumatyanta pratāpanumāgi pāṇḍurājanemba maganakkumambikeya<br/>
sūḻāyteyappāke darahasita vadanāravindeyāgi baravaṁ kaikoṇḍaḷappudaṟindākeya<br/>
magaṁ viduranembananaṅgākāranumācāravantanuṁ buddhivantanumakkumendu pēḻdu<br/>
munipuṅgavaṁ pōdanittaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
varambaḍeda santasaṁ manadoḷāgalonduttarō<br/>
ttaraṁ baḷeva māḻkeyiṁ baḷeva garbhamaṁ tāḷdiyā<br/>
daraṁ berasu pettarandu dhr̥tarāṣṭra vikhyāta pāṁ<br/>
ḍurāja vidurarkaḷaṁ kramade mūvaruṁ mūvaraṁ // ViVi.1.86 [pr̥thvi]<br/>
</p>

<p>
ā vividha lakṣaṇaṅgaḷo<br/>
ḷāvarisida kulada balada caladaḷavigaḷoḷ<br/>
mūvarumanādi puruṣar<br/>
mūvarumenalalladattamattēnembar‌ // ViVi.1.87 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antavarge jātakarma nāmakaraṇānnaprāśana caulōpanayanādiṣōḍaśa<br/>
kriyegaḷaṁ gāṅgēyaṁ tāṁ muntiṭṭu māḍi śastra śāstraṅgaḷoḷati pariṇataraṁ<br/>
māḍi maduveyaṁ māḍalendu dhr̥tarāṣṭaṅge gāndhārarāja saubalana<br/>
magaḷappa gāndhāriyaṁ śakuniyoḍavuṭṭidaḷaṁ tandukoṭṭu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
mattitta negaḻteya puru<br/>
ṣōttamana pitāmahaṅgeśūraṅgemagaḷ<br/>
mattagajagamane yadu vaṁ<br/>
śōttameyene kunti kuntibhōjana maneyoḷ // ViVi.1.88 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 22]<br/>
baḷeyuttirpannegamā<br/>
naḷināsyeya geydudondu śuśrūṣe manaṁ<br/>
goḷe koṭṭaṁdurvāsaṁ<br/>
viḷasita mantrākṣaraṅgaḷaṁ dayeyindaṁ // ViVi.1.89 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu koṭṭaydu mantrākṣaraṅgaḷanāhvānaṅgeydu ninna bagege banda<br/>
pōlveya makkaḷaṁ paḍeveyendu besasidoḍondu divasaṁ konti—<br/>
</p>

<p>
puccavaṇaṁ nōḍuvene<br/>
nnicceyoḷī muniya varada mahimeyanenutaṁ<br/>
duccastani gaṅgege śapha<br/>
rōccaḷita tarattaraṅgegorvaḷe bandaḷ // ViVi.1.90 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
bandu suranadiya nīroḷ<br/>
mindinanaṁ nōḍi ninna doreyane magana<br/>
kkendāhvānaṅgeyyalo<br/>
ḍaṁ dal dharegiḻidanandu daśaśatakiraṇaṁ // ViVi.1.91 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu nabhōbhāgadiṁ bhūmibhāgakkiḻidu tanna munde nindaravinda<br/>
bāndhavanaṁ nōḍi nōḍi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
koḍagūsutanada bhayadiṁ<br/>
naḍuguva kannikeya bemara nīrgaḷa ponalo<br/>
ḻkuḍiyaloḍagūḍegaṅgeya<br/>
maḍu karegaṇmidudu nāṇa pempēṁ piridō // ViVi.1.92 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgaḷādityanākeya manada śaṅkeyamaṁ naḍuguva meyya naḍukamumaṁ<br/>
kiḍenuḍidintendaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
barisida kāraṇamāvudo<br/>
taruṇi munīśvarana mantramē doreyendā[ṁ]<br/>
maruḷiyeneyaṟidumaṟiyade |<br/>
barisideninnēḻimendoḍāgadu pōgal // ViVi.1.93 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 23]<br/>
muṁ bēḍida varamaṁ kuḍa<br/>
dambujamukhi putranenna doreyaṁ ninaga<br/>
kkembudumodavida garbhado<br/>
ḷambujamitranane pōlva maganogetandaṁ // ViVi.1.94 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
oḍavuṭṭida maṇikuṇḍala<br/>
moḍavuṭṭida sahaja kavacamamardire tannoḷ<br/>
toḍardireyuṁ bandākeya<br/>
naḍukamanoḍarisida[nā]gaḷā bā[likeyā] // ViVi.1.95 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu naḍanaḍa naḍugi jaladēvategaḷappoḍaṁ manaṅgāṇbarendu nidhāna<br/>
manīḍāḍuvante kūsaṁ gaṅgeyoḷīḍāḍi bandaḷitta gaṅgādēviyumā kūsaṁ<br/>
muḻugalīyade tanna teregaḷemba naḷitōḷgaḷinoyyanoyyane taḻkaisi tare<br/>
gaṅgātīradoḷirpa sūtanembavaṁ kaṇḍu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
bāḷa dinēśa bimbada neḻal jaladoḷ nelasittomēṇ phaṇīṁ<br/>
drāḷayadindamurcidaphaṇāmaṇi maṅgaḷa raśmiyō karaṁ<br/>
mēḷisidappudennerdeyanendu bodillene pāydu nīroḷā<br/>
bāḷananādamādarade kaṇḍosedaṁ nidhigaṇḍanantevōl // ViVi.1.96 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu kaṇḍu manaṅgoṇḍettikoṇḍu manege tandu rādheyemba tanna nallaḷa<br/>
sōṅkiloḷ kūsaniṭṭoḍāke rāgisi sutana sūtakamaṅkoṇḍāḍe—<br/>
</p>

<p>
aguḻdiralā kuḻiyoḷ to<br/>
ṭṭage nidhigaṇḍante vasudhegasadaḷamāytā<br/>
maga[na]ndamendu[lōgar]<br/>
bagedire vasuṣēṇanemba pesarāytāgaḷ // ViVi.1.97 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu vasuṣēṇanālō<br/>
kāntambaramaḷavi baḷeye baḷadesakamadō<br/>
rante janaṅgaḷakarṇō<br/>
pāntadoḷogedeseye karṇanembanumādaṁ // ViVi.1.98 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 24]<br/>
āgiyātaṁ śastraśāstra vidyeyoḷati pariṇatanāgi navayauvanārambhadoḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
poḍedudu billa jēvoḍeye mīṟuva vairi narēndraraṁ siḍi<br/>
lvoḍedavolaṭṭi muṭṭi kaḍidikkidudādeḍaraṁ nirantaraṁ<br/>
kaḍikaḍidittaponne budhamāgadhavandi janakke koṭṭa kō<br/>
ḍeḍarade bēḍiresp="#ed">mōḍimidu cāgada bīrada mātu karṇanā // ViVi.1.99 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu bhuvana bhavanakkellaṁ negaḻda karṇana pogaḻteyaṁ negaḻteyumanindraṁ<br/>
kēḷdu munde tannaṁśadoḷ puṭṭuvarjunaṅgamātaṅgaṁ dvandva yuddhamuṇṭembudaṁ<br/>
tanna divya jñānadindamaṟiduvintalladītananātaṁ gelal bāradendu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
bēḍidoḍe balada bariyuva<br/>
nīḍāḍugumugidu karṇanendāgaḷe kai<br/>
gūḍida vaṭuvākr̥tiyoḷe<br/>
bēḍidanā sahaja kavacamaṁ kuṇḍaḷamaṁ // ViVi.1.100 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
bēḍidudanaridukoḷḷene<br/>
bēḍidudaṁ muṭṭalāgadenagene negaḻda<br/>
llāḍade koḷḷendaridī<br/>
ḍāḍidanidraṅge kavacamaṁ rādhēyaṁ // ViVi.1.101 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
enduṁ pōgendane mā<br/>
ṇendane peṟatondanīvenendane nondaḥ<br/>
endane seragillade piḍi<br/>
yendanidēṁ kaliyo cāgiyō ravitanayaṁ // ViVi.1.102 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu tanna sahaja kavacamaṁ nettar pana pana pariye tidiyugivantugidu<br/>
koṭṭoḍindranātana kalitanake mecci—<br/>
</p>

<p>
sura danuja bhujaga vidyā<br/>
dhara narasaṅkuladoḷāranādoḍamēnō<br/>
garamuṭṭe kolgamidu nija<br/>
virōdhiyaṁ dhuradoḷendu śaktiyanittaṁ // ViVi.1.103 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 25]<br/>
antindranitta śaktiyaṁ kaikoṇḍu nijabhujaśaktiyaṁ prakaṭaṁ māḍalendu<br/>
rēṇukānandananallige pōgi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
kūriseguru śuśrūṣeyo<br/>
ḷā rāmananugra paraśu pāṭita ripu vaṁ<br/>
śārāmananiṣuvidyā<br/>
pāraganenisidudu balme vaikartananā // ViVi.1.104 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu dhanurdharāgragaṇyanāgirdondu divasaṁ tanna toḍeya mēle<br/>
taleyaniṭṭu paraśurāmaṁ maṟedoṟagidā prastāvadoḷā munige munisaṁ<br/>
māḍalendindranupāyadoḷaṭṭida vajrakīṭaṅgaḷ karṇaneraḍuṁ toḍeyumanuḷiya<br/>
nūṟi koḍantiyoḷ beṭṭidantattamittamurci pōgeyumadanaṟiyadante guruge<br/>
nidrābhighātamakkumendu taleyanugurusuttu mireyire—<br/>
</p>

<p>
ativiśadaviśālōru<br/>
kṣatadindoṟedanitu jaḍeyumaṁ nāndi manaḥ<br/>
kṣatadoḍaneḻcarisidudu<br/>
tthitamāvandasra miśragandhaṁ muniyaṁ // ViVi.1.105 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
anteḻcattu nettara ponaloḷ nāndu naneda maiyyumaṁ toydu taḷpoyda<br/>
jaḍeyumaṁ kaṇḍī dhairyaṁ kṣatriyaṅgalladāgadu pārvanendennoḷ pusidu<br/>
viddeyaṁkaikoṇḍudarke daṇḍaṁ peṟatilla ninagānitta brahmāstramemba divyāstra<br/>
mavasāna kāladoḷ besakeyyadirkendu śāpavanittanantu karṇanuṁ śāpahatanāgi<br/>
maguḻdu bandu sūtana maneyoḷirpannegamittal kuntigavaramāvanappakuntibhōjanuṁ svayambaraṁ māḍe—<br/>
</p>

<p>
sogayipa tamma javvanada tamma vibhūtiya tamma tamma ce<br/>
lvugaḷa vilāsadurmegaḷoḷāvevagāgipevendu banda ce<br/>
nnigarumanāsekāṟarumanollade celviḍidirda rūpu dr̥<br/>
ṣṭigevare pāṇḍurājanane kunti manambuge māle sūḍidaḷ // ViVi.1.106 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 26]<br/>
antu svayambaradoḷ neṟedarasumakkaḷoḷappukeyda kuntiyoḍane<br/>
madrarājana magaḷ śalyanoḍavuṭṭida mādriyumanonde paseyoḷirisi gāṅgēyaṁ<br/>
vidhātraṁ muṇḍāḍuvante tāṁ maduveyaṁ māḍi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
taḷirgaḷasaṁ mukundaravamettida muttina maṇṭapaṁ manaṁ<br/>
goḷipa vitānapaṅkti pasurvandaloḷoldeḍeyāḍuveydeyar<br/>
baḷasida vēda pāragara sandaṇiyembivaṟiṁ vivāha maṁ<br/>
gaḷamadu kuntimādrigaḷoḷaccariyādudu pāṇḍurājanā // ViVi.1.107 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
tuṟugeme nīḷda purvu niḍugaṇ poṟeyallade baṭṭitappa bā<br/>
ydeṟetanurēkhegoṇḍa koraloḍḍida parmole teḷvasiṟ karaṁ<br/>
neṟeda nitambavimbuvaḍeḷdoḍenakkaravaddi(?)tāne pō<br/>
kiṟudoḍeyendu dhātri pogaḻguṁ pogaḻvannare kunti mādrigaḷ // ViVi.1.108 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antākegaḷirvarumeraḍuṁ keladoḷire kalpalategaḷeraḍaṟa naḍuvaṇa<br/>
kalpavr̥kṣamirpantirda pāṇḍurājaṅge dhr̥tarāṣṭranaṅgahīnanendu vivāhadosageyoḍane<br/>
paṭṭabandhadosageyaṁ māḍi nelananāḷise—<br/>
</p>

<p>
mīṟuvavembamāṇḍaḷikarīyadarembadaṭar‌vayalge me<br/>
yduṟuvavemba pūṇigaraḍaṅgikunuṅgisiḍildu jōldu kā<br/>
ypāṟenabhakke pāṟidudu gaṇḍara nettiyoḷotti bāḷani<br/>
nnūṟugumendoḍēṁ pirido tējada daḷḷuri pāṇḍurājanā // ViVi.1.109 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
besakeydattu samudra mudrita dharācakraṁ pratāpakkagu<br/>
rvise gōḷuṇḍegoḷuttumirdudu diśācakraṁ podaḻdājñegaṁ<br/>
pesargaṁ munnamerūpuvōduduviyaccakraṁ samantembinaṁ<br/>
jasamāpāṇḍuramādudā nr̥paroḷārā pāṇḍurājambaraṁ // ViVi.1.110 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu pāṇḍurājanadhika tējanumavanata vairi bhūbhr̥tsamājanumāgi<br/>
negaḻuttirdondu divasaṁ tōpina bēṇṭeyanāḍalaḻtiyiṁ pōgi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 27]<br/>
iniyaḷanaḻteyinde mr̥gimāḍi manōja sukhakke sōltalaṁ<br/>
pinenereyalke divyamuniyuṁ mr̥gamāgi maraldu kūḍe me<br/>
llane mr̥gamendusārdu neṟanaṁ naḍe nōḍi narēndraneccu bhōṁ<br/>
kane mr̥gacāriyaṁ tanage māṇade tandanadondu māriyaṁ // ViVi.1.111 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgaḷ praḷayaduḷkamuḷkuvante tanneccambu munikumārana kaṇṇoḷa<br/>
merdeyoḷa mukke pēḻimennanāvaneccanemba muniya munida saramaṁ kēḷdu<br/>
billanambumanīḍāḍi tanna munde nindirda bhūpanaṁ muni nōḍi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
sannatadiṁ ratakkeḷasi nallaḷoḷōtoḍagūḍidennaniṁ<br/>
tanneyameccudarke peṟatilladudaṇḍamoṟaldu nallaḷoḷ<br/>
nīnnaḍenōḍiyuṁ bayasi kūḍiyumāgaḍe sāveyāgi pō<br/>
ginnene raudra śāpa paritāpa viḷāpadoḷā mahīśvaraṁ // ViVi.1.112 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
enna geydakāmākrāntakkekāma kr̥tamēṁ piridaltu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
etta vanametta mr̥gayā<br/>
vr̥ttakamī tapasiyetta mr̥gameṁdentā<br/>
netteccenātmakarmā<br/>
yattaṁpeṟataltidellamaghaṭitaghaṭitaṁ // ViVi.1.113 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu cintisuttuṁ poḻalge maguḻduvandu gāṅgēya dhr̥tarāṣṭravidurarkaḷge<br/>
tadvr̥ttāntamellamaṁ pēḻdu samasta vastugaḷaṁ dīnānāthajanaṅgaḷge sūṟegoṭṭu<br/>
nija parivāramaṁ barisi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
sāramanaṅgajaṅgamalatālalitāṅgiyarindaltesaṁ<br/>
sāramidembudinnenagetappudu tanmuni śāpadindami<br/>
nnārumidarke vakrisadiriṁ vanavāsadoḷirpenendu du<br/>
rvāra parākramaṁ taḷare bārisi vārisi kunti mādriyar // ViVi.1.114 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
benna bennane bare binna binnane pōgi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 28]<br/>
tuṅga vanya mataṅgaja dantāghāta nipātita sallakī<br/>
bhaṅgamaṁ maṇimauktika nīḷa sthūḷa śilā pravibhāsitō<br/>
ttuṅgamaṁ muni mukhya mukhāmbhōjōdara nirgatamantra pū<br/>
tāṅgamaṁ nr̥paneydidanudyacchr̥ṅgamanā śataśr̥ṅgamaṁ // ViVi.1.115 [khacaraplutaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
ā parvatada vipuḷa vanōpakaṇṭhaṅgaḷoḷ tāpasakanyeyar naḍapideḷalate<br/>
gaḷoḷeṟagi tuṟugi sāmavēda dhvaniyoḷ moreva tumbigaḷumaṁ paṇteṟagida<br/>
tadāśramada tarugaḷa mēgirdu pugil pugilenditta bannimirimemba pombaṇṇada<br/>
kōgilegaḷumaṁ munikumārarōduva vēdavēdāṅgaṅgaḷaṁ tappuviḍidu jaḍidu<br/>
baggisuva padumarāgada baṇṇadaragiḷigaḷumaṁ surabhigaḷa toreda molegaḷanuṇbavaṟa<br/>
maṟigaḷaṁ pōge nūṅki kūṅki molegaḷanuṇba kiśōra kēsarigaḷumaṁ tammoḍane<br/>
nalidāḍuva kiśōrakēsarigaḷaṁ piḍidu tegeva karikaḷabhaṅgaḷumanāgaḷāpaḷuvaṅgaḷinde<br/>
pāyva puligaḷa maṟigaḷoḷ paridāḍuva taruṇa hariṇaṅgaḷumaṁ mattaṁ mutta<br/>
kuruḍatavasigaḷa kaiyaṁ piḍiduydavaraguhegaḷaṁ pugipa poṟamaḍipa capaḷa<br/>
kapigaḷumaṁ hōmāgniyaneṟaṅkeya gāḷiyiṁ nandalīyaduripuva rājahaṁse<br/>
gaḷumaṁmunigaṇēśvararoḍanedāḷivūgoyvoḍane varpa gōḷāṅgūḷaṅgaḷumaṁ<br/>
nōḍi tapōvanada tapōdhanara tapaḥprabhāvakke cōdyambaṭṭu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
vinayadinitta bannimirimembavoliñcaradindamoyyano<br/>
yyane maṟidumbigaḷa morevuvaḻkaṟoḷoldeṟapantetaḷta pū<br/>
vina posagoñcaliṁmaranidēnesedirduvo kaltuvāgadē<br/>
vinayamanī tapōdhanara kaiyoḷeśākhigaḷuṁnagēndra[dā] // ViVi.1.116 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu meccuttumenage nelasiralī tapōvaname pāvanamendu tapōvanada<br/>
munijanada paramānurāgamaṁpercisikāmānurāgamaṁ bercisi<br/>
tadāśramadoḷāśramakke guruvāgi pāṇḍurājanirpannegamitta dhr̥tarāṣṭrana<br/>
[p. 29]<br/>
mahādēviyappa gāndhāri nūrvarmakkaḷaṁ paḍevantu parāśara munīndranoḷ<br/>
barambaḍedaḷembudaṁ kunti kēḷdu tānuṁ putrārthi[ni]yāgal bagedu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
visasanadoḷ virōdhi nr̥paraṁ taṟidoṭṭalumarthigarthamaṁ<br/>
kasavina lekkamendu kuḍaluṁ vipuḷāyatiyaṁ digantadoḷ<br/>
pasarisaluṁ karaṁ neṟeva makkaḷanīyade nōḍe nāḍe nō<br/>
yisidapudikṣupuṣpadavolennaya niṣphala puṣpadarśanaṁ // ViVi.1.117 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu cintākrānteyāgirda kuntiyaṁ kaṇḍu pāṇḍurājanēkānta<br/>
doḷintendaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
cinteyidēno santatige makkaḷe neṭṭane bārteyappoḍi<br/>
nnintiravēḍa divya munipuṅgavaraṁbagedīrpinaṁ nijā<br/>
tyanta pativratā guṇadinarcisi meccisu nīṁ diganta vi<br/>
śrānta yaśarkaḷaṁ vara tanūbhavaraṁ paḍe nīṁ taḷōdari // ViVi.1.118 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endoḍe kontiyintendaḷenna kannikeyā kāladoḷ nānenna māvaṁ<br/>
kontibhōjana maneyoḷ baḷevandu durvāsa mahāmuniyaremma manege niccakkaṁ<br/>
barparavarenna vinayakkaṁ bhaktigaṁ besakeyvudarkaṁ mecci mantrākṣaraṅgaḷanaydu<br/>
varavittarīyaydu mantrakayvarmakkaḷaṁ ninna bagege bandavara nāhvānaṁ geyyalavara<br/>
pōlveya makkaḷaṁ paḍeveyendu besasidoḍīgaḷenna puṇyadiṁ dorekoṇḍu<br/>
doḷḷittembudaṁ divya muni vākyamamōgha vākyamakkumadarkēnuṁ<br/>
cintisalvēḍendoḍante geyvenendu tīrtha jalaṅgaḷaṁ mindu daḷimbavanuṭṭu<br/>
muttina toḍigegaḷaṁ toṭṭu darbhaśayanadoḷirdu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
jñānadinirdu niṭṭipoḍe divya munīndrana koṭṭa mantra saṁ<br/>
tānamanōdiyōdi yamarājananadbhuta tējanaṁ sarō<br/>
jānane jānadiṁ barise bandu yamaṁ besanāvudāvudā<br/>
tmānugatārthamendoḍenagīvudu ninnane pōlva putranaṁ // ViVi.1.119 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 30]<br/>
embuduṁ tathāstuvendu tannaṁśamanākeya garbhadoḷavatarisi yamabhaṭṭāraka<br/>
nantardhānakke sandanannegamā kāntege—<br/>
</p>

<p>
himadhavaḷātapatramane pōle mukhēnduva beḷpu pūrṇa kuṁ<br/>
bhamane nirantaraṁ gele kucaṅgaḷatōrpupatākeyondu vi<br/>
bhramamane pōle purvina poḍarpoḷakoṇḍudavaḷge garbha ci<br/>
hname gaḷa garbhadarbhakana sūcipa mundaṇa rājyacihnamaṁ // ViVi.1.120 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antukontiyagarbhabhāramuṁ tāpasāśramadanurāgamumoḍanoḍane<br/>
baḷeye bandhujanada manōrathaṅgaḷumombattaneya tiṅgaḷumoḍanoḍane neṟeye—<br/>
</p>

<p>
vananidhiyindaṁ candraṁ<br/>
vinatōdaradiṁ garutmanudayācaḷadiṁ<br/>
dinapanogevante puṭṭida<br/>
nanivārya sutējanenipaninajana tanayaṁ // ViVi.1.121 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
puṭṭuvuduṁ dharmamumoḍa<br/>
vuṭṭidudītanoḷe dharmanaṁśadoḷītaṁ<br/>
puṭṭidanendā śiśugose<br/>
diṭṭudu muni samiti dharmasutanene pesaraṁ // ViVi.1.122 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu pesaraniṭṭu parakeyaṁ koṭṭu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
santasadinirdu makkaḷa<br/>
santatigī doreyarinnumāgadoḍentuṁ<br/>
santasamenagillendā<br/>
kānte suta bhrānte munninantevolirdaḷ // ViVi.1.123 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
mantrākṣara niyamadinabhi<br/>
mantrisi barisidoḍe vāyudēvaṁ bandēṁ<br/>
mantraṁ pēḻene kuḍu ripu<br/>
tantrakṣayakarananenage hitanaṁ sutanaṁ // ViVi.1.124 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
embudumadēviridittenendu viyattaḷakkogedoḍātanaṁśamākeya<br/>
garbhasarōvaradoḷage candrabimbadante sogayise—<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 31]<br/>
trivaḷigaḷuṁ virōdhinr̥parutsavamuṁ kiḍevanduvānanēṁ<br/>
duva kaḍuveḷpu kūsina negaḻteya beḷpuvolāytu munneba<br/>
ḷḷuva naḍutōrpa meyyanoḷakoṇḍudupoṅgoḍanaṁ tamāḷa pa<br/>
llavadoḷe muccidandadoḷe cūcukamāntudukarpanākeyā // ViVi.1.125 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
ā sudatiya mr̥du pada vi<br/>
nyāsamumaṁ śēṣanānalāradesuydaṁ<br/>
bēsaṟinendoḍegarbhada<br/>
kūsina baḷedaḷaviyaḷavanaḷevarumoḷarē // ViVi.1.126 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antugarbhanirbharapradēśadoḷarātigaḷgantakālaṁ dorekoḷvante prasūti<br/>
kālaṁ dorekoḷe—<br/>
</p>

<p>
śubha tithi śubha nakṣatraṁ<br/>
śubha vāraṁ śubha muhūrtamene gaṇakaniḷā<br/>
prabhuvogedanuditakāya<br/>
prabheyogedire daḷita śatrugōtraṁ putraṁ // ViVi.1.127 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
bhīmaṁ bhayaṅkaraṁ peṟa<br/>
tē mātī kūsinandamītana pesaruṁ<br/>
bhīmane pōgene munijana<br/>
mīmāḻkeyināytu śiśuge pesaranvarthaṁ // ViVi.1.128 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu bharatakulatilakarappirvarmakkaḷaṁ pettu konti santasadantama<br/>
neydirpudumatta dhr̥tarāṣṭrana mahādēviyappa gāndhāri kēḷdu tanna garbhaṁ<br/>
taḍedudarke kinisi kiṅkirivōgi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
santatige piriya makkaḷa<br/>
nāṁ taḍeyade paḍevenendoḍenniṁ munnaṁ<br/>
kontiye paḍedaḷ garbhada<br/>
cinteyadinnēvudendu basiṟaṁ posedaḷ // ViVi.1.129 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 32]<br/>
posedoḍe pālgaḍalaṁ magu<br/>
ḻdasurar posedalli kāḷakūṭāṅkuramaṁ<br/>
dasadaḷamogedantogeduvu<br/>
basiṟiṁnūṟondu piṇḍavaruṇākīrṇaṁ // ViVi.1.130 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
avaṁ kaṇḍu kinisi kirceḻdivellavaṁ poṟage bisuṭu bannimembuduṁ<br/>
vyāsabhaṭṭārakaṁ bandu gāndhāriyaṁ baggisi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
odavuge ninna santatige nūrvarudagra sutarkaḷonde ga<br/>
rbhadoḷene kemmanintu posedikkide polladugeydeyendu mā<br/>
ṇade muni nūṟupiṇḍamumanāgaḷe tīvida kammanappa tu<br/>
ppada koḍadoḷ samantu maḍagiṭṭoḍe sr̥ṣṭige cōdyamappinaṁ // ViVi.1.131 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu nūrvaroḷorvanagurbu parbi parakalise sampūrṇa vayaskanāgi<br/>
ghr̥ta ghaṭavighaṭanumāgipuṭṭuvuduṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
pratimegaḷaḻtuvumoḻagidu<br/>
dati rabhasade dhātri desegaḷuriduvu bhūta<br/>
pratatigaḷāḍiduvoḷaṟidu<br/>
vatiramyasthānadoḷ śivānivahaṅgaḷ // ViVi.1.132 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antogedanēkōtpātaṅgaḷaṁ kaṇḍu mundaṟiva cadura viduranintendaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
ītane namma kulakkaṁ<br/>
kētudalānaṟivenalladandēkinitu<br/>
tpātaṁ tōrpuvu bisuḍuvu |<br/>
dītana peṟaguḻida sutare santatigappar // ViVi.1.133 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endoḍaṁ putramōha kāraṇavāgi dhr̥tarāṣṭranuṁ gāndhāriyu mēgeydu<br/>
moḍambaḍadirdoḍutpāta śāntika pauṣṭika kriyegaḷaṁ mahā brāhmaṇarindaṁ baḷeyisi<br/>
baddavaṇamaṁ bājisi maṅgaḷamaṁ pāḍisi kūsiṅge duryōdhananendu pesaraniṭṭu<br/>
mattina kūsugaḷgellaṁ duśyāsanādiyāgi nāmaṅgaḷaniṭṭu parakeyaṁ koṭṭu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 33]<br/>
sukamirpannegamitta kunti śataśr̥ṅgādrīndradoḷ divya bā<br/>
lakaninnorvananugra vairimadavanmātaṅga kumbhārdamau<br/>
ktika lagnōjjvala bāṇanaṁpravilasadgīrvāṇa dātavya sā<br/>
yaka sampūrṇa kaḷāpravīṇananiḷā bhāra kṣamākṣūṇanaṁ // ViVi.1.134 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu sarva lakṣaṇa sampūrṇanappa magananamōghaṁ paḍevenembu<br/>
dyōgamanettikoṇḍu pāṇḍurājanuṁ tānuṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
eṟagiyumorme divya munigārtupavāsamanirdumorme ko<br/>
ydaṟikeya pūgaḷiṁ śivananarcisiyuṁ biḍadorme nōntumō<br/>
daṟivara pēḻda nōmpigaḷanorme palarmeyumintu tamma me<br/>
ymaṟevinamirvaruṁ namedarēnavargādudo putradōhaḷaṁ // ViVi.1.135 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
alasade māḍi bēsaṟade sālgumidennade meysogakke paṁ<br/>
balisade niddegeṭṭuniḍujāgaradoḷtoḍardēka pādadoḷ<br/>
balidupavāsadoḷ namedu nōmpigaḷoḷ niyama kramaṅgaḷaṁ<br/>
salisidarantu nōnade guṇārṇavanaṁ paḍeyalke tīrgumē // ViVi.1.136 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antondu varṣambaraṁ bharaṅgeydu nōntu pūrvakramadoḷondu<br/>
divasamupavāsamanirdagaṇya puṇyatīrtha jalaṅgaḷaṁ mindu daḷimbamanuṭṭu<br/>
darbhaśayanadoḷirdu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
sulipal miñcinagoñcaluṭṭa dugulaṁ gaṅgānadī phēnamu<br/>
jjvala muktābharaṇaṁ tarattaraḷatārōdāra bhā bhāramaṁ<br/>
galatālālitasāndra candanarasaṁ beḷdiṅgaḷembondu paṁ<br/>
bala bambalge[ḍe]yāge beḷpasadanaṁ kaṇgoppitā kānteyā // ViVi.1.137 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu tanna kaikoṇḍa beḷpasadanadoḷ kīrti śrīyaṁvākśrīyumana<br/>
nukarisi mantrākṣara niyamadoḷindranaṁ barise—<br/>
</p>

<p>
neneda manaṁ peṟaguḻida<br/>
ttene beḷaguva ratnadīpti suradhanu negeda<br/>
ttene neydilgoḷanalarda<br/>
ttene kaṇgaḷa baḷagamāgaḷindraṁ bandaṁ // ViVi.1.138 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 34]<br/>
besanēnēgeyvudo nina<br/>
gosedēnaṁ kuḍuvudendoḍendaḷ makkaḷ<br/>
osageyanenagīvudu ni<br/>
nnesakada masakamane pōlvamaganaṁmaghavā // ViVi.1.139 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
embudumākeya bageda bageyoḷoḍambaḍuvante kulagirigaḷa biṇpumaṁ<br/>
dharātaḷada tiṇpumanādityana tējadaguntiyumaṁcandrana kāntiyumaṁ madanana<br/>
saubhāgyamumaṁ kalpataruvinudāraśaktiyumanīśvarana prabhuśaktiyumaṁ javana<br/>
ballāḷtanamumaṁ siṁhada kalitanamumanavaravaradesegaḷiṁ tegedondumāḍi<br/>
kontiya divya garbhōdaramemba śukti puṭōdaradoḷtanna divyāṁśavemba<br/>
muktāphalōdabinduvanindraṁ saṅkramisi nijanivāsakke pōdanannegamitta<br/>
kontiyumandina beḷagappa jāvadoḷ sukhanidreyāgi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
kuḍivudanēḻumambudhiyamaṁ kulaśailakuḷaṅgaḷaṁ tagu<br/>
ḷdaḍarvudanondu bāḷa ravi tannaya sōgila mēge rāgadiṁ<br/>
poḍarvudanante dikkarigaḷambujapatrapuṭāmbuviṁ beḍaṁ<br/>
gaḍasire majjanambugipudaṁ sati kaṇḍosedaḷ niśāntadoḷ // ViVi.1.140 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu kaṇḍu munikumārarōduva vēdaninādadiṁ vigatanidreyāgi<br/>
pāṇḍurājaṅgamalliya munijanaṅgaḷgamaṟipidoḍavarā kanasugaḷge<br/>
santōṣambaṭṭu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
kuḍivudaṟindamabdhigaḷanabdhiparīta mahīśanaṁ tagu<br/>
ḷdaḍarvudaṟiṁ kulādri parivēṣṭitanaṁ taruṇārkananaḻkaṟiṁ<br/>
poḍarvudaṟindamendumuditōditanaṁ digibhaṅgaḷeṇṭumo<br/>
ḷpoḍarisi majjanambugise kaṇḍudaṟiṁ kamalābhirāmanaṁ // ViVi.1.141 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
intappa maganaṁ nīnamōghaṁ paḍeveyendu munijanaṅgaḷ pēḻva<br/>
śubhasvapnaphalaṅgaḷoḍanoḍane garbhacihnaṅgaḷuṁ tōṟe pagevara peṇḍira<br/>
[p. 35]<br/>
mogaṅgaḷumākeya kucacūcukaṅgaḷumoḍanoḍane kandiduvākeya vaḷitra<br/>
yaṅgaḷuṁ pagevara śaktitrayaṅgaḷumoḍanoḍane keṭṭuvākeya bāsegaḷuṁ pagevara<br/>
bāḻvāsegaḷumoḍanoḍanasiyavāduvākeya mandagamanamuṁ pagevara<br/>
manaṅgaḷumoḍanoḍanalasikeyaṁ kaikoṇḍuvākeya naḍuvina baḍatanamuṁ pagevara<br/>
siriyumoḍanoḍane keṭṭuvā samayadoḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
urcida bāḷoḷātma mukhabimbamanaḻtiye nōḍaluṁ manaṁ<br/>
perci dhanurlatā guṇa ninādamanālisi kēḷalu manaṁ<br/>
bercade siṁha pōtakamanōvalumākeya dōhaḷaṁ karaṁ<br/>
percidudā guṇārṇavana mundaṇa bīramanandetōrpavōl // ViVi.1.142 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
mattamēḻuṁ samudraṅgaḷa nīranondumāḍi mīyaluṁ vēḷāvana<br/>
latāgr̥hōdara puḷinasthaḷa parisarapradēśadoḷ toḻalalumaḻtiyāge—<br/>
</p>

<p>
baḷeda nitambadekāñcī<br/>
kaḷāpamaṁ kaṭṭalaṇame neṟeyadidenda<br/>
ggaḷisi kuḷikegaḷinēṁ ka<br/>
ṇgoḷisidudōsubhageyāda sudatiya garbhaṁ // ViVi.1.143 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu tekkane tīvida meyyoḷalarda sampageyaralante beḷarta baṇṇaṁ<br/>
guṇārṇavaṅge māḍida baṇṇadante sogayisi baḷedu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
tuḍugegaḷoḷ sarigeyumaṁ<br/>
kaḍuviṇṇittenisi naḍedumōraḍiyanaṇaṁ<br/>
naḍeyalumāṟade kemmane<br/>
biḍadārayvanitumāge baḷedudu garbhaṁ // ViVi.1.144 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antā baḷeda garbhadoḷ sampūrṇaprasavasamayaṁ dorekoḷe grahaṅgaḷellaṁ<br/>
tantammucca sthānaṅgaḷoḷirdu ṣaḍvarga siddhiyanuṇṭumāḍe śubhalagnōdaya<br/>
doḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 36]<br/>
bharatakula gagana dinakara<br/>
narātikuḷakamaḷahimakaraṁśiśu tējō<br/>
viracaneyuṁ kāntiyumā<br/>
varisiregarbhōdayādriyindudayisidaṁ // ViVi.1.145 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
udayisuvudumamr̥tāṁśuvi<br/>
nudayadoḷambhōdhivēlebhōrgarevavolo<br/>
rmodaleseduvu ghanapathadoḷ<br/>
tridaśakarāhatiyinoḍane suradundubhigaḷ // ViVi.1.146 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu moḻaguva suradundubhigaḷuṁ parasuva jayajaya dhvanigaḷuṁ<br/>
berasu dēvēndraṁ bare dēvavimānaṅgaḷellaṁ śataśr̥ṅgaparvatamaṁ musuṟikoṇḍu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
dēvara paṟegaḷa ravadoḷ<br/>
dēvara surivarala sariya beḷsariyoḷ ta<br/>
ddēva vimānāvaḷiyoḷ<br/>
tīvidudormodale gaganadiṁdhare madhyaṁ // ViVi.1.147 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu hiraṇyagarbhabrahmaṁ modalāge vyāsa kaśyapa vasiṣṭha vālmīki viśvāmitra<br/>
jamadagni bhāradvājāgastya pulastya nārada pramukharappa divya munipatigaḷumēkādaśa<br/>
rudraruṁ dvādaśādityarumaṣṭavasugaḷumaśvinīdēvaruṁ modalāge mūvatta<br/>
mūdēvaruṁ indraṁ berasu vaimānika dēvaruṁ neredu pāṇḍurājanumaṁ<br/>
kuntiyumaṁ parasi kūsiṅgejanmōtsavamaṁ māḍi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
nōḍuvanā brahmaṁ muṁ<br/>
ḍāḍuvanamarēndranindranaccaraseyare<br/>
ḻdāḍuvarendoḍe pogaḻa<br/>
lvēḍa guṇārṇavana janmadinada beḍaṅgaṁ // ViVi.1.148 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu piridumosageyaṁ māḍi dēvasabheyuṁ brahmasabheyumoḍanirdu<br/>
nāmakaraṇōtsava nimittaṅgaḷappa nāmaṅgaḷoḷītaṁ sakala bhuvana saṁstūyamānaṁ<br/>
[p. 37]<br/>
cāḷukyavaṁśōdbhavaṁ śrīmadarikēsari vikramārjunanudāttanārāyaṇaṁ<br/>
pracaṇḍa mārtāṇḍanudāra mahēśvaraṁkadanatriṇētraṁ manujamāndhātaṁ pratijñā<br/>
gāṅgēyaṁ śaucāñjanēyanakaḷaṅkarāmaṁ sāhasabhīmaṁpratyakṣa jīmūta vāhanaṁ<br/>
jagadēkamallaṁ parasainyabhairavaṁ atirathamathanaṁvairigajaghaṭāvighaṭanaṁ vidviṣṭa<br/>
vidrāvaṇanarāti kāḷānaḷaṁ ripukuraṅgakaṇṭhīravaṁ vikrāntatuṅgaṁ parākrama dhavaḷaṁ<br/>
samaraikamēru śaraṇāgata jalanidhi vinayavibhūṣaṇaṁ manunidānananūnadāni<br/>
lōkaika kalpadrumaṁ gajagamanarājaputranārūḍhasarvajñaṁ gandhēbhavidyādharaṁ<br/>
nr̥paparamātmaṁ vibudha vanajavanakaḷahaṁsaṁsurata makaradhvajaṁ sahajamanōjaṁ<br/>
āndhrīkucakaḷaśa pallavaṁ karṇāṭī karṇapūraṁ lāṭīlalāmaṁ kēraḷīkēḷi<br/>
kandarpaṁ saṁsārasārōdayaṁ maṟuvakkadallaḻaṁ nōḍuttegelvaṁ pāṇbaraṅkusaṁ<br/>
ammanagandhavāraṇaṁ paḍemecce gaṇḍaṁpriyagaḷḷaṁguṇanidhi guṇārṇavaṁ sāmanta<br/>
cūḍāmaṇiyendintivu modalāge palavumaṣṭōttara śatanāmaṅgaḷaniṭṭu viśēṣā<br/>
śīrvacanaṅgaḷiṁ parasi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
saptasamudra mudrita dharātaḷamaṁ besakeysu mīṟida<br/>
ddr̥pta virōdhi sādhanamanāhavadoḷ taṟidoṭṭu viśvadi<br/>
gvyāptayaśōviḷāsinigevallabhanāgu nirantara sukha<br/>
vyāptige nīne mottamodalāgarikēsari lōkamuḷḷinaṁ // ViVi.1.149 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
idu vividha vibudhajanavinuta jinapadāmbhōja<br/>
vara prasādōtpanna prasanna gambhīravacanaracana<br/>
catura kavitāguṇārṇava viracitamappa<br/>
vikramārjuna vijayadoḷ<br/>
prathamāśvāsaṁ<br/>
</p>

<p>
---------------------------------------------------------------------<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 38]<br/>
[dvitīyāśvāsaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
śrīgagaluramaṁ kīrti<br/>
śrīge digantamumanahitaraṁ gelva jaya<br/>
śrīge bhujaśikharamaṁ nele<br/>
yāgisi nīṁ nelasu nēsaṟuḷḷinamarigā // ViVi.2.1 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
emba parakegaḷa ravadoḷ<br/>
tumbenabhō vivaramamaramunijanamamarēṁ<br/>
draṁ berasu taḷardudāduda<br/>
ḷumbaṁ manadosage kuntigaṁ tatpatigaṁ // ViVi.2.2 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu guṇārṇavana puṭṭidosageyoḷosagemaruḷgoṇḍu kuntiyuṁ<br/>
pāṇḍurājanumire mādri tanage makkaḷilladudarke virakteyāgi posedu bisuṭa<br/>
raktāśōka pallavadante karaṁ koragi cintisutirdoḍākeyabinnanādamogadandamaṁ<br/>
kaṇḍu kunti karuṇisi putrōtpatti nimittaṅgaḷappa mantrākṣaraṅgaḷanupadēśaṁ<br/>
geydoḍākeyuṁ tadukta kriyeyoḷaṁ niyama niyamiteyāgi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
āhvānaṁgeydaśvini<br/>
dēvaranavaritta varadoḷavaraṁśame saṁ<br/>
bhāvise garbhadoḷamaḷara<br/>
nā vanajadaḷākṣi paḍedu santativettaḷ // ViVi.2.3 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgaḷā pāṇḍurājanā kūsugaḷge jātakarmamaṁ munigaḷiṁ baḷeyisi<br/>
nakula sahadēvarendavargamaḷvesaraniṭṭu putra sampūrṇa manōrathanāgirpinamayvar<br/>
kūsugaḷumēḻgevāḍivada candranantuttarābhivr̥ddhiyoḷ sogayisi baḷeye<br/>
bharatakulakke viśada yaśōṅkuraṅgaḷuṁ bandhujanakke puṇyāṅkuraṅgaḷuṁ vandijanakke<br/>
kalpavr̥kṣāṅkuraṅgaḷumarātijanakke kāḷakūṭāṅkuraṅgaḷumaṁ pōltu pañcāṅga<br/>
mantra[ṁ]svarūpadoḷ mūrtimantaṁ gaḷādante sogayisi baḷeye—<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 39]<br/>
toḍardamarda bāḷavaṇṇada<br/>
tuḍuge paḷañcaleva pañca jaḍe nosaloḷoḍaṁ<br/>
baḍuvaraḷeleyivaṟiṁ ce<br/>
lviḍidirdudu bāḷa kēḷi dharmātmajanā // ViVi.2.4 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antātaṁ baḷeyevaḷeye—<br/>
</p>

<p>
naḍeva taḷarnaḍeyoḷ puḍi<br/>
vuḍiyāduvu śilegaḷoḍedu karigaḷ bhīmaṁ<br/>
piḍidaḍardoḍe bāyviṭṭe<br/>
lvaḍagāduvu muddadantu sogayisavēḍā // ViVi.2.5 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
munivanamane bisuṭuvumuṁ<br/>
muniyara sōṅkiloḷe baḷeda siṅgaṅgaḷ mu<br/>
ddinoḷaḍarva piḍiva gurduva<br/>
manegeḻevanitarkamalasimarudātmajanā // ViVi.2.6 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antātaṁ baḷeye—<br/>
</p>

<p>
bēḍadudaṁ bēḍuva puḍi<br/>
yāḍuva todaḷodave nuḍiva nagisuva bāla<br/>
krīḍe murāriya bāla<br/>
krīḍeyananukaripudādudarikēsariyā // ViVi.2.7 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
paredaḍarda dhūḷi kiṟunage<br/>
verasida todaḷodave nuḍivanuḍi nagemogadoḷ<br/>
parakalisida kāḍigevera<br/>
sarikēsari tāya manamaniḻkuḷigoṇḍaṁ // ViVi.2.8 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
ogetarpa palgaḷā nage<br/>
mogada sarasvatiyanāgaḷarcisida poda<br/>
ḷdagalada celvina molleya<br/>
muguḷgaḷaniḷisire gaṇārṇavaṁ sogayisidaṁ // ViVi.2.9 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 40]<br/>
karikaḷabhaṅgaḷa śiśu kē<br/>
sarigaḷa baḻiyaṁ taguḷdu baḍavugaḷanavaṁ<br/>
tiripi piḍiyuttumarigaṁ<br/>
paridāḍuvasamavaya[skaro]ḷsogayisidaṁ // ViVi.2.10 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
deyvabalaṁ sogasikemuṁ<br/>
geyva balaṁ bāḷa kāladoḷ toḍarda poḍa<br/>
rdayvara bālakriyeyuṁ<br/>
muyvaṁ nōḍisitu tāyumaṁ tandeyumaṁ // ViVi.2.11 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antā kūsugaḷ nija jananī janakara manamaniḻkuḷigoḷisiyumarātijanaṅgaḷa manamanasuṅgoḷisiyuṁ baḷeye baḷeye—<br/>
</p>

<p>
alardadirmutte pūta posa mallige kampanavuṅkutirpa teṁ<br/>
belarumidaṅgelalbageva tumbi gaḷadhvaniyiṁ kukilva kō<br/>
gile nanedōṟi nuṇpeseva māmaranormodalalladuṇmuvu<br/>
yyala posagāvaraṁ pugiloḷēnesedatto basanta māsadoḷ // ViVi.2.12 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgaḷā basantarājana baraviṅge guḍigaṭṭidante baḷvaḷa baḷeda miḷirvaśōkeya<br/>
taḷirgaḷumātana baraviṅge tōraṇaṅgaṭṭidante banda māmaraṅgaḷanaḍardu<br/>
toḍardeḷakombugaḷviḍidu maradiṁ marakke dāṅguḍiviḍuva mādhavīlategaḷumātana<br/>
baraviṅge neṟeye sogayise keygeyva nallaḷante naneya birimuguḷgaḷa tuṟuga<br/>
ḷoḷeṟagi tuṟugida kalpalategaḷumātana baraviṅge baddavaṇaṁ bājipante bhōrgaredu<br/>
moreva tumbigaḷumātana baraviṅge raṅgavaliyikkidante puḷinasthaḷaṅgaḷoḷudirda<br/>
kaḻivūgaḷumātana baraviṅge vanavanite mecci neṟeye keygeydante niṟiniṟigoṇḍu<br/>
sogayisuva niṟigana niṟidaḷira goñcalgaḷumātana mēlvāye rāgisi rōmāṅkura<br/>
mogedantogeda kaḷikāṅkuraṅgaḷumātanaṅgasaṅgadoḷ kāmarasamuguvantuguva<br/>
soneyasōnegaḷumanoḷakoṇḍu tadāśramada nandanavanaṅga[ḷ]janaṅgaḷa<br/>
nanaṅgaṅgetoḻtuvesaṅgeysiduvu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 41]<br/>
birayiya miḻtuveṁmididoḍalladaṇaṁ muḷisāṟadendu pa<br/>
lmoredapanilli manmathanidaṁ pugaliṁgaḍimendu bēṭakā<br/>
ṟaraniradūṟi sāṟi jaḍivanteseguṁ sahakāra kōmaḷāṁ<br/>
kura parituṣṭa puṣṭa parapuṣṭagaḷadhvani nandanaṅgaḷoḷ // ViVi.2.13 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
kaviva madāḷiyiṁ masuḷanāgi payōjarajaṅgaḷoḷ kavi<br/>
lgavilanuvāgi banda malayānilanūdeteraḷva cūta pa<br/>
llavada teraḷke tadvana viḷāsiniyuṭṭa dukūladondu pa<br/>
llavada teraḷkeyanteseye kaṇgesedirduvu nandanāḷigaḷ // ViVi.2.14 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
pōgade pāḍutirpaḷiye br̥ṁhitamāgire candrakānti kā<br/>
ypāgire bīsuvondelare bīsuvudāgire kāygaḷindamiṁ<br/>
bāgire sōrva sōne madamāgire māvina banda kōḍe kō<br/>
ḍāgire kōḍugoṇḍu paridattu vasantagajaṁ viyōgiyaṁ // ViVi.2.15 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu banda basantadoḷ mādri tāṁ garvavyāleyuṁkrīḍānu<br/>
śīleyumappudaṟiṁ vanakrīḍā nimittadiṁ pōgi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
vanakusumaṅgaḷaṁ bagegevanduvanaḻtiyoḷāydu koydu me<br/>
llane vakuḷāḷavāḷa taḷadoḷ suridambujasūtradinde ma<br/>
ttanitaṟoḷaṁ muguḷsarige tōḷvaḷe kaṅkaṇavāramendubē<br/>
ḻpanitane māḍitoṭṭukaramoppidaḷāke basanta kāntevōl // ViVi.2.16 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu toṭṭa pūduḍuge madanana toṭṭa pūgaṇegeṇeyāgire—<br/>
</p>

<p>
miḷirva kuruḷgaḷoḷ toḍardu dēsiyanāvagamīva cenna pū<br/>
gaḷanavanoyyanōsarisutuṁ vadanābjada kampanāḷduṇal<br/>
baḷasuva tumbiyaṁ piḍida neydiloḷoyyane sōvutuṁ beḍaṁ<br/>
goḷakoḷe sorkidaṅgaja mataṅgajadantire barpa mādriyaṁ // ViVi.2.17 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
tāpasāśramadiṁ poṟamaṭṭante banamaṁ toḻalva pāṇḍurājaṁkaṇḍu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
sogayise toṭṭa pūduḍuge mellerdeyoḷ taḍamāḍe gāḍidi<br/>
ṭṭigaḷoḷanaṅgarāgarasamuṇmuvinaṁ naḍe nōḍi nōḍi to<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 42]<br/>
ṭṭage koḷe mēle pāydavaḷanappidanā vibhu tanna śāpamaṁ<br/>
bageyademiḻtudēvateyanaḻkaḷurkeyinappuvantevōl // ViVi.2.18 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antappuvuduṁviṣamaviṣavalliyanappidante taḷta nallaḷa mr̥dumr̥ṇāḷa<br/>
kōmaḷa bāhupāśaṅgaḷe yamapāśaṅgaḷāge—<br/>
</p>

<p>
bigidamardirda tōḷ saḍile jōle mogaṁ mogadindamoyyago<br/>
yyage nagegaṇgaḷālimaguḻdantire muccire suyyaḍaṅge me<br/>
llage maṟasondidandadoḷe jōlda nijēśananā latāṅgi to<br/>
ṭṭage koḷe nōḍi keṭṭeniniyaṁ maṟasondidanō baḻaldanō // ViVi.2.19 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu paṟipaṭṭa suyyumaṁ kōḍuva meyyumaṁ kaṇḍu paralōka<br/>
prāptanādudanaṟitu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
tāpasana śāpamembudu<br/>
pāpada rūpaṟitumaṟiyadantēke manaṁ<br/>
gāpaḻidu bandu muṭṭide<br/>
yōpane nīnenna pāpakarmiya meyyaṁ // ViVi.2.20 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
nīnninna sāvanadanena<br/>
sunneneyade nerevenemba bageyoḷ bandai<br/>
ninnoḍane vandu dinadoḷ<br/>
ninna manōrathamanarasa neṟapade māṇeṁ // ViVi.2.21 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
unnata dhavaḷacchatra<br/>
cchanna viyattaḷananindukuḷatiḷakananiṁ<br/>
tanneyadindī paḻuvino<br/>
ḷennarasananintubidiyetandikkuvudē // ViVi.2.22 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu vanadēvategaḷgellaṁ karuṇamāge paḷayisuva mādriya saramaṁ<br/>
kunti kēḷdu bhōṅkanerdedeṟedu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 43]<br/>
ā deseyoḷbhūbhujanō<br/>
ā deseyoḷmādri negeva karuṇāravamaṁ<br/>
tā deseyoḷbhūpatigē<br/>
nādudo pēḻ bidiye keṭṭenaḻidenenuttuṁ // ViVi.2.23 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
baḻiyane makkaḷ bhōrgare<br/>
daḻutuṁ peṟa peṟaganante paritare muḍi bi<br/>
ṭveḻale naḍunaḍuge kaṇṇīr<br/>
gaḻagaḻanormodalesuriye paritandāgaḷ // ViVi.2.24 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu tanna nallana kaḷēvaramaṁ taḻkaisikoṇḍu tanna sāvaṁ paricchēdisi<br/>
pallaṁ suliyuttumirdamādriyaṁ kaṇḍu kunti neladoḷ meyyanīḍāḍi<br/>
nāḍāḍiyallade paḷayisi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
aḍaviyoḷennumanennī<br/>
naḍapida śiśugaḷumanirisi nīṁ pēḻade pō<br/>
doḍamēnō ninna baḻiyane<br/>
naḍetarpeṁ ninnarasa bisuṭentirpeṁ // ViVi.2.25 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu nīnī kūsugaḷaṁ kaikoṇḍu naḍapu nallananenagoppisānātanādu<br/>
danappenene mādriyintendaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
enagindinondu sūḻuma<br/>
niniyaṁ dayegeydanenna sūḻaṁ ninagā<br/>
nenitādoḍamīvenema<br/>
ttanayarkeyyeḍepalumbadir‌ peṟapeṟavaṁ // ViVi.2.26 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu tapōvanada munijanamuṁ vanadēvatājanamuṁ tannaṇmaṁ<br/>
pogaḻe mādri pāṇḍurājanoḍanedāhōttaradante(?) kirciṅgekuladoḷaṁ<br/>
caladoḷamāvakanduṁ kundumillade tannoregaṁ doregamārumillenisidāgaḷ<br/>
kunti śōkākrānteyāgire tapōvanada tapōvr̥ddharākānteyanintendu santaisidar—<br/>
</p>

<p>
kaḻidavargaḻvudaḻtoḍavarēḻvoḍamantavariṁ baḻikke tā<br/>
muḻivoḍamēḻarantavaraṇaṁ tamagaṁ bardukilla dharmamaṁ<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 44]<br/>
gaḻiyisikoḷvudonde cadurintuṭu saṁskr̥ti dharmamēke bā<br/>
yaḻivudidēke cintisuvudēke palumbuvudēke nōvudō // ViVi.2.27 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antumallade—<br/>
</p>

<p>
biḍadaḻalva bandhujanado<br/>
ḻkuḍiyada kaṇṇīra pūramā prētamanō<br/>
gaḍisade suḍuvudu gaḍami<br/>
nnuḍuguvudī śōkamaṁ sarōjadaḷākṣi // ViVi.2.28 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
nīnintu śōkākrānteyāgi saṁsāra sthitiyanaṟiyadajñānigaḷante<br/>
vipraḷāpaṅgeydeyappoḍī kūsugaḷ manamikkiyumerdeyikkiyuṁ kiḍuvarendanē<br/>
kōpaśāntavacanaṅgaḷindamākeyubbegamanāṟe nuḍidumalliya munijanamellamā<br/>
kūsugaḷumaṁ kuntiyamaṁ mundiṭṭoḍagoṇḍu nāgapurakke vandu gāṅgēya<br/>
dhr̥tarāṣṭra vidurarkaḷgamambālegaṁ pāṇḍurājana vr̥tāntamanaṟipidoḍāgaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
tuṟugida himabindugaḷiṁ<br/>
deṟagida nava vanajavanadavōl śōkadinaṁ<br/>
doṟeva nayanōdabinduvi<br/>
neṟagidudormodale bandhumukha vanajavanaṁ // ViVi.2.29 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgaḷ putra snēhadindati praḷāpaṅgeyvambāleyumaṁ bandhu jana<br/>
nirīkṣaṇadiṁ śōkaṁ maṟukaṇisebāyaḻidu paḷayisuva kuntiyumaṁ gāṅgēya<br/>
dhr̥tarāṣṭra vidurarkaḷumaṁ satyavatīdēviyumaṁ santaisi pāṇḍurājaṅge<br/>
jaḷadānādikriyegaḷaṁ nirvartisi tadanantaradoḷaduve nirvēgamāge vyāsavacana<br/>
doḷ satyavatiyumambikeyumambāleyuṁ saṁsāraviśīrṇeyarāgi munivanamanā<br/>
śrayisidaritta gāṅgēyanayvar kūsugaḷumaṁ tanna toḍeye toṭṭilāgi<br/>
naḍaputtamire duryōdhana prabhr̥tigaḷ nūrvaruṁ dharmaputrādigaḷayvaruṁ<br/>
sahapāṁsukrīḍitarāgi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
oḍanāḍiyumoḍanōdiyu<br/>
moḍavaḷeduṁ guḷḷegoṭṭi baṭṭuḷiseṇḍuṁ<br/>
poḍeseṇḍembivanāḍu<br/>
ttoḍavaḷedar tammoḷeḷase tantaṅgeḍegaḷ // ViVi.2.30 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 45]<br/>
antā kūsugaḷ kūsāṭavāḍuttirdondu divasaṁ maragerasiyāḍalendu<br/>
munde tamma page parvuvantepannirmattarparvidālada marada modalge vandu<br/>
bhīmanaṁmaṟemāḍikōlanīḍāḍi palavu sūḻ kāḍi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
paridanibarumoḍanaḍardire<br/>
maranaṁ muṭṭalke paḍeyadanibargaṁ kiṁ<br/>
kirivōgi bhīmasēnaṁ<br/>
maranaṁ piḍidalgepaṇvolanibarumudirdar // ViVi.2.31 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu biḻdu sulida moḻakālgaḷuṁ kaḻalda palgaḷumelvaḍagāda<br/>
meyguḷumuḍida keygaḷumāgi berasaḻuttuṁ bandu gāṅgēya dhr̥tarāṣṭrarge<br/>
kāraṇambēḻdoḍavarinditta bhīmanoḍanāḍadirimendu mudugaṇgal bārise tamma<br/>
nonda siggiṅganibarumondāgi pōgi poṟavoḻala marada keḷage maṟasondida<br/>
bhīmananaḍasi piḍidu nūrvaruṁ gaṇṭalaṁ meṭṭi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
pāvugaḷaṁ koḷisi mahā<br/>
grāvamanuṟadaḍasi kaṭṭi koraḷoḷ gaṅgā<br/>
dēviya maḍuvinoḷaḻdida<br/>
rāvarisade tamma kulamanaḍigaḻduvavōl // ViVi.2.32 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antaḻduvuduṁ gaṅgādēviya varaprasādadoḷ viṣama viṣadharaṅgaḷ<br/>
pariye koraloḷ toḍarda śileyaṁ paṟidīḍāḍi gaṅgeya nīraṁ tōḷoḷ<br/>
tuḷuṅki maguḻdu bandaṅge viṣada laḍḍugeyanikkiyumenitānumupadravaṅgaḷoḷ<br/>
toḍarikkiyuṁ gelalāṟade manamikkiyumerdeyikkiyumirdarantayvar kūsugaḷgaṁ<br/>
gāṅgēyaṁ caulōpanayanādi kriyegaḷaṁ māḍi sukhamirpannegamitta<br/>
gaṅgādvāradoḷ māyāpuramemba r̥ṣyāśramadoḷ gautamanembaṁ brahmar̥ṣi<br/>
tapaṅgeyyutirpinamā r̥ṣige billumambuṁverasorva magaṁ puṭṭidanātaṅge<br/>
śaradvatanendu pesaraniṭṭu naḍape baḷedu tapaṅgeyvātanallige jalakrīḍā<br/>
nimittadindindranaccarase jalacareyembavaḷ bandoḍākeyaṁ kaṇḍu kāmāsakta<br/>
cittanāgi kūḍi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 46]<br/>
ogeda śarastambadoḷi<br/>
rbagiyāgi manōja rāgarasamugutare to<br/>
ṭṭage bisuṭu billanambuma<br/>
nagaldanāśramadinudita lajjāvaśadiṁ // ViVi.2.33 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
annegamā tapōvanakke bēṇṭeyāḍalbanda śantanuvinoḍaneyavarā<br/>
śarastambadoḷ parikalisirda munīndranindriyadoḷogeda peṇgūsumaṁ<br/>
gaṇḍugūsumanavaṟa keladoḷirda divya śarāsana śaraṅgaḷumaṁ kaṇḍu koṇḍupōgi<br/>
śantanuge tōṟidoḍātanumā śiśudvayamaṁ nija gajapurakkuydu kr̥peyiṁ<br/>
naḍapidanappudaṟiṁ kr̥panuṁ kr̥peyumendu pesaraniṭṭu naḍaputtirpannegamavarayyaṁ<br/>
śaradvatanallige bandu kiṟiyātaṅge caulōpanayanādi kriyegaḷaṁ māḍi<br/>
dhanurvidyōpadēśaṅgeyye sarva vidyā viśāradanādanā kr̥pācāryara pakkadoḷ<br/>
kūsugaḷaṁ vidyābhyāsaṅgeyse—<br/>
</p>

<p>
bareyade banda suddageyesūtramanonde muhūrtamātradiṁ<br/>
barisidudantu sūtrisida sūtradavr̥tti nijātmavr̥ttivōl<br/>
pariṇamisittu mattuḻida vidyegaḷōjarecaṭṭarembinaṁ<br/>
nereduvu tannoḷār gaḷaguṇārṇavanantukuśāgrabuddhigaḷ // ViVi.2.34 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu pañcāṅga vyākaraṇada vr̥ttibhēdamappachandovr̥ttiyoḷaṁ<br/>
śabdālaṅkāra niṣṭhitamappalaṅkāradoḷaṁ vyāsa vālmīki kaśyapa prabhr̥ti viracitaṅgaḷappa<br/>
mahākāvyaṅgaḷoḷaṁ nāndīparōca[nā]prastāvanētivr̥ttasandhi pravēśa<br/>
viṣkambha kapōtikā vyāḷikādi lakṣaṇōpētaṅgaḷappa nāṭakaṅgaḷoḷaṁ padineṇṭu<br/>
dharmaśāstraṅgaḷoḷaṁ nālku vēdadoḷamāṟaṅgadoḷamaydu teṟada<br/>
mantraṅgaḷoḷamāṟuṁdarśanadoḷaṁ pratyakṣānumāna pramāṇaṅgaḷoḷaṁ bharata<br/>
praṇīta nr̥tyaśāstradoḷaṁnāradādi praṇīta gāndharvavidyāviśēṣaṅgaḷoḷaṁ<br/>
gajāgamajña rājaputra gautama vādvākipāḷa kaśyapasupatiśrīharṣādi purāṇa<br/>
puruṣaviracitaṅgaḷappahastiśāstraṅgaḷoḷaṁ citrakarma patracchēda graha gaṇita<br/>
[p. 47]<br/>
ratnaparīkṣegaḷoḷaṁ dārukarma vāstuvidyāpūrvayantraprayōgavi[ṣā]pa<br/>
haraṇasarabhēda ratitantēndrajāla vividha vidyegaḷoḷamanēkākṣara svarūpaṅgaḷoḷaṁ<br/>
cāpa cakra paraśu kr̥pāṇa śakti tōmara musala musuṇḍi bhiṇḍivāḷa mudgara<br/>
gadādi vividhāyudhaṅgaḷoḷamati pravīṇanumārūḍha sarvajña mahēndra<br/>
jāṇa(?)[nu]māgi —<br/>
</p>

<p>
uḷḷōdugaḷoḷagenitaṟi<br/>
vuḷḷargaṁtiḷipalariyadenipeḍegaḷumaṁ<br/>
teḷḷagiretiḷipuguṁ besa<br/>
goḷḷa guṇārṇavana lekkamaṁpokkamumaṁ // ViVi.2.35 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu lōkamellaṁ pogaḻte negaḻda pogaḻtegaṁ negaḻgegaṁ tāne<br/>
guṟiyāgi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
mānasadoḷ haṁseyavōl<br/>
mānasavāgvanite tanna mānasadoḷivaṁ<br/>
mānasanendagalade nile<br/>
mānasanādaṁ sarasvatīkaḷahaṁsaṁ // ViVi.2.36 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antadayvaruṁ samasta śastra śāstra prayōga pravīṇarāge dharmaputraṁ<br/>
dharmaśāstraṅgaḷoḷaṁ śrutismr̥tigaḷoḷaṁ pravīṇanādaṁ bhīmasēnaṁ vyākaraṇa<br/>
doḷārindamaggaḷa[ṁ]kuśalanādaṁ nakulaṁ kunta śastradoḷati pravīṇanumāgi<br/>
aśvavidyeyoḷārindaṁ piriyanādaṁ sahadēvaṁ jyōtirjñānadoḷati pariṇatanādaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
baḷeduvu tōḷgaḷekkeyinamaḷ baḷevantire muyvugaḷ kuḷā<br/>
caḷaśikharaṅgaḷaṁ masuḷevanduvu parvida vakṣamī kṣamā<br/>
taḷa kuḷalakṣmigāytu kuḷamandiramendu mahītaḷaṁ manaṁ<br/>
goḷe neṟedattudātta nava yauvanamormeye dharmaputranā // ViVi.2.37 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu sogayisuva rūpinoḷ ponna baṇṇadantappa tanna meyya<br/>
baṇṇamaḷavalladoppe—<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 48]<br/>
kuḷagiriyaṁ sarōjanilayaṁ manujākr̥tiyāge māḍidaṁ<br/>
toḷavenipantuṭappa posa baṇṇadoḷondida pārijātama<br/>
ggaḷamesedoppuvante taḷiriṁ muguḷiṁ navayauvanaṁ manaṁ<br/>
goḷe karamoppidaṁ daśa sahasra madēbha baḷaṁ vr̥kōdaraṁ // ViVi.2.38 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antoppuva gaṇḍa gāḍiyoḷindra nīladantappa baṇṇaṁ kaṇgevare—<br/>
</p>

<p>
śaradada candranaṁ vimala candrike bāḷadinēśanaṁ tamō<br/>
harakiraṇaṁ kiśōra hariyaṁ navakēsara rāji mikka di<br/>
kkariyananūna dāna pariśōbhe manaṅgoḷe porduvante suṁ<br/>
dara navayauvanaṁ neṟeye porde guṇārṇavanoppi tōṟidaṁ // ViVi.2.39 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu navayauvanaṁ neṟeye neṟeye niṟi niṟigoṇḍa guṇārṇavana<br/>
talenavirgaḷ lāvaṇyarasamaniḍidiḍidu tivida kamalāsanana beralaccugaḷannavāduvu<br/>
mūṟuṁ lōkada mūṟu paṭṭamanāḷalke takka lakṣaṇa sampūrṇamappa sahaja<br/>
manōjana lalāṭa[ṁ]paṭṭaṅgaṭṭida nosalge lakṣaṇamanaṟasalvēḍembantādudu karbina<br/>
billa koṅkinante koṅkiyuṁ paravaniteyarerdege koṅkilladeyuṁ sogayisuva<br/>
surata makaradhvajana parvugaḷ kāmadēvana vijaya vaijayantigaḷantāduvu nīḷpaṁ<br/>
beḷpumaṁ tāḷdi paravaniteyara desege kisugaṇcidante kisu serevaridu sogayisuva<br/>
śaucāñjanēyana kaṇgaḷembaralambugaḷ gaṇikājanaṅgaḷerdeyaṁ naṭṭu keṅkamādaṁ<br/>
tāduvu ripujanada perciṅgaṁ parāṅganā janadamecciṅgaṁ mūgiṟivante<br/>
sogayisuva gandhēbha vidyādharana mūgu tanna suyya kampanallade peṟara<br/>
kampanāsevaḍadantādudu posa javvanada mumbaṇṇadantekarpaṁkaikoṇḍu<br/>
katturiyalbaredantappa vikrānta tuṅgana mīsegaḷātana tīvra pratāpānaḷa<br/>
dhūmalēkheyantāduvu puḷiyoḷaleda pavaḷada baṭṭinante sogayisuva<br/>
saṁsārasārōdayana bimbādharamanaṅgarāgarasa duruḷiyantādudu rasadāḍimadabittumaṁ posa muttumaṁ mukkuḷisidantappa vibudhavanajavana kaḷahaṁsana<br/>
dantapaṅktigaḷamr̥takiraṇana kāntigaḷaniḷisuvantāduvu maḍidu tandiṭṭa posaneydila<br/>
kāvanāvagaṁ gelda ratnakuṇḍalaṅgaḷa poḷapanoḷakoṇḍante nasunēlva karṇāṭī<br/>
[p. 49]<br/>
karṇapūranapālegaḷuṁ sarasvatiyāḍuva līlāndōḷadantāduvu baḷvaḷa<br/>
beḷedeḷagauṅginante lōkada celvellamanoḷakoṇḍu rēkhegoṇḍa lāṭīlalāmana<br/>
pariṇaddha kandharaṁ yuvarāja kaṇṭhikābharaṇamaṁ kaṭṭuvudarke nōntu tanna celvanallade<br/>
peṟara celvanāsevaḍadantādudu kulada calada maimeyoḷ tannane nōḍida<br/>
santōṣadoḷutsāhamādante sogayisuva samaraikamēruvina bhujaśikharaṅgaḷ<br/>
kula śikhariśikharaṅgaḷantāduvu vyāḷagajaṅgaḷumanaṅkada bardeyarumanugibagi<br/>
māḍida santōṣadoḷ baḷvaḷa baḷeda vikrāntatuṅgana niḍudōḷgaḷ gaṇikājanakke<br/>
kāmapāśaṅgaḷumarātijanakke yamapāśaṅgaḷumāduvu raktāśōka pallavadante<br/>
toḷatoḷaguvāndhrī kucakalaśa pallavana karataḷapallavaṅgaḷ samada gajakumbha<br/>
sthaḷāsphāḷana karkaśaṅgaḷāduvu poḍarva pagevaranuṟadekoṇḍasantōṣadoḷaṁ<br/>
śrīyanoḷakoṇḍa santōṣadoḷaṁ tekkane tīvida kēraḷīkēḷi kandarpanagaluraṁ<br/>
lakṣmige kulabhavanamuṁ nivāsabhavanamumādudu poḍarva maṇḍaḷikara manadante<br/>
karamasidāda parākramadhavaḷana madhyapradēśaṁ nārāyaṇaṁ tannāḷdaṁ māḍi<br/>
tānāḷmāḍiyuṁ tānaḷḷāḍeyuṁ bardeyara manavanaḷḷāḍisuvantādudu<br/>
gambhīraguṇadoḷamāvartana siddhiyoḷaṁ jaḷanidhiyane pōlva śaraṇāgata jaḷanidhiya<br/>
nimna nābhi celviṅge tāne nābhiyādudu siṁha kaṭitaṭamaniḷisuva ripukuraṅga<br/>
kaṇṭhīravana kaṭitaṭamoldu nōḍuva gāḍikārtiyara kaṇge kāmanaḍḍaṇadante<br/>
doḍḍittāgi mīṟuvudvr̥tta vr̥ttateyanīḻdukoṇḍantudvr̥ttaṅgaḷāduvu<br/>
udāttanārāyaṇanūru yugmaṅgaḷ māniniyara manōgajaṅgaḷaṁ kaṭṭalkālāna<br/>
stambhaṅgaḷāduvu antapūrvaṅgaḷāgi toḷaguva kiṟudoḍegaḷuḍuvaḍardannamārūḍha<br/>
sarvajñana doḍḍamārgaṅgaḷeḷavāḻeyadiṇḍinoḷ sāṇegaṭṭidantāduvu<br/>
gū[ḍha]gulphapārṣṇigaḷanoḷakoṇḍa manujamāndhātana poṟa aḍigaḷ virōdhi<br/>
bhūpāḷaranaḍigeṟagisida santōṣadoḷunnataṅgaḷādante kūrmōnnataṅgaḷāduvu<br/>
nosalaṁ suṭṭi tōrpannavappuṅguṭaṅgaḷoḷ miñcaṁ kīlisidante toḷagi poḷeva<br/>
pracaṇḍamārtāṇḍana pādanakhaṅgaḷ gaṇḍara peṇḍirañjidaḷkida mogamaṁ nōḍalke<br/>
kannaḍigaḷannavāduvu posatalarda kendāvareya kempumaṁmelpumaniḻkuḷigoṇḍu<br/>
[p. 50]<br/>
toḷaguvarikēsariya pādataḷaṅgaḷaḍigeṟagidari narapālara makuṭamāṇikyamarīcijāla<br/>
bāḷātapaṅgaḷanaledu keṅkamādantāduvu posavesaṟageya baṇṇadante sogayisuva<br/>
sāmanta cūḍāmaṇiya meyya baṇṇaṁ vidhātranemba cittāriya varṇakramaṅgeyda<br/>
kadaḷīgarbhaśyāmamemba baṇṇadantādudu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
manadoḷoṟaldu jōldaḷipi nōḍaloḍaṁ seṟegeydu kaṇṇumaṁ<br/>
manamumanaṅgajanmaralambugaḷiṁdemaruḷci banda mā<br/>
vina banadoḷ teraḷci poḷevindumarīcigaḷinduruḷci pū<br/>
vina paseyoḷ poraḷcidanaḷurkeya bardeyaraṁ guṇārṇavaṁ // ViVi.2.40 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu nakula sahadēvar sahitamayvaruṁ navayauvanada paramasukhamaneydi<br/>
santōṣadinirdaritta gaṅgādvāradoḷ bharadvājanemba brahmar̥ṣi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
snānārthamondu kaḷaśama<br/>
nā niyama nidhānaneḻale piḍidamaḷina gaṁ<br/>
gānadige vandu surata ni<br/>
dhāniyanamarēndragaṇikeyaṁ muni kaṇḍaṁ // ViVi.2.41 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu kāṇbudumamr̥tābdhiyembaccaraseya kanakakāñcīkaḷāpadoḷ<br/>
toḍarda dēvāṅga vastraduḷḷuḍeyoḷuliva sūsakadanūlatoṅgalveraseḻalva mundaṇa<br/>
sōge kārgālada sōgeyante sogayise—<br/>
</p>

<p>
ādelara sōṅkinoḷ teṟa<br/>
pādoḍe beḷpeseye maseda madanana bāḷaṁ<br/>
tāduvu poḷevoḷdoḍeteṟa<br/>
pāderdeyaṁ naṭṭuvandutanmunipatiyā // ViVi.2.42 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu kantuśaraparavaśanāgi dhairya kṣaraṇeyumindriya kṣaraṇeyu<br/>
moḍanoḍanāge—<br/>
</p>

<p>
māṇade sōrvindriyamaṁ<br/>
drōṇadoḷāntalliyogeda śiśuvaṁ kaṇḍī<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 51]<br/>
drōṇadoḷe puṭṭidītaṁ<br/>
drōṇane pōgendu pesaraniṭṭaṁ munipaṁ // ViVi.2.43 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu bharadvājanātmatanūjaṅge pesaraniṭṭu tanna keḷeyaṁ pāñcāḷa<br/>
dēśadarasaṁ pr̥ṣatanembanātana magaṁ drupadanumaṁ drōṇanumanoḍagūḍi<br/>
yajñasēnanemba brahmar̥ṣiya pakkadoḷ bilviddeyaṁ kalalvēḻdoḍe drōṇanuṁ<br/>
drupadanuṁ dhanurdharāgragaṇyarāge bharadvājaṁ drōṇaṅge kr̥pana taṅgeyappa<br/>
śāradvateyaṁ tandu maduveyaṁ māḍidoḍātaṅgamākegaṁ triṇētranaṁśadoḷorva<br/>
magaṁ puṭṭi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
divijāśvatthāmadoḷī<br/>
bhuvanaṅgaḷ naḍuge śiśu saraṅgeydoḍe na<br/>
kkavayavade kumbhasambhava<br/>
nivanaśvatthāmanendu pesariḍe negaḻdaṁ // ViVi.2.44 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu negaḻdu tammayyana kaiyoḷ dhanurvidyōpadēśadoḷ<br/>
dhanurdharāgragaṇyanumāgi sanda[ṁ]drupadanuṁ tanna rājyadoḷ ninda[ṁ]drōṇanuṁ<br/>
tanage baḍatanamaḍase aśvatthāmananoḍagoṇḍu nāḍu nāḍaṁ toḻaldu<br/>
paraśurāmanallige vandaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
kṣitiyoḷaguḷḷa bhūbhujara bittu modalgiḍe munnamēkaviṁ<br/>
śati parisaṅkhyeyiṁ tavisi sarvanivēdakamemba yajñadoḷ<br/>
kṣiti pogaḻvannamittu gurudakṣiṇeyāgire kaśyapa prajā<br/>
patige samudra mudrita dharitriyanondaḻiyūranīvavol // ViVi.2.45 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu valkalāvr̥ta kaṭitaṭanumāgirdajaṭākalāpanumāgi tapōvanakke<br/>
pōpa bhārgavaṁ dravyārthiyāgi banda kumbhasambhavanaṁ kaṇḍu kanakapātrakkupāya<br/>
millappudaṟiṁ mr̥tpātradoḷarghyamettipūjisi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
oḍameyanarthigittenavanītaḷamaṁ gurugittenīgaḷoṁ<br/>
daḍakeyumilla kaiyoḷeredaṁ śrutapāraganentu santasaṁ<br/>
baḍisuveninnidondu dhanuvirdudu divyaśarāḷiyirdudi<br/>
lloḍame samantu pēḻivaṟoḷāvudanīvudo kumbhasambhavā // ViVi.2.46 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 52]<br/>
embuduṁ drōṇanenage vidyādhaname dhanamappudaṟiṁ divyāstraṅgaḷaṁ<br/>
dayegeyvudene vāruṇa vāyavyāgnēyapaurandarādi pradhānāstraṅgaḷaṁ kuḍe<br/>
koṇḍu paraśurāmanaṁ bīḻkoḍu tannoḍanāḍiyappa keḷeyaṁ drupadaṁ<br/>
chatrāvatiyoḷarasugeydapanendu kēḷdā poḻalge vandu drupadanaramaneya<br/>
bāgiloḷ nindu paḍiyaṟanaṁ karedu nimmoḍanāḍida keḷeyaṁ drōṇanemba pārvaṁ<br/>
bandanendu nimmarasaṅgaṟiye pēḻembudumātanā māḻkeyoḷe bandaṟipuvuduṁ<br/>
drupadaṁ rājyamadirāmadōnmattanuṁ garvagrahavyagracittanumāgi mēgillade—<br/>
</p>

<p>
antembanārge piriduṁ<br/>
bhrāntu dalēṁ drōṇanembanēṁ pārvane pē<br/>
ḻentenage keḷeyanē nūṁ<br/>
kantappananaṟiyenendu sabheyoḷ nuḍidaṁ // ViVi.2.47 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu nuḍidudaṁ paḍiyaṟaṁ bandāmāḻkeyoḷaṟipe drōṇa<br/>
nottambadindoḷagaṁ pokku drupadanaṁ kaṇḍu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
aṟiyire nīmumāmumoḍanōdidevembudanaṇṇa ninnanā<br/>
naṟiyenadelli kaṇḍeyo mahīpatigaṁ dvijavaṁśajaṅgamē<br/>
taṟa keḷeyintu nāṇiligarappare mānasaremba mātugaḷ<br/>
neṟagoḷe kumbhasambhavananā drupadaṁ kaḍu siggu māḍidaṁ // ViVi.2.48 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu māḍidudumalladī nāṇili pārvananeḻedu kaḷeyimembuduṁ<br/>
drōṇanintendaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
nuḍi taḍavappudondu mogadoḷ maṟukaṁ dorekoḷvudondu nā<br/>
ṇgeḍeguḍadirpudondu nuḍigaḷ moṟeyaṁ maṟeyippudondu ka<br/>
ḷguḍidavarandamintu siri sārtaresārvudadarke sandeyaṁ<br/>
baḍade jalakkanīgaḷaṟideṁ siri kaḷḷoḍavuṭṭitembudaṁ // ViVi.2.49 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu sairisade—<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 53]<br/>
khaḷa noḷaviṅgekuppevaramembavolāmbaramuṇṭe ninnadoṁ<br/>
daḷavoḍanōdidondu beragiṅge kolalkenagāgadī sabhā<br/>
vaḷayadoḷennanēḻisida ninnananākuḷamenna caṭṭariṁ<br/>
taḷaveḷagāge kaṭṭisade māṇdoḍe kemma[ne]mīsevottenē // ViVi.2.50 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endārūḍhapratijñanāgi nāgapurakke vandu tamma bhāvaṁ kr̥pana maneyoḷa<br/>
pagatapariśramanāgirdondu divasaṁ pāṇḍavaruṁ kauravaruṁ poṟavoḻaloḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
neredisutiretōlvulleya<br/>
niradadu biḻdoḍe purāṇa kūpadoḷadani<br/>
nnaridu tegevandamendava<br/>
rire baḷasiyumalli kaṇḍu nakkaṁ drōṇaṁ // ViVi.2.51 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
bharatakuḷatiḷakarir‌ vara<br/>
śarāsana vyagrahastarir‌ baḷayutarir<br/>
neredinibarumī lakṣyama<br/>
niradakkaṭa sarade tegeyalārtirumillā // ViVi.2.52 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu tanna maganappaśvatthāmanaṁ karedī lakṣyamaṁ tegeyembudu<br/>
mātanantegeyvenendu naiṣṭhikamemba muṣṭiyoḷaṁ puṅkhānupuṅkhamemba śara<br/>
sandhānadoḷavayavadoḷe tegedoḍanibaruṁ cōdyambaṭṭu gāṅgēya<br/>
dhr̥tarāṣṭrargaṟipidoḍe nadītanūjaṁ bhāradvājaṅge baḻiyanaṭṭi barisi pūrva<br/>
sambhāṣaṇārghyametti madhuparka vētrāsana tāmbūla dānādigaḷiṁ santasaṁ baḍisi<br/>
tadīya kula vidyāvr̥ttigaḷaṁ besagoṇḍu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
madamaṁ mukkuḷisirdibhaṅgaḷanudagrāśvaṅgaḷaṁ takkina<br/>
ggada bāḍaṅgaḷanāydu koṭṭu taṇideṁ pō sālgumembannamaṁ<br/>
didiroḷ nūṟaṟuvar kumārarumaniṭṭī kūsugaḷ yōgyara<br/>
ppudaninnolvoḍe śastravidyegovajaṁ nīnāgu kumbhōdbhavā // ViVi.2.53 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
embudumantegeyvenendu kalaśajananibara mogamaṁ nōḍi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 54]<br/>
ī neredinibarumenduda<br/>
nēnīvire pēḻimendoḍanibarumirdar<br/>
maunavratade guṇārṇava<br/>
nānīveṁ nimma bayasi bēḻpudanendaṁ // ViVi.2.54 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
embudumā mātiṅge mecci jagadēkamallanaṁ toḍeyanēṟisikoṇḍu<br/>
kumbhasambhavaṁ gāṅgēyananintendaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
inibaroḷagītanorvane<br/>
dhanurāgamadeḍege kuśalanakkumadarkēṁ<br/>
kinisadiriṁ munnaṟipide<br/>
nene bhīṣmanalampu mige muguḷnage nakkaṁ // ViVi.2.55 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu drōṇācāryanācāryapadaviyaṁ kaikoṇḍu pāṇḍava kauravarge<br/>
caturaṅga dhanurvēdamumaṁ divyāstraṅgaḷumaṁ śakti tōmara musala musuṇḍi<br/>
bhiṇḍivāḷa mudgara gadādi vividhāyudhaṅgaḷumaṁ gaja ratha turaga padāti<br/>
yuddhaṅgaḷumanupadēśaṁ geyyuttumireyire—<br/>
</p>

<p>
yādava vaṁśajaruṁ nā<br/>
nā dēśa narēndraruṁ ghaṭōdbhavana dhanu<br/>
rvēdamane kalal bandā<br/>
ḷādar vidyāprabhāvamā dorete valaṁ // ViVi.2.56 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
drōṇaṁ gaḍamiṣuvidyege<br/>
jāṇaṁ gaḍamendu kēḷdu kauravargellaṁ<br/>
prāṇaṁ barpākr̥tiyoḷe<br/>
bāṇāsana bāṇapāṇi karṇaṁ bandaṁ // ViVi.2.57 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu bandu vairigajaghaṭāvighaṭananoḷ vighaṭisi bilgaltu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
keḷeyuṁ guṟiyuṁ goṭṭiyu<br/>
maḷavige piridāge tanage duryōdhananoḷ<br/>
muḷisuṁ nōvuṁ kaluṣamu<br/>
muḷumbamene tanagarātikāḷānaḷanoḷ // ViVi.2.58 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 55]<br/>
antu karṇaṁ guṇārṇavanoḷ seṇasi pageyanabhyāsaṅgeyvante<br/>
vidyābhyāsaṅgeyye—<br/>
</p>

<p>
manadoḷogedanyajanmada<br/>
munisadu kaṇṇiṁ tuḷuṅke sairisadavanu<br/>
rvina kalitanakke duryō<br/>
dhananuṁ bhīmanoḷe seṇasi gadeyaṁ kaltaṁ // ViVi.2.59 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu bhāradvājanāgāmika saṅgrāmaraṅgakke pātraṅgaḷaṁ sameyisuva<br/>
sūtradhāranante śastravidyābhyāsaṁ geysuttire dēśādhīśvararappa palambar‌<br/>
rājakumārara naḍuve tārāgaṇaṅgaḷa naḍuvaṇa sakaḷa kaḷādharanante śastrakaḷādharanāgi<br/>
tannumaṁ gelevanda sāmanta cūḍāmaṇiya śarapariṇatiyanārayalendu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
chāyā lakṣyamanoḍḍiyu<br/>
māyada nīroḷage tannanaḍasida negaḻaṁ<br/>
bāyaḻivinamisisiyumare<br/>
hōyaja bāppendu hariganaṁ guru pogaḻdaṁ // ViVi.2.60 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu pogaḻdu tanna pagevanappa drupadananītanamōghaṁ gelal neṟegumendu<br/>
niścaisi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
aṇuginoḷenna caṭṭaroḷagītane jeṭṭiganendu viddeyaṁ<br/>
guṇakaṟugoṇḍu koṭṭenage santasamappinamīva ninna da<br/>
kṣiṇeyadu bēgamā drupadanaṁ gaḍa kōḍagagaṭṭugaṭṭi taṁ<br/>
daṇiyaramoppisintidane bēḍidenāṁ parasainyabhairavā // ViVi.2.61 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
embudamī besanadāvudu gahanamendu pūṇdu pōgi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
oḍavandaṅkada kauravar drupadanambēṟiṅge meyyoḍḍado<br/>
ḍḍoḍedōḍuttire sūse bīḻva talegaḷsūḻpaṭṭanāgaḷ javaṁ<br/>
piḍidīḍāḍuva māḻkeyante palaraṁ kondikki meymuṭṭevaṁ<br/>
deḍeyoḷ māṇaduruḷci kaṭṭi ripuvaṁ mundikkidaṁ drōṇanā // ViVi.2.62 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgaḷā kumbhasambhavaṁ parākramadhavaḷana parākramakke mecci kadampaṁ karci<br/>
drupadanaṁ tanna mañcada kāloḷ kaṭṭavēḻdu taleya mēle kālanavaṣṭambhadiṁ nīḍi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 56]<br/>
sirimeyyoḷagandaṟivire<br/>
neraviyoḷāraṟivarorme kaṇḍaranaṟiya<br/>
lkaridemmaṁ baḍapārvara<br/>
narasare nīmīgaḷaṟiviraṟiyiro pēḻiṁ // ViVi.2.63 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu sāye sarasaṁ nuḍidu mattamintendaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
ādi kṣatriyarē nī<br/>
mādityananiḷipa tējarirpārvana kāl<br/>
mōde naḍutaleyalirpudu<br/>
mādudu nimagendu nuḍidu kāypinoḷodedaṁ // ViVi.2.64 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
odedu ninnaninitu paribhavambaḍisidudu sālguṁ ninnaṁ kolalāgadu<br/>
kondoḍe mēlappa pagegañji kondantāgirkumendu kaṭṭida kaṭṭugaḷellamaṁ tāne<br/>
biṭṭu kaḷedu pōgembuduṁ drupadaṁ paribhavānaḷanaḷavalladaḷure ninnaṁ kolvanna<br/>
