norva maganumaṁ vikramārjunaṅge peṇḍatiyappannaḷorva magaḷumaṁ paḍedalladire<br/>
nendu mahā pratijñārūḍhanāgi pōdanitta bhāradvājaṁ pāṇḍava kauravarkaḷa meyyoḷe<br/>
viddeyaṁ neṟeye saṅkramisida tanna vidyāmahimeyaṁ meṟeyalke bāhlīka<br/>
bhūriśravassōma datta gāṅgēya dhr̥tarāṣṭra vidurarkaḷgintendaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
neṟeye dhanurvidyeya ka<br/>
ṇdeṟevinegaṁ kaltanimma makkaḷa meyyoḷ<br/>
meṟedappenenna viddeya<br/>
naṟidoykane neredu nōḻpudanibarumīgaḷ // ViVi.2.65 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endoḍantegeyvamendanibarumoḍambaṭṭu poṟavoḻaloḷuttara<br/>
diśābhāgadoḷ sama caturasramāge nelananaḷedu kallaṁ pullumaṁ sōdisi śubhadina<br/>
śubhamuhūrtadoḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
gaṭṭisi sindhuradoḷ nela<br/>
gaṭṭisi cembonna neleya caupaḷigegaḷoḷ<br/>
kaṭṭisi paḻayigegaḷanaḷa<br/>
vaṭṭire biyamalli moḻage palavuṁ paṟegaḷ // ViVi.2.66 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 57]<br/>
antu sameda vyāyāma raṅgakke gāṅgēya dhr̥tarāṣṭra vidura sōmadatta<br/>
bāhlīka bhūriśravādi kulavr̥ddharuṁ kunti gāndhārigaḷuṁverasu bandu kuḷḷire—<br/>
</p>

<p>
arasiyaranaṇugaraṁ bē<br/>
ḻparumaṁmonegāṟaraṁ pragītaranimbā<br/>
gire caupaḷigegaḷoḷ ku<br/>
ḷḷirisidaroḍaneseye nereda purajana sahitaṁ // ViVi.2.67 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgaḷ kumbhasambhavaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
posa muttina tuḍige poda<br/>
ḻdeseye dukūlāmbaraṁ nijāṅgadoḷ saṁ<br/>
desedire beḷmugilindaṁ<br/>
musukida nīlādri barpa teṟadoḷ bandaṁ // ViVi.2.68 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu bandu raṅgabhūmiya naḍuve nindu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
negaḻdire puṇyāha svara<br/>
mogedire paṭu paṭaha kāhaḷā ravavāgaḷ<br/>
pugavēḻdaṁ vividhāstra<br/>
pragalbharaṁ tanna caṭṭaraṁ kaḷaśabhavaṁ // ViVi.2.69 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu pugavēḻvuduṁ di<br/>
gdantigaḷuṁ kulanagaṅgaḷuṁ gaḍaṇaṅgoṁ<br/>
ḍentu kavitarkamante ne<br/>
laṁ taḷarvinegaṁ pracaṇḍa kōdaṇḍadharar // ViVi.2.70 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu dharmaputranaṁ muntiṭṭu bhīmārjuna nakula sahadēvaruṁ<br/>
duryōdhananaṁ muntiṭṭu yuyutsu duśyāsana dussaha dussaḷa jarāsandha satyasandha<br/>
nissaharājasandha vinda anuvinda durmati subāhu dusparśana durmarṣaṇa<br/>
durmukha duṣkarṇa vikarṇa viviṁśati sulōcana sunābha citra upacitra nanda<br/>
upananda sucitrāṅgada citrakuṇḍala suhasta dr̥ḍhahasta pramāthi dīrghabāhu<br/>
mahābāhu pratima supratima sapramāthi durdharṣaṇa duṣparājaya mitra upamitra<br/>
cauḷōpa dvandvahasta pratīpa supratīpa prahasta pratāpa pramada sadbāhugaḷ<br/>
modalāgi nūrvaruṁ bandu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 58]<br/>
gadeyoḷ billoḷ gajadoḷ<br/>
kudureyoḷaṁrathadoḷastrakauśalade beḍaṁ<br/>
godaviretōṟidaravaro<br/>
rmodale janaṁ pogaḻe negaḻe jaḷanidhi ninadaṁ // ViVi.2.71 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antavariṁ baḻiyaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
āda muḷisindamāgaḷ<br/>
mōduva bage baḷeye piḍida gadegaḷinipaṁ<br/>
tādudu suyōdhanōgra vr̥<br/>
kōdararormodale śikharamuḷḷeraḍagamaṁ // ViVi.2.72 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antirvarumorvarorvaroḷ seṇasi bahuprayōga gadā kauśalamaṁ<br/>
tōṟalendu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
geḍevaccirvar managoṁ<br/>
ḍoḍanoḍanōrantu taguḷdu jhēṅkarisidoḍe<br/>
lvaḍagāge mōdalendi<br/>
rdeḍeyoḷ guru tanna magananeḍevugavēḻdaṁ // ViVi.2.73 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu mēredappal bageda mahāsamudraṅgaḷeraḍaṟa naḍuve<br/>
kulagiriyirpantirdaśvatthāmanaṁ kaṇḍirvarumeraḍuṁ desege tolagi nindāgaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
ā dūrvāṅkura varṇado<br/>
ḷādamoḍambaṭṭa kanaka kavacaṁ rāja<br/>
tkōdaṇḍamamarda doṇe ka<br/>
ṇgādame bare bandu munde nindaṁ harigaṁ // ViVi.2.74 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgaḷ kumbhasambhavanuliva janada kaḷakaḷa ravamumaṁ moḻaguva<br/>
paṟegaḷumaṁ bārisi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
ītaṁ guṇārṇavaṁ vi<br/>
khyāta yaśaṁ vairigajaghaṭāvighaṭananiṁ<br/>
tītana sāhasamupamā<br/>
tītamidaṁ nōḍimendu neravige nuḍidaṁ // ViVi.2.75 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 59]<br/>
ā prastāvadoḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
oḍegumajāṇḍaminninisu jēvoḍedāgaḷe bommanuṁ manaṁ<br/>
giḍugumadēvudendu miḍidoyyane jēvoḍedāgaḷambanaṁ<br/>
[bo]ḍanoḍanīmbuvembanitu sandeyamappinamastra jāladiṁ<br/>
taḍeyade pañjarambaḍedanandu viyattaḷadoḷ guṇārṇavaṁ // ViVi.2.76 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
mattamaindra vāruṇa vāyavyāgnēya pārvatādi bāṇaṅgaḷaṁ tuḍe—<br/>
</p>

<p>
kaviduvu kāḷa nīḷa jaḷadāvaḷi vāridhigaḷ dharitriyaṁ<br/>
kaviduvu gāḷigaḷ praḷayakālamanāgisalende lōkamaṁ<br/>
kaviduvu mokkaḷaṁ kaviduvugra layāgnigaḷante beṭṭugaḷ<br/>
kaviduvivembanittu bhayamāytu guṇārṇavanastrakauśalaṁ // ViVi.2.77 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgaḷā parākramadhavaḷana śarapariṇatiyaṁ kaṇḍu duryōdhanana mogaṁ<br/>
talenavira gaṇṭiṁ kiṟidāge drōṇa bhīṣma kr̥pa vidura prabhr̥tigaḷa mogamaralda<br/>
tāvareyiṁ piridāge—<br/>
</p>

<p>
toḷaguva tējaṁtoḷatoḷa<br/>
toḷaguva divyāstramamarda kōdaṇḍamasuṁ<br/>
goḷisemanaṅgoḷise bhayaṁ<br/>
goḷisesabhāsadaranuṟade karṇaṁ bandaṁ // ViVi.2.78 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
bandu drōṇācāryaṅge poḍamaṭṭu śaradhiyiṁ divyāstraṅgaḷa<br/>
nurcikoṇḍu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
arigana bilbalmayoḷaṁ<br/>
deraḍillade bagedamuḷisumēvamumerdeyoḷ<br/>
barediretōṟidanāyata<br/>
karaparighaṁkarṇanātma śarapariṇitiyaṁ // ViVi.2.79 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 60]<br/>
antu tōṟeyumerdeya muḷisu nālagege vare sairisalāṟade vidviṣṭa<br/>
vidrāvaṇananintendaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
saṅgatadinīgaḷintī<br/>
raṅgame raṇaraṅgamāge kāduvamaḷavaṁ<br/>
poṁgadiridircadēṁ gaḷa<br/>
raṅgambokkāḍuvante peṇḍire gaṇḍar // ViVi.2.80 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
embudumatirathamathananintendaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
ī nereda gurujanaṅgaḷa<br/>
māniniyara munde karṇa polladu nuḍidai<br/>
nīnennī niḍudōḷgaḷa<br/>
tīnaṁ maḻgisuveyappoḍānolladanē // ViVi.2.81 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
embuduṁ drōṇanuṁ kr̥panumeḍege vandu karṇananintendar—<br/>
</p>

<p>
ēvada muḷisina kāraṇa<br/>
māvudo nīṁ ninna tāya tandeya deseyaṁ<br/>
bhāvisade karṇa nuḍivaṁ<br/>
tāvudu samakaṭṭu ninagamarikēsarigaṁ // ViVi.2.82 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
embudumā mātiṅge maṟuvātuguḍalaṟiyade pandeyaṁ<br/>
pāvaḍardantummane bemaruttumirda karṇanaṁ duryōdhanaṁkaṇḍudrōṇanumaṁ<br/>
kr̥panumanintendaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
kulamembuduṇṭe bīrame<br/>
kulamallade kulamanintu pikkadiriṁ nī<br/>
molidelli puṭṭi baḷediro<br/>
kulamirdude koḍadoḷaṁ śarastambadoḷaṁ // ViVi.2.83 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu nuḍidu karṇananīgaḷe kulajanaṁ māḍi tōrpenendu keyyaṁ<br/>
piḍidoḍagoṇḍu pōgi kanakapīṭhada mēle kuḷḷirisi kanaka kaḷaśadaltīvidagaṇyapuṇya<br/>
tīrthōdakaṅgaḷaṁ caturvēdapāragarindabhiṣēkaṅgeysi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 61]<br/>
maṅgaḷavaṟegaḷ śubha vaca<br/>
naṅgaḷ camarīruhaṅgaḷā śvētaccha<br/>
traṅgaḷamardeseye karṇaṁ<br/>
gaṅgamahītaḷa vibhūtiyaṁ neṟeyittaṁ // ViVi.2.84 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antittu nityadānakke dēva sabaḷada padineṇṭu kōṭi ponnumanittu<br/>
nīnenagondanīyalvēḻpudendu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
poḍamaḍuvar jīyembar<br/>
kuḍu dayegeyyēṁ prasādamembivu peṟaroḷ<br/>
naḍegemma ninnayeḍeyoḷ<br/>
naḍeyalvēḍenage keḷeyanai rādhēyā // ViVi.2.85 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu bēḍikoṇḍu karṇanaṁ mundiṭṭoḍagoṇḍu pōgi dhr̥tarāṣṭraṅgaṁ<br/>
gāndhārigaṁ poḍamaḍisidāgaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
intu suyōdhanaṁ ninage māḍida rājya vibhūtigunte mu<br/>
yvāntiradir guṇārṇavaninastamayakkidu sālgamīgaḷeṁ<br/>
bantevolandu mundaṟidu tanna magaṅge samantu buddhivē<br/>
ḻvantevo[latta]lastagiriyaṁmaṟegoṇḍudu sūrya maṇḍalaṁ // ViVi.2.86 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgaḷ duryōdhananaṁ mundiṭṭoḍagoṇḍu dhr̥tarāṣṭra karṇa śalya śakuni<br/>
saindhava prabhr̥tigaḷ nelaṁ mūriviṭṭantesabhākṣōbhamāge taḷerdu nānā vidha<br/>
vāhanaṅgaḷanēṟi nija nivāsaṅgaḷge pōdaritta dharmaputranaṁ mundiṭṭu bhīmārjuna<br/>
nakula sahadēvaruṁ gāṅgēya drōṇa kr̥pa vidura prabhr̥tigaḷ nānā vidha<br/>
vāhanaṅgaḷanēṟi bare purajanaṅgaḷellamōrōrvarane piḍiyaccuviḍidu nuḍiye<br/>
kelaranāgatamanaṟiva buddhiyoḍeyarintembar—<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 62]<br/>
avarivarannarinnarenavēḍarikēsarigāmpanilla mī<br/>
ṟuva taledōrpa gaṇḍaraṇamilleḍeyoḷ geḍevaccugoṇḍu pāṁ<br/>
ḍavaranakāraṇaṁ keṇakidī posa poḻtaṟoḷāda kircu kau<br/>
ravargidu nāḍeyuṁ tiṇukanāgisadēṁ gaḷa saytu pōkumē // ViVi.2.87 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endorvarorvarondondane nuḍiyuttuṁ pōge beḷaguva kaidīvigegaḷ<br/>
kaḻtaleyaṁ taledōṟalīyade pracaṇḍamārtāṇḍana tējōṅkuraṅgaḷ beḷaguvante<br/>
beḷage pāṇḍavar nijanivāsakke pōdarāgaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
eseva nijavaṁśamaṁ pe<br/>
rcisuva guṇārṇavanoḷunte seṇasalkendi<br/>
rpa suyōdhanaṅgemuḷisiṁ<br/>
kisugaṇcidateṟadinamr̥takaranudayisidaṁ // ViVi.2.88 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgaḷ duryōdhanaṁ bhīmasēnana ballāḷtanadaḷavumaṁ vikramārjunana<br/>
divyāstra kauśaḷamumaṁ kaṇḍu tannerdeyuṁ poḷḷumaranaṁ kircaḷurvantoḷagoḷa<br/>
gaḷure sairisalāṟade karṇanaṁ karedāḷōcisi tammayyanallige pōgi poḍamaṭṭu<br/>
kaṭṭēkāntadoḷintendaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
piriyar‌ nīmire pāṇḍurājane valaṁ muṁ paṭṭamaṁ kaṭṭe bhū<br/>
bharamaṁ tāḷdidanīgaḷātana sutar tāmāgaḷē yōgyarā<br/>
gare paṭṭakke taguḷdu pālaneṟevir pāviṅge dāyādyaraṁ<br/>
piriyarmāḍidiremma sāvumuḻivuṁ daivēccheyāytāgadē // ViVi.2.89 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
adalladeyuṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
male taledōṟadendudanekoṭṭudaḍaṅgamaḍaṅgi bandoḍo<br/>
kkaligavesarge pūṇdudu kuṟumbu taṟumbade mikka śatru maṁ<br/>
ḍaḷikare mitramaṇḍaḷikarādaranākuḷamindu nāḷe mā<br/>
rmaledaranikki nammaneḻedikkugumī neleyiṁ guṇārṇavaṁ // ViVi.2.90 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu vikramārjunaṁ bilgoḷaluṁ bhīmasēnaṁ gadegoḷalu<br/>
māmpudaridupāṁśuvadhade keyge māḍuvuduttamapakṣamantumalladeyuṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 63]<br/>
svāmyārtha svāmya vikrāntaṁ marmajñaṁ vyavasāyinaṁ<br/>
ardharājyaharaṁ bhr̥tyaṁ yō na hanyātsa hanyatē // ViVi.2.90 [anuṣṭubh]<br/>
</p>

<p>
embudarthaśāstra sadbhāvaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
mēṇkulamilleyō namage dāyigarallarośastravidyeyoḷ<br/>
pūṇkegaḷilleyō dharege munnavarayyane mukhyanallanō<br/>
jāṇkiṟidāgavēḍa manadal nimagayya vidhātr̥yōgadiṁ<br/>
kaṇkuruḍādoḍēno kuruḍāgalevēḻpude nimma buddhiyuṁ // ViVi.2.91 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu tanna manadoḷoḍambaḍe nuḍida magana mātaṁ dhr̥tarāṣṭraṁ<br/>
manadegoṇḍu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
ēnerdegoṇḍa kajjamane pēḻdeyō cintisutirpenānumē<br/>
nānumupāyamaṁ bagevarantavargaḷ ninagende kanda pēḻ<br/>
nīnire paṭṭamuṁ nelanumappudanolvene vairigaḷge nī<br/>
nēnumadarke cintisadirilliralīvene pāṇḍuputraraṁ // ViVi.2.92 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu duryōdhananaṁ bīḍiṅge pōgalvēḻdu pāṇḍavarayvarumaṁ barisi<br/>
dhr̥tarāṣṭraṁ toḍeyanēṟisikoṇḍu duryōdhananappoḍe pollamānasanātanuṁ<br/>
nīmumondeḍeyoḷire kisuṟuṁ kalahamumenduṁ kundadadukāraṇaṁ gaṅgānadiya<br/>
dakṣiṇa taṭadoḷ vāraṇāvatamembudu poḻal kurujāṅgaṇa viṣayakke tiḷakamappaṁ<br/>
tirdudallige pōgi sukhamirimendoḍantegeyvemendu bīḻkoṇḍu bīḍiṅgevandu<br/>
gāṅgēya drōṇa kr̥pa vidurarkaḷgaṁ kuntigaṁ tadvr̥ttāntamanaṟipidarannegamitta<br/>
duryōdhananavara pōganaṟidu purōcananemba tanna manadannanappa pergaḍeyoḷ<br/>
lākṣāgr̥hōpāyamaṁ carcisi vāraṇāvatamanondē divasadoḷeydu vantāge<br/>
rathamaṁ samakaṭṭi nālku lakka balamaṁ nerambēḻdu kaḷipidanāgaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
uditōditanai nīṁ nina<br/>
gudayadamēludayamendu negaḻdarigaṅga<br/>
bhyudayamanaṟipuva teṟadiṁ<br/>
dudayācaḷa cumbi bimbaninanudayisidaṁ // ViVi.2.93 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 64]<br/>
ā prastāvadoḷ maṅgaḷa pāṭhakara maṅgaḷa vr̥ttōccāraṇegaḷindaṁ<br/>
pāṇḍavarayvarumunmīlitanayanarāgi nityaniyamaṅgaḷaṁ nirvartisi maṅgaḷavasadanaṁ<br/>
goṇḍu mahābrāhmaṇar parasuva parakegaḷumanikkuva sēsegaḷumanāntukoḷuttuṁ<br/>
palavuṁ teṟada prayāṇa paṭahaṅgaḷeseye śubha lakṣaṇa lakṣitaṅgaḷappājānēya<br/>
kāmbhōja vājirājigaḷoḷ pūḍida divya rathaṅgaḷanēṟi divyabāṇāsana<br/>
bāṇapāṇigaḷāgi nijaparijanaṁ berasu gāṅgēya drōṇa kr̥pa vidurar kaḷiputtuṁ<br/>
bare purajanaṅgaḷellaṁ neredavara pōgiṅgaḻaldu sairisalāṟade—<br/>
</p>

<p>
manadoḷalampu poṇme nuḍiduṁ naḍe nōḍiyumāṭapāṭamuṁ<br/>
binadamumārumaṁ maṟeyisuttire bīdigaḷoḷ viḷāsado<br/>
ḍḍenisi toḻalva pāṇḍavara pōginoḷunte beḍaṅgugeṭṭu ha<br/>
stinapura[mi]ndu rakkasana tinda poḻalgeṇeyāgadirkumē // ViVi.2.94 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu kaṇṇanīraṁ negape—<br/>
</p>

<p>
parasuva pauravr̥ddhara kulāṅganeyarkaḷa sādhu vādadoḷ<br/>
berasi samantu sūsuva jalārdralasaddhavaḷākṣataṅgaḷoḷ<br/>
berasida taṇpanetti kavidettida bāsigadondu kampinoḷ<br/>
poredu madāḷigaḷverasu bandudadondanukūla mārutaṁ // ViVi.2.95 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu poḻalaṁ poṟamaḍe baḻiyane taguḷdu barpa tammoḍanāḍigaḷappa<br/>
mēḷadasabbavada nageya tegaḻinavaranemma baḻiyaṭṭidandu bannimendu priyaṁ<br/>
nuḍidirisi kiṟidantaraṁ bandondu tāvaregeṟeya modaloḷ nindu bhīṣma drōṇa<br/>
kr̥pa vidurarkaḷanemage takka buddhiyaṁ pēḻdu maguḻimene—<br/>
</p>

<p>
naḍapiyumōdisiyuṁ bi<br/>
lviḍiyisiyuṁ keccuvirda kūrmegaḷerdeyaṁ<br/>
naḍe pāṇḍusutaragalkege<br/>
niḍusuydar drōṇa bhīṣma kr̥pa vidurarkaḷ // ViVi.2.96 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 65]<br/>
āgaḷ viduraṁ kelanaṟiyadantumavaraṟivantu[ṁ]sāmānya sthitiyoḷe<br/>
baṭṭeya nañjina kircina desege karaṁ prayatnapararāgimendoḍante geyvemendavara<br/>
niralvēḻdu payaṇambōgi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
poḷapina kiraṇada gāḷiya<br/>
poḷapane sairisadakusuma daḷa sukumārar<br/>
taḷardu neleyindamāgaḷ<br/>
koḷadiṁ poṟamaṭṭa haṁsegaḷgeṇeyādar // ViVi.2.97 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgi tāvādigarbhēśvararappudaṟiṁ taḷardeḍeyeḍeya maraṅgaḷa toṟegaḷa<br/>
bāḍaṅgaḷa pesargaḷaṁ besagoḷuttuṁ mahāgrahāraṅgaḷa mahājanaṅgaḷa koṭṭa ponna<br/>
jannaviraṅgaḷumanavara parakeyumaṁ keykoḷuttumavarge bādheyāgadantu kāpaṁ<br/>
niyamisuttuṁ kālūrgaḷa gaṇḍara peṇḍira naḍeyuḍeya nuḍiya muḍiya gāmpiṅge<br/>
muguḷnage naguttumalligalligoḍeda keṟegamaḻidāyatanakkaṁ dhanamanittu<br/>
jīrṇōddhāraṅgaḷaṁ māḍisuttuṁ bīḍudāṇaṅgaḷoḷikkida baḷḷigāvaṇaṅgaḷoḷaṁ<br/>
naneya jompaṅgaḷoḷaṁ viśramisuttuṁ bandu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
eḍaṟaṟidīva kalpataruvendu vanīpaka kōṭi santasaṁ<br/>
baḍe poḍevondakāḷa viḷayāśaniyendu virōdhigaḷ manaṁ<br/>
giḍe biyamuṁ parākramamumoppire tannoḍavuṭṭida‌r samaṁ<br/>
toḍavare vāraṇāvatamaneydidanammanagandhavāraṇaṁ // ViVi.2.98 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
idu vividha vibudhajanavinuta jinapadāmbhōja<br/>
varaprasādōtpanna prasanna gambhīra vacana racana<br/>
catura kavitāguṇārṇava viracitamappa<br/>
vikramārjuna vijayadoḷ<br/>
dvitīyāśvāsaṁ<br/>
</p>

<p>
---------------------------------------------------------------------<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 66]<br/>
[tr̥tīyāśvāsaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
śrīyanarātibaḷāsr̥e<br/>
ktōyadhiyoḷ paḍeda vīranuṟadarigaḷanā<br/>
tmīya padasphurita nakha<br/>
cchāyegaḷoḷ niṟisi ninda gaṇḍaṁ harigaṁ // ViVi.3.1 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
ā poḻala poṟavoḻalaneyde varpāgaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
katturiya sagaṇanīr biḍu<br/>
muttina raṅgavali miḷirva dugulada guḍi saṁ<br/>
pattina bittaradettida<br/>
muttina maṇḍavige poḻala manegaḷoḷellaṁ // ViVi.3.2 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antāgaḷonduttaraṁ baḷeye sogayisuva poḻaloḷaṣṭaśōbheyaṁ māḍi<br/>
duryōdhanana saṅkētadoḷ munname samedirda purōcanaṁ gōrōcanā<br/>
siddārtha dūrvāṅkura mātuḷuṅgaśr̥ṅgāradarpaṇa pūrṇakaḷaśakaḷamāvr̥ta<br/>
karapallaveyarappa purandhriyaruṁ baddavaṇada paṟegaḷuṁ berasidirvandu meyyikki<br/>
poḍamaṭṭu pāṇḍavarumaṁ mundiṭṭoḍagoṇḍu bandu poḻalaṁ pugise pokku<br/>
bīḍanelli biḍuvamene nimmayyaṁ dhr̥tarāṣṭrana besadal munname māḍamaṁ<br/>
samediṭṭenallige bijayaṅgeyyimene—<br/>
</p>

<p>
aragu modalāge ghr̥ta sa<br/>
jvarasaṁ bellaṁ saṇambivembivaṟiṁ vi<br/>
starisi samedindra bhavaname<br/>
dharegavatarisirdudenisuvaragina maneyaṁ // ViVi.3.3 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
tāne mundiṭṭoḍaṅgoṇḍu bandu pugise pāṇḍavarayvaruṁ kontiverasu<br/>
kiṟidānuṁ bēgamirdu dāna sanmānādigaḷiṁ santasambaḍisi purōcananaṁ bīḍiṅge<br/>
[p. 67]<br/>
pōgalvēḻdu dharmaputranā maneyaṁ parīkṣisi nōḍaloḍamaṟidu nijānuja<br/>
sahitaṁ kontiverasēkāntadoḷintendaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
idu maneyandamalturiva daḷḷuriyuggaḍadandamāgi tō<br/>
ṟidapudu kaṇge sajjarasadeṇṇeya tuppada kampidella[me]ṁ<br/>
bude bagedalli nōḍuvoḍamiṭṭage kalmaranembudilla kū<br/>
radanidanoḍḍidaṁ pagege santasamāgire māri suygumē // ViVi.3.4 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
adalladeyumatyādarassambhramamutpādayatiyembudī purōcananemba<br/>
būtu suyōdhanana besadiṁ namaginitādaraṁ geyvudellaṁ nammaṁ meḷpaḍisalende<br/>
māḍidaṁ nāmidanaṟiyadantu bēṇṭeya nevadoḷ baṭṭegaḷaṁ sōdisuvamendu<br/>
niccaṁ bēṇṭevōge purōcananuṁ peṟagaṇa kāpaṁ kaṇgāpi nale kādirpannegaṁ<br/>
vidurana viśvāsa dāsaṁkanakanembaṁ bandu pāṇḍavaraṁ kaṇḍēkāntadoḷ viduranaṭṭida<br/>
vinnāṇaṅgaḷaṁ pēḻdu nambisi nīmentuṁ ballirante poṟamaṭṭu pōgimendujatugr̥ha kavāṭapuṭa sandhigaḷoḷ suraṅgamaṁ gaṅgeyoḷ mūḍuvantāge samedu<br/>
pēḻdu pōpuduṁ pāṇḍavaruṁ purōcanaṁ tammaṁ maṟudivasaṁ chidrisuvenenaluṁ<br/>
munnina divasamoḷagaṇa parijanamellamaṁ pārvaranūḍuva nevadoḷe poṟamaḍisi<br/>
sūryāstamayadoḷ pārvaranūḍi niṣāditiyemba bēḍitigamayvar<br/>
magandirgamuṇalikkidoḍe taṇiyuṇḍu beṇḍu maraldu maṟasundida‌r<br/>
purōcananumā maneyoḷondōvariyoḷ maṟakendidanā prastāvadoḷardharātri<br/>
yādāgaḷ kontiverasayvarumaṁ munnamoyyanoyyane suraṅgadiṁ poṟamaḍisi<br/>
bhīmasēnaṁ purōcanaṁ maṟakendirdōvariyoḷ kiccaṁ koḷisaloḍaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
aḍevottade kiṟikiṟidane<br/>
suḍadinisare porekanāgade[ye]sasidandoṁ<br/>
deḍeyoḷagoṭṭirdaraḷeya<br/>
noḍanaḷurvantaḷurdananalanaragina maneyaṁ // ViVi.3.5 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 68]<br/>
mēlāda pāṇḍusutaranu<br/>
pālambhaṅgeyyutirpa duryōdhananaṁ<br/>
līleye nuṅguva mr̥tyuva<br/>
nālageyene negeduvuriya nālage palavuṁ // ViVi.3.6 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgaḷ bhīmasēnaṁ tanna taleyoḷaṁ meyyoḷaṁ karagi surivaragi nuriya<br/>
bambalgaḷaṁ posedu bidirdu kaḷedu suraṅgadoḷagaṇindame tannoḍavuṭṭidar kūḍe<br/>
vandanannegamittaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
aragina maneyoḷ pāṇḍava<br/>
ruridaḻgidarakkaṭayyo duryōdhananeṁ<br/>
beraleyinendaḻutuṁ ta<br/>
tpurajanamaḻalodave paridu nōḍittāgaḷ // ViVi.3.7 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
nōḍi rūpaṟiyalāgadantu karimurikanāgirda bēḍitiyumanavaḷayvar‌<br/>
makkaḷumaṁ kontiyuṁ pāṇḍavarumapparēnuṁ tappallendu purapradhānarkaḷ<br/>
tadvr̥ttāntamellamaṁ pēḻdu dhr̥tarāṣṭaṅgaṁ pēḻalaṭṭidoḍe—<br/>
</p>

<p>
manadoḷ traibhuvanamanā<br/>
ḷdanituvaraṁ tanage santasaṁ perciyumaṁ<br/>
dinisandhanr̥paṁ tannaya<br/>
janadoḷ kelanaṟiye kr̥taka śōkaṅgeydaṁ // ViVi.3.8 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgaḷ nadī tanūja bhāradvāja kr̥paraviraḷa bāṣpavāri durdina<br/>
dīnānanarāgire viduraṁ tānaṟidumaṟiyadante śōkākrāntanāgi dhr̥tarāṣṭrana<br/>
besadoḷ vāraṇāvatakke pōgi tadardha dagdha kaḷēvaraṅgaḷaṁ saṁskarisi jaḷadānādi<br/>
kriyegaḷaṁ māḍi maguḻe vandanannegamitta pāṇḍavar suraṅgadiṁ poṟamaṭṭu<br/>
tārāgaṇaṅgaḷ ninda neleyiṁ deseyaṁ poḻtumanaṟidu teṅka mogade<br/>
payaṇambōgi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
taḍakuṁpiṭṭeyumotte mellaḍigaḷaṁ baḷkuttumaḷkuttumō<br/>
raḍigormorme kuḷuttumēḻutire kaṇḍintāgadinnēḻimeṁ<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 69]<br/>
doḍanandayvarumaṁ nijāṁsayugadoḷ pottetti taḷtoḷva sī<br/>
ṟuḍuvindadbhutadā hiḍimbavanamaṁ pokkaṁ marunnandanaṁ // ViVi.3.9 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
adu madadanti danta musala pravibhagna mahāmahīruhā<br/>
spadamadu siṁhanāda janita pratiśabdamahā bhayānaka<br/>
pradamadu nirjharōccaḷita śīkara śītaḷa vāta nartitō<br/>
nmada śabarījanāḷakamadāyata vētralatāvitānakaṁ // ViVi.3.10 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
ā vanāntarāḷa madhyasthita viśāḷa vaṭa viṭapiyaneytandadaṟa keḻagayvaru<br/>
maniḻipidoḍadhvānapada pariśrama śrāntar nidrābharaparavaśarāgire bhīmaṁ<br/>
jāvamirdu tannoḍavuṭṭidargāda pravāsāyāsaṅgaḷgaṁ desegaṁmanyumikku bare<br/>
kaṇṇa nīraṁ tumbi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
bharatana vaṁśadoḷ negaḻda pāṇḍugevuṭṭiyumī samasta sā<br/>
gara parivēṣṭitāvanige vallabhanāgiyumī mahōgra kē<br/>
sari kari kaṇṭha garjita mahāṭaviyoḷ maṟakendi nīmumī<br/>
maradaḍiyoḷ śivāśiva ravaṅgaḷineḻcaṟuvantuṭādudē // ViVi.3.11 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu nuḍiyuttirpannegaṁ kōkanada bāndhavanudayācaḷaśikhara<br/>
śēkharanādanāgaḷā banamanāḷva hiḍimbanembanavara baravanaṟidu tanna taṅge<br/>
hiḍimbeyembaḷaṁ karedu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
niḍiyar ballāyada ba<br/>
ldaḍigar vandirdarayvarālada keḻagiṁ<br/>
toḍardar nammaya bhakṣado<br/>
ḷaḍu paṇṇiḍu pōgu nīnumānuṁ timbaṁ // ViVi.3.12 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
embudumantegeyvenendu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgasadoḷagondu mahī<br/>
bhāgadoḷinnondu dāḍeyāgire manadiṁ<br/>
bēgaṁ barpaḷa diṭṭiga<br/>
ḷāgaḷe pattiduvu geṇṭaṟoḷ mārutiyaṁ // ViVi.3.13 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 70]<br/>
antondambuvīḍineḍeyoḷ kāmanambuvīḍiṅgoḷagāgi tāṁ kāma<br/>
rūpeyappudaṟiṁ divya kanyakāsvarūpamaṁ keykoṇḍu tannatta mogade barpaḷaṁ<br/>
kaṇḍu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
khēcariyō bhūcariyō ni<br/>
śācariyō rūpu baṇṇisalkārgamavā<br/>
ggōcaramī kānanamuma<br/>
gōcaramivaḷilligēke bandaḷo pēḻiṁ // ViVi.3.14 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
embannegamāke madanana keyyiṁ barduṅkidaralambu barpante bandu bhīma<br/>
sēnana keladoḷ kuḷḷire nīnārgēnembeyēke bandeyendūḍākeyendaḷeraḍaṟi<br/>
yadoldu ninnoḷeraḍaṁ nuḍiyalāgadenage yī banaṁ hiḍimbavanamembudidanāḷvaṁ<br/>
hiḍimbanembasuranemmaṇṇanānuṁ hiḍimbeyenembenātana besadiṁ nimminibarumaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
piḍidaḍasi tinal bandi<br/>
rdeḍeyoḷ ninagāgi madananennane tine kēḷ<br/>
paḍenōḍal bandavaraṁ<br/>
guḍivoṟisidarembudāytuninnenneḍeyoḷ // ViVi.3.15 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endī maṟalundidarārgendoḍenna tāyvirumoḍavuṭṭidarendoḍe hiḍimbaṁ<br/>
bandavaraṁ tindoḍaṁ tinge nīnenna pegalanēṟu gaganataḷakkuyvenene bhīmasēnanā<br/>
mātiṅge muguḷage nakku—<br/>
</p>

<p>
aḻipideyantumallade niśācariyai ninagappudappudī<br/>
yaḻinuḍibarkeninna piriyaṇṇane paṇṇane nōḻpamātano<br/>
ḍḍaṟiyada gaṇḍavātanenutantire taṅge[ya]māṇdudarkavaṁ<br/>
moḻagi siḍildadondu siḍilēḻgeyineytare vandu bhīmanaṁ // ViVi.3.16 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
kaṇḍu kaṇgaḷiṁkeṇḍada taṇḍaṅgaḷumuriya taṇḍaṅgaḷuṁ sose<br/>
nīnorvayennoḷagēṁ kāduve ī maṟalundidaranettinibarumanormeye<br/>
posedu mukkuvenenesāhasa bhīmaṁ mallantigeyanappoḍaṁ saḍalisadavana<br/>
navayavadoḷintendaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 71]<br/>
ēṁ gāvilanayo ninnaṁ<br/>
nuṅguvudarkivaranettavēḻkume neramaṁ<br/>
saṅgaḷisalvēḻkume mā<br/>
taṅgavirōdhige kuraṅga saṅgara dhareyoḷ // ViVi.3.17 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
embuduṁ hiḍimbanāḍambaraṅgeydu tumburukoḷḷiyatambarambaraṁ<br/>
siḍildu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
kaḍupine pottu pāsaṟeyaneytare bhīmanumōtti kiḻtu bē<br/>
roḍane mahījamondaniḍeyuṁ biḍe poyyeyumā banaṁ paḍa<br/>
lvaḍutire kalloḷaṁ maradoḷaṁ baḍidoyyane jōldaṁ daityanaṁ<br/>
piḍidu mr̥ṇāḷanāḷamane sīḷvavolormeye sīḷdu bīsidaṁ // ViVi.3.18 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgaḷā kaḷakaḷakke maṟalundidayvarumeḻcattidēnendu besagoḷe<br/>
tadvr̥ttāntamellamanaṟipi hiḍimbe ḍambavillade bhīmasēnanoḷappoḍambaḍaṁ nuḍiye<br/>
kontiyuṁ dharmaputranumīke sāmānya vaniteyallivaḷ rākṣasa strīyendu<br/>
bhāvisalvēḍīkeyaṁ keykoḷvude kajjamendākegaṁ bhīmasēnaṅgaṁ gandharvavivāhamaṁ<br/>
māḍidoḍe hiḍimbe nīmilliralvēḍa parvatada mēle kaṟaṅgi kaḻtalisida maradu<br/>
ṟugala naḍuve sudhā dhavaḷitōttuṅga ramya harmyaṅgaḷaṁ kāṇbirappoḍadu<br/>
hiḍimbapuramembudemma puramallige pōpaṁ bannimendu mundiṭṭoḍagoṇḍu<br/>
pōgi mahāvibhūtiyiṁ poḻalaṁ pugisi tanna sampattumaṁ śrīyumaṁ meṟedu<br/>
majjana bhōjana tāmbūla lēpanaṅgaḷiṁ patha pariśramamellamaṁ kaḷedu<br/>
bhīmasēnanuṁ tānuṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
elli koḷanelli taṇbuḻi<br/>
lelli latā bhavanamelli dhārāgr̥hamaṁ<br/>
talliye toḍardalliye niṁ<br/>
dalliye ramiyisidaḷāke marudātmajanoḷ // ViVi.3.19 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu ramiyisi poḻalge maguḻdu bandoḍākegaṁ bhīmaṅgaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
kāriruḷa tiruḷa baṇṇaṁ<br/>
kūriduvene toḷapa dāḍe miḷirvurigēsaṁ<br/>
pēroḍalesedire puṭṭida<br/>
nārumagurvise magaṁ ghaṭōtkacanembaṁ // ViVi.3.20 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 72]<br/>
antu puṭṭuvudumīśvarakalpitadiṁ rākṣasarge sadyōgarbhamuṁ sadyaḥ<br/>
prasūtiyuṁ sadyōyauvanamumuḷḷa kāraṇadindāgaḷe ṣōḍaśa varṣada<br/>
kumāranāgire pāṇḍavarumalli mūṟu varuṣamirdu kr̥ṣṇadvaipāyanōpadēśa<br/>
dindēkacakrakke vōpa kajjamanāḷōcisi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
barisi hiḍimbeyaṁ karedu sāre ghaṭōtkacanaṁ manōmudaṁ<br/>
berasosedirdevinnevaraminniralāgadu pōpevendoḍā<br/>
daradoḷe koṭṭa vastugaḷanondumanollade kūrtu buddhivē<br/>
ḻdirisi sukhaprayāṇadoḷe pāṇḍavareydidarēkacakramaṁ // ViVi.3.21 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
alli sogayisuva kr̥taka girigaḷiṁ<br/>
kalpatarugaḷane pōlva maragaḷiṁ<br/>
nandanaṅgaḷoḷ suḻiva birayiyiṁ<br/>
kampu kaṇmaleye pūta surayiyiṁ<br/>
suttaluṁ pariva jarivonalgaḷiṁ<br/>
dettaluṁ naliva posa navilgaḷiṁ<br/>
beḷedu magamagipa gandha śāḷiyiṁ<br/>
dalli suḻiva giḷiviṇḍinōḷiyiṁ<br/>
īṇṭu jaḷadhiyenipagaḻa nīḷpiniṁ<br/>
negedu sogayisuva kōṇṭeyoḷpiniṁ<br/>
vividha dēva gr̥hadāṭapāṭadiṁ<br/>
maṟugi baṭṭeyara nōḻpa nōṭadiṁ<br/>
pañcaratunadoḷe neṟeda pasaradiṁ<br/>
tōraṇaṅgaḷoḷe toḍarda tisaradiṁ<br/>
dhanadarannarivarenipa paradariṁ<br/>
dēvarannarivarenipa birudariṁ<br/>
neṟeye sogayipā yēkacakramaṁ<br/>
meccida hariganamita vikramaṁ // ViVi.3.22 [ragaḷe]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu mecci tammutayvaruminnavu poḻalgaḷillī poḻalge nālku<br/>
yugadoḷaṁ vasumati padmanagaramēkacakraṁ bahudhānyamemba nālku pesarādudendu<br/>
manaṅgoṇḍu nōḍuttuṁ banda caturvēdapāragara maneya mundaṇa catuśyāle<br/>
yoḷ bīḍaṁ biṭṭu dharāmara vēṣadoḷondu varuṣa mirpannegamondu<br/>
divasaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 73]<br/>
tumbida raktateyiṁ nija<br/>
bimbaṁ vāruṇiyanosedu sēvise nāṇge<br/>
ṭṭambōl tējaṁ masuḷvina<br/>
mambaramaṁ bisuṭanāgaḷambuja mitraṁ // ViVi.3.23 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgaḷ sandhyāvandanege dharmaputrārjuna nakula sahadēvar<br/>
pōdarannegamitta bīḍinoḷirda kontiya bhīmana karṇōpāntadoḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
sāreyoḷaḻva mahā dvija<br/>
nāriya mamatā[vipūritō]rjita ravadiṁ<br/>
kāruṇyākrandanamani<br/>
vāritamormodale bandu tīḍittāgaḷ // ViVi.3.24 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
adaṁ kēḷdēnānumondu kāraṇamāgalevēḻkumī puyyalanāraydu<br/>
barpenendu bhīmananirisi konti tāne pōgi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
aḻekuḍalāda kūsu neladoḷ poraḷuttire dharmapatni bā<br/>
yaḻidu koralge pāydu paridāḍuva bālakanāda śōkadiṁ<br/>
gaḻagaḻa kaṇṇanīr suriye cintipa pārvana śōkadondu poṁ<br/>
puḻiyane nōḍi nāḍe karuṇaṁ tanagāgire konti cinteyiṁ // ViVi.3.25 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
ninagintī piridu śōkamentādudembudamā pārvaṁ kontigintendaṁ<br/>
bakanembanorvasuranī poḻala teṅkaṇa beṭṭadoḷirpanātaṅge niccamondu<br/>
maneyoḷeraḍemmevōṟiyoḷ pūḍida pannirkaṇḍugadakkiyakūḻuma[na]darke takka<br/>
parikaramumanorva mānasaṁ koṇḍu pōpanantātaṁ berasadellamaṁ tindu taṇiyade<br/>
pallaṁ timbanadondu divasaṁ tappidoḍī poḻalanitumaṁ timbaṁ nāḷina bāriyemma<br/>
mēle bandudemma maneyoḷānumemma dharmapatniyuṁ maganuṁ magaḷumintī<br/>
nālvare mānasaremmapeṇḍatiyanīvenappoḍākeyiṁ baḻiyimī kūsugaḷaṁ<br/>
naḍapuvarilla magaḷanīvenappoḍe koḍagūsembudu peṟaroḍave magananīvenappoḍe<br/>
santaticchēdamuṁ piṇḍacchēdamumakkumadaṟindennane kuḍalvēḻkumembuduṁ<br/>
kontiyintendaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 74]<br/>
nimmī nālvaroḷorvaru<br/>
mimmiḍukalvēḍa makkaḷoḷarenagayvar<br/>
tammoḷagesevayvaroḷaṁ<br/>
nāmmāṇade bakana bārigorvananīveṁ // ViVi.3.26 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
embuduṁ pārvanintenalvēḍa makkaḷoḷāda mōhamellā jīvakkaṁ<br/>
samānamembuduṁ nīmaṟiyirusiradirimadarke takka savakaṭṭaṁ māḍimendu bandu<br/>
tadvr̥ttāntamellamaṁ bhīmasēnaṅgaṟipidoḍe nāḷinuṇisanenage dorekoḷisibandudu<br/>
karamoḷḷitāytendunagutirpannegaṁ mattina nālvaruṁ bandu tadvr̥ttāntamellamaṁ<br/>
kēḷdu namagī poḻaloḷondu parōpakārārthaṁ saypiniṁ dorekoṇḍudendi<br/>
ruḷellaṁ bakana paḍemātane nuḍiyuttirpannegaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
ōḍe tamōbaḷamagida<br/>
ḷḷāḍe niśācara balaṁ rathāṅgayugaṅgaḷ<br/>
kūḍe bage kūḍe nēsaṟ<br/>
mūḍidudu bakaṅge miḻtu mūḍuva teṟadiṁ // ViVi.3.27 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgaḷ sāhasabhīmaṁ tanna sāhasamaṁ tōṟalendu bandu pārvana maneya<br/>
mundaṇa baṇḍiya kūḻaṁ keykoṇḍu nilvuduṁ pārvantiyuṁ pārvanuṁ parasi<br/>
sēseyanikki kaḷipe poḻaliṁ baṇḍiyanaṭṭikoṇḍu rakkasanirdeḍegeytandu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
dāḍegaḷanaṟeyoḷimbiṁ<br/>
tīḍuttuṁ tīvramāge baṇḍiya baravaṁ<br/>
nōḍuttirdā bakanaṁ<br/>
nāḍeyeantarade kaṇḍu muḷidaṁ bhīmaṁ // ViVi.3.28 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
kaḍegaṇṇoḷe rakkasanaṁ<br/>
naḍe nōḍi kolalke sattvamappantire muṁ<br/>
poḍeveṁ kūḻaṁ baḻiyaṁ<br/>
poḍeveṁ rakkasananendu sāhasabhīmaṁ // ViVi.3.29 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu tanna tanda baṇḍiya kūḻellamaṁ patteṇṭu tuttinoḷe sameye<br/>
[p. 75]<br/>
tuttuvudaṁ kaṇḍu rakkasanivana pāṅgaṁ meccalāṟenennumanintu sameye tuttugumendu<br/>
bakaṁ bakavēṣadiṁ peṟagaṇa desege mellanōsarisi bandu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
eraḍuṁ kelanumaneraḍuṁ<br/>
kara parighadinaḍasi gurdi peṟapiṅguvanaṁ<br/>
muridaḍasi piḍidu ghaṭṭisi<br/>
piriyaṟeyoḷ poydanasagavoylaṁ bhīmaṁ // ViVi.3.30 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu poydoḍe poḍeseṇḍaṁ poydante mēgogedu seṇase—<br/>
</p>

<p>
bāriyaniṭṭu kūḍe poḻalaṁ tave tindananārtarillaṇaṁ<br/>
bārisalārumin javanabāriyoḷikkuvenendu parve bhō<br/>
rbhōrene bīse tadvadana gahvaradiṁ bisunettaruṇme bhō<br/>
rbhōrene kondanaṅkada baḷādhikanaṁ bakanaṁ vr̥kōdaraṁ // ViVi.3.31 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu kondu nīlagiriyane piḍideḻevante rakkasana kariya piriyoḍalaneḻedu<br/>
tandu poḻala naḍuvikkidāgaḷ poḻalellaṁ cōdyambaṭṭu baddavaṇada paṟegaḷaṁ<br/>
poysi sāhasabhīmana sāhasamanaḷavallade pogaḻdu tammāḷdanumaniṣṭa daivamumaṁ<br/>
koṇḍāḍuvantayvarumaṁ koṇḍāḍe kelavu divasamirpannegamondu divasa[ma]śiśira kiraṇanapara jalanidhi taṭanikaṭavartiyādanāgaḷorva pārvaṁ vistīrṇa<br/>
jīrṇa karpaṭāvr̥ta kaṭitaṭanumāgi bandu kaṇmuccaleḍevēḍe tanagavar‌ pāsalkoṭṭa<br/>
kr̥ṣṇājinamaṁ pāsipaṭṭirdanaṁ dharmaputranāva nāḍiṁ bandirellige pōdapi<br/>
rendoḍuttarāpathada hastinapuradiṁ bandemendoḍalli pāṇḍavara paḍe mātāvudu<br/>
dhr̥tarāṣṭra suyōdhanarirpandamāvudendu besagoḷe—<br/>
</p>

<p>
manadoḷ kūrada pāṇḍurāja sutaruṁ lākṣāgr̥hōgrāgniyā<br/>
nanadoḷ maḻgidarennapuṇyamaṟiyar vēmāṟa(?)rinnāro bē<br/>
rane kiḻtikkidenīgaḷāytu dhare nirdāyādyamendā suyō<br/>
dhananāḷuttire sanda hastinapuraṁ santaṁ basantaṁ karaṁ // ViVi.3.32 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 76]<br/>
adalladeyuṁ yajñasēnanemba modala pesara pāñcāḷadēśadarasaṁ<br/>
drupadanembaṁ drōṇanoḷāda paribhavamaṁ nenedātanaṁ kolvannanorva maganumaṁ<br/>
vikramārjunaṅge peṇḍatiyappannaḷorva magaḷumaṁ paḍedalladirenendu pūṇdu<br/>
pōgi payōvratanemba divya munipatiyiṁ putrakāmēṣṭi geyse hōmakuṇḍadalli<br/>
dhagadhagisuva jvālāmālegaḷoḷ kiḻtabāḷumattaparamumabhēdya kavacamuṁ<br/>
berasogeda dhr̥ṣṭadyumnanemba maganumaṁ jvāḷāmāḷiniyogevantogeda kr̥ṣṇeyemba<br/>
magaḷumaṁ paḍedanā hōmāgniyoḷ puṭṭidondu divya cāpamumaydu divya<br/>
śaramoḷavā billanēṟisi ā saralgaḷindātana maneya munde nabhadoḷ<br/>
nalinalidāḍuva jantrada mīnaneccanumākege gaṇḍanakkumendādēśamantappa<br/>
sāhasapuruṣaṁ vikramārjunanallade peṟarillembaradaṟindinnu pāṇḍavaroḷaremba<br/>
mātugaḷaṁ buddhiyoḍeyarārānuṁ nuḍivar‌ drupadanumīgaḷā kūsiṅge<br/>
sayambaramaṁ māḍalendu neladoḷuḷḷarasumakkaḷellargaṁ baḻiyanaṭṭidoḍe<br/>
duryōdhanādigaḷ modalādanēka dēśādhīśvararellaṁ chatravatiyembudu drupadana<br/>
poḻalā poḻalge vandirdarānallindaṁ bandenendu pēḻe tadvr̥ttāntamellamaṁ<br/>
kēḷdu tammoḷāḷōcisi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
taleyoḷ sīreyanikki kemmanenitaṁ pūṇdirpamugrāri vaṁ<br/>
śalatāvallarigaḷge dāvaśikhivol meydōṟitaddraupadī<br/>
lalanā vyājadinīgaḷonde poḻaloḷ sandirda bhāsvatsuhr̥<br/>
dbalakaṁ mārvalakaṁ guṇārṇava śaraprāgalbhyamaṁ tōṟuvaṁ // ViVi.3.33 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu niścayisi tamma bageda bageyoḷ parāśaramunīndrōpadēśa<br/>
moḍambaḍe pāṇḍavarēkacakradiṁ poṟamaṭṭu śakunaṅgaḷellamuttarōttaraṁ<br/>
tirduvinamuttarābhimukharāgi payaṇaṁ bōgi kelavānuṁ divasakke yamunānadī<br/>
taṭanikaṭavartiyappaṅgadaparṇavembaḍaviyoḷagane barevare dinakarabimbāmbuja<br/>
mambara sarōvaradiṁ pattuviḍuvuduṁ kavida kaḻtaleyagurvāge tamōpaśamana<br/>
nimittamuriva koḷḷiyaṁ piḍidu jaguneyaṁ pāyvāgaḷā banamanāḷva<br/>
kubēranāyakanaṅgadaparṇanemba gandharvaṁ jaḷakrīḍeyāḍutirdanibariṁ munde<br/>
barpa vikramārjunana pādābhighātadoḷuccaḷisuva nīra sappuḷumaṁ kēḷdu piḍida<br/>
koḷḷiya beḷagumaṁ kaṇḍu beḷagaṁ kaṇḍa pataṅgadante māṇadeytandu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 77]<br/>
banamennāḷva banaṁ niśābalamidintasmadbalaṁ dhūrtanay<br/>
ninagī poḻtaṟoḷitta barpadaṭanintārittarendāntoḍā<br/>
tananā koḷḷiyoḷiṭṭoḍantadu layāntōgrāgniyantaḻve baṁ<br/>
denasuṁ māṇade bāgidaṁ padayugakkārūḍha sarvajñanā // ViVi.3.34 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu tāgi bāgidantāgi gandharvaṁ kontiverasaṟuvarumaṁ tanna<br/>
bīḍiṅgoḍagoṇḍoydati prītiyiṁ birdanikki—<br/>
</p>

<p>
idu ninna koṭṭa tale nina<br/>
gidanittapenendu nuḍiyalāgadu mārko<br/>
ḷḷadirendu giḷiya baṇṇada<br/>
kudureyanaynūranittanaṅgadaparṇaṁ // ViVi.3.35 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
ittoḍivannegamemagāgirkendu priyaṁ nuḍidaṅgadaparṇananiravēḻdu<br/>
mārtāṇḍōdayame nijōdayamāge payaṇambōgi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
puṇyanadīnada naga[lā]<br/>
vaṇya vibhūṣaṇeyanoldu nōḍuttumiḷā<br/>
puṇya strīyaṁ sañcita<br/>
puṇyar pāñcāladēśamaṁ pugutandar‌ // ViVi.3.36 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu tadviṣaya viḷāsinige piḍida kanakacchatradante sogayisuva chatravatīpurada<br/>
poṟavoḻalaneytarpāgaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
pāḍuva tumbi kōḍuva puḻil naḍapāḍuva rājahaṁse baṁ<br/>
dāḍuva toṇḍuveṇburuḷi tīḍuvatemberaloldu nallaroḷ<br/>
kūḍuva nallarārerdegamāra manakkamanaṅgarāgamaṁ<br/>
māḍe manakke banduvarikēsarigalliya nandanāḷigaḷ // ViVi.3.37 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu nōḍuttuṁ barevare—<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 78]<br/>
madagaja br̥ṁhita dhvani turaṅgamahēṣita ghōṣamādamo<br/>
rmodale payōdhimanthana mahāravamaṁ gele taḷta baṇṇava<br/>
ṇṇada guḍi tombegoñca[lele]yikkida kāvaṇamelliyuṁ poda<br/>
ḻdodavire kaṇge kaṇḍuvakhiḷāvanipāḷara biṭṭa bīḍugaḷ // ViVi.3.38 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu nōḍuttuṁ meccuttuṁ barevare—<br/>
</p>

<p>
ī trijagaṅgaḷoḷ negaḻda peṇḍirumaṁ gelevanda padmanī<br/>
patra vicitra nētrege sayambaradoḷ varanappevādoḍī<br/>
dhātriyanāḷvemāme valamendu teraḷda samasta rājaka<br/>
cchatradinandu chatravatiyembabhidhānamanāḷdudā poḻal // ViVi.3.39 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu sogayisuva poḻalaṁ pokkelliyuṁ bīḍu biḍaleḍevaḍeyadondu<br/>
bhārgavaparṇaśāleyoḷeḍemāḍikoṇḍu brahmalōkamirpantirda brahmasabheyoḷage<br/>
dēva brāhmaṇarāgirdarannegaṁ drupadanittal—<br/>
</p>

<p>
nereda samasta rājakamanādaradindidirgoṇḍanēka ra<br/>
tna racitamāge māḍisisayambara[sā]leyanōḷiyiṁ narē<br/>
śvarargiralendu caupaḷigegaḷ palavaṁ samedalli ratnadiṁ<br/>
berasida baṇṇadoḷ meṟeye kaṭṭisi puṭṭisi raṅgabhūmiyaṁ // ViVi.3.40 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
ā neleya caupaḷigegaḷoḷanēka prāsādada mēle citrada paḻavigegaḷaṁ<br/>
tuṟugaluṁ bambalgaḷumāge kaṭṭisi pacceya hārada tōraṇaṅgaḷaṁ dugulada<br/>
guḍigaḷaṁ kaṭṭi[si]kambhaṅgaḷoḷellaṁ suyyāṇada cinnada paḻiya sakaḷavaṭṭegaḷaṁ<br/>
sutti[si]muttina maṇḍavigegaḷaneḍeyaṟidettisi ponna māṅgāya goñcalgaḷumaṁ<br/>
muttina bumbhukaṅgaḷumaneḻale kaṭṭisi mattamā prāsādaṅgaḷa caupaḷigegaḷa ponna<br/>
poṅgaṟige nīḷpuṁ beḷpumaṁ tāḷdi karpinoḷupāśrayambaḍedu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
tuṟugida pūgoñcala kā<br/>
yteṟagida māvugaḷa beḷeda kauṅgina gone ta<br/>
ḷteṟagire māḍadoḷalliye<br/>
tiṟidukoḷalkimbinesakamesedudupavanaṁ // ViVi.3.41 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 79]<br/>
nāḷe sayambaramene pāṁ<br/>
cāḷa mahīpāḷanakhiḷa bhūbhr̥nnikara<br/>
kkōḷiye sāṟidoḍavanī<br/>
pālar keygeyyalendupaṟivaṟiyādar // ViVi.3.42 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgi maṟudivasaṁ nēsaṟ mūḍe—<br/>
</p>

<p>
tantamma rājya cihnaṁ<br/>
tantamma mahāvibhūti tantamma balaṁ<br/>
tantammeseva viḷāsaṁ<br/>
tantammirpeḍeyoḷōḷiyiṁ kuḷḷirdar // ViVi.3.43 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgaḷ drupadaṁ tanna purakkamantaḥpurakkaṁ parivārakkaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
sāsira poṁgeyduṁciḥ<br/>
kāsaṭamendondu lakkageyvudidarkaṁ<br/>
māsaramuḍalendadhika vi<br/>
ḷāsadinuḍalikki neṟeye biyamaṁ meṟedaṁ // ViVi.3.44 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu meṟedu kūsaṁ neṟeye keygeysimendu munna[ṁ]keyge[ysutirda]<br/>
taṟada guṟugeyarappantaḥpura purandhriyaraṁ karedu pēḻvudumantegeyvemendu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
ī poḻtiṅgīrutuviṁ<br/>
gīpasadanamintuṭappa meyvaṇṇakkiṁ<br/>
tī pūvinoḷī tuḍugeyo<br/>
ḷī puṭṭigeyoḷ beḍaṅguvaḍedesedirkuṁ // ViVi.3.45 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu neṟeye pasadanaṅgoḷisi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
tuḍisadehāramaṁmoleya biṇpinoḷaṁ naḍu baḷkidappudī<br/>
naḍuguvuvallavē toḍe nitambada biṇpinoḷēvudakka pō<br/>
biḍu kaṭisūtramaṁ toḍeya biṇpu padāmburuhakke tiṇṇamēṁ<br/>
tuḍisuvudakka nūpuramanī toḍavēvudo rūpe sāladē // ViVi.3.46 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 80]<br/>
endendōrorvarākeya rūpaṁ vakrōktiyoḷe pogaḻdu maṅgaḷa<br/>
vasadanamikkiyuṁ posa madavaḷigeyappudaṟiṁ tuḍisalevēḻkumendu neṟeye<br/>
pasadanaṅgoḷise—<br/>
</p>

<p>
masedudu madanana bāḷ kū<br/>
rmaseyiṭṭudu kāmanambu bāygūḍidudā<br/>
kusumāstrana cakramideṁ<br/>
besakamanāḷdattu pasadanaṁ draupadiyā // ViVi.3.47 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu neṟeye pasadanaṅgoḷisi biḍumuttina sēseyanikki tāygaṁ tandegaṁ<br/>
poḍamaḍisi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
niṭṭise hōmānalanoḷ<br/>
puṭṭida ninagakka parake yāvudo ninnaṁ<br/>
puṭṭisida bidi negaḻteya<br/>
jeṭṭiganoḷ nerapugīgaḷarikēsariyoḷ // ViVi.3.48 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu parasi kanatkanaka khacitamuṁ mauktika stambhamumappa sarvatōbhadramemba<br/>
sivigeyanēṟisi cāmarada kuñcadaḍapada ḍavakeya vāra viḷāsiniyareraḍuṁ keladoḷ<br/>
suttiṟidu baḷasi bare talevaridōjeya piḍiyanēṟi peṇḍavāsadoḷveṇḍir baḷasi<br/>
bare taḷtu piḍida kanaka padmada sīgurigaḷa neḻaleḍevaṟiyade bare drupadanuṁ<br/>
dhr̥ṣṭadyumnanuṁ muttina māṇikada maṇḍanāyōgaṅgaḷoḷ neṟeye paṇṇida<br/>
madāndha gandhasindhuraṅgaḷanēṟi bare munde pariva dhavaḷacchatra candrāditya<br/>
pāḷikētanādi rājya cihnaṅgaḷu moḻaguva maṅgaḷa tūryaṅgaḷeseye peṟapeṟagane<br/>
draupadi śr̥ṅgāra sāgarame mēredappi barpante bare—<br/>
</p>

<p>
pareduguva pañca ratnada<br/>
paralgaḷudirdeseye saudhadoḷe kedaṟida ka<br/>
ppuravaḷkugaḷeseye sayaṁ<br/>
bara sāleyaneseva līleyiṁ pugutandaḷ // ViVi.3.49 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 81]<br/>
nuḍivudane maṟedu peṟataṁ<br/>
nuḍiye kelar nōḍadante nōḍe kelar pā<br/>
vaḍardavolire kelaroyyane<br/>
tuḍugeyanōsarise kelarudagrāvanipar // ViVi.3.50 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
oḍane neredarasumakkaḷa<br/>
niḍugaṇgaḷa baḷagameṟage tannaya meyyoḷ<br/>
naḍe baḷasi palarumambaṁ<br/>
tuḍe naḍuvirdondu pulleyirpantirdaḷ // ViVi.3.51 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
moneyambugaḷoḷe pūṇdapa<br/>
nanibarumaṁ kiṟidu bēgadiṁ hariganada<br/>
rkenageḍevēḻkumeembavo<br/>
lanibarumaṁ pūṇdanatanunaneyambugaḷiṁ // ViVi.3.52 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgaḷ pāṇḍavar tammaṁ peṟaraṟiyadantu brāhmaṇavēṣadoḷe<br/>
brahmasabheyoḷ bandire—<br/>
</p>

<p>
iḷeyoḷudagra vīra bhaṭa tuṅga mataṅgaja vāji rāji cau<br/>
paḷigegaḷoḷ dharādhara dhurandhara bandhura rājakaṁ viya<br/>
ttaḷadoḷanēka kimpuruṣa kinnara khēcara siddha br̥ndama<br/>
vvaḷisire mūṟu lōkamane pōltudu mūneleyiṁ svayambaraṁ // ViVi.3.53 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgaḷ vidita vr̥ttānteyāgi draupadiya keladoḷirda sundaramāleyemba<br/>
cēṭi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
kanakōccāsana saṁsthitaṁ nr̥panavaṁ beṅgīśanuttuṅga pī<br/>
na nijāṁsārpita lambahāranavanā pāṇḍyaṁ manaṅgoṇḍu ni<br/>
nnane kiḻgaṇṇoḷe nōḍutirpavanavaṁ cērammanāditya tē<br/>
janavaṁ nōḍu kaḷiṅgadēśadarasaṁ paṅkēja patrēkṣaṇē // ViVi.3.54 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
mattitta bīsuva cāmaraṅgaḷa poḷapinoḷamettida beḷgoḍegaḷa beḷpinoḷaṁ<br/>
desegaḷellaṁ dhavaḷisidannavāge pogaḷute varpavara saraṅgaḷoḷaṁ pāḍuva<br/>
pāṭhakāṟariñcaraṅgaḷoḷellaṁ digbhittigaḷ tekkane tīve maṇimaya pīṭhada mēle<br/>
kālanavaṣṭambhadiṁ nīḍi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 82]<br/>
alarambiṁduṟadenna mellerdeyaniṁturcittideṁmbante ne<br/>
ydila kāvaṁ tiruputtumo[ṁ]dananibar tammandiraṁ tannera<br/>
ḻkeladoḷ bandire nōḍi sōltu ninagā gēyakke sōltantevōl<br/>
taleyaṁ tūguvavaṁ suyōdhanannapaṁ nīnātanaṁ nōḍugē // ViVi.3.55 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
mattitta miñcaṁntaṭṭimeḍaṟidante suttiṟida kālgāpina kaḍitaleya baḷasidagaṇya<br/>
paṇyāṅganā janada naḍuve maṇimaya pīṭhaṅgaḷanēṟi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
āyatayaduvaṁśa kula<br/>
śrīyaṁ taḻkaisidadaṭaratiratharavara<br/>
tyāyata bhuja parighar nā<br/>
rāyaṇa baladēvarembarambujavadanē // ViVi.3.56 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu kiṟidantaraṁ pōgi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
intivarinnarī doreyarendaṟivantire pēḻduvēḻdu rā<br/>
jāntaradinde rājasuteyaṁ nayadindavaḷuydaḷantu sa<br/>
dbhrānta samīraṇōtthita viśāḷa viḷōḷa taraṅga rēkhe pa<br/>
dmāntaradindamimbaṟidu mānasahaṁsiyanuyvamārgadiṁ // ViVi.3.57 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu neredarasumakkaḷārumaṁ meccade maguḻevare drupadanidaṟoḷella<br/>
mēniṁ hōmāgni sambhavamappa divya cāpamanēṟisiyumīyaydu<br/>
śaradoḷākāśadoḷ‌ nalidu poḷeyuttirpa jantrada mīnanisalārpoḍe<br/>
bandēṟisiyumeccu gellaṅgoṇḍenna magaḷaṁ maduveyappudembudumāmāme<br/>
billanēṟisidapevendenibarānumarasumakkaḷ bandu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
ēṟipevendavar neladinettalumāṟade biḻdu nettaraṁ<br/>
kāṟiyumetti kayyuḍidumāgaḷe kāluḍiduṁ baḻaldu pa<br/>
llāṟi poḍarpugeṭṭusiralappoḍamāṟade pōdoḍāgaḷā<br/>
nēṟipenendu poccaṟisi bandu suyōdhananugracāpamaṁ // ViVi.3.58 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
mūṟu sūḻ balavandu poḍamaṭṭu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 83]<br/>
piḍidārpa bharadinetta<br/>
lkoḍarisidoḍe neladinaṇame taḷarade bil ni<br/>
ltoḍe guḍu guḍu guḍu goḷḷeṁ<br/>
doḍanāre suyōdhanaṁ karaṁ siggādaṁ // ViVi.3.59 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgi pōgi karṇana mogamaṁ nōḍidoḍe karṇanāḷdana siggāda mogamaṁ<br/>
kaṇḍu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
ānēṟipenendā kā<br/>
nīnaṁ bandetti billanēṟisi tegeyal<br/>
tānārtanillategevaṁ<br/>
tā nr̥patigaḷariganidiroḷēṁ puṭṭidarē // ViVi.3.60 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antā billaṁ piḍidavarellaṁ billumbeṟagumāgi siggāgi pōgi<br/>
tantammirpeḍe yoḷire pāñcāḷa rājanī neredarasumakkaḷoḷārumī billa<br/>
nēṟisalārtarillamī janavaḍeyoḷārānumī billanēṟisalārpoḍe bannimendu<br/>
sāṟuvuduṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
musukida nīradāvaḷigaḷaṁ kiraṇaṅgaḷoḷotti tējama<br/>
rvisuvinamāgaḷormodale mūḍuva bāḷa dinēśa bimbadoṁ<br/>
desakadinā dvijanmasabheyaṁ poṟamaṭṭoḍe māsidandamuṁ<br/>
pasadanadante kaṇgesedu tōṟidudā kadanatriṇētranā // ViVi.3.61 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu poṟamaḍuvarātikālānalanaṁ kaṇḍukaḍḍuvanda doḍḍarellaṁ<br/>
musuṟi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
saṅgatasatvarkuru rā<br/>
jaṅgaṁ karṇaṅgamēṟisalkaridanidaṁ<br/>
tāṁ gaḍamēṟipanī pā<br/>
rvaṅgakkaṭa meyyoḷondu maruḷuṇṭakkuṁ // ViVi.3.62 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu bāyge vandudane nuḍiye raṅgabhūmiya naḍuve nindu divya<br/>
cāpakke poḍavaṭṭadanavayavadineḍageyyoḷettikoṇḍu tanna bageda kajjamaṁ<br/>
golegoḷisuvantā billa goleyanēṟe nūṅki—<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 84]<br/>
dese kampaṅgoḷe koṇḍu divya śaramaṁ karṇādigaḷ kaṇḍu be<br/>
kkasamāgirpinamonde sūḻe tegedākarṇāntamaṁ tāge ni<br/>
ṭṭisalārgārgisalakkumembesakadā mīnaṁ samanteccu me<br/>
ccisidaṁ dēvarumaṁ dhanurdhararumaṁ vidviṣṭavidrāvaṇaṁ // ViVi.3.63 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgaḷā piḍida billekarbinabillāgeyumambugaḷe pūvinambugaḷāgeyu<br/>
mecca mīne[mīna]kētanamāgeyuṁ sahajamanōjanaṁ manōjanende bagedu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
naḍe kaḍegaṇ manaṁ bayase taḷtamardappale tōḷgaḷāseyoḷ<br/>
toḍardirepoṇmegharmajalamuṇme bhayaṁ kiḍe nāṇ‌ vikāradoḷ<br/>
toḍardire keytavummaḷipa kannege sundaramāle māleyaṁ<br/>
taḍeyade nīḍe māṇade guṇārṇavanaṁ sati māle sūḍidaḷ // ViVi.3.64 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgaḷ drupadaṁ baddhavaṇada paṟegaḷaṁ bājisalvēḻdu suratamakaradhvajanaṁ<br/>
draupadiyoḍane sivigeyanēṟisi dhr̥ṣṭadyumna yudhāmanyūttamaujaśśikhaṇḍi<br/>
cēkitānaremba tanna magandiruṁ tammandiruṁ berasu nelaṁ mūriviṭṭante bare<br/>
mundiṭṭu poḻalgoḍagoṇḍuvarpudumitta duryōdhanaṁ karṇa śalya śakuni<br/>
duśśāsanādigaḷoḷālōcisi pēḻimēgeyvamene karṇanintendaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
janamellaṁ neredakkaṭaṇṇarivarindēvandarēvōdareṁ |<br/>
binamēṁ pōpame nāḍa kūṭakuḷigaḷgēdōsamēṁbannamon<br/>
danekēḷāntaranikki mikka vijayaśrīkāntegaṁ kāntegaṁ<br/>
ninagaṁ dōrvaladindamonde paseyoḷ pāṇigrahaṁ geyyenē // ViVi.3.65 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
ene śalyanintendaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
kuḍuvoḍenistrapaṁkuḍuvudēṟisidaṁ besekōlanendu pēḻ<br/>
kuḍuvude kanneyaṁ dvijakulaṅgidu viśvanarēndra vr̥ndadoḷ<br/>
toḍarda parābhavaṁ drupadanaṁ taṟidoṭṭade kemmagānidaṁ<br/>
kaḍegaṇisirdoḍenna kaḍugorvida tōḷgaḷa korvadēvudō // ViVi.3.66 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 85]<br/>
endu keḷardu nuḍidu sayambarake neredarasumakkaḷellaranutsāhisinōḍe<br/>
nōḍe—<br/>
</p>

<p>
pakkareyikki banduvu hayaṁ ghaṭe paṇṇiduvāyudhaṅgaḷiṁ<br/>
tekkane tīvi banduvu rathaṁ puliviṇḍuvolādaḷurke kai<br/>
mikkire bandudondaṇi raṇānaka rāvamaḷumbamādudār<br/>
mikku barduṅkuvannarivargembinegaṁ masagittu rājakaṁ // ViVi.3.67 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu nelaṁ mūriviṭṭante taḷardu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
teregaḷa bambalaṁ miḷirva kētanarājigaḷōḷivaṭṭa be<br/>
ḷnoregaḷa piṇḍanettisida beḷgoḍegaḷ makaraṅgaḷaṁ bhayaṁ<br/>
kara karigaḷ teṟamboḷeva mīṅgaḷanuḷkuva kaidugaḷ nirā<br/>
karisire mēredappi kavidattu narādhipa sainya sāgaraṁ // ViVi.3.68 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu kavida ripubaḷa jaḷanidhiya kaḷakaḷa ravamaṁ kēḷdu poḻalaṁ pugalollade<br/>
ninda manujamāndhātanaṁ pāñcāḷarājanintendaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
dhanuvaṁ nīṁ tegedeccu mīnanaḷavaṁ keykoṇḍudarkaṁ karaṁ<br/>
ninagī kannike sōltudarkamerdeyoḷ kōpāgni kaigaṇme baṁ<br/>
dinituṁ rājakulaṁ samastabharadiṁ mēleḻdudin kāvanā<br/>
vano nīnallade kāvudenna taleyaṁ vidviṣṭavidrāvaṇā // ViVi.3.69 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
embudumarāti kāḷānaḷanidarkēnuṁ cintisalvēḍa nīmenna kāḷegamaṁ<br/>
peṟagirdu nōḍimendu tānuṁ bhīmasēnanuṁ divyaśarāsanaṅgaḷaṁ koṇḍu pūṇe<br/>
puguvarāti balamaṁ mārkoṇḍu tege neṟedise—<br/>
</p>

<p>
saraḷa podaḷda balsariya kōḷgiralāṟade bil teraḷdu du<br/>
rdharahayamaḻgi sandaṇisi sandaṇi kōḻgudigoṇḍudagra bhī<br/>
kara rathamaḻgidantighaṭegaḷ peṟagiṭṭoḍe kaṭṭegaṭṭidaṁ<br/>
tire taḷardattarāti balamāmpavarār kadanatriṇētranaṁ // ViVi.3.70 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgaḷ karṇanārṇavaninādadindārdu guṇārṇavanoḷ bandu tāgi<br/>
śalyaṁ bhīmasēnanoḷ tāgi kiṟiduṁ poḻtu kāde—<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 86]<br/>
aridu gelalke pārvana śarāsana vidyeyanendu nondu ni<br/>
ttarisade pārvanoḷ kalahamāgadu ciḥ doreyaltidendu bhā<br/>
skarasutanoyyanōsarise madramahīśanumaṁ marutsutaṁ<br/>
virathanemāḍi taḷtu nelakikkidanormeye mallayuddhadoḷ // ViVi.3.71 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgaḷā balada naḍuvirda nārāyaṇaṁ baladēvaṅge suṭṭitōṟi<br/>
bhīmārjunarkaḷivaramōghamapparendavara sāhasakke mecci santasambaṭṭirdāgaḷuḻi<br/>
darasumakkaḷellaṁ karṇa śalyar‌ mogandiridudaṁ kaṇḍu manaṅgeṭṭu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
karamosedā drupadajeyoḷ<br/>
neredosagege tamma bīramaṁ biṅkamumaṁ<br/>
teṟavuṁ tellaṇṭiyumeṁ<br/>
darikēsarigāgaḷīvavōl bennittar // ViVi.3.72 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgaḷ vikrāntatuṅgaṁ billa koppina mēle keyyanūṟi muguḷnage naguttuṁ<br/>
pāñcāḷarājatanūjegintendaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
ninnanuḻugisalumājiyo<br/>
ḷennaṁ beṅkoṇḍu kādalu bandīgaḷ<br/>
binnane mogadiṁ bīrar<br/>
bennittudaninisu nōḍa sarasiruhamukhī // ViVi.3.73 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
embannegaṁ drupadaṁ bandavar pāṇḍavarappudumaṁ tannaḷiyaṁ<br/>
vikramārjunanappudumaṁ tappilladaṟidu mahāvibhūtiyiṁ poḻalaṁ pugisi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
poḻaloḷagoppe kannaḍiya kañcina tōraṇadōḷigaḷ taḷa<br/>
ttaḷise vicitra kētutatigaḷ miḷirdāḍe purāṅganā janaṁ<br/>
gaḷa jaya jīyamāna ravamikkuva sēse manōnurāgamaṁ<br/>
baḷeyise pokkanā drupada mandiramaṁ parasainyabhairavaṁ // ViVi.3.74 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgaḷ drupadaṁ pacceya nelagaṭṭinoḷaṁ rājāvartada kambadoḷaṁ pavaḷada<br/>
janteyoḷaṁ padmarāgada bōdigeyoḷamindranīlada bhadradoḷaṁ karkētanada<br/>
jāḷarigeyoḷaṁ paḷukina citrabhittiyoḷaṁ candrakāntada candraśāleyoḷamoppuva<br/>
[p. 87]<br/>
vivāha gēhamaṁ sameyisiyadaṟa naḍuvaṇārdra mr̥ttikā viracitamappa<br/>
caturāntaradoḷ muttina caukada naḍuvaṇa cembonna paṭṭavaṇeya mēgaṇa dugulada<br/>
paseyoḷ guṇārṇavananā drupadajeyanoḍane kuḷḷirisi hita purōhita<br/>
prājyājyāhuti huta hutavaha samakṣadoḷ keynīreṟedu pāṇigrahaṁ geyse—<br/>
</p>

<p>
iḍidire mañjinoḷ tuṟugi teṅkaṇa gāḷiyoḷāda sōṅkinoḷ<br/>
naḍuguvaśōkavallariya pallavadoḷ navacūta pallavaṁ<br/>
toḍardavolāge gharmajaladiṁ naḍupākeya pāṇipallavaṁ<br/>
biḍidu beḍaṅganāḷdudu guṇārṇavanoppuva pāṇipallavaṁ // ViVi.3.75 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antorvarorvara kiṟu kuṇikegaḷaṁ piḍidu ratiyuṁ kāmadēvanuṁ<br/>
barpante bēḷveya koṇḍada modalge vandu kanakagiriyaṁ balagoḷvapataṅga<br/>
[dampati]yantādampatigaḷ saptārciyaṁ mūṟu sūḻ balavandu<br/>
nindimbaḻiyamāke purōhitana pēḻdōjeyoḷ lājeyanagni kuṇḍadoḷ<br/>
suridu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
adaṟa podaḷdu nīḷda pogeyaṁ luḷitāḷaketanna vaktra pa<br/>
dmadinosedāntoḍākeya kapōladoḷānavadhūmalēkhe be<br/>
ḷpidirgoḷe gāḍivettaḍardu katturiyoḷ madavaṭṭeyaṁ viḷā<br/>
sade tegedante kaṇgesedu tōṟidudā kadanatriṇētranā // ViVi.3.76 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu sogayise pāḍuva maṅgaḷaravaṅgaḷumōduva r̥cegaḷuṁ parasuva<br/>
parakegaḷumeseye paseyoḷirdu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
parijeyanaṇṭu(?)kennegaḷanoyyane nīvuvacinnapūvanō<br/>
sarisuva hāramaṁ piḍidu nōḍuva kaṭṭida nūla toṅgalaṁ<br/>
tiripuva keytadondu nevadiṁ lalitāṅgiya śaṅkeyaṁ bhayaṁ<br/>
berasida nāṇumaṁ kramade piṅgisu bēsaṟadir guṇārṇavā // ViVi.3.77 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu keladoḷirda daṇḍurumbegaḷ buddhivēḻe—<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 88]<br/>
kānte podaḷda nāṇa bharadindadharīkr̥ta candrabimba sa<br/>
tkāntiyanānanāmbujamanoyyane bāgire kādalaṅge sa<br/>
ytantiru nāṇcadendaṇugeyar piḍidaḻkaṟoḷetti buddhi vē<br/>
ḻdante kadampinoḷ poḷeduvākeya hāra marīci mālegaḷ // ViVi.3.78 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antoppuva vivāha maṅgaḷadosageyoḷ maṅgaḷa pāṭhakareḻdu nindirdu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
indrānōkahamoppuvindra turaṅgaṁ sandindra gēhaṁ poda<br/>
ḷdindrānēkapamoppuvindranakhiḷēndraiśvaryamindrāṇi saṁ<br/>
dindrānarghya vibhūṣaṇaṅgaḷaribhūpāḷāvaḷī dustama<br/>
ścandraṅgīgarigaṅge maṅgaḷamahāśrīyaṁ jayaśrīyumaṁ // ViVi.3.79 [śārdūlavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu maṅgaḷa vr̥ttaṅgaḷanōde kiṟidumbēgamirdettida bōnadoḷ<br/>
kalyāṇāmr̥tāhāramanārōgisi baḻiyaṁ yakṣakardamada keygaṭṭiyoḷ keyyaṁ<br/>
timirdu tambulamaṁ koṇḍu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
kavi gamaki vādi vāgmi<br/>
pravarara paṇḍitara negaḻda mātaṟivara sa<br/>
bbavadavaroḍanantoseda<br/>
nnavāsadōlagadoḷirdanāgaḷ harigaṁ // ViVi.3.80 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
ā prastāvadoḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
bēsaṟe lōkamaṁ taguḷdu suṭṭaḻalinde kharāṁśu nārakā<br/>
vāsadoḷāḷvavōlapara vārdhiyoḷāḻvudumitta vanda saṁ<br/>
dhyā samayātta rakta ruci piṅge baḻikkudayādriyoḷ padaṁ<br/>
gāsida ponna puñjiyavolirdudu kaṇge himāṁśu maṇḍalaṁ // ViVi.3.81 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgaḷ drupadaṁ nijāntaḥpura parivāraṁ berasudāramahēśvaranalligōlagakke<br/>
vandu nr̥tya vādya gītātōdyaṅgaḷoḷ kiṟiduṁ bēgamirdōlagamumaṁ<br/>
pareyalvēḻdu mattina nālvargaṁ kontigu bēṟevēṟe māḍaṅgaḷaṁ bīḍuvēḻdu<br/>
guṇārṇavanaṁ sejjege bijayaṅgeyyimene kāmaṁ kaḷanēṟuvante sejjeyanēṟi<br/>
seḍedirdanallaḷaṁ nōḍi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 89]<br/>
nōṭadoḷaḻkajambaḍedu melnuḍiyoḷ bagevokku jāṇoḷa<br/>
ḷḷāṭamanellamaṁ kiḍisi sōṅkinoḷoyyane meyvoṇarci bā<br/>
ygūṭadoḷaḻkaṟaṁ paḍedu kūṭadoḷuṇmida becca taḻkeyoḷ<br/>
kūṭa sukhaṅgaḷaṁ paḍedanēṁ caduraṁ gaḷa baddedallaḻaṁ // ViVi.3.82 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
bēḍisuvappugaḷgoreva lalleya melnuḍigaḷge kūḍe nā<br/>
ṇūḍida kendugaḷge bagegoṇḍinisaṁ taledūguvantevōl<br/>
nāḍe podaḷdu nīḷdavara suygaḷa gāḷiyoḷoyyanoyyana<br/>
ḷḷāḍuvudāytu tatsurata mandiradujjvaḷa dīpikāṅkuraṁ // ViVi.3.83 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antā yiruḷa nālku jāvamuṁ kāmana jāgaradantavarge kendinoḷe<br/>
beḷagāge—<br/>
</p>

<p>
ninaginisappoḍaṁ manadoḷōvada kaḻtaleyemba pāpa ka<br/>
rmana maṟigaḷ karaṁ palavumaṁseṟegeydevivendu tamma na<br/>
ṇpinoḷavanoppipante muguḷoḷ maṟasundida tumbi pāṟe kō<br/>
kanada kulaṅgaḷuḷḷalarduvembinamandogedaṁ divākaraṁ // ViVi.3.84 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu mārtāṇḍanuṁ pracaṇḍamārtāṇḍanumuditōditarāge—<br/>
</p>

<p>
kacabhārāḷasagāminī parivr̥taṁ gaṅgātaraṅgōpamā<br/>
na caḷaccāmara vāta pīta nija gharmāmbhaḥkaṇaṁ draupadī<br/>
kucakumbhārpita kuṅkumadrava viliptōrasthaḷaṁ dāṇṭe kī<br/>
rti caturvārdhiyanirdanandu sukhadiṁ vidviṣṭa vidrāvaṇaṁ // ViVi.3.85 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
idu vividha vibudhajanavinuta jinapadāmbhōja<br/>
vara prasādōtpanna prasanna gambhīra vacana racana<br/>
catura kavitāguṇārṇava viracitamappa<br/>
vikramārjunavijayadoḷ<br/>
draupadī kalyāṇa varṇanaṁ<br/>
tr̥tīyāśvāsaṁ<br/>
</p>

<p>
---------------------------------------------------------------------<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 90]<br/>
[caturthāśvāsaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
śrīramaṇiyaṁ dviṣadbaḷa<br/>
pārāvāradoḷudagra bhuja vijaya mahā<br/>
mēruvine kaḍedu paḍedaḷa<br/>
vārumaniḻisidududāttanārāyaṇanā // ViVi.4.1 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu drupadana poḻaloḷ pāṇḍavar cāgakke būtuṁ bhōgakke poḻtuṁ<br/>
neṟeyadenisi sukhasaṅkathā vinōdadiṁ rājyaṁ geyyuttirpannegamittal—<br/>
</p>

<p>
cararāgeydidareydi hastinapurakkā pāṇḍavar tammuta<br/>
yvarumirdar drupadādhirāja puradoḷ keykoṇḍu pāñcāḷiyaṁ<br/>
dhuradoḷ karṇananāntu geldavanavaṁ sandarjunaṁ taḷtu saṁ<br/>
garadoḷ śalyananikkigeldadaṭanābhīmaṁ gaḍaṁ kāṇirē // ViVi.4.2 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
emba mātaṁ dhr̥tarāṣṭra duryōdhanādigaḷ kēḷdu billumbeṟagumāgi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
kāyvaḻaluṟe jatugr̥hadoḷa<br/>
gayvarumaṁ mantrabalade suṭṭoḍamavaraṁ<br/>
deyvabalamonde kādudu<br/>
deyvamanārayya mīṟi bāḻal neṟevar // ViVi.4.3 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
embuduṁ bhīṣma drōṇādigaḷ niścita mantrarāgi viduranaṁ<br/>
karedāḷōcisi pr̥thātanūjaraṁ ninna balla māḻkeyiṁ nuḍidoḍaṅgoṇḍu barpu<br/>
dendu pēḻdaṭṭuvudumātanante geyvenendu rathārūḍhanāgi pāñcāḷa rājapurakke<br/>
vandu pāṇḍuputraraṁ kaṇḍu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
adu piriduṁ pramādamaduvuṁ kururājanināytu pōytu saṁ<br/>
dudu maṟeyalkevēḻpudadanāḷvudu tappade pāṇḍurājanā<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 91]<br/>
ḷdudaneḷeyaṁ manaṁ basade barpudu nīmene pōpa kajjamaṁ<br/>
viduranoḷayvaruṁ samedu pēḻvudumā drupadaṅge rājadiṁ // ViVi.4.4 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
ātana baḻivaḻigoṭṭa madakari karēṇu jātyaśvaśaśitārahāra vastugaḷaṁ<br/>
keykoṇḍu drupadajeyanoḍagoṇḍu drupadananiravēḻdu katipaya prayāṇaṅgaḷiṁ<br/>
madagajapuramaneyde vandāgaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
ghana pathamaṁ paḷañcaleva saudha cayaṅgaḷināḍutirpa kē<br/>
tana tatiyiṁ karīndragaḷagarjaneyiṁ paṭaha praṇādamaṁ<br/>
ghanaravamendenartisuva kēkigaḷiṁ kaḍu rayyamappa ha<br/>
stinapuramaṁ jitēndrapuramaṁ paramēśvararāgaḷeydidar // ViVi.4.5 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgaḷā poḻala bīdigaḷoḷellaṁ gandhōdaka pañcagavyaṅgaḷaṁ taḷiyisi<br/>
guḍiyaṁ tōraṇaṅgaḷumaṁ tuṟugaluṁ bambalumāge kaṭṭisi dhr̥tarāṣṭraṁ<br/>
duryōdhana karṇa śalya śakuni nadītanūja bhāradvāja kr̥pādigaḷverasidirvandu<br/>
yathōcita pratipattigaḷindayvarumaṁ nibiḍāliṅganaṅgeydu mundiṭṭoḍagoṇḍu<br/>
vandu poḻalaṁ pugisi munname sameda bīḍugaḷoḷ bīḍaṁ biḍisi sūḻsūḻoḷe<br/>
birdanikki vividha vinōdaṅgaḷaṁ tōṟi kelavu divasamirdu drōṇa bhīṣma kr̥pa<br/>
vidurarkaḷ tammoḷālōcisi enna naḍapidudarkaṁ kūrtudarkaṁ pāṇḍuputrarge<br/>
nelanaṁ paccukoṭṭu paṭṭamaṁ kaṭṭuvenene duryōdhananēgeydumoḍambaḍadire<br/>
bhīṣmar munidu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
oḍeyaradēvarendu ninagittoḍe paṭṭamanurkidappe pēḻ<br/>
poḍavigadhīśarantavargaḷayvarumaṁ kramadinde paṭṭamaṁ<br/>
taḍeyade kaṭṭi bhūtaḷamanāḷisadirdoḍadarke sorki nīṁ<br/>
nuḍiyadiraṇṇa ninna nuḍigāṁ taḍedirpene pēḻ suyōdhanā // ViVi.4.6 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
kramamaṟidenna koṭṭudane koṇḍu manōmudadinde bāḻvudaṁ<br/>
tavarivarellaruṁ samanadallade mārmaledurkibhīmanoḷ<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 92]<br/>
samaradegarvadiṁ poṇaralārpire gāvilarinnumellaraṁ<br/>
yamasutanuṁ surēndrasutanuṁ posedīgaḷe mukki tōṟarē // ViVi.4.7 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
adalladeyuṁ pāṇḍuputrarappoḍe pāṇḍurājaṅge besakeyyadudanenage<br/>
besakeyvarennendudaṁ mīṟuvarallarānavarge paṭṭamaṁ kaṭṭi nelanaṁ paccukoḍu<br/>
vāgaḷaḍḍaṁ barpa gaṇḍaraṁ nōḻpenendu bhīṣmar baggisidoḍe duryōdhananati<br/>
sambhramākuḷitanāgi nīmendudanendu bāḻvenendoḍappudendu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
dharaṇī nārige pāṇḍuviṁ baḻiyamillāruṁ peṟar gaṇḍaraṁ<br/>
tiralēvaṁ baḍedirdoḍaḻdu kiḍuguṁ saptāṅgamī rājaka<br/>
kkarasaṁ dharmajanakkumendu nayadiṁ niścaisi kalyāṇa kā<br/>
ryaratar kaṭṭidarā yudhiṣṭhira nr̥paṅgutsāhadiṁ paṭṭamaṁ // ViVi.4.8 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
kaṭṭi sētubandhamaṁ tāge gaṅgānadiya teṅkaṇa paḍuvaṇa nelanaṁ nīmāḷvudu<br/>
mūḍaṇa baḍagaṇa nelanaṁ duryōdhananāḷvudendu dhr̥tarāṣṭraṁ pūrva sthitiyoḷ<br/>
paccukoṭṭu duryōdhananappoḍe pollamānasaṁ nīmuṁ tāmundeḍeyoḷire<br/>
kisuruṁ kalahamumenduṁ kundadadu kāraṇadindilligaṟuvattu yōjanadoḷindraprastha<br/>
membudu poḻalallige pōgi sukhadiṁ rājyaṅgeyyuttirimembudumante geyvemendu<br/>
samasta parivāra parivr̥tarāgi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
oḍavarpugra madēbha vāji gaṇikānarphyādi ratnaṅgaḷoḷ<br/>
toḍardopputtire lakṣmi danti turagaṁ śrī divyakāntājanaṁ<br/>
toḍevembondumanā surāsurarinā gōvindaniṁ munne kō<br/>
ḷpaḍedambhōnidhiyante bandu negaḻcindraprasthamaṁ dharmajaṁ // ViVi.4.9 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
eyduvuduṁ tatpuradupavanaṅgaḷaviraḷa maḷayāniḷa kampitaṅga<br/>
ḷaviraḷa kusumāvaḷi kampuvēṟe sogayipa kiṟu miḍigaḷoḷoppi tōṟe<br/>
lavaṇābdhiye baḷasidudenisuvagaḻa baḷasesedire kōṇṭeya celvu pogaḻa<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 93]<br/>
laridenisire negedudu nabhamaneyde miḷirva patākāvaḷi divamaneyde<br/>
baḷasida kembonna madilgaḷoḷage maṇimaya bhavanāvaḷi toḷagi beḷage<br/>
rasa rasada bāvi mane manege bēṟe kisugalgaḷa rajada kaṇiverasu tōṟe<br/>
surakujada neḻaloḷaṅgaṇadoḷēnumalapillade kaṭṭire kāmadhēnu<br/>
paradara pārvara sūḷeyara manegaḷavu dhanadana maneyumanēḻipa manegaḷavu<br/>
poḻala beḍaṅgaṁ mecci mecci nōḍi divijēndra viḷāsadoḷintu kūḍi<br/>
paritandāgaḷ piridosageverasi purakānteyarādaradinde parasi<br/>
sūsuva śēṣākṣatamaṁ samantu piriduṁ mana santasadindamāntu<br/>
karumāḍamanādaradindamēṟi keladoḷmāḍaṅgaḷanaṟidu tōṟi (?)<br/>
maṇi kanaka rajata vastugaḷanittu bēḍida nāḍugaḷanavayavadindamittu<br/>
kari turaga balaṅgaḷpercuvantu maleyuṁ maṇḍalamuṁ bercuvantu<br/>
koṇḍāḍuva nālvarumanujaroḷage negaḻdarigana tējame toḷagi beḷage<br/>
nelanaṁ pratipālisi dharmasūnu sukhamirdaṁ ripubaḷa timira bhānu // ViVi.4.10 [maṭṭaragaḷe]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antajātaśatru śatrupakṣa kṣayakara karavāḷa daṁṣṭrābhīḷa bhujaṅga mūrti<br/>
viśva viśvambharādhāramapparikēsariya tōḷvaladoḷ rājyaṁ geyyutirpannegaṁ<br/>
vikrāntatuṅganondeḍeyoḷirpiraviṅgummaḷisi digaṅganā mukhāvalōkanaṁ<br/>
geyyal bagedu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 94]<br/>
seṇasuḷḷudvr̥ttaraṁ taḷtiṟiyade caturambhōdhi paryantamaṁ dhā<br/>
riṇiyaṁ tāṁ pōgi bāykēḷisade munijanakkiṣṭivighnaṅgaḷaṁ dā<br/>
ruṇa daityar māḍe nīḍillade sale caladāṭandu kondikkadorvaṁ<br/>
guṇamuṇṭenduṇḍu paṭṭirpananaṇame nirudyōgiyaṁ bhūpanembar‌ // ViVi.4.11 [mahāsragdhare]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu vijigīṣuvr̥ttōdyuktanāgal bagedu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
aṟipidoḍenna pōganiniyaḷge manaṁ maṟukakke nīḷda ka<br/>
ṇṇoṟeduguvaśruvārige todaḷnuḍi lallege pakkugoṭṭu kā<br/>
lgeṟagire pōgukeṭṭapudu mōhamayaṁ nigaḷaṁ kaḷatrameṁ<br/>
daṟipade naṭṭiruḷ maṟedu sārcida nallaḷa taḷta tōḷgaḷaṁ // ViVi.4.12 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
mellamellane pattuviḍisi tanna toṭṭa divyābharaṇaṅgaḷellamaṁ kaḷedu divya<br/>
śaradhigaḷaṁ bigidukoṇḍu divyacāpamaṁ piḍidu prathama caḷita dakṣiṇa caraṇanāgi<br/>
nija nivāsadiṁ poṟamaṭṭu khāṇḍava prasthadinduttarābhimukhanāgi<br/>
kāmyakavanadoḷagane nīlaparvatada mēgane pōgi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
sagarara mēle gaṅgeyananākuladiṁ taralā bhagīrathaṁ<br/>
negaḻe tapō niyōgadoḷavaṅgamarāpage mecci pāyvuduṁ<br/>
gaganadinandhaka dviṣa jaṭāṭaviyoḷ baḻikāda śailadoḷ<br/>
sogayise pāydudintiduve bandhura kūṭa kuḷaṁ himācaḷaṁ // ViVi.4.13 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
vilasatkallōla nādaṁ negaḻdire nija kūṭāgradoḷ pāyva gaṅgā<br/>
jaladiṁ mūrdhābhiṣēkōnnati nile camarī lōla lāṅgūla mālā<br/>
vali vikṣēpaṅgaḷiṁ taccamararuha mahāśōbhe kaigaṇme viśvā<br/>
cala cakrēśatvamaṁ tāḷdidudakhiḷa dharā ramya haimācaḷēdraṁ // ViVi.4.14 [mahāsragdhare]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu mecci—<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 95]<br/>
cāru vividhāgni kārya<br/>
prārambha mahā dvijanma ghōṣadinaṁhō<br/>
dūramumavanitaḷāḷaṁ<br/>
kāraṁ saṁsāra sāra gaṅgādvāraṁ // ViVi.4.15 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
ene sogayisuva gaṅgādvāradoḷ munijanaṅgaḷa bēḷvegaḷgupadravaṅgeyva<br/>
niśāṭa kōṭiyaṁ niśita śarakōṭiyindamuccāṭisi kelavu divasamirdallipaḍemecce<br/>
gaṇḍana gaṇḍagāḍiyaṁ kaṇḍu phaṇīndrana kanne madanalateyemba nāgakanne<br/>
kaṇbēṭaṅgoṇḍu tanna lōkakkoḍagoṇḍu pōgal—<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgaḷumindu sūryaraṇamillade kaḻtaleyembudilla ta<br/>
dbhōgi phaṇāmaṇi dyutiye kaḻtaleyaṁ taledōṟalīyadā<br/>
nāgara nāgakanneyara rūpugaḷiṭṭaḷamāgebhōgigaḷ |<br/>
bhōgigaḷemba bhōgigaḷe bhōgigaḷalliya bhūganāyakar // ViVi.4.16 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu nāgakanne nāgalōkada viḷāsaṅgaḷaṁ tōṟuttuṁ tanna keḻagaṇa<br/>
nāgavimānakke vandu nāgakanneyaruṁ tānuṁ manambugisuvante majjanambugisi<br/>
rasarasāyanaṅgaḷanūḍuvante divyāhāraṅgaḷanūḍi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
nāgavibhūṣaṇa pratati nāgarakhaṇḍamapūrvamappa pu<br/>
nnāgada bāsigaṁ bageda baṇṇada puṭṭige nāgajālameṁ<br/>
dāgaḍe nāgalōka vibhavaṅgaḷoḷāḻisināgaśayyeyoḷ<br/>
nāgiṇi nāgabandhadoḷe taḷtu guṇārṇavanaṁ maruḷcidaḷ // ViVi.4.17 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antākeya mudduverasida todaḷnuḍigaṁ pūmāḷeverasida baḻalmuḍiga<br/>
malampuverasida nōṭakkamimbuverasida kūṭakkaṁ puruḍuverasida koṅkiṅgaṁkaddavaṇi(?) verasida sōṅkiṅgaṁ gāḍiverasida hāvakkaṁ nāṇverasida bhāvakkamoldu<br/>
moṟaldumireyire dēvēndraṅgamindrāṇigaṁ jayantanentante—<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 96]<br/>
antā phaṇikāntegamari<br/>
kāntāḷika phaḷaka tiḷaka haraneniparigaṁ<br/>
gaṁ tanayanadhika tējō<br/>
vantaniḷāvantanindumaṇḍaḷa kāntaṁ // ViVi.4.18 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu puṭṭuvudumātana bālakrīḍeyumākeya surata krīḍeyuṁ tanna<br/>
nōṭakkaṁ kūṭakkaṁ sogayise kelavu divasamirdalliṁ poṟamaṭṭu bandu<br/>
himavadgirīndra taṭa nikaṭavartigaḷappagastya vaṭamuṁ vasiṣṭhaparvataṅgaḷemba<br/>
tīrthaṅgaḷoḷōlāḍuttumā diśābhāgamanātmīya śāsanāyattaṁ māḍuttuṁ<br/>
bandindubimbavigaḷadamr̥tabindu durdinārdra candanānvitamumaśiśira kara ratha<br/>
turaga khura śikhara nikhaṇḍita lavaṅga pallavamumairāvata karalūna sallakīśabaḷa<br/>
mumappudayagiriyiṁ sogayisuva mūḍaṇa desege vandu nandeyaparanandeyaśvini<br/>
mahānandeyemba tīrthajalaṅgaḷoḷōlāḍuttumudvr̥tta ripu nr̥patigaḷa<br/>
nēsāḍuttumalliṁ taḷardu capaḷa kapibaḷa vilupta vigaḷita latābhavanamumadhika<br/>
baḷa naḷa karataḷagaḷita kuḷaśaiḷa sahasra santāna kaḷita sētubandhura mumappa dakṣiṇa<br/>
samudrada taḍiviḍidu bandu rāmacandraṁ viharisideḍegaḷaṁ nōḍi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
andidu sīteyoḷ neredu nindeḍe tatkharadūṣaṇarkaḷaṁ<br/>
kondeḍe pōgi pommareyanecceḍe tappadidappudendu kā<br/>
ypiṁ daśakaṇṭhanaṁ tridaśa kaṇṭakanaṁ kolalendu rāmanā<br/>
dandina sāhasaṁ manadoḷāvarisittakaḷaṅkarāmanā // ViVi.4.19 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu rāma janmōtpattiyoḷāda tannaya munnina sāhasaṅgaḷaṁ neneyuttuṁ<br/>
bandagastyatīrthamaṁ kaṇḍu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
baḷeyalkaṇmidudilla vindhyagiriyuṁ tannājñeyindorme mu<br/>
kkuḷisalkambudhi sāldudilla jagamaṁ tindirda vātāpipo<br/>
kkaḷurvātmōdara vahniyiṁ poṟamaḍal tānārtanillaḻdudi<br/>
lleḷe tēṅkirdudu bhāradiṁ baḍagenal pempārgagastyambaraṁ // ViVi.4.20 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endagastyatīrtha saubhadra pauḷōma kāmbhōja bhāradvāja<br/>
membaydu tīrthaṅgaḷoḷ vardhamānanemba r̥ṣiya śāpadoḷugragrāha<br/>
[p. 97]<br/>
svarūpadoḷirdaccaraseyarumaṁ viśāpeyar‌ māḍi maḷayaparvatama<br/>
neydevandu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
idu maḷayācaḷaṁ maḷayajaṁ maḷayāniḷanendu pempuve<br/>
ttudu sirikaṇḍamuṁ padedu tīḍuva gāḷiyumilli puṭṭipō<br/>
gadu posa suggi mūguvaḍadilliya kōgile bandamāvu bī<br/>
yadu kusumāstranājñe tavadelliyumilliya nandanaṅgaḷoḷ // ViVi.4.21 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
idaṟabhraṅkaṣa kūṭa kōṭigaḷoḷirdambhōja ṣaṇḍaṅgaḷaṁ<br/>
pudiduṣṇāṁśuvinūrdhvagāṁśunivahaṁ meyyiṭṭalarcuttumi<br/>
rpudu mādyadgaja gaṇḍa bhitti kaṣaṇaprōdbhēdadiṁ sārdu baṁ<br/>
didiroḷ kūḍuvudilli candana rasaṁ kembonna ṭaṅkaṅgaḷoḷ // ViVi.4.22 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
negaḻdī karpūra kāḷāgaru maḷaya mahījaṅgaḷēḷā latāḷī<br/>
sthagitaṅgaḷ kaṇgevaṁdirduvanivanevalaṁ kombugoṇḍaṅgajaṁ me<br/>
llage pārdārdāgaḷuṁ kinnara yuvati mr̥gī vrātamaṁ tanna nallaṁ<br/>
bugaḷindecceccu meccaṁ salisuvanadaṟiṁ ramyamintī nagēndraṁ // ViVi.4.23 [mahāsragdhare]<br/>
</p>

<p>
idiroḷ nindoḍe vajri sairisaniralvēḍemmoḷoḷvokku ni<br/>
lvudu nīnendu kaḍaṅgi kālviḍivavōl tannūrmigaḷ banduvaṁ<br/>
didaṟiṁ pōda tapōpaḷaṁ(?) gaganamaṁ mārpoyye kaṇgoppi tō<br/>
rpudidutprēṅkhadasaṅkhya śaṅkha dhavaḷaṁ gambhīra nīrākaraṁ // ViVi.4.24 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
caḷadaniḷāhata kṣubhita bhaṅgura tuṅgataraṅga māḷikā<br/>
vaḷana samuccaḷanmaṇigaṇātta marīci latā pratāna saṁ<br/>
vaḷayita vidruma druma viḷāsa viśēṣita bāḍavānaḷā<br/>
viḷa jaḷamaṁ manaṁ bayasi nōḍidanarṇavamaṁ guṇārṇavaṁ // ViVi.4.25 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu nōḍuttuṁ bandu mundondeḍeyoḷa[da]bhrābhra vibhrama<br/>
bhrājitōttuṅgaśailamaṁ kaṇḍu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 98]<br/>
vinatāputrana vajra tuṇḍahatigaṁ meyyāntu kaṇḍaṅgaḷu<br/>
ḷḷinamaṅgaṅgaḷanoḍḍiyoḍḍi tanuvaṁ koṭṭantu jīmūtavā<br/>
hananembaṅkada cāgi niccaṭikeyindī śaiḷadoḷ śaṅkhacū<br/>
ḍananānandade kāda pempeseye nāgānandamaṁ māḍidaṁ // ViVi.4.26 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endabhinava jīmūtavāhanaṁ jīmūtavāhanana parōpakārada bīrada<br/>
pempaṁ meccuttuṁ bandu gōkarṇanāthanaṁ gaurīnāthananavani pavana gagana dahana<br/>
taraṇi salila tuhinakara yajamāna mūrtiyaṁ triḷōkaika saṅgīta kīrtiyaṁ<br/>
kaṇḍu keygaḷaṁ mugidu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
pracaṇḍa laya tāṇḍava kṣubhitayāśu yasyānayā<br/>
sadigvaḷayayābhuvāsa giri sāgara dvīpayā<br/>
kulāla kara nirbhara bhramita cakralīlāyitaṁ<br/>
sa sarva jagatāṁ gururgirisutā patiḥ pātunaḥ // ViVi.4.27 [pr̥thvi]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu bāḷēndumauḷiyaṁ stutisi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
sogayisi banda māmarane taḷtelevaḷḷiye pūta jāti saṁ<br/>
pageye kukilva kōgileye pāḍuva tumbiye nallaroḷmogaṁ<br/>
nagemogadoḷ‌ paḷañcaleye kūḍuva nallare nōḻpoḍāva be<br/>
ṭṭugaḷoḷamāva nandana vanaṅgaḷoḷaṁ banavāsidēśadoḷ // ViVi.4.28 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
cāgada bhōgadakkarada gēyada goṭṭiyalampinimpuga<br/>
ḷgāgaravāda mānasare mānasarantavarāgi puṭṭalē<br/>
nāgiyumēno tīrdapu[de]tīradoḍaṁ maṟidumbiyāgi mēṇ<br/>
kōgileyāgi puṭṭuvudu nandanadoḷ vanavāsidēśadoḷ // ViVi.4.29 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
teṅkaṇa gāḷi sōṅkidoḍamoḷnuḍigēḷdoḍamimpanāḷda gē<br/>
yaṁ kivivokkoḍaṁ birida malligegaṇḍoḍamāda kendalaṁ<br/>
paṁ geḍegoṇḍoḍaṁ madhumahōtsavamādoḍamēnanembenā<br/>
raṅkusaviṭṭoḍaṁ nenevudenna manaṁ vanavāsidēśamaṁ // ViVi.4.30 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 99]<br/>
amardaṁ mukkuḷipantuṭappa susilondimpuṁ taguḷdondu gē<br/>
yamumādakkaragoṭṭiyuṁ caduraroḷvātuṁ kuḷir‌ kōḻpa joṁ<br/>
pamumēvēḻpudanuḷḷa meysukamumintennaṁ karaṁ nōḍi nā<br/>
ḍe manaṅgoṇḍire teṅkanāḍa maṟeyalkinnēṁ manaṁ barkumē // ViVi.4.31 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endarikēsari teṅkanāḍaṁ nāḍāḍiyallade meccuttumānāḍanonde<br/>
billoḷuṇḍige sādhyaṁ māḍi paścima digvibhāgābhimukhanāgi bandu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
sāra vastugaḷiṁ neṟedambhōrāśiye kādige kāvanuṁ<br/>
sīrapāṇi viḷāsadināḷdaṁ cakradharaṁ bagevaṅge saṁ<br/>
sārasāravidembudanandeytandanasañcaḷa kāñcana<br/>
dvāra bandhura bandha gr̥hōdyaddvāravatīpuramaṁ naraṁ // ViVi.4.32 [khacaraplutaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
annegaṁ tanna maydunanappamōghāstra dhanañjayana baravina santasadosage<br/>
paḍemātaṁ munduvaridaṟipuvante—<br/>
</p>

<p>
palavuṁ janmadoḷāda ninna keḷeyaṁ bandappanātaṅge beṁ<br/>
balaminnīṁ ninagātanātananiḷā vikhyātanaṁ kūrtu nō<br/>
ḍalumaḻkartamardappaluṁ paḍeveyindembante kettittu dal<br/>
balagaṇṇu baladōḷumābali bala pradhvaṁsigaṁdiṭṭaḷaṁ // ViVi.4.33 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu dakṣiṇākṣi spandanadoḷaṁ sūcisuva śubhasūcaneyoḷaṁ<br/>
nārāyaṇanudāttanārāyaṇana baravanaṟidu baladēva sātyaki kr̥tavarmādigaḷappa<br/>
tannoḍavuṭṭidaruṁ vr̥ṣṇi kāmbhōjakuḷatiḷakarappa yādavaruṁ berasu madakari<br/>
karēṇu turagādi nānā vidha vāhanaṅgaḷanēṟi maydunaṅgidirvandu tammalampi<br/>
naḻkaṟina rūpane kāṇbante kaṇḍu dikkarikarānukārigaḷappa bāhugaḷindamōrorvaraṁ<br/>
tegedappi nibiḍāliṅganaṅgeydānandajaḷa paripūrṇa vistīrṇa vilōcanaṁ<br/>
gaḷindaṁ muhurmuhurālōkanaṁ geyyuttumuttuṅga matta vāraṇaṅgaḷanēṟi<br/>
poḻalaṁ puge—<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 100]<br/>
sura nara kinnarōraga nabhaścara kānteyarēvarendu māṁ<br/>
karisuva keytadandada murāriya taṅgeyanappukeydu ca<br/>
ccaramoḷapoydu nīṁ ninage māḍuvudendamarēndraputranaṁ<br/>
karevavolāduvā purada vāta vidhūtavinūtakētugaḷ // ViVi.4.34 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgaḷ moḻaguva baddavaṇada paṟegaḷuṁ piḍida kembonna taḷigeyoḷ<br/>
tekkane tīvida biḍumuttina sēseyuṁ berasu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
odavida nūla toṅgaluli dēseyanāntu viḷāsadindiṟuṁ<br/>
kida niṟi gaṇḍaraḷḷerdegaḷaṁ tuḻivōjeyanuṇṭumāḍuvaṁ<br/>
dade niḍugaṇgaḷoḷnaḍe manōbhavanoḍḍaṇadante taṇḍa taṁ<br/>
ḍade paritandu sūsidudu sēseyanandu purāṅganā janaṁ // ViVi.4.35 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
miḷirva kuruḷgaḷoḷ poḷeva kaṇgaḷa beḷpu paḷañci cinna pū<br/>
gaṇegeṇeyāge purvumemegaḷ biḍadaḷḷiṟidikṣucāpadoḷ<br/>
khaḷa kusumāstraniṭṭa goṇeyakkeṇeyāgire niḷki niḷki kō<br/>
maḷe naḍe nōḍidaḷ kariyanēṟidanaṁ paḍemeccegaṇḍanaṁ // ViVi.4.36 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
mattorvaḷati sambhrama tvaritadiṁ mēkhaḷākaḷita ruciraluḷitādhara pallave<br/>
nōḻpa daṇḍugaḷoḷaṇḍugoṇḍu sorkidāne barpante bandu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
kāyade kāmanārdise tovalviḍivanteḍagayyoḷoppetō<br/>
rpāyele nōṭa bēṭada konar taledōrpavolāge bāyoḷi<br/>
rdāyele kaṇgevandeseye kayyele kayyoḷe bāya tambulaṁ<br/>
bāyoḷa tōṟe meymaṟedu nōḍidaḷā samaraikamēruvaṁ // ViVi.4.37 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
mattōrvaḷ karvinabilla tiruviṁ barduṅki barpalarambu barpante<br/>
bandu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
smaranaṁ rūpinoḷindranaṁ vibhavadoḷ pō meccenānāva gaṁ<br/>
ḍarumaṁ kacceyoḷiṭṭu kaṭṭuvenenuttirpāke gandhēbha kaṁ<br/>
dhara bandha pravibhāsiyappariganaṁ kāṇutte kaṇsōltu kā<br/>
marasaṁ bhōṅkane sūse tāḷdalaridendirkacceyaṁ kaṭṭidaḷ // ViVi.4.38 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 101]<br/>
antu nōḍida peṇḍirellaṁ kāmadēvanemba bēṇṭekāṟaṅgoḍḍida<br/>
pullegaḷantaralambina monege pūṇe pokku pakkāgire poḻaloḷagaṇiṁ bandu divijēndra<br/>
viḷāsōpahāsitamappa nija mandiramaṁ puge—<br/>
</p>

<p>
lategaḷ jaṅgamarūpadiṁ nereduvō divyāpsarōvr̥ndamī<br/>
kṣitigēnindrana śāpadindiḻiduvō pēḻemba śaṅkāntaraṁ<br/>
matigaṁ puṭṭuvinaṁ karaṁ parakegaḷ taḷpoyye sēsikkitiṁ<br/>
dratanūjaṅgidirvandu ṣōḍaśa sahasrāntaḥpuraṁ kr̥ṣṇanā // ViVi.4.39 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgaḷ nārāyaṇana taṅge subhadreyemba kanne kemmugila tereya poreyoḷ<br/>
negedu poṟamaḍuva vidyādhariyante tanna cembonna kannemāḍada mēgaṇa neleya<br/>
caupaḷigeya bāgiloḷ nindu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
baḷasida gujjugaḷ nereda mēḷada kanneyarettamikke saṁ<br/>
caḷisuva cāmaraṁ kanaka padmada sīguri toṭṭa māṇikaṁ<br/>
gaḷa beḷagiṭṭaḷaṁ tanagoḍambaḍe dēse viḷāsamaṁ puduṁ<br/>
goḷise maraldu kanne naḍe nōḍi guṇārṇavanembanītanē // ViVi.4.40 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu tanna mēḷadākegaḷaṁ besagoṇḍoḍākeya pattida kaṇṇumanuḻgida<br/>
manamumaṁ jōlda nāṇumaṁnēldasaramumanaṟidu sahajamanōjana kulada<br/>
calada cāgada bīrada bhāgyada saubhāgyadaguntigaḷanantumaḷavallade pogaḻe—<br/>
</p>

<p>
odavida tanna javvanada rūpina meyyoḷe tappudappu nō<br/>
ṭadoḷe poḍarputappu bage tappu manōjana pūvinambu tī<br/>
vida doṇetīvitannanise jāṇane tappade tappudappa nō<br/>
ḍidudadaṟiṁ guṇārṇavananā sati tappade tappu nōṭadoḷ // ViVi.4.41 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu taḷataḷa toḷaguva dukūlada sakaḷavaṭṭeyoḷnimirci<br/>
dantānumaralda tāvareyesaḻgaḷoḷ pudidu puduṅgoḷisidantānu<br/>
manaṅgāmr̥tavarṣamanodavisidantānumerdeyoḷeḍevaṟiyada poḷapinoḷ<br/>
taḷpoydu kaḍegaṇṇa beḷpugaḷ sogayisuva kuvaḷayadaḷanayaneya nōṭaṁ tanna<br/>
manadoḷaḷḷāṭamaṁ paḍeye—<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 102]<br/>
naneyambambane karci pāṟidapudō śr̥ṅgāra vārāśi bhōṁ<br/>
kane beḷḷaṅgeḍedatto kāma neṟemeyvercitto pēḻīkegeṁ<br/>
binegaṁ sōlamanuṇṭumāḍe harigaṁ karṇānta viśrānta lō<br/>
cananālōcana gōcarambaregamoldā kanneyaṁ nōḍidaṁ // ViVi.4.42 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu suratamakaradhvajana kaḍegaṇṇa nōṭaṁ kāmana kisugaṇcida<br/>
nōṭadantormodale tanna manadoḷaḷḷāṭamaṁ paḍeye—<br/>
</p>

<p>
sōladoḷeyde pīrda teṟadindemeyikkade nōḻpa kaṇge kaṇ<br/>
pīlivolāge bandu peṟatondu manambuge patti cittadoḷ<br/>
kīlise kāvanambavaṟa biṇpinoḷoyyane jōldavōle tāṁ<br/>
būla karaṅkavāhiniya mēle neṟaldire bāle līleyiṁ // ViVi.4.43 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgaḷā nārāyaṇanumudāttanārāyaṇanumāneyindamiḻidu nava<br/>
kisalaya vandanamāḷāḷaṅkr̥tamappa sapta tāḷōttuṅga ramya harmyaderaḍaneya<br/>
mogasāleyoḷiṭṭa ponna paḍigaṅgaḷoḷamikkida paḻiya sukhāsanaṅgaḷoḷaṁ kaṭṭida<br/>
cinnada bondarigeyoḷamesedirda maṇimaya pīṭhadoḷoḍanēṟi kiṟidu poḻtu<br/>
kuḷḷirdu majjana bhōjana tāmbūlānulēpana vibhūṣaṇa surabhi kusuma<br/>
dāmādigaḷiṁ santasambaḍisi dāmōdaranudaradoḷiṭṭukoḷvanitaḻkaṟoḷapagata patha<br/>
pariśramanaṁ māḍi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
ītaṁ birdinanītaṁ<br/>
bhūtaḷapatiyenisidariganoḍeyaṁ hari tā<br/>
nītane birdinanene vi<br/>
khyātaṅge naraṅge seṟapugeydananantaṁ // ViVi.4.44 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antenitānumandadoḷ seṟapugeydu vividha vinōdaṅgaḷaṁ tōṟi munne<br/>
badarikāśramadoḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
āyatiyindaṁ nara nā<br/>
rāyaṇarene negaḻdevariga nāvirvarumiṁ<br/>
tī yugadoḷīgaḷāṁ nā<br/>
rāyaṇaneṁ nīnudāttanārāyaṇanai // ViVi.4.45 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 103]<br/>
adaṟiṁ ninagamenagamētaṟoḷaṁ vikalpamuṁ vicchinnamumillendu<br/>
nuḍiyutirpannegamittal—<br/>
</p>

<p>
navanaḷinīvanaṅgaḷa parāga rajaṅgaḷanuṇḍu munnamaṁ<br/>
tavane viyattaḷa bhramaṇa vihvalanāgi baḻaldu kāṟuvaṁ<br/>
tevolire kempu tatkamaḷa kānana kaṇṭakalagnapādanā<br/>
davoluḍuguttumātma karamaṁ ravi pordidanastaśailamaṁ // ViVi.4.46 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
ā prastāvadoḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
ā sarasīja bāndhavana pimbaḍinoḷ kaḍuvinnanāduviṁ<br/>
tī sarasīruhaṅgaḷavanī padadoḷ bisuṭentu pōpeveṁ<br/>
bī samakaṭṭinoḷ nelasidanteṟagirduvu ṣaṭpadaṅgaḷu<br/>
tkēsara kōṭi saṅkaṭa kuśēśayakōśa kuṭīrakaṅgaḷoḷ // ViVi.4.47 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
caṇḍamarīcigastamayamilladudondeḍe nimma kēḷduduṁ<br/>
kaṇḍudumuḷḷoḍiṁbesasimāmiradallige pōpevendu me<br/>
ygoṇḍolavindagalkegaṇamāṟade pakkigaḷellamaṁ maru<br/>
ḷgoṇḍavolūḷdu kūḍe besagoṇḍu baḻalduvu jakkavakkigaḷ // ViVi.4.48 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu kamaḷavanaṅgaḷādityaṅge keyyaṁ mugivante mugiya jakkavakkigaḷ<br/>
suratamakaradhvajana subhadreya viraha paritāpamaṁ paccu koṇḍasuṅgoṇḍagale<br/>
sandhyārāgamavara manadanurāgamananukarisuvantuṭāge baḻiyaṁ kramakramadoḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
masiyindaṁ jagamellamaṁ ditisutaṁ muṁ pūḻdanō kālamē<br/>
gha samūhaṁ deseyellamaṁ kavidudō gandhēbha carmaṅgaḷaṁ<br/>
pasaraṁ geydano śambhuvemba bageyiṁ taḷpoydu kaḻpēṟi sū<br/>
cisalārgaṁvaśamāgadantu kavidattuddāma bhīmaṁ tamaṁ // ViVi.4.49 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgaḷā tārāgaṇaṅgaḷ diśāvaniteyara makuṭa māṇikaṅgaḷantenitubeḷagiyuṁ<br/>
kaḻtaleyanaleyalāṟavāduvu kanaka prāsāda paṁṅktigaḷ paḻapaḻane beḷaguva<br/>
[p. 104]<br/>
soḍargaḷanādityana naṇṭarendu tamōrājakaṁ muḷidu seṟegeydabeḷagina seṟeya<br/>
manegaḷannavāduvu madagaja gaṇḍasthaḷaṅgaḷoḷeṟagi moreva tumbiya bambalgaḷe<br/>
vimukhībhūtaṅgaḷāduvu taṇḍataṇḍadōlagakke puguva poṟamaḍuva vāraviḷāsiniyara<br/>
nūpuraṅgaḷa ravaṅgaḷoḷ nr̥pabhavanōpavana dīrghikāhaṁsakuḷaṅgaḷ taḷaveḷagāduvu<br/>
rājahaṁsa pārāvata mithunaṅgaḷuttuṅga prāsādaśikhara maṇigavākṣāntarāḷa vividha<br/>
gr̥hāntaragataṅgaḷāduvu udayagiri kaṭaka kuhara parikar[niśākaraṁ]hari[da]ḷita nija<br/>
hariṇa ru[dhi]ra nicaya nicitamādante lōhitāṅganāge—<br/>
</p>

<p>
neredai sañjeyoḷendu kāydodedoḍēnātmāṅgadoḷ rōhiṇī<br/>
caraṇālaktaka rāgamacciṟidudō mēṇkāmigaḷgīva rā<br/>
garasaṁpoṇmidudō tamōgajada kōḍēṟindamēṁ nondudō<br/>
hariṇaṁ tānenisittu raktaruciyiṁ bimbaṁ sudhāsūtiyā // ViVi.4.50 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgaḷ tanna rāgamaṁ rāgigaḷgellaṁ paccukoṭṭante kempu pattuviṭṭāgaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
munidīśaṁ tave suṭṭu muṁ karuṇadindittaṁ punarjanmamaṁ<br/>
ninagendārati pāpamuṁ paḍaṇamuṁ pōpante kāmaṅge maṁ<br/>
jjanakendettida candrakānta ghaṭadoḷ tandaḻtiyiṁ puṣpa vā<br/>
sanegendikkida nīḷa nīraruhamaṁ pōldattu kaḻpinduvā // ViVi.4.51 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āvarisitto nabhōnta<br/>
rbhūvivaramanamardinesakamene virahigaḷō<br/>
vōvidumadanana sōdana<br/>
dīvigeyene toḷagi beḷagidaṁ tuhinakaraṁ // ViVi.4.52 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu sogayisuvacca beḷdiṅgaḷoḷ sudhādhavaḷitōttuṅga ramya<br/>
harmyaderaḍaneya neleya caupaḷigeya mundaṇa ramya harmyāgradoḷe<br/>
siriyōlagaṅgoṭṭu vinōdaṅgaḷoḷ vikramārjunaṁ berasu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 105]<br/>
āgaḷanantananantapha<br/>
ṇāgaṇamaṇikiraṇameseye dugdhārṇavadoḷ<br/>
rāgadinirpantirdaṁ<br/>
bhōgi taḻattaḻisi beḷage keydīvigegaḷ // ViVi.4.53 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
atta subhadreyumoḍaluri<br/>
yuttire maravaṭṭu vijayanirdattale nō<br/>
ḍuttire susāḷabhañjike<br/>
gettudu keḷadiyara taṇḍamākeya rūpaṁ // ViVi.4.54 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
kannetanaṅgeyyalbage<br/>
gunnāṇ‌ mige manamumiḻduvariyal bageguṁ<br/>
kannaḍikuṁ tannaḷipaṁ<br/>
tannale tānintu kanne taḷaveḷagādaḷ // ViVi.4.55 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
nuḍiyisi kēḷguṁ harigana<br/>
paḍemātane mātu tappoḍaṁ mattamadaṁ<br/>
nuḍiyisuguṁ modalindā<br/>
nuḍi paṟipaḍe muḷidu nōḍugaṁ keḷadiyaraṁ // ViVi.4.56 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
aṟimaruḷantuṭe sorkina<br/>
teṟadantuṭe manamoṟalvuderdeyurivudu me<br/>
yyeṟaguvudu padevudānida<br/>
naṟiyenidēkendu kanne taḷaveḷagādaḷ // ViVi.4.57 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āneyanēṟi sauṣṭhavade barparikēsariyondu gāḍiyu<br/>
ddāni taguḷdu kaṇṇoḷe toḻalderdeyoḷ taḍamāḍe bēṭadu<br/>
ddāniyanāne manmatha mahībhujanōvade tōṟikoṭṭudoṁ<br/>
dāneye tannanānegolego[ṁ]dapudendu latāṅgi bercidaḷ // ViVi.4.58 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 106]<br/>
manamārādhita hōma bhūmi paśugaḷ kāmāturar banda mā<br/>
vanituṁ sthāpita yūpakōṭi baḷavatkāmāgni hōmāgni caṁ<br/>
dana karpūra mr̥ṇāḷanāḷame podaḷdidhmaṅgaḷintāge tā<br/>
ninituṁ kāmana bēḷveyendu sugidaḷ tanvaṅgi beḷdiṅgaḷoḷ // ViVi.4.59 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu kāmadēvanemba mantravādiya divya mantradiṁ stōbhaṅgoṇḍa<br/>
divya grahadante kāmagraha gr̥hīteyāgiremanōvaikalyarōmāñcaka stambhaka<br/>
kampa[svēda vaivarṇya]santāpānāhāravyāmōha gadgadāśrumōkṣa mūrchādi<br/>
nānā vikāraṅgaḷanoḍanoḍane tōṟuvudumākeya dādiya magaḷ<br/>
cūtalatikeyembaḷ kaṇḍu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
*padeverde batte kettuvadharaṁ desegeṭṭalargaṇṇa nōṭamu<br/>
ṇmida bemarōḷivaṭṭa niḍusuy todaḷiṅgeḍegoṇḍa mātu kuṁ<br/>
dida latikāṅgamondida vikāramadīkeyoḷīgaḷādudiṁ<br/>
tidu kusumāstranembadaṭanikkida sorkina goḍḍamāgadē // ViVi.4.60 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu tannoḷe bagedu mattamintendaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
kaḻiyalarāda sampageya baṇṇadavōle beḷarta baṇṇadoḷ<br/>
gaḻiyise kempu kaṇgaḷa modalgaḷoḷoyyane tōṟebāḍi pā<br/>
ḍaḻidu baḻaldu jōldiravu meyyoḷe meyviḍidenna kaṇgaḷoḷ<br/>
suḻiduvutāme kannaḍisidappuvukanneya kannevēṭamaṁ // ViVi.4.61 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
adaṟinīkeya bageyanaṟiyalvēḻkumendu mellamellane kelakke vandu<br/>
kuñcadaḍapada ḍavakeya paricārikeyarellarumaṁ kaṇgetti kaḷedēkāntadoḷ<br/>
kanneyanintendaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
mr̥gamada patrarēkhegaḷanēkege tāḷdiradāduvīkadaṁ<br/>
pugaḷuramēke hāra maṇimañjariyillade binnagirdudī<br/>
jaganamidēke hēma raśanā dhvaniyillade mūguvaṭṭudī<br/>
bageyoḷalaktaka dravadoḷondade ninduvu pādapaṅkajaṁ // ViVi.4.62 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 107]<br/>
nagegaṇ sōrva kaduṣṇa vāricayadiṁ bimbādharaṁ suyya beṁ<br/>
kegaḷiṁ nāḍe beḍaṅgugeṭṭiravidibtēkāraṇaṁ majjanaṁ<br/>
bugadārōgisalolladirpiravidēṁ nāṇaḷkidēṁ kāmanaṁ<br/>
bugaḷattitteḍeyāḍe sōṅkave valaṁninnaṁ sarōjānanē // ViVi.4.63 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu munname muṭṭi nuḍiyade poṟapoṟagane baḷasi kanneya śaṅkeyaṁ<br/>
kiḍisi mattamintendaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
vanabhr̥tkuntaḷeyā śirīṣa kusumābhāṅgakke kandaṁ kana<br/>
tkanakāmbhōjanibhānanakke piriduṁ dīnatvamaṁnīḷda mā<br/>
vina pōḻandada kaṇge bāṣpajalamaṁ cittakke santāpamaṁ<br/>
ninagaṁ māḍidanāvanātane valaṁ gandhēbhavidyādharaṁ // ViVi.4.64 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu tanna manamanaṟidu muṭṭi nuḍida keḷadiya nuḍige<br/>
peṟatēnumanenalaṟiyade nāṇci taleyaṁ bāgi nelanaṁ bareyuttuṁ nīroḷ<br/>
muḻugidarantummane bemaruttummaḷike vandu beccane suydoḍe—<br/>
</p>

<p>
usiradire manadoḷerdeyaṁ<br/>
pasarisuguṁ maṟukamadaṟinenagintuṭe eṁ<br/>
dusirusirdoḍe bage tīrguṁ<br/>
bisiduṁ beṭṭittumusiradēṁ tīrdapudē // ViVi.4.65 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
pēḻembudumā[ṁ]ninageḍe<br/>
vēḻade pēḻārge pēḻvenindina bandā<br/>
kāḻāda vāḻtegoṇḍoḍe<br/>
pāḻādudu manamumerdeyumēnaṁ pēḻveṁ // ViVi.4.66 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
bhōṅkane manamaṁ kadaḍi ka<br/>
laṅkidapudu biḍade manamanonalisidapudā<br/>
daṁkeḷadi pāṇbaraṅkusa<br/>
naṅkusadā poḷapumavana kaṇgaḷa beḷpuṁ // ViVi.4.67 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 108]<br/>
manasinajanambaralda posa mallige teṅkaṇa gāḷiyembiviṁ<br/>
tanubaladindamennanaledappuvavennane peṭṭuvercicaṁ<br/>
drana baladindamennanaledappuvadarkenagīgaḷondi caṁ<br/>
drana balamoḷḷitāgi saleyilladoḍāvudumoḷḷikeygumē // ViVi.4.68 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu manada maṟukamumanerdeya kudipamumaṁbageya<br/>
kuṟipamumaṁ meyya baḍatanamumanaṟiye tōṟi nuḍidoḍe rāja haṁsi mānasa<br/>
sarōvaramanallade peṟatanēke bayasuguṁ kaḷahaṁsagamaneyā suratamakaradhvajananallade<br/>
peṟatanēke bayasugumendu manadoḷe mantaṇamirdu bageyoḷe guḍigaṭṭi<br/>
santasambaṭṭintendaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
naneyambaṁ tegedeccanaṅgajana tappēnānumaṁ tōṟe kā<br/>
ṇbanitaṁ māḍade padmajaṁ madananaṁ baidantuṭē bēḍamī<br/>
binadaṁ tappale kalpitaṁ pariyadātaṅgendu ninnī manaṁ<br/>
ninagātaṁ dore neṭṭanādi puruṣaṁgēkakkanīnnāṇcuvai // ViVi.4.69 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
nīnidarkēnumaṁ bageyalvēḍa ninna bageyaṁ bagedante tīrcuvenendanēka<br/>
