prakāra vacana racanegaḷindākeya manamanāṟe nuḍiyuttirpinamitta vikramārjunanu<br/>
mōlagaṁ parediṁ baḻiyaṁ tanna pavaḍisuva māḍakkoḍanoḍanōlagisuttuṁ banda<br/>
paṇḍitarkaḷumanucita pratipattigaḷiṁ visarjisi subhadreya rūpu kaṇṇa pāpeyante<br/>
kaṇṇoḷe toḻale kaṇmuccade tanna jasadante pasarisidaccaveḷdiṁ gaḷanākeya kaṇgaḷa<br/>
beḷpina taḷarpenuttuṁ peḷpaḷisi candranaṁ nōḍi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
priya satiyānanēnduvoḷaminduvoḷaṁ bidi munnamāvudaṁ<br/>
nayadoḷe nōḍi māḍidanadāvudanendaṟiyalke nāḍe saṁ<br/>
deyamadu nīḷa nīraja vanaṅgaḷa celvugaḷembuvā latāṁ<br/>
giya kaḍegaṇṇa beḷpugaḷa silkida silkina silkivallavē // ViVi.4.70 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 109]<br/>
adalladeyuṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
ā navamāḷikā kusuma kōmaḷe rāga rasa prapūrṇaṁ caṁ<br/>
drānana lakṣmiyiṁnabhadoḷirdamr̥tāṁśuvinudghakāntisaṁ<br/>
tānamanāvagaṁ tanage māḍidaḷendoḍe tadgr̥hāntarō<br/>
dyāna sarassarōja ruciyembudidākeya keyyadennirē // ViVi.4.71 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu tanna manamumanerdeyumanuṟe seṟeviḍidirdapūrva rūpeya<br/>
rūpumaṁ manadoḷe bagedu bhāvisi mattamintendaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
kusuriya rūpaneyde pogaḻalkaṟiyeṁ naḍu purvu bāse ka<br/>
ṇgosageyanuṇṭumāḻpa jaghanaṁ beḷarvāy molegaḷ kadampugu<br/>
rvasiṟane nōḍe mokkaḷamadār naḍe nōḻpoḍamantumintuṁ mū<br/>
ṟasiyavu mūṟu doḍḍiduvu mūṟeḍe teḷḷiduvambujākṣiyā // ViVi.4.72 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
mr̥gaśiśu nētreya naḍuverde<br/>
yugurgaḷ karamasidukanaka kāñcī ninada<br/>
pragaṇitamagalda nallaḷa<br/>
jaganamidennerdeyanentu pokkaḷipuvudō // ViVi.4.73 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu sairisade—<br/>
</p>

<p>
molegaḷ baṭṭiduvāgi kargida kuruḷ koṅkāgi kaṇgeyde nī<br/>
ḷdalargaṇgaḷ capaḷaṅgaḷāgi jaghanaṁ kāñcī kaḷāpa prabhō<br/>
jjvalamudvr̥ttamumāgitāmalege madhyasthaṅgaḷāgirduva<br/>
kkaleyaltakkude kennamā trivaḷigaḷgennaṁsarōjākṣiyā // ViVi.4.74 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu kiṟiduṁ bēgamaṟimaruḷantu palumbi pambalisi mattamākeya<br/>
hāva bhāva viḷāsa vibhrama kaṭākṣēkṣaṅgaḷ manamanonaliseyumerdeyaṁ<br/>
kanaliseyumanaṅgamataṅgaja kōḷāhaḷākuḷīkr̥tānta raṅganāgi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 110]<br/>
jagamaṁ māḍida padmajaṁ paḍedanillī kanneyaṁ māḍuva<br/>
llige candraṁ maḷayāniḷaṁ maḷayajaṁ nīrējamimmāvu ma<br/>
lligeyendintivanaḻkaṟindamardinoḷ tānaḻtiyiṁ toydu me<br/>
llage sandaṅgajanembajaṁ paḍedanantākāntiyiṁ kānteyaṁ // ViVi.4.75 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antaltappandākānteyaṁ vidhātraṁ māḍuvandu kosagina kēsaraṅgaḷa<br/>
namr̥tarasadoḷaṁ śr̥ṅgārarasadoḷaṁ bhāvisi rasa siddhamappa ponna lateya meyyumaṁ<br/>
nīlada tale navirumaṁ pavaḷada bāydeṟeyumaṁ muttina pallumaṁ rājāvartada<br/>
seḷḷugurumaṁ dhūpada suyyumaṁ ratiya saubhāgyamumaṁ sīteya<br/>
sairaṇeyumanadrijāteya śr̥ṅgāramumaṁ manōmathana madanamōhana santāpana<br/>
vaśīkaraṇaṅgaḷemba kāmadēvanaydalarambina śaktigaḷumanondumāḍi lōkamellamaṁ<br/>
maruḷmāḍalendu peṇmāḍidanakkumendu mattamākeya nōḍida nōṭamaṁ bhāvisi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
neṟegoḷe gāḍi nōḻpa bage barpudumāne dalandu dantiyaṁ<br/>
niṟisi maraldu nōḍuvudumennumanā sati sōladatta ma<br/>
tteṟagi baḻaldu jōldaḷipi nōḍidaḷintele satta potta ka<br/>
ṇṇaṟiyada beḷḷanallenaṟideṁ dhavaḷākṣiya nōṭadandamaṁ // ViVi.4.76 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
daḷita kamalacchāyāṭōpaṁ manōja rasa prabhā<br/>
vaḷaya niḷayaṁ prōdyadbhrūvibhramaṁ mukuḷīkr̥taṁ<br/>
laḷita madhuraṁ lajjāḷōḷaṁ smarākuḷitaṁ manaṁ<br/>
daḷitamapasanmugdhaṁ snigdhaṁviḷōkanamōpaḷā // ViVi.4.77 [hariṇīplutaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
uḍamogamemba tāvareya nīḷdesaḻoḷ maṟidumbi pāydoḍaṁ<br/>
baḍanoḷakoṇḍu kaṇmalara beḷpugaḷāliya kaḻpinoḷ poda<br/>
ḷdoḍanoḍanōḍuvaṭṭenage santasamaṁ maṟukakke māṇdoḍī<br/>
naḍegiḍe satvamaṁtamamumaṁ kaḍegaṇṇoḷe kaṇḍenōpaḷā // ViVi.4.78 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 111]<br/>
odavida bēṭavappoḍenagattaḷagaṁ bagevēḻvoḍenna mē<br/>
ḷada keḷeyarkaḷillavaḷumappoḍejavvana mattenāṇa kā<br/>
padu piridōtu mātaḍakalondida dūdavarilla neṭṭana<br/>
ppudaṟinadintaraṇyaruditaṁvalavennolavinduvaktreyā // ViVi.4.79 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endintu nallaḷaṁ nenedu kaṇgāpane kādu cintā samudrāntara parivr̥tanāgi<br/>
sairisalāṟade poḻalaṁ toḻaldu nōḻpa bagedandu rājamandiradiṁ poṟamaṭṭu<br/>
bare tannaṁ kāṇaloḍamaṟidu nuḍiyisi mecci mēḷada nāgarika viṭa vidūṣaka<br/>
pīṭhamardakarkaḷverasu kāmadēvanōlagakke barpante sūḷegēriyoḷagane<br/>
barpudumalli—<br/>
</p>

<p>
mr̥gabhūr̥ddhaviḷāsinī kabarikā bandhaṅgaḷaṁ pottu ma<br/>
lligeyoḷ bhāvisi dhūpadoḷ poredu tatkāntārati svēda biṁ<br/>
dugaḷoḷ nāndu kuruḷgaḷoḷ suḻidu mundondirda saubhāgya<br/>
ṭegaḷondiñcaradoḷ‌ paḷañci suḻidattandondu mandāniḷaṁ // ViVi.4.80 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgaḷāṟuṁ r̥tugaḷa pūgaḷanondumāḍi pūvinambugaḷaṁ paṇṇalendu<br/>
kāmadēvaṁ māḍidōjana sāleyirpantirda pūvina santeyoḷ<br/>
vasantakānteyarante—<br/>
</p>

<p>
ettida tōḷa mottamodalaṅgajalaṁpaṭa viddegettidaṁ<br/>
tettamapūrvamāge posavāsigamaṅgajacakravartigeṁ<br/>
dettida mīnakētanamanottarisuttire callavāḍi pū<br/>
vettuva mālegārtiyaranandarikēsari nindu nōḍidaṁ // ViVi.4.81 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
nōḍi nāḍāḍiyalladākegaḷa jōḍe geytaṅgaḷaṁ kaṇḍidu maneyāṇmanaṁ<br/>
māruvandamallade pū māruvandamaltendu muguḷnage nagutuṁ<br/>
barpanondeḍeyoḷ maneyāṇmana kaṇṇemeye kāṇḍapaṭamāgeyuṁbageyāṇmana<br/>
kaṇṇemeye dūdaviyāgeyuṁ bagedeḍeyaneydi bageda bageyaṁ bagedante tīrci<br/>
pōpa jōḍeyaraṁ kaṇḍu vikramārjunanintendaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 112]<br/>
kuṟupaṁ purvina jarve tōṟe bageyaṁ kaṇsannegaḷ pēḻeta<br/>
nneṟakaṁ tanna manakke kūḍe kelakaṁ gaṇḍaṅgamoḷpaṁ karaṁ<br/>
meṟevā prauḍheye jōḍeyakkumeḍeyoḷ dūṇṭinde dūṇṭiṅge pe<br/>
rvaṟeyaṁ poysi kelakke nāṇci taleguttirpākeyēṁ jōḍeyē // ViVi.4.82 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
kūriduvappa kaṇmalargaḷaḷḷerdeyoḷ taḍamāḍe tāme kaṇ<br/>
pērise purvu nālagevolāge manambugisalke balloḍā<br/>
jāreye jāre pāṟene karaṁ piriduṁ gaḻaputtumirpaḷaṁ<br/>
sārikeyembaralladabhisārikeyembare buddhiyuḷḷavar // ViVi.4.83 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu pāṇbaraṅkusanā pāṇbeyara geyva geytaṅgaḷumaṁ tōrpa<br/>
sannegaḷumaṁ āḍuva miḻtugoḍḍaṅgaḷumaṁ kaṇḍu cōdyambaṭṭu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
alargaṇṇoḷ smaranirdanakkumeḍevōpā jōḍe kāmaṅge kā<br/>
daleyakkuṁ peṟatēnopāradaradoḷ saṁsāra sarvasvamaṁ<br/>
gelevandimpinalampanāḷda saviyuṇṭakkuṁ samantāvagaṁ<br/>
taleyaṁ mūgumanotteyiṭṭu nerevantuntēnavar gāmparē // ViVi.4.84 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
enuttuṁ barpanondeḍeyoḷ manasijana naḍapida jaṅgamalategaḷante<br/>
manōjana kāpina kalpalategaḷante manōjanemba dīvagāṟana pullegaḷante tantamma<br/>
maneya mundaṇa pacceya jaguligaḷoḷaṁ maṇimaya matta vāraṇaṅgaḷoḷamaḷa<br/>
vigaḻida viḷāsaṅgaḷoḷaṁ taṇḍataṇḍade neredirda peṇḍavāsadoḷveṇḍiraṁ kaṇḍu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
manasijanīkegaṇḍu ratiyaṁ bisuṭaṁ haranīkegaṇḍu nū<br/>
tana girijāteyaṁ toṟedanā narakāntakanīkegaṇḍu to<br/>
ṭṭane nijalakṣmiyaṁ maṟedanemba negaḻteyanappukeydu ja<br/>
vvanada viḷāsadandada beḍaṅgina peṇḍire peṇḍiralliyā // ViVi.4.85 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
tisaramidāvudakka dharaṇīndrana koṭṭudu vajradāḷi ka<br/>
ṇgesevudidāvudolladuḻidaṭṭidoḍandu kubēranittude<br/>
kkasaramidāvudāṁ muḷiye kālviḍidindrana koṭṭudalte pō<br/>
pusiyadiremba sūḷeyare sūḷeyaralliya peṇḍavāsadā // ViVi.4.86 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 113]<br/>
embudaṁ kēḷuttuṁ barevare mattamā peṇḍavāsagēriyoḷage saubhāgyada<br/>
bhōgada cāgada rūpugaḷ mānasa rūpādante—<br/>
</p>

<p>
sīguricāpi nāṇkuṇidu meṭṭuvagujjarigaḻte bīramaṁ<br/>
cāgada pempumaṁ pogaḻva saṅgaḍavarpavaroḷpininde me<br/>
yyōgamaḷumbamappa biyamāgerdegaṁ bare barpa pāṅgagu<br/>
rvāgire celvanāytarabojaṅgara līle surēndra līleyiṁ // ViVi.4.87 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
mattamalli kōṭi poṅge ghaṇṭeyaluguva kiṟukuḷabojaṅgarumaṁ<br/>
suṇṇadeleyanotteyiṭṭu madadāneyumaṁ māṇikamumanotte viḍisalaṭṭuvacikka<br/>
pōrkuḷi bojaṅgarumaṁkatturi biyamaṁ meṟedu katturiyoḷ pūḻdu katturi<br/>
migadantirpa katturibojaṅgarumaṁ nōḍi poḻalabojaṅgarabiyadaḷavige<br/>
manadoḷ meccuttuṁ barpanondeḍeyoḷkaḷḷoḷamamardinoḷaṁ puṭṭida<br/>
peṇḍirante sogayisuva palarumoḷveṇḍirondeḍeyoḷirdu kāmadēvanemba<br/>
baḷamardukāṟana māḍida mardinante baḷedu daḷambaḍedu mūnūṟaṟuvattu<br/>
jātiya kaḷgaḷaṁ mundiṭṭu madhumantradiṁ madhudēvategaḷanarcisi ponna beḷḷiya<br/>
padmarāgada pacceya giḷiya kōgileya koñceyañceya kuntaḷikeya māḻkeya<br/>
sippugaḷoḷ tīvi madhumantraṅgaḷiṁ mantrisi neladoḷeṟedu taleyoḷ taḷidu<br/>
kaḷḷoḷ boṭṭaniṭṭukoṇḍu keladargellaṁ boṭṭiṭṭu kiṟiyar piriyaraṟidu<br/>
poḍavaṭṭu dharmagaḷguḍivargellaṁ mīsalgaḷḷaneṟedu ponna beḷḷiya sippugaḷoḷ<br/>
kiṟi kiṟidaneṟedu kuḍi bidira kuḍiya māvina miḍiya mārudina meṇasugaḍaleya<br/>
puḍiyoḷaḍasidallavallaṇigeyacakkaṇaṅgaḷaṁ savisavidu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
madhusītuṁ kaṭu sīdu pō puḷita kaḷḷaltuṁkaraṁ kaytuba<br/>
rpudu mārīci toḍarpuḷinde saradiṁkampilla sorkippalā<br/>
ṟadu cintāmaṇigēvudakka daḷamillī kakkarakkintuṭa<br/>
ppudu kaḷḷappudu tappadendu kuḍidar kāmāṅgamaṁ kānteyar // ViVi.4.88 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 114]<br/>
antu kuḍiye kakkarageytadiṁ tudinālageyoḷ todaḷverasu nuḍiva<br/>
nuḍigaḷuṁpoḍarva niḍiya purvugaḷuṁniḍiyalargaṇgaḷoḷ vikāraṁ berasu<br/>
negaḻdabhinayaṅgaḷuṁ maḷamaḷipa rūpu kaṇgaḷoḷ beḷpa naḻiye sōṅkuva<br/>
kempugaḷuṁtamma kempaṁ kaṇgaḷge koṭṭu kaṇgaḷa beḷpantamage māṟugoṇḍante<br/>
tanigettuverasubatti sogayisuva beḷarvāygaḷoḷimpaṁ tāḷdi poṟamaḍuva<br/>
taṇgampugaḷumamr̥tabindugaḷante negaḻva bemara bindugaḷumaḷavalladoppe<br/>
palarumoḷveṇḍirondeḍeyoḷirdalliyorvaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
beḷarta beḷarvāy karaṁ poḷeva pāṅge kaṇṇindaḷu<br/>
rtuḷuṅke niḍuvurvugaḷ poḍare bāya kampiṅgesā<br/>
rvaḷiprakaramandu sīguḍivolāge nāṇgeṭṭu mo<br/>
kkaḷaṁjatige meṭṭuvaḷ piḍidu meṭṭuvaḷ nōḻparaṁ // ViVi.4.89 [pr̥thvi]<br/>
</p>

<p>
mattamorvaḷūrvaśiyane pōlvāke tanna gambhīra nava yauvana<br/>
madadoḷaṁ madirāmadadoḷamaḷavigaḻiye sorki—<br/>
</p>

<p>
muḍi makaradhvajamboleḻaluttire bembiḍidoyyanoyyanu<br/>
ḷḷuḍe kaṭisūtradottinoḷe jōldire nāṇ‌ taledōṟe kūḍe kū<br/>
kiḍuvakukilva bikkuḷipa tēguvatanna toḍaṅkadeydenū<br/>
rmaḍi manadoḷ‌ paḷañcaleye ḍakkeyoḷaḻkajavāgeyāḍidaḷ // ViVi.4.90 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antākegaḷ tūgi toneva tonepaṅgaḷumaṁ marasarigeviḍidu bilviḍidāḍuva<br/>
būtāṭaṅgaḷumaṁ nōḍi gandhēbavidyādharanintendaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
nuḍivare nōḍa kaḷguḍivarembudidāgadasūruḷantadaṁ<br/>
kuḍivanumante kaḷguḍivarendoḍe nāṇcuvarantuṭappudaṁ<br/>
kuḍidumivandirārerdeyumaṁ seṟegeydapareyde dōṣadoḷ<br/>
toḍarvudumondupāśraya viśēṣadoḷoḷpane taḷvudāgadē // ViVi.4.91 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 115]<br/>
enutuṁ barpanondeḍeyoḷorvaṁpaḻikeyda nallaḷanuḻiyalāṟade<br/>
suḻiye muḷidātana keḷeyanintendaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
basanadoḍambaḍiṅgalasi māṇdoḍamintidanīvenendanaṁ<br/>
pusidoḍamāsedōṟe bagedōṟadoḍaṁ neradirdoḍaṁ sagā<br/>
ṭisadoḍamāyamuṁ calamumuḷḷoḍe pēsadavaḷge mattamā<br/>
ṭisuvude mattamañjuvude mattamaḻalvude mattamīvudē // ViVi.4.92 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu nuḍidu bisuḍisidaṁ mattorvaṁ tanageraḍaṟiyadolda nallaḷanē<br/>
taṟoḷappoḍamēvamaṁ māḍade bēṭamaṁ salisuvudarke santasaṁ baṭṭu muntaṇge<br/>
kāpaniṭṭintendaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
iniyaṁ noydumoḍambaḍaṁ nuḍidoḍendendappoḍaṁ ninnoḷe<br/>
ḷḷanituṁ dōṣamanuṇṭumāḍadireyuṁ kaṇpinte sandappudoṁ<br/>
dane kēḷdōpaḷe kūrmegeṭṭenage nīnēnānumondēvamaṁ<br/>
manadoḷ māḍidoḍande dīvaḷigeyaṁ mānāmiyaṁ māḍenē // ViVi.4.93 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu nuḍidaṁ mattamondeḍeyoḷorva[norva]ḷa naḍeya nuḍiya<br/>
muḍiya gāmpiṅge muguḷḷage nakku tanna kaḷeyaṅge tōṟi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
nayadoḷe nōḍi nōṭadoḷe mēḷisi mēḷadoḷappukeydu go<br/>
ṭṭiyoḷoḷapoydu pattisuva sūḷeyarandamaneyde pōlva sū<br/>
ḷeyaratuṟumbu sūḷeyara melnuḍi sūḷeyarirpa pāṅgu sū<br/>
ḷeyara negaḻte nāḍe tanagaḻti dalakkanesūḷeyāgaḷē // ViVi.4.94 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
ene kēḷdu muguḷnage naguttuṁ barpanondeḍeyoḷondu kandada<br/>
modalumaṁ vr̥ttada tudiyumanondumāḍi padamikkiyōdi paṇḍitikkige<br/>
muyvāntumāva kāḷegadoḷaṁ tāneōḍiyārōḍidarembante[bī rakke]muyvāntumondu vīsavanappoḍamārgamittaṟiyade cāgakke mayvāntu[ṁ]tamma[ṁ]naguvaranaṟiyadeṇbarēṟidakaḻteyante desedesege beseva paccapasiyeggarumaṁ<br/>
kaṇḍu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 116]<br/>
iṟiyada bīramillada kulaṁ tamagallada cāgamōdadō<br/>
daṟiyada vidde sallada cadur neṟekallada kalpi kēḷa mā<br/>
taṟiyada mātu tamma baṟuvātugaḷoḷ pudideggareyde ka<br/>
ṇdeṟevinamārpaḻiyadēneḷeyaṁ kiḍisalke ballarō // ViVi.4.95 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
ene naguttuṁ bareyondeḍeyoḷ nālvarayvar‌ gāḻdoḻtirirdalli<br/>
gōrvaneggaṁ goṭṭige vandu kaṇṇaṟiyade sōṅkeyuṁ manamaṟiyade<br/>
nuḍiyeyumātananākegaḷ bāseyoḷintendar‌—<br/>
</p>

<p>
bhāvakanendoḍaṁ caduranendoḍamār‌ peṟarāro nīne ni<br/>
nnāva guṇaṅgaḷaṁ pogaḻvoḍellavaṟiṁ neṟedemmoḷintu sa<br/>
dbhāvade goṭṭiral bayasi bandeyadīgaḷidoḷḷitāytu mā<br/>
dēvara mundaṇātanenalallade pēḻ peṟatēnanembudō // ViVi.4.96 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endātananākegaḷ kāḍi koṟacāḍi kaḷedar‌ mattamondeḍeyoḷorvaḷ<br/>
tannanuḻida posa bēṭadāṇmananēgeyduṁ pōgalīyade tannaḷipane tōṟi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
maneyanivaṁ manōbhavanivaṁ posa suggiyoḷādadonduki<br/>
ttanivanidennanēnuḻiyalīgume nīnuḻidāgaḷendu pō<br/>
pananiradōpanaṁ miḍukalīyade kālviḍidaḻtu tōra ka<br/>
ṇbanigaḷanikkidaḷ taraḷalōcane saṅkaleyikkidantevōl // ViVi.4.97 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
mattorvaṁ tanna sūḷeyoḷāda bēsaṟaṁ tanna keḷeyaṅgintendaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
muḷisaṟidañji bāḻteyaṟidittu manaṅgoḷeyuṁ kanalvuda<br/>
rkaḷaviyumantumilla saniyannaḷe kuṇṭaṇi pōda māriya<br/>
nnaḷe manedoḻtu sīrkaraḍiyannaḷe nāduniyoldumollada<br/>
nnaḷe gaḍa sūḷeyendoḍinitaṁ talevēsaṟanentu nīguveṁ // ViVi.4.98 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu nuḍidu geṇṭādaṁ mattorva bēṭakārtitāya kaṇṇaṁ bañcisitanna mopinākeya manege pōpa bēṭadāṇmanaṁ piḍidu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 117]<br/>
tappudu mātudūdavara keyyoḷe kālviḍidaṭṭi kaṇṇanīr<br/>
tappuvu niccamaccigadoḷaḻtu karaṁ bisusuyyesuydasuy<br/>
tappudu tappudenna tanu bēṭada kāṭadoḷintu kaṇḍumi<br/>
nnappoḍamāsevātanenagōpane nīṁ dayegeyyalāgadē // ViVi.4.99 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu karuṇambaḍe nuḍidoḍagoṇḍu pōdaḷ mattamondeḍeyoḷorvaḷ<br/>
kuṇṭaṇiyuparōdhakke piridīva mudupananuḻiyalañji tanna bēsaṟaṁ tanna<br/>
sabbavadākegintendaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
korevoḍe beṭṭugaḷbiruvuvuṇmuva lāḷeya lōḷegaḷ pona<br/>
lvarivuvu kemmi kummidoḍe tōḷoḷe jīva viyōgamappudeṁ<br/>
diraderdegappudattaḷagamā narepaṁnerevandupoṅgaḷaṁ<br/>
surivoḍamāro sairisuvarātana pallilivāya nātamaṁ // ViVi.4.100 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu nagisuttirdaḷ mattamondeḍeyoḷorvaḷ tanna nallanallige<br/>
dūduvōgi banda dūdavigēgeyva teṟanumanaṟiyade padedu paḍe mātaṁ<br/>
besagoḷvaḷaṁ kaṇḍu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
birayisibēṭadoḷ biriva nallaragaldu kanaldonalduna<br/>
llara deseyindamaḻtivare kōgileyakkelarakke tumbiya<br/>
kkaragiḷiyakke bandoḍamoṟalderdeyāṟuvarendūḍōta dū<br/>
tare tare banda sabbavada mātugaḷaṁ guḍigaṭṭi kēḷarē // ViVi.4.101 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antumalladeyuṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
manadoḷalampanāḷdiniyanaṭṭida dūdara sīyanappa mā<br/>
tina rasadoḷ konarvudu taḷirvudu pūvudu kāyvudantu kā<br/>
ytanitaṟoḷantu nindu manadoḷ todaḷillada nalmeyemba naṁ<br/>
dana vanamōparoḷ neredoḍantu rasaṁ biḍepaṇtudāgadē // ViVi.4.102 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antumalladeyuṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 118]<br/>
anuvise bēṭakāṟanolavirmaḍiyappudu bayye bēṭakā<br/>
ṟana bagenilladikkegoḷagappudu niṭṭise bēṭa bēṭakā<br/>
ṟana ruci bambaluṁ tuṟugaluṁ koḷutirpudu nūṅke bēṭakā<br/>
ṟana manavaṭṭi pattuvudu bēṭavidēṁ viparīta vr̥ttiyō // ViVi.4.103 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
indumī dūdavaremba[r]bēṭakāṟara bēṭamemba lategaḷaḍarpirpaṁ<br/>
tirdarentappa bēṭaṅgaḷumavar posa[yi]se posatappudu kiḍise kiḍuvudantu<br/>
malladeyuṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
nuḍigaḷoḷāseyuṇṭenaloḍaṁ taḷedantire nilvudentumā<br/>
veḍeyoḷamāsegāṇenene toṭṭane pōpuvu nallarirvarī<br/>
roḍaloḷagirpa jīvamadukāraṇadindame pōpa barpoḍaṁ<br/>
baḍanoḷakoṇḍa dūdavara keyyoḷekeyyeḍeyirpudāgadē // ViVi.4.104 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu nuḍiyuttuṁ barevare mattondeḍeyoḷorvaṁ garbhēśvaraṁ tanna<br/>
hr̥dayēśvariyanagaldu bandu peṟarārumaṁ meccadākeyaṁ nenedu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
miṟaguva tōra hāramumanappina kāḷasegaḍḍamemba bē<br/>
saṟinoḷe kaṭṭalolladanitaḻkaṟaniḻkuḷigoṇḍalampina<br/>
tteṟagida nallaḷaḷḷerdeyoḷakkaṭa beṭṭugaḷuṁ banaṅgaḷuṁ<br/>
toṟegaḷumīgaḷoḍḍaḻiyadoḍḍise sairisuvantuṭādudē // ViVi.4.105 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
munisinoḷādamēvayisi sairisadādaḻaloḷ kanaldu kaṁ<br/>
gane kanaluttumummaḷisi sairisalāṟade mēle vāydu ba<br/>
ydanuvisi kāḍi nōḍi tiḷidaḻkaṟaniḻkuḷigoṇḍalampugaḷ<br/>
kanasinoḷaṁ paḷañcalevuvennerdeyoḷ taraḷāyatēkṣaṇē // ViVi.4.106 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu sairisalārade tanna prāṇavallabheyoḍanirdandina muḷisosagegaḷaṁ<br/>
nenedu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
bage gelalendu kāḍi pusi niddeyoḷānire lallegeydu la<br/>
llege maṟedirdoḍaḻkaṟinoḷondi mogaṁ mogadatta sārci be<br/>
ccage niḍusuyda nallaḷa mukhāmbuja saurabhadoḷ podaḷdadēṁ<br/>
magamagisitto katturiya kappuradondu kadambadambulaṁ // ViVi.4.107 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 119]<br/>
endu tannoḷ palumbutirdanaṁ kaṇḍītanumemmandiganumemma<br/>
naṇṭanumakkumendu muguḷnage naguttuṁ barpanondeḍeyoḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
olavinoḷāda kāypu mige kādalanaṁ bisuṭante pōpa kā<br/>
dalaḷaḻutuṁ teṟandiridu nōḍida nōṭadoḷeyde taḷḷa pe<br/>
rmole poṟamuyvubenninitumormeyenāmbinamuṇmi poṇmika<br/>
ṇmalargaḷineccu pāyduvaralambugaḷante vilōcanāmbugaḷ // ViVi.4.108 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
mattamondeḍeyoḷondu kāḷāgaru dhūpa dhūma malina śyāmalāṁlaṅkr̥ta<br/>
vicitra bhitti virājita ramya harmyataḷadoḷ palakāla magalda nallarirvarumondeḍe<br/>
yoḷ kūḍi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
samasandaḻkaṟalampanīye śayanaṁ gharmāmbuviṁ nāne mu<br/>
nname nāṇoḻkuḍivōgi sūsuva padaṁ gaṅgāmbuvaṁ pōle vi<br/>
bhramamaṁ kaṇṭharavakke tāḍana ravaṁ tandīye tacchayyeyoḷ<br/>
samahastambiḍivantuṭāytu surata prārambha kōḷāhaḷaṁ // ViVi.4.109 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antanēkaprakāra pura janajanita vikāraṅgaḷaṁ toḻaldu nōḻpannegaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
soḍarguḍiyoyyanāge posa mallige mellagekampu nāṟeta<br/>
ṇpiḍidelarūde gāvarada melluli tumbiya gāvaraṅgaḷaṁ<br/>
geḍegoḷe candrikāprabhe modalgiḍe nāḍe vitarkadiṁ bera<br/>
lmiḍidu guṇārṇavaṁ neṟeye niṭṭisidaṁ beḷagappa jāvamaṁ // ViVi.4.110 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgaḷ tannoḍane toḻalva nāgaraka viṭa vidūṣaka pīṭhamardakarkaḷani<br/>
ralvēḻdu rājamandiramaṁ pokku tanna pavaḍisuva māḍakkevandu haṁsa dhavaḷa<br/>
śayyātaḷadoḷ gaṅgānadī puḷina parisara pradēśadoḷ maṟedoṟaguvairāvatadante<br/>
pavaḍisi kiṟidānuṁ bēgadoḷ subhadreyaṁ kanasinoḷ kaṇḍu nanasendu bagedu<br/>
maṅgaḷa pāṭhaka ravaṅgaḷoḷ bhōṅkaneḻcanannegaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 120]<br/>
pudida tamaṁ madīya kiraṇāḷiyanānadavōle ninnanā<br/>
vadaṭarumānarennudayamabhyudayaṁ ninagendu kanneyaṁ<br/>
padedoḍagoṇḍu pōgiradirendu guṇārṇava bhūbhujaṅge ka<br/>
ṭṭidiroḷe baṭṭedōṟuvavolandogedaṁ kamalaikabāndhavaṁ // ViVi.4.111 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
idu vividha vibudhajanavinuta jinapadāmbhōja<br/>
varaprasādōtpanna prasanna gambhīra vacana racana<br/>
catura kavitā guṇārṇava viracitamappa<br/>
vikramārjuna vijayadoḷ<br/>
caturthāśvāsaṁ<br/>
</p>

<p>
---------------------------------------------------------------------<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 121]<br/>
[pañcamāśvāsaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
śrī vīraśrī kīrti<br/>
śrī vākśrīyemba peṇḍiragalade tannoḷ<br/>
bhāvisida peṇḍirenisida<br/>
sauvāgyada hariganemmanēnoldapanō // ViVi.5.1 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
emba bageyoḷ subhadre pa<br/>
lumbi manambasade tanuvanāṟisalalariṁ<br/>
tumbigaḷiṁ taṇṇelariṁ<br/>
tumbida tiḷigoḷadineseva banamaṁ pokkaḷ // ViVi.5.2 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
taḷataḷisi poḷeva māvina<br/>
taḷirgaḷaśōkegaḷa misupa lategaḷa nele ba<br/>
ḷvaḷa baḷeda bēṭaduruḷiya<br/>
baḷagamidendeḷeyaḷeḷasi taḷaveḷagādaḷ // ViVi.5.3 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
koḷada taḍiviḍidu beḷedeḷa<br/>
daḷirgaḷaśōkegaḷa lateya manegaḷoḷe teṟaṁ<br/>
boḷevalara basade suḻivaḷi<br/>
gaḷa baḷagada danige kinisi kiṅkiṟivōdaḷ // ViVi.5.4 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
surayiya biri muguḷgaḷa pore<br/>
voreyoḷpoṟevorakanalladalluguva rajaṁ<br/>
boredu parakalisidaḷikuḷa<br/>
parikaramumanatanu śikhiya kiḍigaḷe gettaḷ // ViVi.5.5 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu naneya koneya taḷira niṟidaḷira muguḷa birimuguḷa miḍiya<br/>
kiṟumiḍiya bilmiḍigaḷoḷeṟagi tuṟugida banamaṁ pokkalliyuṁ meyyanāṟisalāṟade<br/>
pūta cūta lategaḷoḷ taḷpoydaposa muttina bāsaṇigeyoḷ bāsaṇisida biri<br/>
muguḷgaḷoḷ tuṟugidadirmutteya suttinoḷesedupāśrayambaḍeda sāndra<br/>
candrakāntada śileyanoḷagumāḍi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 122]<br/>
idiroḷ kaṭṭida tōraṇaṁ niṟidaḷir pūgoñcalandettame<br/>
ttida pūmāle parāga rāgamuditāśā bhā samudyanmadhū<br/>
nmada bhr̥ṅga dhvani maṅgaḷa dhvaniyenal sālvanegaṁ tāne ta<br/>
kkudu kāmaṅge vivāhamaṇṭapamenalkā mādhavī maṇṭapaṁ // ViVi.5.6 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
ā mādhavī latāmaṇṭapamaṁ kāmana ḍāmarakkaḷḷi vanadurgaṁ buguvante<br/>
pokkadaṟoḷage kappuravaḷukina jagaliyanagalitāgi samedu candanadeḷadaḷirgaḷaṁ<br/>
pāsi malligeyalargaḷaṁ pūvāsi mr̥ṇāḷanāḷadoḷ sameda sarigegaṅkaṇaṅgaḷumaṁ<br/>
yava kaḷikegaḷoḷ sameda kaṭisūtramumaṁ sāra karpūradoḷ viracisida<br/>
hāramumaṁ kariya neydila kāvinoḷ bhāvisida nūpuramumanadaṟa<br/>
birimuguḷgaḷoḷ citrisida karṇapūramumaṁ biḷiya tāvareyeḷagāvinasiya<br/>
nūloḷ kōda tōra malligeya birimuguḷa sarigeyumaṁ kappuravaḷukina<br/>
lambaṇamumaṁ toṭṭu kuḷirkoḻpa candana rasamanerdeyoḷaṁ meyyoḷaṁ<br/>
taḷkiṟidu kariya karbina kāvineḷa mainda vāḻeyeleya bijjaṇigegaḷiṁ bīsalvēḻdu<br/>
taṇpugeyye manada meyya santāpadoḷ bisusuydubisupinoḷanitumaṁ geldu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
kendaḷirvāsusēkadatovalgeṇeyāytu mr̥ṇāḷa nāḷavoṁ<br/>
doṁda[ḍe]votti pattiduvu sūsuva śītaḷa vāri maiyyane<br/>
ytandiradetta battiduvu tacchaśikānta śiḷātaḷaṁsiḍi<br/>
ldandoḍedattidēṁ bisido bēṭadabeṅkemr̥gāṅka vaktreyā // ViVi.5.7 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
arigana bēṭadonde posa bēṭada kēsuriyindameyde da<br/>
ḷḷuri negedandukendaḷira pāsugaḷiṁ kuḷirvālinīrgaḷiṁ<br/>
turipade sūsutuṁ keḷadiyarnadiputtire nōḍe dāhamo<br/>
ttarisidudondu ponna salagirpavolirdudu mey subhadreyā // ViVi.5.8 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
madana davānalārci tanuvaṁ suḍe taḷtemeyoḷ paḷañci bī<br/>
gida beḷarvāyoḷuccaḷisi tuṅga kucaṅgaḷa poyloḷettaluṁ<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 123]<br/>
kedaṟi vaḷitrayaṅgaḷa toḍarpugaḷoḷ toḍardoyyanoyyane<br/>
ydiduvu vilōlanētra jalabindugaḷākeya nimna nābhiyaṁ // ViVi.5.9 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
nagemogamaṁ podaḷdalarda tāvareyemba vimōhadiṁ mogaṁ<br/>
bugaloḍamā taḷōdariya suygaḷa beṅkeyoḷiccegeṭṭuto<br/>
ṭṭage koḷe munde biḻdu maguḻdā satiyikkida kaṇṇa nīra dhā |<br/>
regaḷoḷe nāndelarci podaḷdormeye pāṟiduvunmadāḷigaḷ // ViVi.5.10 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antā bāle kāyda puḍiyoḷage bisuṭṭeḷavāḻeyante surata<br/>
makaradhvajanoḷāda bēṭadoḷ mammala maṟugurtirdaḷatta manuja manōjanuṁ<br/>
madanaparitāpakkāṟadummaḷisi madhumathanana kaṇṇaṁ bañcisi vijr̥mbhamāṇa nava<br/>
naḷina parikarākr̥ṣṭa madhukara ramaṇīyapuḷina parisara pradēśa nivēśita virahi<br/>
jananicaya nicita mānasōnmatta kāminī gaṇḍūṣa sīdhu sēka puḷakita vakuḷa<br/>
mukuḷa vidaḷita manōharāśōka latā[ra]maṇīramaṇīya nūpura[rava]ramyamanaviraḷa kusumadhūḷī dhūsarapuḷina dhavaḷita dharātaḷamanutphulla<br/>
pallava līlāyamāna mattakōkilōllāsita śīkarōddāma durdina<br/>
vanamaneydevandu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
biridalaroḷ teṟamboḷeva tumbi taḷirteḷamāvu māvinaṁ<br/>
kurumane karci biccaḻipa kōgile kampanavuṅki pottu ni<br/>
ttariperalembivēvuvo madīya manōgata kāma rāga sā<br/>
garadodaviṅge nallaḷa vilōkana candrikeyonde sāladē // ViVi.5.11 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
enuttuṁ bandu birida birimuguḷgaḷoḷeṟagi tuṟugidaśōkalateyanaḻkartu<br/>
nōḍi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
alaralargaṇ muguḷ nage maḍal toḍe tumbi kuruḷ taḷir taḷaṁ<br/>
gole molekempu kempukone seḷḷugurgaḷ kuḍi tōḷ nayaṁ nayaṁ<br/>
nele nele bhaṅgi bhaṅgipadavaṇ beḷarvāy peṟatallidentō kō<br/>
mala late pēḻimenniniyaḷaṁ maṟegoṇḍudo sūṟegoṇḍudō // ViVi.5.12 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 124]<br/>
endu kiṟidānuṁ bēgamaṟimaruḷādantā lateyoḷ paḻigāḷegaṅgādi<br/>
barevare kāmadēvanimmāvina naneya[na]mbugaḷumanavaṟa balmiḍiyane miṭṭe[yumaṁ]māḍi tannanēsāḍi kāḍe—<br/>
</p>

<p>
asiyaḷanolgumollanaṇamennade rūpane nōḍi kūḍalā<br/>
ṭisi parideydi pattidalargaṇgaḷanēnumanennadantupē<br/>
kṣisi manamellamaṁ kavardapaṁ tanuvaṁ baḍamāḍi kāḍi daṁ<br/>
ḍisidapanaṅgajanmana kavarteya daṇḍada pāṅgidentuṭo // ViVi.5.13 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu nandanavanōpakaṇṭhaṅgaḷoḷanaṅgaśaravaśanāgi toḻaldu nōḍuttuṁ<br/>
tanna manadoḷintendu bageguṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
uriverdeyāṟe cintipa manaṁ guḍigaṭṭe maraldu nōḍuva<br/>
ccariyoḷe becca kaṇmalarge santasadāgaramāge bēṭadoḷ<br/>
birivoḍaloyyanaṅkurise saipinoḷintenagīgaḷī vanāṁ<br/>
taradoḷe kāṇalakkumo madīya manōratha janmabhūmiyaṁ // ViVi.5.14 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu bageyuttumākeyirda mādhavīmaṇṭapakke mogasi palara palavuṁ<br/>
teṟada bēṭada paḍemātugaḷaṁ kēḷdalliyārānumemmandigarirdarakkumenuttuṁ barpa<br/>
gandhēbhavidyādharanaṁ subhadre bhōṅkane kaṇḍu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
paḍideṟevandadindamerdeyuṁ teṟedattu podaḷda saṅkeyiṁ<br/>
naḍukamumāgaḷubbadigamādudu sādhvasadiṁ bemar bema<br/>
rveḍegaḷinuṇmi poṇmidudu kaṇ naḍe nōḍade tappu nōḍi nā<br/>
ṇeḍeyoḷamādudā satige nōḍaloḍaṁ paḍemeccegaṇḍanaṁ // ViVi.5.15 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgaḷ suratamakaradhvajanumanaṅgāmr̥ta payōdhiyoḷ mūḍi<br/>
muḻugāḍidarante kiṟidu bēgamanirdu tanniṁ tāne cētarisi subhadreya rūpanā<br/>
pādamastakambarameyde nōḍi tannoḷāda bēṭadoḷ baḍavaṭṭumēḻgevāḍivada<br/>
sasiyante sogayisuvasiyaḷaṁ kaṇḍu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 125]<br/>
sarasa mr̥ṇāḷanāḷavaḷayaṅgaḷoḷujjvaḷa vr̥tta mauktikā<br/>
bharaṇa gaṇaṅgaḷoḷ śaśikaraṅgaḷoḷāṟade bēṭadoḷ kana<br/>
lduriverde nōḍa nōḍaloḍanāṟidudēnamardinde toydu ka<br/>
ppuravaḷukindajaṁ kaḍedu kaṇḍaripaṁvalamenna nallaḷaṁ // ViVi.5.16 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
vr̥tta kucaṅgaḷindudirda candanadoḷ taḷirvāsu beḷpanā<br/>
ḷdattu dukūladondu maḍivāsidamāḻkevolāytu meyyani<br/>
kkuttire patti kendaḷirgaḷaccugaḷacciṟidante kāmana<br/>
ccottida bēṭadaccugaḷa māḻkeyoḷirdudu mey subhadreyā // ViVi.5.17 [utpalamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
adaṟinīkeyumenageraḍaṟiyada nalla manandōṟuvudu salge dōṟuvudu<br/>
māvudu dōsamendāke kuḷḷirda taḷira sejjeyoḍane kuḷḷirpuduṁ nāṇci<br/>
pogalendeḻda kanneyaṁ cūtalatikeyemba keḷadi jaḍidu kuḷḷirisi gandhēbha<br/>
vidyādharananintendaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
madanana kāypu māṇge sarasīruhajanmana meccu tīrge kō<br/>
ḷgudi manadindamindu poṟamāṟuge candrakaraṅgaḷindu ta<br/>
ṇṇiduverdegakke kendaḷira sejjeyajiñjiṇipōke ninna kū<br/>
ṭadoḷinidakke matsakhige bēṟe paḷāḷadoḷēṁ guṇārṇavā // ViVi.5.18 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
beḷaguva sāndracandra kiraṇāḷigaḷōḷigaḷindamettamu<br/>
jjvaḷisuviruḷgaḷaṁ kaḷedumeyde taḷirteḷamāvumaṁ manaṁ<br/>
goḷe naḍe nōḍiyuṁ kiviyanindoḷadiñcarakāntumintu kō<br/>
maḷeyasu mattamīyoḍaloḷirdudidemmaya saipu bhūpatī // ViVi.5.19 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
embannegaṁ suratamakaradhvajana subhadreya viraha paritāpadoḷāda paḍemātaṁ<br/>
karṇaparampareyiṁ kēḷdu santasambaṭṭu cakri, cakrikāvartiyappudaṟindā<br/>
vanāntarāḷakkorvane bandu mādhavī maṇṭapamaṁ pokku avarirvara nāṇumaṁ<br/>
naḍukamaṁ pattuviṭṭu nuḍidu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
kuḍalirpaṁ baladēvanennanujeyaṁ duryōdhanaṅgānoḍaṁ<br/>
baḍenīvaḻtiyadāgaḷuṁ ninage dal padmāsanaṁ tāne nē<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 126]<br/>
rpaḍisal kūḍidanirpudaltu nayaminnī poḻtepoḻtāge nī<br/>
noḍagoṇḍuyvudu kanneyaṁ taḍeyadir vidviṣṭavidrāvaṇā // ViVi.5.20 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu pōgevōge baladēvananumatadoḷ peṟagaṁ taguḷva yādava<br/>
balumuṇṭappoḍadanambugāṇisal nīne sālveyuḻidudaṁ māṇisalāne sālveniduve<br/>
muhūrtavāgi naḍevudendu śaibya baḷāhaka mēghavarṇa sugrīvaṅgaḷemba nālku<br/>
kuduregaḷoḷ pūḍida divya rathamanesagal dārukanemba sārathiyanīvudumā<br/>
rathamaṁ manōrathamberasēṟi cūtalatikeverasu subhadreyanēṟalvēḻdudātta<br/>
nārāyaṇaṁ nārāyaṇana parasida parakegaḷumaṁ keykoṇḍu bīḻkoṇḍindraprasthada<br/>
baṭṭeyoḷ sukha prayāṇaṅgeydanannegamitta baladēvaṁ subhadreyaṁ sāmanta<br/>
cūḍāmaṇiyuydanembudaṁ kēḷdu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
uṟadennaṁ kuḍalirda kūsanoḍagoṇḍuyvātanaṁ tāgi ta<br/>
ḷtiṟiyal kōḍagagaṭṭugaṭṭi taralinnārārparantappa po<br/>
ccaṟa sāmantare pōgimendu palaraṁ pēḻdāgaḷeytandaraṁ<br/>
toṟekoḷvantire koṇḍuvandariganeccugrēṣu dhārājaḷaṁ // ViVi.5.21 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgaḷ tanna pēḻda nāyakara sāvaṁ kēḷdu yādavabala jaḷanidhiverasu<br/>
viḷayakāla jaḷanidhiyanteteraḷalbageda baladēvanaṁ vāsudēvanintendaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
kulamaṁ pēḻvoḍe sōmavaṁśatilakaṁbillāḷtanambēḻvoḍu<br/>
jvala tīvrāstranighāta pātita ripuvyūhaṁ balambēḻe dō<br/>
rvaladoḷ kēḷ ninagaṁ balasthanoḍeyaṁ kūsiṅge koṇḍuyvudē<br/>
calamēdōṣamadarke nīn muḷivudē nīn pēḻvoḍān sālenē // ViVi.5.22 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu baladēvana manadoḷāda muḷisemba kiccaṁ tanna mr̥du madhura<br/>
vacanaracanājalaṅgaḷaṁ taḷiduna[di]pidanitta vikramārjunanuṁ katipaya<br/>
dinaṅgaḷindanēka sahakārāśōkānōkahanandanavanaprasthamanindraprasthamaneydevandu<br/>
munname tanna baravanaṟidu poḻaloḷaṣṭaśōbheyaṁ māḍi tanagidirvanda kontiya<br/>
[p. 127]<br/>
dharmaputra bhīmasēnādigaḷa pādapadmaṅgaḷaṁ tanma karakamalaṅgaḷindarcisi<br/>
tadīyāśīrvacanaṅgaḷanāntu tanage poḍamaṭṭa nakula sahadēvaraṁ parasi punaḥ<br/>
punarāliṅganaṅgeydu muhurmuhurāḷōkanaṅgeyyuttuṁ bandu divijēndra<br/>
viḷāsadiṁ poḻalaṁ puge—<br/>
</p>

<p>
parasuva purajanadodavida<br/>
parakegaḷambudhininādamaṁ mige tamma<br/>
yvarumoḍane meṟedu paramā<br/>
nurāgadiṁ bandu pokkarandaramaneyaṁ // ViVi.5.23 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu rājamandiramaṁ pokku dharmaputrananagalda panneraḍumāsadoḷāda<br/>
digvijaya prapañcamumaṁ subhadrāharaṇamumaṁ puruṣōttamana parama<br/>
mitratvamumanaṟidu santasambaṭṭu tamma nibarumēkastharāgi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
eredintaṭṭalevēḻpa kanne baḻiyaṁ bandaḷ maruḷdambujō<br/>
daranintaṭṭidanintu nōntaroḷarē saipiṅge nāminniḷā<br/>
dharanuṁ yādava vaṁśajarverasu barpantaṭṭi māḻpaṁ manō<br/>
haramappantu vivāhamaṅgaḷamanendandaṭṭidar dūtaraṁ // ViVi.5.24 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
aṭṭidoḍavar‌ pōgi baladēvanumaṁ vāsudēvanumaṁ kaṇḍu tamma<br/>
banda kajjamanoḍambaḍisi yādavarverasu mundiṭṭoḍagoṇḍu bare baravanaṟidu<br/>
pāṇḍavarayvarumidirvōgi yathōcita pratipattigaḷiṁ kaṇḍu poḻalgoḍagoṇḍu<br/>
bandu śubhadina nakṣatra yōgakaraṇaṅgaḷaṁ niṭṭisi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
pasurvandar pase vēdapāraga ravaṁ kaṇbēṭaduddāniyaṁ<br/>
pasaraṁ geydavolappa poccaṟa mahā sāmanta sīmantinī<br/>
prasaraṁ maṅgaḷa tūryanādameseyuttirpannegaṁ cakri rā<br/>
gisi keynīreṟedaṁ guṇārṇava mahīpālaṅgamā kanneyaṁ // ViVi.5.25 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 128]<br/>
antavarirvara bēṭememba lateya beḷasiṅge poynīreṟevante keynīrēṟedu<br/>
biyamaṁ meṟedu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
toṭṭa tuḍugegaḷ kaustubha ratnamanōronde masuḷise pālgaḍaloḷ<br/>
puṭṭidāneyanānegaḷ gelevare kuduregaḷ kudureyaṁ kīḻmāḍe<br/>
toṭṭa madanana pūgaṇegeṇeyāge gaṇikeyar gaṇidamaṁ bageyadintu<br/>
koṭṭaṁ taṅgege baḻivaḻiyendintu sarvasvamellamaṁ puruṣōttamaṁ // ViVi.5.26 [piriyakkaraṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu baḻivaḻigoṭṭimbaḻiyaṁ dharmaputraṁ baladēvananenitānumucita<br/>
pratipattigaḷiṁ santasambaḍisi dvārāvatige kaḻipidanā vivāhōtsavānantaradoḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
taḷirgaḷa pāsinoḷ poraḷutirdaḻalaṁ kiḍe sōṅke sōṅkugaḷ<br/>
kaḷeduvu meyya suyya padaveṅkegaḷaṁ bigiyappidappugaḷ<br/>
kaḷeduvu nāṇumaṁ kiṟidu jāṇumanaḻkaṟanīva cumbanaṁ<br/>
kaḷeduvugarmamaṁ kaḷeduvantavarirvara manmatha dravaṁ // ViVi.5.27 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
abhinava madalēkhā lālitaṁ vibhrama bhrū<br/>
rabhasa gativiḷāsaṁ dīpta kandarpa darpa<br/>
kṣubhitagaḷa nināda[ṁ]prasphuradgharma vāri<br/>
prabhavamesedudantā kāntegā kānta saṅgaṁ // ViVi.5.28 [mālini]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu kāmadēvanuṁ ratiyuṁ vasiṣṭhanumarundhatiyumīśvaranuṁ<br/>
pārvatiyumenisi samarūpa samasatva samarataṅgaḷoḷe samānurāgamaṁ paḍeye<br/>
sukhamirpannegaṁ subhadrege garbhacihnaṅgaḷ tōṟe—<br/>
</p>

<p>
oṭṭajeyiṁ bhāratadoḷ<br/>
kaṭṭāḷgaḷaniṟidu tavisalā jeṭṭigaraṁ<br/>
puṭṭidanembavoladaṭaṁ<br/>
puṭṭidanabhimanyu kalitanaṁ puṭṭuvavōl // ViVi.5.29 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 129]<br/>
antātaṁ puṭṭuvuduṁ tamage santasaṁ puṭṭi sukhamirpannegaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
agaruva meccuvacca sirikaṇḍadoḷaggalisittusūḍu śa<br/>
yyegaḷa biyakke jōmpadalarvāsugaḷoḷ nelasittu pūta go<br/>
jjagegaḷa sinduraṅgaḷoḷagōgaragampane bīṟutirpa ma<br/>
lligeyoḷaralda sampageyoḷaggalisittu basantamāsadoḷ // ViVi.5.30 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
muṁ mahiyellamaṁ śiśira rājane biccatamāḷdanīgaḷā<br/>
taṁ miḍukalkesalliradepōpudadēkene kāmadēvani<br/>
ttaṁ madhu pettanī nelananintidupattaḷeyendu sāṟuvaṁ<br/>
daṁ mige karci pāṟiduvu kendaḷiraṁ giḷiviṇḍinōḷigaḷ // ViVi.5.31 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
keḻagaṇa kendaḷir pudida mēgaṇa pandaḷirondidondu ke<br/>
ygaḻida pasurpumaṁ poḷeva kempumanāḷdire bēṭadoḷ kana<br/>
lduḻida viyōgiyaḷḷerdeyanāydadanāṭisalende manmathaṁ<br/>
ghaḻiyisi kempuvāsidavolirduvu māmaragaḷ basantadoḷ // ViVi.5.32 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
pareye pasurpu beḷpaḍare balmuguḷoḷ poredōṟe tamberal<br/>
porevoreyaṁ saḍilce naḍu poṅgire malligegaḷ basantadoḷ<br/>
biridoḍe nallaraṁ neneda nallara mellerdegaḷ basantadoḷ |<br/>
biriduvadento malligege nallara mellerde vēḷegoṇḍudō // ViVi.5.33 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
naneyeḷagampanettiyumaṇaṁ nanenāṟadaraldanēka kō<br/>
kanada vanaṅgaḷoḷ suḻidu taṇṇasamāgade kūḍe banda mā<br/>
vina posa pūvinoḷ poredu poṇmidakampu mogaṅgaḷaṁ caḷi<br/>
llene koḷe poyye tīḍidudu teṅkaṇa gāḷi vasantamāsadoḷ // ViVi.5.34 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
muguḷvadanādasampage maḍaltadirmutte maraldaralda ma<br/>
llige nanegarci kākaḷiyoḷāṇati geyva madāḷi pō pugal<br/>
pu[ga]lenutirpa pakki manamaṁ kavaruttire yōgigaṁ viyō<br/>
gigamuridāytu pokka pugilintu vasantakacakravartiyā // ViVi.5.35 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 130]<br/>
antu bhuvanakkellamosagevarpante banda vasantadoḷondu divasamannavāsa<br/>
dōlagadoḷudāttanārāyaṇanuṁ nārāyaṇanumirdalligorvaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
toṭṭekkavaḍaṁ maravil<br/>
kaṭṭida paṇekaṭṭu bēṇṭevaṟe doreyoḷoḍaṁ<br/>
baṭṭasiya suragi daḷivada<br/>
toṭṭaṅgige tannoḷamare bēṇṭeyanorvaṁ // ViVi.5.36 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
bandu poḍavaṭṭu kaṇḍiṁ<br/>
tendaṁ polanuḍugi banduduḍidudu pul kā<br/>
ḍuṁ daleleyikkeghaḷilene<br/>
ninduvu taṇiduvu mr̥gaṅgaḷettalumīgaḷ // ViVi.5.37 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
suḻiyadu gāḷi mr̥gaṁ ke<br/>
yvaṟigaḷa mētadoḷe taṇidapuvu pandigaḷuṁ<br/>
paḻa navirikkiduvāḷaṁ<br/>
paḻu paridāḍal karaṁ beḍaṅgavanipatī // ViVi.5.38 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
baravaṁkāḍaṁ bēgege<br/>
karamaṟideraḍuṁ mr̥gaṅgaḷuṁ taṇbuḻiloḷ<br/>
neredoḍavanduvu tappadi<br/>
darikēsari kaṇḍu meccuvai kōḷvāṅgaṁ // ViVi.5.39 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
kāḍoḍamevēḷe saleke<br/>
ygūḍidudene neladoḷirda nelliya kāyuṁ<br/>
nōḍa nelamuṭṭalaḻtiyo<br/>
ḷāḍuvoḍī devasamalte bēṇṭeya devasaṁ // ViVi.5.40 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
mattaṁ bēṇṭejāṟallade bēṇṭeya mātaṁ binnapaṅgeyveṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 131]<br/>
āḍalāḍisal pāḻiyaṁ niṟisaluṁ parigoḷal tovalikkaloḷagambaral<br/>
kāḍa bēliyaṁ mārkāḍanaṟiyaluṁ mūḍigekakkumbaṁ suḻisi jōmpaṁ<br/>
bīḍu biḍuvimbu kadaḷi teṅgina tāṇaṁ jāṇiṁ nīrdāṇamendeḍe yaṟiduṁ<br/>
māḍal māḍisal paḍe mecce nīṁ balle nīṁ mecce hariga kēḷāne balleṁ // ViVi.5.41 [piriyakkaraṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
mr̥gadolavaramumanarasana<br/>
bageyumanaṟidalasadeḷasalōlagisal ne<br/>
ṭṭage ballanuḷḷoḍavana<br/>
lte guṇārṇava bēṇṭekāṟanōlagakāṟaṁ // ViVi.5.42 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
mr̥gamaṁ gāḷiyanirkeyaṁ pakkeyaṁ gaṇidamaṁ kaṇḍiyaṁ mārkaṇḍiyaṁ<br/>
pugilaṁ pōgaṁ bāriyaṁ sanneyaṁ nūṟuvamarcuva nilveḍeyaṁ<br/>
bageyaṁ tegeyanallāṭamaṁ kāṭamaṁ nōvudaṁ sāvudanellandadiṁ<br/>
bagedāgaḷarasaroḷellakēḷnīṁ balle bēṇṭekāṟaroḷellavāne balleṁ // ViVi.5.43 [piriyakkaraṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
mattaṁ nelanuṁgāḷiyuṁ keyyuṁ mr̥gamumanaṟidu kālāḷoḷaṁ<br/>
kudureyoḷamoḷagaṁ baralāne ballenidu pervēṇṭeyandaṁ dīvada bēṇṭeyaṁ<br/>
binnapaṅgeyvoḍe gāḷiyuṁ kaḻivu[mu]ḻivuṁ kāpuṁ mēphuṁ tōḍuṁ bīḍuṁ<br/>
deseyuṁ koseyuṁ meccuṁ beccuṁ pōguṁ mēguṁ bedaṟuṁ[kedaṟuṁ]percuṁ<br/>
kundumanaṟidu kāṇaluṁ kāṇisaluṁ kaḍaṅgaluṁ kaḍaṅgisalumaḍaṅgisalumoḍḍalu<br/>
moḍḍisaluṁ pugisaluṁ migisaluṁ kāṇadudaṁ kāṇisaluṁ māṇadudaṁ māṇisalumē<br/>
ṟadudanēṟisaluṁ jāṇanāgi mūṟu kombumanāṟu nāṇpōgumaneraḻpajjeyumaṁ<br/>
mūṟu poḻtumaṁ mr̥gada mūṟiravumanāṟāraykeyumaṁ gāḷiyu<br/>
[mane]ṟaṅkeyumaṁ ballanāgi nambida baravumaṁ nambada baravumanaṟidu<br/>
maleyadudaṁ maleyisaluṁ maledudaṁ tolagisaluṁ nambadudaṁ nambisaluṁ<br/>
[p. 132]<br/>
nambidudaṁ biḍisalumoḷapuguvudarkeḍe māḍalumeḍeyāgada mr̥gamanavuṅkisalu<br/>
moldumollada nallarante miḍukisaluṁ paṇamuḍidaraṁ taḍḍaṁmāḍalumeseda<br/>
desegaḷgōḍisaluṁ kumārasvāmiya nimmaḍiyakeladoḷāne balleṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
baredante bennakarpese<br/>
dire sūcamanurci pullegāṭisi maleta<br/>
rperaleya sōlamanaḻtiyo<br/>
ḷarikēsari nindu nōḻpudondarasaltē // ViVi.5.44 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
padamumanimbumanaṇamaṟi<br/>
yadadēvudu badde beḷmigaṁ pajjedaleṁ<br/>
budaneraḍumanaṟivātane<br/>
caduraṁ caduraṅge badde vajjegaḷoḷavē // ViVi.5.45 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
mattaṁ pandivēṇṭeya mātaṁ binnapaṅgeyveṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
nelanaṁ niṟugeyaṁ naḍevondu padamumaṁ sōvaḷi mēvaḷi bisuvaḷiyaṁ<br/>
balamaṁ śakunamanoḷḷittupāyamaṁ piḍivandītane vandi kuruḍu kuṇṭeṁ<br/>
dalasadaṟidintu balmege beraletti pajjeyaṁ nelegaḷaṁ kiḍalīyade<br/>
sileya mēlādoḍaṁ śakunamaṁ niṟipante niṟisuveṁ pandiyaṁ nīṁ meccaluṁ // ViVi.5.46 [piriyakkaraṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
mattaṁ pandivēṇṭeya nāyentappuvendoḍasiya naḍuvumagaluramuṁ<br/>
taḷtu kaṭṭida kiviyuṁ kavida purvuṁ tōramāginirmāṁsamappa kālgaḷuṁ nelanaṁ<br/>
muṭṭadugurgaḷumanuḷḷudāgi jātyaśvadante bēgamāgi kōḷi kāḷikāṟanante<br/>
baḻiyaṟiviḍidu tumbina nīranurcidāgaḷaḍe paridumanneyarāḷante kādiya<br/>
lasade sūḷeyantekōḷampaṭṭaṭṭisade takkanante nambisiyumottaradantotti<br/>
yumuriyaḷurvantaḷurdukoḷvudidu pandivēṇṭeya nāy mattaṁ<br/>
kiṟuvēṇṭeya nāya[ṅ]koṇḍuṁ jāṟiyuṁ nelanuṁ poḻtuṁ polanumanaṟidu<br/>
[p. 133]<br/>
baḻiyoḷ posatuṁ paḻadumanaṟidu pariyisal nīne balleyadanāne ballenendu<br/>
binnapaṅge yvenantumallade balmegaṁ basanakkaṁ saviyappa kiṟuvēṇṭeyuṁ pervēṇṭe<br/>
yumalla duḻida bēṇṭeyaṁ bēṇṭeyenneṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
pasivu dorekoḷgumuṇisugaḷinikeygumāvandadoḷ kanaldāda meyya<br/>
nasiyanāgipuduḷiduvappuvu bagegoḷalappudu mr̥gada meyyoḷ<br/>
nisadamesevudaṁ ballāḷa bilbalme tannoḷamisutelēsappudu<br/>
basanamendaṟiyadēḷisuva‌r bēṇṭeyaṁ bēṇṭeyebinadaṁ gaḷarasaltē // ViVi.5.47 [piriyakkaraṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu binnapaṅgeyda bēṇṭeyātaṅge mr̥ga vyāyāma kārtikēyaṁ mecci<br/>
meccugoṭṭutovalanikkendu munde pēḻdaṭṭi nārāyaṇanuṁ tānumantaḥpura<br/>
parivāraṁ berasu bēṇṭege poṟamaṭṭu pariya tāṇakke vandu bēliya keladoḷallade<br/>
peṟagaṇulipiṅgamuḷḷoḷakkaṁ geṇṭāgi bīḍaṁ biḍisi bēṇṭekāṟana sameda<br/>
makaratōraṇamumaṁ guṇaṇeya bāṇasina majjanada rāṇivāsada manegaḷumaṁ<br/>
naneya pandarumaṁ taḷira kāvaṇaṅgaḷumaṁmā[ḍa]daneleyacaupaḷigegaḷumanavaṟa<br/>
mēlirdeleyaḍakeyumaṁ teṅgineḷanīrumaṁ koḷalimbappantire māḍi naṭṭa kauṅgina<br/>
teṅgina maraṅgaḷumaṁpaṇverasunaṭṭa maindāvaḻegaḷumaṁ tovalverasu naṭṭālaṁ<br/>
gaḷumanamare māḍida biṭṭuḷiyakakkumba toḍambeya mūḍigeya kadaḷikeya<br/>
kaṇḍapaṭaṅgaḷumaṁ palavuṁ teṟada palavuṁ poṟeyāgi kaṭṭida balegaḷumaṁ<br/>
paḍigaḷanamarcibilluṁ kudureyuṁ kālāḷuṁ nāygaḷumaṁ tiṇṇamirisi keyyaṁ<br/>
nēṇumanaḷaviyoḷ kūḍi naḍeyalvēḻdu bēṇṭe vasadanaṅgoṇḍukaṇḍiya<br/>
bāgiloḷudāttanārāyaṇanuṁ nārāyaṇanumirdu pugila pulleya modalu<br/>
ramumaṁ peṟagaṇa pulleyanaḍuvumanaydaṟoḷ mūṟumaṁ mūṟoḷeraḍu<br/>
maneraḍaṟoḷondumaneccu billa balmeyaṁ meṟedu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 134]<br/>
mundaṇa migamaṁ kaḻipade<br/>
sandisi baḻigoḷva migamumaṁ kaḻipade tā<br/>
nondaḷavidappadeccu ba<br/>
lindamaniṁ billa balmeyaṁ pogaḻisidaṁ // ViVi.5.48 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
mattaṁ berci poḷeduparivapoḷevullegaḷumaṁ taleyaṁ kutti viśālambariva<br/>
karaḍigaḷumanaḍaṅgi pariva puligaḷumaṁ sōṅki pariveygaḷumaṁ taḍaṁmeṭṭi pariva<br/>
kaḍavina kāḍemmeya mareya piṇḍugaḷumanaḷavidappa dondondanisuvante<br/>
palavaneccu nelaṁ biriye gajaṟi garjisi pāyva siṅgaṅgaḷumaṁ kaṇḍu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
āsukaraṁ gaḍa tamagati<br/>
bhāsura mr̥garāja nāmamuṁ gaḍamendā<br/>
dōsakke muḷidu negaḻdari<br/>
kēsari kēsarigaḷanitumaṁ taḷtiṟidaṁ // ViVi.5.49 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
iṟidavaṟa nettaroḷ ta<br/>
ḷkiṟidaṁ tannuramanuru gajaṅgaḷanāṭaṁ<br/>
daṟasi kolutirpuvembī<br/>
kaṟupinoḷarigambaraṁ gajapriyaroḷarē // ViVi.5.50 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu nara nārāyaṇarirvarumanavarata śarāsāra śūnyīkr̥ta kānanamāgeccu<br/>
mr̥gavya vyāpāradiṁ baḻaldu manadante pariva jātyaśvaṅgaḷanēṟi barevare—<br/>
</p>

<p>
javamuḻidondu sōgenaviloyyane karkaḍegāsiyāgi pā<br/>
ṟuvudumidenna nallaḷa rati śramaviślathakēśapāśadoḷ<br/>
sava savanāgitōṟidapudembude kāraṇadindadaṁ guṇā<br/>
rṇavaniḍaloldanilla haya valgana sañcaḷa ratna kuṇḍaḷaṁ // ViVi.5.51 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 135]<br/>
antu bēṇṭeyanāḍi baḻaldu bēsageya naḍuvagaloḷ vanakrīḍegaṁjalakrīḍegamāsaktarāgi yamunānadī taṭa nikaṭavartigaḷādaralli—<br/>
</p>

<p>
saraḷa tamāḷa tāḷa haricandana nandana bhūja rājiyiṁ<br/>
surivalarōḷi tadvanalatāṅgiya sūsuva sēseyāytu bhr̥ṁ<br/>
ga ravamadondu maṅgaḷa ravakkeṇeyāytu manōnurāgadiṁ<br/>
karevavolāytu matte kaḷahaṁsaravaṁ paḍemeccegaṇḍanaṁ // ViVi.5.52 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
yamunānadī taraṅgama<br/>
namuṅki vanalateya manegaḷaṁ sōṅki vana<br/>
bhamaṇa pariśramamaṁ mu<br/>
nname kaḷedudu bandadondu mandaśvasanaṁ // ViVi.5.53 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu kāḷindī jala śiśira śīkara vāri cāriyuṁ mr̥gayā paribhrama<br/>
śramōtthita svēda jala lavahāriyumāgi banda mandānilakke meyyanāṟisuttumā<br/>
puṇyanadiyaneydevandu tanna bāḷa nīrante kaṟaṅgi kargida nīraṁ nōḍi<br/>
vikramārjunaṁ kāḷāhimathanana mogamaṁ nōḍi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
tannoḷagaṇa pannaganaṁ<br/>
munnīn piḍidogeye kāyalāṟade piriduṁ<br/>
bannada karpesedudu toṟe<br/>
ginnuṁhara gaḷa tamāḷa nīḷacchaviyiṁ // ViVi.5.54 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
taḍiviḍidu pūta lategaḷa<br/>
noḍanoḍanelaraleye biḍade surivalargaḷanaṁ<br/>
deḍeguḍade nūṅki mellane<br/>
taḍiyaṁ sārcidapudidaṟa bambalderegaḷ // ViVi.5.55 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
vidaḷita nuta śatapatrada<br/>
paduvinoḷiradagalevōda haṁsananaṟasal<br/>
padedeḷasuva peṇṇañceya<br/>
pada koraliñcarada sarame savi kivigidaṟoḷ // ViVi.5.56 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 136]<br/>
neṟeyalardambhōruhadala<br/>
rduṟugalanaledogeduveseye jaladēvategaḷ<br/>
niṟiviḍiduḍal nimircida<br/>
kuṟuvaḍiya taraṅgadante bambalderegaḷ // ViVi.5.57 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
turagacayaṅgaḷantire taraṅgacayaṁ camarīruhaṅgaḷaṁ<br/>
tire kaḷahaṁse beḷgoḍegaḷantire beḷnore goṭṭi gāṇaraṁ<br/>
tire maṟidumbi mēḷadavarantire sārike rājagēhadaṁ<br/>
tire koḷanalli tāmarasarantire tāmarasaṅgaḷoppuguṁ // ViVi.5.58 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu bhāskara tanūjeyanubhaya taṭa nikaṭa kusuma nivaha tatparāgapaṭaḷa<br/>
piśaṅga tarattaraṅga sarōjeyaṁ mecci pogaḻdu jalakrīḍeyāḍal bagedu<br/>
tānumanantanumantaḥpura parivāraṁ berasu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
ottida taḷkettida taṟe<br/>
muttina posaduḍuge taḷira sōrmuḍi manamaṁ<br/>
pattisi jottise madanō<br/>
nmatteyaravayavade bandararasiyararebar // ViVi.5.59 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
idu mr̥du kaḷahaṁsada rava<br/>
midu nūpura ninadamidu rathāṅgayugaṁ ma<br/>
ttidu kuca yugamidu sarasija<br/>
midu mogamenisidudu nereda peṇḍira taṇḍaṁ // ViVi.5.60 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu madanana manōrājyamebarpante bandu taṇḍataṇḍade ramaṇīya<br/>
ramaṇījanaṁ berasu pañcaratnaṅgaḷiṁ kedaṟisi sāndina sausavada kuṅkumada katturiya<br/>
kadaḍaṁ kadaḍi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
nīlada beḷḷiya gāḍiyu<br/>
mī lalitāṅgiyara kaṇgepōltuṁ[nāṁ]ka<br/>
ṇgēḷidamāgirevendeḷa<br/>
vāḷegaḷōḍiduvu bāleyar puguvāgaḷ // ViVi.5.61 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 137]<br/>
antu pokkāgaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
ādale nīr guṇḍitteṁ<br/>
dīdaleyoḷe nindu satige harigaṁ tōṟu<br/>
ttādarade jānudaghnamu<br/>
rōdaghnaṁ kaṇṭhadaghnamembaḷavigaḷaṁ // ViVi.5.62 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu jaguneya maḍuvaṁ tammarasiyara vikaṭa nitamba bimbaṅgaḷa<br/>
ghaṭṭaṇeyoḷamare bagidogeda molegaḷaḷḷēṟinoḷaḷḷāḍi taḷḷaṅkaguṭṭi<br/>
nīrāṭamāḍuvāgaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
posatalardondu tāvareyegettu mukhābjamanondu tumbi cuṁ<br/>
bise sati berci peḷpaḷisi nōḻpudumākeya kaṇṇa beḷpugaḷ<br/>
pasarise tumbigaḷ kuvalayaṅgaḷaralduve gettu matteyuṁ<br/>
musuṟuvuduṁ guṇārṇavananāgaḷavaḷ bhayadindamuppidaḷ // ViVi.5.63 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
asiyaḷavuṅki kendaḷadoḷottuva nīr mogamaṁ paḷañce baṁ<br/>
cisalinisānumaṁ muḻugidāgaḍe bhōṅkane bandu bāḷemīn<br/>
musuṟi nirantaraṁ karduke satkaviyoḷ samanāgi mārgamaṁ<br/>
posayisi dēsiyaṁ posatu māḍidaḷorvaḷapūrva rūpadiṁ // ViVi.5.64 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
ā sakaḷa strī nivahada<br/>
pūsida mr̥gamadada muḍiyapūvina rajadiṁ<br/>
vāsisida nīra kadaḍiṁ<br/>
dāsavadoḷ sorki beṇṇḍumaguḻduvu mīṅgaḷ // ViVi.5.65 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
muḍi biḍe paredesaḻgaḷa posa<br/>
duḍugeya muttugaḷa kucada sirikaṇḍada be<br/>
ḷpoḍanoḍanesedire jaguneya<br/>
maḍu gaṅgeya maḍuvaninisananukarisirkuṁ // ViVi.5.66 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu nāḍeyuṁ poḻtu jalakēḷī līleyoḷ meṟedu nimirda kuruḷgaḷuṁ<br/>
kempēṟida kaṇgaḷuṁ beḷpēṟida bāydeṟegaḷuṁ paḷañcida baṇṇaṅgaḷumeseye<br/>
[p. 138]<br/>
sogayisuva nija vadhū janaṁ berasu poṟamaṭṭāgaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
teṟapuvaḍedaṅgajaṁ ke<br/>
yseṟegoḷe nōṭakara manamanāgaḷ koḷadiṁ<br/>
poṟamaḍe jigiltu pattida<br/>
kuṟuvaḍigaḷe meṟeduvavara nāṇgaḷa teṟapaṁ // ViVi.5.67 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgaḷ maḍiya bhaṇḍārada māṇikya bhaṇḍārada niyōgigaḷ tandu<br/>
mundiṭṭa ponna paḍaligegaḷoḷoṭṭida dēvāṅga vastraṅgaḷumananēka vidhada<br/>
tuḍugegaḷumanenitānuṁ teṟada sugandha dravyaṅgaḷumanarasiyargamarasumakkaḷgamittu<br/>
tāmirvaruṁ uṭṭu toṭṭuṁ pūsiyuṁ neṟeye keygeydu divyāhāraṅgaḷa<br/>
nārōgisi keygaṭṭigoṇḍu tambulaṅgoṇḍimbaḻiyamacyutaṁ vikramārjunana<br/>
keyyaṁ piḍidukoṇḍu tanna bāla krīḍeya sāhasaṅgaḷaṁ tōṟalendu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
kondenavuṅki sanda khara dhēnukaraṁ muḷisindamilli kā<br/>
ḷindiya pāvanappaḷisideṁ piḍidī sileyalli mattamā<br/>
ṭandaranugra daityaranaḷurkeyinikkidenilli munnameṁ<br/>
dandu guṇārṇavaṅge madhu kaiṭabhahāritoḻaldu tōṟidaṁ // ViVi.5.68 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antā vanāntarāḷamaṁ toḻaldu tōṟuttirpannegamanūna dāniya<br/>
dānaduddāniya dānamanānalānallade peṟar‌ neṟeyarembante toṭṭane<br/>
kaṭṭidiroḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
urivuriyane talenaviranu<br/>
karisire santapta kanakavarṇamumuriyoṁ<br/>
duruḷivolire jaṭharānaḷa<br/>
nurivinamantorvanuriya baṇṇada pārvaṁ // ViVi.5.69 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu varpanaṁ kaṇḍu sāmantacūḍāmaṇi tannoḷintendu bagedaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 139]<br/>
tapaniyama niyatanī ba<br/>
rpa pārvanēnaḻti tanagadaṁ bēḍidoḍi<br/>
nnapagata duritar sampū<br/>
rṇa puṇyarānalladilla pēḻ peṟaroḷarē // ViVi.5.70 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
embannegaṁ sāmantacūḍāmaṇiyaneydevandu nālkuṁ vēdaṅgaḷoḷ<br/>
nālkuṁ r̥caṅgaḷaṁ pēḻdu sita dūrvāṅkura vimiśraṅgaḷappa śēṣākṣategaḷaṁ koṭṭu<br/>
munde nindanaṁ nimage bāḻteyappudaṁ bēḍikoḷḷimene—<br/>
</p>

<p>
maṇi kanakādi vastugaḷanondumanollenavēvuvādavi<br/>
nnuṇisenagaḻti mey pasidujommanepōdapudenna vēḻpudaṁ<br/>
taṇiyuṇalīvoḍīvudene pārthanadēviridittenāvudu<br/>
ṇbuṇisene pēḻvenemba padadoḷ narakāntakanagnidēvanaṁ // ViVi.5.71 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
kāṇaloḍamaṟidu śaraṇāgatajaḷanidhiyaneyde vandanī bakavēṣi<br/>
ninnanēnaṁ bēḍidaṁ nīnītaṅgēnanitteyene—<br/>
</p>

<p>
pasiduṇavēḍidaṁ baḍavanānuṇalittenadalladilli dal<br/>
kusuriya mātugāṇenene kēḷdu murāntakanēṁ taguḷde yi<br/>
nnusiradirīva mātanivanuṇbudu khāṇḍavamītanagni muṁ<br/>
pusidivaninte pāyisidanindranoḷādi narēndrarellaraṁ // ViVi.5.72 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
ītanajamukhavyāghraṁ śvētakr̥ṣṇakārakanītana mātu mātallavendoḍā<br/>
mātu tannaṁ mūdalisidantāge vidviṣṭavidrāvaṇanintendaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
eredana pempuvēḻvoḍanalaṁ poṇarvātana pempuvēḻvoḍā<br/>
surapati koṭṭa tāṇadeḍevēḻvoḍamā yamunānadī taṭāṁ<br/>
taramosedittanānereye kēḷdaniḷādhara nīnadarke mā<br/>
teraḍaṇamāḍalāgadidu saipinoḷallade kūḍi barkumē // ViVi.5.73 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
danujārī divijēndra śāśvataguṇā ninnaḷkadēṁbēḍidā<br/>
nanalaṁ tīrtha samīpamambunivaha vyāḷōḷa kāḷindiyā<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 140]<br/>
vanamuṁkēḷduvubhūtamaydumaṟiguṁ koṭṭirdudādantaṟiṁ<br/>
denagiṁ māṇbudu sūḻe khāṇḍavamanāṁ taḷvilladindūḍuveṁ // ViVi.5.74 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
otti taṟumbi ninda ripubhūjasamājada bērgaḷaṁ nabha<br/>
kkettade bandu tanna maṟevokkoḍe kāyade cāgadoḷpina<br/>
ccottademāṇpu bāḻva puḻuvānasanembanajāṇḍamembudoṁ<br/>
dattiya paṇṇoḷirpa puḻuvallade mānasanē murāntakā // ViVi.5.75 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu maṟumātiṅgeḍeyilladantire nuḍida paḍemeccegaṇḍana gaṇḍavātumaṁ<br/>
nannivātumaṁ murāntakaṁ mecci—<br/>
</p>

<p>
samakaṭṭiṅgoregārumillariga kēḷ ninnoḷ samaṁ dhātriyoḷ<br/>
himakr̥dbhūdharadante ninna guṇa sandōhaṅgaḷaṁ kāṇala<br/>
kkume mattorvanoḷāgadentene samastōrvīdharāśēṣa śē<br/>
ṣamahānāgaphaṇāmaṇi dyutiyanēṁ khadyōtadoḷ kāṇbarē // ViVi.5.76 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
muniyisidaṁ karaṁ piriyanappudu bēḻpana bēḻpa vastu kāṁ<br/>
cana giriyindamaggaḷamenippudadādoḍamēno jīvamu<br/>
ḷḷinamiṟidarthamuḷḷinegamittu negaḻteyanāmpudemba peṁ<br/>
pina samakaṭṭu kaṇge doreyārarikēsari ninnavōl peṟaṁ // ViVi.5.77 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu tanage koṭṭa kōḍiṅgoḍambaṭṭa ditijakula dāvānalanu manarāti<br/>
kālānalanumananalaniṣṭārtha siddhiyakkumendu parasi manaḥpavana vēgadiṁ<br/>
pālgaḍalaneydi tanna baytiṭṭa divya sambhavaṅgaḷappa śvētāśvaṅgaḷoḷ pūḍida<br/>
divya rathamumaṁ dadhīci gaṇḍasthamappa gāṇḍīvavemba billumaṁ divya śaraṅgaḷoḷ<br/>
tekkane tīvida tavadoṇegaḷumaṁ tandenna pratijñeyaṁ tīrcuvoḍamindranaṁ<br/>
gelvoḍamivanamōghaṁ keykoḷalvēḻkumendoḍatirathamathananagnidēvaṅge poḍavaṭṭu<br/>
keykoṇḍu br̥handaḷanemba sārathiverasu rathamanēṟaloḍaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
pāvakanaḻvi khāṇḍavanamanuṇḍapanarjunanūḍidappanai<br/>
rāvatavāhanaṁ neṟedu sādhana saṁyutanāmpanalli nā<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 141]<br/>
nā vidha yuddhamuṇṭenute śaibya baḷāhaka mēghavarṇa su<br/>
grīva hayaṅgaḷindesevudaṁ rathamaṁ hari tānumēṟidaṁ // ViVi.5.78 [utpalamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu dārukaṁ rathamaṁ cōdisaloḍaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
cōdisuvudumirvara ratha<br/>
cōdakaravareraḍu rathada gāliya kōḷiṁ<br/>
dāda rajaḥpaṭalaṁ kavi |<br/>
dādame tīvidudu divija vadhuvira kaṇṇoḷ // ViVi.5.79 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
anteydi yamunānadiya teṅkaṇa deseyoḷ nūṟu yōjana<br/>
dagaladoḷamanite nīḷadoḷaṁ neṟedu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
kakubhāśōka kadamba luṅga lavalī bhūjārjunānōkaha<br/>
prakaraṁ puṣpita hēma paṅkaja rajassaṁsakta bhr̥ṅgāṅganā<br/>
nikaraṁ sārasa haṁsa kōkiḷa kuḷadhvānōtkaraṁ celvanā<br/>
ytu karaṁsaktaniḷimpa dampatigaḷindā nandanaṁ nandanaṁ // ViVi.5.80 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
ene sogayisuva khāṇḍava vanamaṁ vanaruhanābhaṁ vikramārjunaṅge<br/>
toḻaldu tōṟi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
alaraṁ nōyisadoyyanoyyanaḷigaḷ baṇḍuṇpuvāṭandu baṁ<br/>
daleyalkaṇmadu gāḷi sūrya kiraṇānīkakkamendappoḍaṁ<br/>
salavilluddhata siddha khēcarare tāmāḷvēriyāgintu ni<br/>
ccalumōrantire kāvarī doretu kāpī nandanakkindranā // ViVi.5.81 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
orme toḻaldu nōḍi banamaṁ maghavaṁ śaci pūta cūtamaṁ<br/>
nermidaśōkavallariya pallavamondane koydu rāgadiṁ<br/>
sōrmuḍiyoḷ taguḷcidoḍe sūḻane bārisidaṁ dalendoḍiṁ<br/>
kūrmeya mātu meccuvanitarke baḷārimurāsurāri[yēṁ] // ViVi.5.82 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 142]<br/>
intappa banamanidani<br/>
nnentanalananūḍalendu pūṇday muṁ pū<br/>
ṇdantūḍu pūḍu[śita]śara<br/>
santatiyaṁ billoḷēke nīṁ taḍedirpay // ViVi.5.83 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
paramāṇuvanitu banadoḷ<br/>
carācaraṁ pōge taṇiyananalanadarkāṁ<br/>
neramappenugra kinnara<br/>
sura danujōragara kadanamēṁ ninagaridē // ViVi.5.84 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
embudumante geyvenenna sāhasamaṁ nōḍimendu vikrānta tuṅganuttuṅga<br/>
bhujaparighaderaḍu deseyoḷaṁ tavadoṇegaḷaṁ bigidu gāṇḍīvamanēṟisi nīvi<br/>
jēvoḍedu divyāstraṅgaḷaṁ piḍidu keytīvikoṇḍagnidēvanaṁ nōḍi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
ōḍuge nimma meyya pasivānta virōdhigaḷenna keyyoḷa<br/>
ḻkāḍuge koḷḷimuṇṇimene kēḷdanalaṁ parasuttumā laya<br/>
krīḍeyoḷī carācaramumaṁ suḍuvandina meygamaggaḷaṁ<br/>
māḍi taguḷdu nīḷdu baḷedarviseparvidanā vanāntamaṁ // ViVi.5.85 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
phaḷa karpūra lavaṅga luṅga lavaḷī hintāḷa tāḷī tamā<br/>
ḷa ḷatā sundara nandanakkaḷuremuṁ tannarcigaḷabandu mo<br/>
kkaḷamettaṁ suriyuttumirpa rasamaṁ muṁ pīrdukoṇḍaṁ manaṁ<br/>
goḷe saptārci podaḷdu nīḷdosageyindāpōśanaṅgoḷvavōl // ViVi.5.86 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
nanekoneya taḷira pūvina<br/>
banamanituṁ śikhegaḷaḷure beṅkeya poydu<br/>
rvinoḷe koragirda lategaḷa<br/>
konegoneyane dahananaḷurdu konegonegoṇḍaṁ // ViVi.5.87 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgaḷā banamanindrana besadoḷ kāva kinnara kimpuruṣa garuḍa gandharva<br/>
siddha vidyādhara balamanitumondāgi vikramārjunanoḷ tāge—<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 143]<br/>
koṇḍapuduri banamanadaṁ<br/>
kaṇḍentiralakkumendu tāgida negaḻdo<br/>
ḷgaṇḍara gaṇḍōḍuvinaṁ<br/>
koṇḍuvu gāṇḍīvamukta bāṇa gaṇaṅgaḷ // ViVi.5.88 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu kāde vidviṣṭavidrāvaṇana moneyambinambēṟiṅgaḷki hatavihata<br/>
kōḷāhaḷarāgi siddharasiddharāgeyuṁ kinnararinnāra maṟeyaṁ puguvameneyuṁ kiṁ<br/>
puruṣar kāpuruṣarante bāyaṁ biḍeyuṁ gandharvar garvamanuḻidondorvaraṁ<br/>
migeyōḍeyuṁ vidyādhararadhararāgeyuṁ pannagar pannatikeyiṁ bandāntoḍe—<br/>
</p>

<p>
nāgara khaṇḍaṅgaḷanā<br/>
nāgara khaṇḍadoḷe toḍare naranisuvudumā<br/>
nāgara khaṇḍaṅgaḷumaṁ<br/>
nāgara khaṇḍamumanaḷurdukoṇḍaṁ dahanaṁ // ViVi.5.89 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
virahigaḷa suyya beṅkeyo<br/>
ḷiradoṇagiduvakkumīgaḷenalurivuriyiṁ<br/>
karimurikanāduvunmada<br/>
parabhr̥ta ṣaṭcaraṇa rājakīra kulaṅgaḷ // ViVi.5.90 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
uri koḷe desegāṇade dese<br/>
varivaridu kujaṅgaḷaṁ paḍalvaḍisi bhayaṁ<br/>
berasoḷaṟe negedudā vana<br/>
kariśarabhakiśōra kaṇṭhagarjane banadoḷ // ViVi.5.91 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
saṅgata dhūmāvaḷiyani<br/>
bhaṅgaḷe gettoḷaṟi pāydu poge puge kaṇṇaṁ<br/>
siṅgaṅgaḷaḷure garjisi<br/>
laṅgisi puḍapuḍane puḻgi sattuvu palavuṁ // ViVi.5.92 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
mattamalli kelavu latāgr̥haṅgaḷoḷaṁ dhārāgr̥haṅgaḷoḷaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 144]<br/>
oḍanaḷure kircu tōḷaṁ<br/>
saḍilisadā prāṇavallabha[r]prāṇamanaṁ<br/>
doḍagaḷedarōparōparo<br/>
ḷoḍasāyalpaḍedarinnavuṁ saypoḷavē // ViVi.5.93 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu khāṇḍava vanamellamananalaṁ praḷaya kāḷānaḷanantaḷurdukoḷe baḷasi<br/>
bandu kāva nārāyaṇana sudarśanavemba cakrada kōḷumaṁ vikramārjunana<br/>
divāstraṅgaḷa kōḷumanagnidēvana śikhā kaḷāpada kōḷumanentānuṁ bañcisi bale<br/>
paṟida kōkanantorva vanapālakaṁ pōgi dēvēndrana kaṇḍu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
dēva binnapamindu khāṇḍavamaṁ kr̥śānu taguḷdu nā<br/>
nā vidhaṁ suḍe nōḍalārade taḷtadēvara kāpināḷ<br/>
dēva kinnara pannagāvaḷi moṭṭanappinameccu koṁ<br/>
dēvarendaṟidirdanorvanagurvu parvire dēvaraṁ // ViVi.5.94 [mallikāmāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
eraḍu rathamoḷavu nōṭa<br/>
kkeraḍaṟoḷavanondu rathametōṭige palavā<br/>
gire paridu kaṇṇoḷinnuṁ<br/>
tiridapuduridapudu namma banamenitanituṁ // ViVi.5.95 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
embuduṁ pauḷōmīpati tanna divyajñānadoḷ nōḍi cakriyuṁ<br/>
vikramārjunanumappudanaṟidu gajaṟi garjisi viḷaya kāḷāmbudadante<br/>
moḻagumaṁ siḍila baḷagamanoḷakoṇḍa drōṇa mahādrōṇa puṣkaḷāvarta<br/>
suvartakaṅgaḷemba mugilgaḷaṁ besasidāgaḷavu vindhyācaḷa kūṭa kōṭigaḷe<br/>
kiḻteḻdubarpante bandu desegaḷellamaṁ musuri kaḻtalisi kavidu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
kaviduvu saptasāgara jalaṅgaḷe lōkamanīgaḷembinaṁ<br/>
kavidu mugilgaḷalli kaṟeyuttire pāvakanurkugeṭṭideṁ<br/>
tuvo todaḷāytu dānamene māruta bāṇade mēgha mālikā<br/>
nivahamaneccu kūḍe śarapañjaramaṁ paḍedaṁ guṇārṇavaṁ // ViVi.5.96 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 145]<br/>
antu puṅkhānupuṅkhamāge pāyva śarasandhānadoḷeḍevaṟiyadanteraḍuṁ<br/>
keyyoḷ tōḍuṁ bīḍuṁ kāṇalāgadantise tuṟugi kavivambina maḻeye maḻeyaṁ<br/>
māṇise divyāstraṅgaḷiṁ nūṟu yōjanadaḷaviya khāṇḍavavana mellamaṁ taṭṭi<br/>
meḍaṟi maśaka mātramappoḍaṁ misukal chidramilladantāge śarapañjaradoḷ<br/>
mucci musukidāgaḷabhinava jīmūtavāhanana divyāstrada kōḷgiralāṟade<br/>
jīmūtaṅgaḷellaṁ teraḷdōḍidoḍagnidēva nāvageya kircinantoḷagoḷagaḷurdu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
vana khaga vana mr̥ga vana taru<br/>
vanacara vana vanaja nivahamuḷḷanituṁ sī<br/>
ranitumaṇamuḻidudilleṁ<br/>
binamuṇḍaṁ dahananaḷurdu khāṇḍavavanamaṁ // ViVi.5.97 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antā vana gahanamellaṁ dahanamayamāda prastāvadoḷ vismayamāge<br/>
mayanemba dānava viśvakarmaṁ negedurivurimālegaḷaṁ gadeyoḷ bīsuttuṁ<br/>
poṟamaḍe poṟamaḍalīyade—<br/>
</p>

<p>
ondu deseyoḷ taguḷva mu<br/>
kundana karacakramondu deseyoḷ narane<br/>
ccondu śaravondu deseyoḷ<br/>
kundade dahanārci sutti muttuva padadoḷ // ViVi.5.98 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
śaraṇakkenagarikēsari<br/>
yeraḍu padāmbujamumīgaḷembudumāgaḷ<br/>
hari cakraṁ koḷḷade nara<br/>
śaramurcade dahana śikhegaḷaḷurade avanaṁ // ViVi.5.99 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgaḷ mayaṁ vismayambaṭṭu poḍavaṭṭu pōdanāgaḷā<br/>
vanāntarāḷadoḷirpa takṣakana maganappaśvasēnanemba pannagaṁ tanna tāyaṁ tanna bālamaṁ<br/>
karcelvēḻdu dahanārcigaḷiṁ barduṅki negedu pāṟuvāgaḷadaneraḻkhaṇḍamappina<br/>
mākhaṇḍaḷatanayanisuvuduṁ tanna bālamberasuriyoḷ biḻdu miḍumiḍu<br/>
miḍukutirda jananiyaṁ kaṇḍu pāvugaḷuḷḷa pageyaṁ maṟeyavembudaṁ nannimāḍi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 146]<br/>
page sāṟuvuduṁ kolleṁ<br/>
page sāṟida ninnanāra maṟeyaṁ pokkuṁ<br/>
pageyaṁ neṟapene neṟapuva<br/>
bageyoḷe pokkaṁ kaḍaṅgi karṇana doṇeyaṁ // ViVi.5.100 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antaśvasēnanardhāvalikamembamōghāstramāgi karṇana doṇeyoḷirdanitta<br/>
khāṇḍavavanadoḷage mandapālanemba munigamondu lāvagegaṁ puṭṭida nālkuṁ<br/>
lāvagegaḷagnisūktaṅgaḷanōduttumadiradidiraṁ bare mecci baravanagnidēvaṁ<br/>
bēḍikoḷḷimendoḍemmanvayakke nīn taṇṇideyāgendu bēḍuvuduṁ<br/>
tadastuvendanittalindraṁ tanna balamellamaḷkimeḷkidantādudembudaṁ kēḷdu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
maganenagendu pēḻ piḍidu kaṭṭade māṇpene pārthanaṁ dhari<br/>
trige guruvendu vajradoḷuruḷcade māṇpene cakriyaṁ karaṁ<br/>
bageyade goḍḍamāḍidarge takkudanīgaḷe māḻpenendu to<br/>
ṭṭage poṟamaṭṭanēṟi nijavāhanamaṁ divadiṁ surādhipaṁ // ViVi.5.101 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu dēvanikāyaṁ berasu yuddha sannaddhanāgi parasainya bhairavanoḷiṟivenemba<br/>
paḻuvageyoḷbhairavambāyvante bandu ninda purandaranallige sarasijasambhavaṁ<br/>
bandu mārkoṇḍu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
banamane kāyalendiṟiveyappoḍe munname pōdudandu pā<br/>
rthanoḷenagēvamemba bageyuḷḷoḍe ninnaya putranacyutaṁ<br/>
giniserde nōveyappoḍadu kūḍadu mūvaroḷorvanemma mā<br/>
tinite guṇārṇavaṅge kuḍu gellamanintide kajjadujjugaṁ // ViVi.5.102 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu kamalāsananāsedōṟi nuḍiduḷḷudane nuḍidoḍante geyvenendu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
surivaralondu beḷsariyadātma tanūbhavanuttamāṅgadoḷ<br/>
dorekoḷe nilladalli kusumaṁ kelavalluge tanna ratna vi<br/>
sphurita kirīṭamaṁ kavidu tāne naraṅge kirīṭi nāmamaṁ<br/>
sarasadināgaḷuccarisi sāhasamaṁ pogaḻdaṁ surādhipaṁ // ViVi.5.103 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 147]<br/>
antu pogaḻdu khāṇḍavana dahanadoḷāda pogeyoḷamalliya mahā<br/>
nāgaṅgaḷa viṣamberasu suyva suyya pogeyoḷaṁ kaṟaṅgi kaḻgida meyyumaṁ<br/>
pracaṇḍa gāṇḍīva vyāghātadoḷindranīlaṅgaḷanaḍasidantappa muṅgeyyumaṁ kaṇḍu<br/>
kr̥ṣṇanemba pesaraniṭṭanāgaḷ brahmaṁ brahmāyuvakkendu parasidanīśvaraṁ nīnudāra<br/>
mahēśvaranappudaṟiṁ ninagamenagamētaṟoḷaṁ vikalpamuṁ vicchinnamumillendanantu<br/>
mūdēvaruṁparasi nija nivāsaṅgaḷge pōdarāgaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
anitinitennadānta sura pannaga kinnara sainyamellamaṁ<br/>
bina moneyoḷ paḍalvaḍe latābhavanaṁ kr̥takācaḷaṅgaḷeṁ<br/>
binitumavaḻgi taḻge nuḍiyaṁ nuḍidante negaḻcalagnidē<br/>
vananamarēndra nandanamanūḍidanandanarēndranandanaṁ // ViVi.5.104 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgaḷsvāhāṅganānāthaṁ sampūrṇa manōrathanāgi khaṭvāṅganembarasana<br/>
yajñadoḷātana tanda ghr̥ta samudramaṁ kuḍidoḍāda rōgamindu pōdudendu<br/>
nīroganāgi mahānurāgamberasu parasi pōdanāgaḷirvarumindra prasthakkeyde<br/>
vandu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
idirvare dharmajaṁ berasu tannoḍavuṭṭidareyde taḷtu ka<br/>
ṭṭida guḍi raṅgavalligaḷe dāṅguḍiyantire sūse sēseyaṁ<br/>
sudatiyarikke cāmaramanaṅganeyar nijakīrti lōkamaṁ<br/>
pudidire pokkanandu nija mandiramaṁ parasainyabhairavaṁ // ViVi.5.105 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
idu vividhavibudhajanavinuta jinapadāmbhōja<br/>
varaprasādōtpanna prasannagambhīra vacana racana<br/>
catura kavitāguṇārṇava viracitamappa<br/>
vikramārjuna vijayadoḷ<br/>
pañcamāśvāsaṁ<br/>
</p>
