<p>
antu gāṇḍīvi gāṇḍīvaṁ modalāgedivya śarāsana śaradhi<br/>
vicitratanutraṅgaḷellamaṁ gellamaṁ tanagāvagaṁ koḷvante koṇḍu pagevara gaṇṭala<br/>
baḷeyanoḍedu kaḷevudananukarisuvante tīvi toṭṭa muṅgaiyya baḷegaḷanoḍedu<br/>
kaḷedu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 220]<br/>
biḍe piṇilaṁ kurudhvajini toṭṭane bāyane biṭṭudandu gaṁ<br/>
ḍuḍeyuḍe gaṇḍugeṭṭudu negaḻteya gāṇḍivamaṁ taguḷdu jē<br/>
voḍeye siḍilsiḍildu poḍevantevolāytene gaṇḍagāḍi nū<br/>
rmaḍi migilādudā rathamanēṟaloḍaṁ paḍemeccegaṇḍanā // ViVi.8.101 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
annegamatta parasainyabairavana baraviṅgaḷki gāḷigoḍḍida soḍarante naḍanaḍa<br/>
naḍuguva kurudhvajiniyaṁ kaṇḍu suyōdhanaṅge gāṅgēyanintendaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
avadhiya lekkamaṁ neṟapi nannige māṇade kādalendu baṁ<br/>
davanivanarjunaṁ toḍardu nillade nīnoḍagoṇḍu pōgu gō<br/>
nivahamanaṅgarāja kr̥pa kumbabhava pramukha pravīrareṁ<br/>
bivarverasāmpenāninisanī yeḍeyoḷ kadanatriṇētranaṁ // ViVi.8.102 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
embuduṁ suyōdhanaṁpiridumākuḷamberasugōkulamaṁ<br/>
koṇḍupōge pōgalīyaduttaranaṁ rathamaṁ cōdisendu muṭṭevandu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
page tīrguṁ bage tīrgumā kurukuḷa prakhyātanaṁ kādi to<br/>
ṭṭage gōvr̥ndamanāṁ maguḻcidapenendārdeccu tannaṅkadaṁ<br/>
bugaḷondondaṟalondulakka balamandaḻkāḍe duryōdhanaṁ<br/>
mige sōltōḍe maguḻcidaṁ tuṟugaḷaṁ vidviṣṭavidrāvaṇaṁ // ViVi.8.103 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
adaṭara cennapoṅgara sabaṅgaḷa toḻtuḻiyoḷ toḍaṅki ni<br/>
llade poṟamaṭṭutamma manadoḷ migebeccisidante tōṟuva<br/>
ggada niḍugōḍu mēḍumamaruttumiṟuṅkida keccalettame<br/>
ttida kuḍivālamandeseye karbasugaḷ parigoṇḍuvājiyoḷ // ViVi.8.104 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu tuṟuvaṁ maguḻci maguḻade tanagidiroḍḍi nindarinr̥pa<br/>
balamanaredu sadedu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 221]<br/>
paḻuvaḻiyaṁtaguḷdaḷurva bēgevolecca śarāḷigaḷ chaḻil<br/>
chaḻilene pāye pāyva bisunettara suṭṭure cāturaṅgamaṁ<br/>
kaḻakuḻamāge pēḻepesarillene pāyisi tēraneyde to<br/>
ttaḻaduḻidattu vairi balamellamanammanagandhavāraṇaṁ // ViVi.8.105 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
kurubaladoḷ karaṁ negaḻda bīrara cennara sanda cennapoṁ<br/>
gara tale tāḻapaṇ kedaṟidante nirantaramājiraṅgadoḷ<br/>
paredire lōhitāmbudhiyoḷānegaḷaṭṭegaḷāḍe nōḍala<br/>
ccariyumagurvumadbhutamumāytu raṇaṁ kadanatriṇētranā // ViVi.8.106 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgaḷadaṁ kaṇḍaṅgarājaṁ rājarājana naḍapidudumaṁ tanna ballāḷtana<br/>
mumaṁ neneduvikarṇamberasarṇavaninādadindāruttuṁ bandu guṇārṇavanoḷ<br/>
tāge—<br/>
</p>

<p>
samedudu pōgu gōgrahaṇadalliye bhāratamemba mātanaṁ<br/>
damara narōragar nuḍiye raudraśaraṅgaḷineccu yuddhadoḷ<br/>
samasamanāgi kādidoḍekarṇanavakṣamaneccu garvamaṁ<br/>
sameyisi kondanaṅkada vikarṇananonde vikarṇadiṁnaraṁ // ViVi.8.107 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu karṇana nōvumaṁ vikarṇana sāvumaṁ kaṇḍu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
takkina kumbhasambhava nadīja kr̥pa pramukha pravīrare<br/>
kkekkeyinorvarorvare bigurtiradāntu niśāta bāṇa jā<br/>
lakke siḍildu jōldu seragaṁ bagedōḍidarondu poḻtumoṁ<br/>
darkamidircalāṟade manaṅgaligaḷ kadanatriṇētranā // ViVi.8.108 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
manadoḷ karuṇisi saṁmō<br/>
hanāstradindeccu bīraraṁ bīrada śā<br/>
sanamane niṟisuva bageyiṁ<br/>
danibara paḻavigeyaneḻedukoṇḍaṁ harigaṁ // ViVi.8.109 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 222]<br/>
antuvaraśaśi viśadayaśaḥpaṭaṅgaḷaṁ nanni paṭaṅgoḷvante vividha<br/>
dhvajapaṭaṅgaḷaṁ koṇḍu gellaṅgoṇḍu tānumuttaranuṁ virāṭapurakke maguḻdu<br/>
barpāgaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
sūsuva sēse bīsuva caḷaccamarīruhamekkeyiṁ raṇā<br/>
yāsa pariśramāmbu lavamaṁ tave pīre purāṅganā mukhā<br/>
bjāsava gandhadoḷ berasidondelaroyyane tīḍe pokkanā<br/>
vāsavanantematsyamahipāḷaka mandiramaṁ guṇārṇavaṁ // ViVi.8.110 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
idu vividha vibudhajanavinuta jinapadāmbhōja<br/>
varaprasādōtpanna prasanna gambhīra vacanaracana<br/>
catura kavitāguṇārṇava viracitamappa<br/>
vikramārjuna vijayadoḷ<br/>
aṣṭamāśvāsaṁ<br/>
</p>

<p>
---------------------------------------------------------------------<br/>
[navamāśvāsaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 223]<br/>
śrīge negaḻtege vīra<br/>
śrīgāgaramappenemba kaḷa kaḷa vijayō<br/>
dyōgadoḷe negaḻvenembu<br/>
dyōgige malevanyanr̥pati maṇḍaḷamoḷavē // ViVi.9.1 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu jagajjanamaḷavana<br/>
gundaleyāgaḍare biḍade pogaḻuttire kuṁ<br/>
dēnduyaśaṁ rathadindiḻi<br/>
tandeṟagidanagrajanma padasarasijadoḷ // ViVi.9.2 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
aṟamagana pavanatanayana<br/>
neṟedāśīrvacana śatamanāntanunayadiṁ<br/>
deṟagidamaḷarumanaḻkaḻi<br/>
noṟaldu tegedappi parase nalvarakegaḷiṁ // ViVi.9.3 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
cala caladinuṟade pagevara<br/>
talegaḷanaridandu bandu pāṇḍutanūjar<br/>
taledōṟire rāgamaguṁ<br/>
daleyuṁ pompuḻiyumāytu matsyaṅgāgaḷ // ViVi.9.4 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
guḍiyaṁ kaṭṭisi poysi baddavaṇamaṁ prāṇakkamarthakkami<br/>
nneḍaṟēnētaṟoḷappudendu kuruḍaṁ kaṇbettavōl‌ rāgadiṁ<br/>
doḍeyantāṁbageduḷḷa sāra dhanamaṁ mundiṭṭati prītiyaṁ<br/>
paḍedaṁ matsyamahēśanandu manadoḷ tatpāṇḍu putrarkaḷā // ViVi.9.5 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
kēḷire kaṅkabhaṭṭane yudhiṣṭhiranā valalaṁ vr̥kōdaraṁ<br/>
bāḷeyaraṁ dalāḍipa br̥handaḷe phalguṇanaṅkadaśvagō<br/>
pāḷakarembarā nakuḷanuṁ sahadēvanumādarēṁmahī<br/>
pāḷaroḷāda kāryagatigaḷ bageyalkebahuprakāramō // ViVi.9.6 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 224]<br/>
emba purajanāḷāpaṅgaḷ negaḻe virāṭana mahādēvi sudēṣṇe<br/>
kr̥ṣṇagāgaḷeṟagi poḍevaḍe dharmatanūjaṅge virāṭanavanatamaṇimakuṭanintendu<br/>
binnapaṅgeydaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
iraduḻidāva maṇḍaladoḷaṁ nr̥pa nīṁ dayeyindamilli baṁ<br/>
dire dorevettudenna maṟevāḷvesanenna tanūjegaṅkadu<br/>
ttarege vivāha maṅgaḷamaninnabhimanyuge māḻpuduttarō<br/>
ttaramene māḍu ninna dayeyiṁ meṟeveṁ yamarājanandanā // ViVi.9.7 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
embudumantegeyveṁ nimmamma naṇpugaḷīgaḷāduvalla hiraṇya garbha<br/>
brahmariṁ taguḷdavyavacchinnamāgi banduvu ninna doreya naṇṭanumanelli paḍevenendu<br/>
virāṭanaṁ santasambaḍe nuḍidu cāṇūrāriyaṁ subhadreyumanabhimanyuvumanoḍa<br/>
goṇḍu barpudendu baḻiyanaṭṭi baravaṟidu pāṇḍavarayvaruṁ virāṭa<br/>
samētamidirvōgi kaṇḍāgaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
muraripu dharmanandana padābjayugakke marutsutādigaḷ<br/>
hari caraṇāmbujakkeṟageyutsavadindabhimanyu tammutai<br/>
vara lalitāṅghri padmanivahakkeṟaguttire tanmukhābjadoḷ<br/>
parakegaḷuṇmi poṇmiduvu paṅkajadiṁ makarandadantevōl // ViVi.9.8 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu mandaradharanuṁ tāmumondorvaranagaldiṁ baḻiyamāda<br/>
sukhaduḥkhagaḷananyōnya nivēdanaṁ geydānandadiṁ poḻalampokku majjana<br/>
bhōjanādigaḷindamapagata pariśramanaṁ māḍi murāntakananantakanandananabhimanyu<br/>
vivāhakārya paryālōcaneyoḷoḍambaḍisi śubha lagnōdayadoḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
vāridhi ghōṣadanteseva maṅgaḷa tūryaravaṅgaḷiṁ biyaṁ<br/>
mēruva ponnaṇaṁneṟeyadembinamiṭṭaḷamāge vāranā<br/>
rī ramaṇīya nr̥ttamamaruttire sanda virāṭanandu ke<br/>
ynīreṟedīye geydarabhimanyugamuttaregaṁ vivāhamaṁ // ViVi.9.9 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 225]<br/>
antā vīranaṁ vīraśrīyoḷ nerapuvantuttareyoḷ nerapi kaṁsa<br/>
dhvaṁsiyaṁ dvārāvatige kaḷipi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
malepar maṇḍaḷikar kaṟumbaradaṭar vīrarkaḷuṁ tamma bā<br/>
ḻdaleyaṁ bēḍida vastuvāhanamumaṁ mundiṭṭu mūviṭṭiyo<br/>
kkalavōliṁ besakeyye santamirutuṁ kuntīsutar tamma tō<br/>
ḷvalamaṁ naccare dāyiga‌r dhareyanāḷdaṁdaḻdarembēvadiṁ // ViVi.9.10 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu tamma pūṇda varṣāvadhi neṟedoḍamarātigaḷgantya kālaṁ<br/>
neṟeyadudarkummaḷisi namage kemmagiralāgadu duryōdhananappoḍe śvēta<br/>
kr̥ṣṇakārakaṁ kr̥ṣṇanaṁ tanage māḍadannegaṁ munname pannagaśayananaṁ namage<br/>
māḍuvuduttamapakṣamembī pradhāna kāryamaṁ tammoḷāḷōcisi<br/>
vikramārjunanaṁ nīne pōgalvēḻkumembudumapratirathaṁ rathamanēṟi manaḥ<br/>
pavana vēgadiṁ dvārāvatiyaneydi rājamandiramaṁ pokku dugdhābdhidhavaḷa<br/>
śayyātaḷadoḷ maṟedoṟagida madhumathanananettalaṇmade kāla deseyoḷusirade<br/>
kuḷḷire duryōdhananumāgaḷe bandu balibandhanana taledeseyoḷ kuḷḷire<br/>
kiṟidānuṁ bēgadiṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
pavaḍisidanantanosedu<br/>
ppavaḍisi tanneraḍumaḍiyanottuttirdā<br/>
hava vijayiyappa vijayana<br/>
ne valaṁ muṁ kaṇḍu baḻike nr̥panaṁ kaṇḍaṁ // ViVi.9.11 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
kaṇḍu tanage poḍevaṭṭirvarumaṁ parasi nīnirvaruṁ bandandamumaṁ<br/>
manevāḻteyaṁ pēḻimendoḍemmemmaṁ keykoṇḍu gelisalvēḻkumendu<br/>
bandevene—<br/>
</p>

<p>
mannaṇegenagirvarumō<br/>
rannare vijayanane munne kaṇḍudaṟindā<br/>
nennaṁ koṭṭeṁ ninagaṁ<br/>
pannagakētana caturvalaṅgaḷanitteṁ // ViVi.9.12 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 226]<br/>
endu tannoḷ samāna balanappa tanna tammaṁ kr̥tavarmanumaṁ<br/>
tannoḍanāḍigaḷappa tombattāṟu sāsira gōpakumāraroḍane kūḍi kaḷipi<br/>
vikramārjunanuṁ tānuṁ virāṭapurakke vandu majjana bhōjanādigaḷoḷ vigata<br/>
pariśramarāgi maṟudevasamaṟuvarumāṟuṅguṇaṅgaḷe mūrti mantaṅgaḷādante<br/>
mantraśāleyaṁ pokkirdāgaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
priya viṣayakāṅkṣeyindiṁ<br/>
driyaṅgaḷenteyde manamanāśrayisugumaṁ<br/>
taya naya pararayvarumā<br/>
śrayisirda‌r viṣayakāṅkṣeyiṁ muraripuvaṁ // ViVi.9.13 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
lōkakkidarthaśāstrada<br/>
ṭīkenisida tanna nuḍi manaṅgoḷise daḷa<br/>
tkōkanada jaṭharanaṁ ni<br/>
rvyākuḷamintendu dharmatanayaṁ nuḍidaṁ // ViVi.9.14 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
eḷe raseyoḷaḻdudaṁ bhuja<br/>
baḷadiṁ munnettidante viṣayāmbudhiyoḷ<br/>
muḻugirdemmayvarumaṁ<br/>
baḷihara piḍidettalendu bandai baravaṁ // ViVi.9.15 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
basiṟoḷ jagatī trayamuma<br/>
nosediṭṭōrante kāda pempina nimmī<br/>
basiṟaṁ pokkemmayvara<br/>
nasurakuḷāntaka kaḍaṅgi kāvudu piridē // ViVi.9.16 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
enna nanniya pempu ninna mahatvadindame sandudeṁ<br/>
tenna pannaga kētanaṅge dharā vibhāgamanittu saṁ<br/>
panna yōga niyōgadindamaraṇyadoḷ nelasirduṇal<br/>
bannamillade bāḻvudēṁ puḻuvānasaṅgenagakkumē // ViVi.9.17 [mallikāmāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
adalladeyumī sūḻondumoḍambaḍillade gōgrahaṇamane nevaṁ<br/>
māḍi suyōdhananemba pāpakarmana māḍidanuvaraṁ nimmanubaladoḷamari<br/>
kēsariya bhujabaladoḷamemagimbuvandudu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 227]<br/>
kādade pannaga dhvajaniḷātaḷamaṁ kuḍanānumirpuduṁ<br/>
sōdararendu nāṇci seḍedirdapenirdoḍavastubhūtaneṁ<br/>
dādame bhūtaḷaṁ paḻiye tējame keṭṭapudintidarke pa<br/>
dmōdara nīne pēḻ bagedu kajjamanīgaḷe divyacittadiṁ // ViVi.9.18 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
embudumambujōdaraṁ nayada vinayada mātu nīnendantu toṟege<br/>
nīraḍakalumādityaṅge soḍariḍalumindraṅge dēvalōkamaṁ baṇṇisuvanteyuṁ<br/>
ninagēnendu kajjaṁ bēḻvudādoḍaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
besamār koṇḍavolakkumonde nayamaṁ kēḷ ninna mundīgaḷā<br/>
nusirdappeṁ sale melpu balpanaḻiguṁ kaivāramuṁ kūḍe kū<br/>
risuguṁ nikkuvamappa kāraṇadinintī sāmamaṁ mumprayō<br/>
gisadēkeṭṭapudendu daṇḍamane muṁ muntikkuvaṁ mantriyē // ViVi.9.19 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
baliyaṁ vāmana rūpadindame valaṁ muṁ bēḍideṁ bhūri bhū<br/>
talamaṁ kundenagāyte koṇḍeniḷeyaṁ kaṭṭiṭṭeninnuṁ rasā<br/>
taladoḷ daityananante nīnumiḷeyaṁ muṁ bēḍiyaṭṭaṭṭemā<br/>
rmaledātaṁ kuḍadirdoḍandiṟiya nīṁ lōkaṁ guṇaṅgoḷvinaṁ // ViVi.9.20 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu nuḍida mandaradharana nuḍige kinisi kiṅkiṟivōgi bhīmasēna<br/>
nintendaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
nija matamanenage mīṟa<br/>
lkajāta doreyallavalladirdoḍamenniṁ<br/>
dajanisi nuḍiyisiduvahi<br/>
dhvajanōvade munne negaḻda duścaritaṅgaḷ // ViVi.9.21 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
ā lākṣāgr̥ha dāhamonde viṣasaṁyuktānnamantonde pāṁ<br/>
cālī nigrahamonde ṭakkuvageyiṁ geldirda jūdonde śā<br/>
rdūlābhīla vanaṅgaḷoḷ tiripidīyurkonde lekkaṅgoḷal<br/>
kālaṁ sālave kaṇḍumuṇḍumemaginnātaṅgaḷoḷ pāḻiyē // ViVi.9.22 [śārdūlavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 228]<br/>
jaṭamaṭisikoṇḍu nimmī<br/>
ghaṭiyisuvī sandhi kauravarkaḷoḷenniṁ<br/>
ghaṭita jarāsandhōra<br/>
staṭa sandhivolonde poḻtaṟoḷ vighaṭisadē // ViVi.9.23 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
tōḍuvenorvanoḷgaruḷanurvige nettaraneyde pīrduvi<br/>
rdāḍuvenōrvanūrugaḷanenna gadāśani ghātadinde nu<br/>
rgāḍuvenendu lōkamaṟiyuttire pūṇdenagante santasaṁ<br/>
māḍade sandhi māḍi kuruputraroḷennane jōḍumāḻpirē // ViVi.9.24 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu masagida madāndha gandhasindhuradante desege masagida vāyuputranaṁ<br/>
dharmaputraṁ santaisi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
baka kimmīra jaṭāsurōddhata jarāsandharkaḷaṁ sanda kī<br/>
cakaraṁ nūrvarumaṁ paḍalvaḍisidī tvaccaṇḍadōrdaṇḍamu<br/>
gra kurukṣmāpa mahīruhaprakaramaṁ mattēbhavikrīḍita<br/>
kke karaṁ pōlvege vandu bhīma raṇadoḷ nurgāḍadēṁ pōkumē // ViVi.9.25 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu nārāyaṇanuṁ dharmaputranuṁ vr̥kōdarana manamanāṟe<br/>
nuḍidu mattaṁ nārāyaṇaṅge yudhiṣṭhiraṁ niṣṭhita kāryamananuṣṭhisaleṁ<br/>
dintendaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
avanīnāthana geyda pollamegamennoḷpiṅgamiṁ sakkiyā<br/>
gavanīvantuṭanīyadantuṭanadaṁ ballantu kālguttinō<br/>
ḍavanī bhāgadoḷenna bhāgamanadaṁ tānīyadirdāgaḷe<br/>
nnavanī rakṣaṇa dakṣa dakṣiṇa bhujastambhaṁ kolal sāladē // ViVi.9.26 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu dharmarājaṁ rājarājanallige nirvyājadiṁ ditijakuḷa<br/>
vijayiyappajitanane dūta kāryakkaṭṭidoḍasuravijayiyuṁ katipaya<br/>
prayāṇaṅgaḷiṁ madagajēndra puramaneydi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 229]<br/>
mada gaja br̥ṁhita dhvani turaṅgama hēṣita ghōṣadoḷ poda<br/>
ḻdodave gabhīra dhīra murajadhvani yauvana mattakāminī<br/>
mr̥dupada nūpura kvaṇitadoḷ peṇedondire cakriguṇṭumā<br/>
ḍidudu poḻal surādri mathitāmbudhi jāta nināda śaṅkeyaṁ // ViVi.9.27 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu nāgapuramaniḻisuva nāgapuramanā nāgaśayanaṁ pokku viduraṁ<br/>
pāṇḍava pakṣapātiyappudaṟindātana manege vare tanagidirvanda konti<br/>
gasurāntakaneṟagi tanageṟagida viduranaṁ parasi rathadindamiḻidu maṇimaya<br/>
pīṭhadoḷ kuḷḷirdu pāṇḍutanūjara kuśalavārteyanaṟipe tadanantaraṁ<br/>
vidurana3jananēgeyva teṟanumanaṟiyade—<br/>
</p>

<p>
tīvida majjanadiṁ sa<br/>
dbhāvadinosedettidondu bōnadoḷaṁ nā<br/>
nā vidhada padepinoḷ hari<br/>
gāvagamāṟidudu patha pariśramamellaṁ // ViVi.9.28 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu viduranajananucita pratipattigaḷiṁ santasambaḍisi banda baravanāgaḷe<br/>
suyōdhanaṅgaṟipuvuduṁ rājarājanuṟade kiṟunage nakku nāḷinōlagadoḷ<br/>
tandu kāṇisembuduṁ maṟudivasaṁ nēsaṟ mūḍidāgaḷādityanantanēka maṇi<br/>
mayūkhavijr̥mbha[mā]ṇākhaṇḍaḷa viḷambitābhīḷa kōdaṇḍaviḷāsavibhrama<br/>
siṁhāsanāsīnanuṁ pramadāhastavinyastavāmakramakamaḷanumanavarata sphurita<br/>
tārakākāra muktābharaṇa kiraṇa nikara viḷasita viśālōrasthaḷanumananta sāmanta<br/>
makuṭa māṇikyamayūkha mañjarī jāḷa pallavitāsthānamaṇṭapanumāgi<br/>
sabhāmaṇṭapadoḷoḍḍōlagaṅgoṭṭeḍē vaṟiyadavaravara paḍeda pratipattigaḷa<br/>
naṟidikkida lōhāsanaṅgaḷoḷaṁ maṇikhacita kanakapīṭhaṅgaḷoḷaṁ kaṭṭida cinnada<br/>
bondarigeyoḷaṁ bhīṣma drōṇāśvatthāma kr̥pa kr̥tavarma śalya śakuni bāhlīka<br/>
sōmadatta bhagadatta bhūriśravaḥ prabhr̥tigaḷanirisi mattamanēka dēśādhīśvara<br/>
rellarumaneḍeyaṟidu kuḷḷirisi peṇḍavāsadoḷveṇḍiraneraḍōḷiyoḷamirisi<br/>
nūrvar tammandirumaṁ pintirisi lakkaṇaṁ modalāge nūrvar makkaḷumaṁ<br/>
[p. 230]<br/>
muntirisi yuvarājanappaṇuga duśyāsananumanaṅgarājanappaṇugāḷ<br/>
karṇanumaneraḍuṁ keladoḷaṁ toḍe sōṅke kuḷḷirisi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
naneyambaṁ masedannarappa palaroḷveṇḍir manaṅgoṇḍoṟa<br/>
lvinamettaṁ koḷe pāḍe jēnamaṟekoṇḍantappa gēyaṁ mana<br/>
kke nelakkiṭṭaḷamāge sanda rathikar kaṇgoḷvinaṁ tatsuyō<br/>
dhananoḍḍōlagamindranōlagamumaṁ kīḻmāḍi kaṇmoppuguṁ // ViVi.9.29 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu piridōlagaṅgoṭṭirpannegaṁ munname mūṟaneya bāgiloḷ<br/>
bandirdanantana baravaṁ paḍiyaṟaṁ binnapaṅgeyye kururājaṁ sindhutanūjana<br/>
mogamaṁ nōḍi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
lōka guru śaṅkha cakra ga<br/>
dā karanatiśaya caturbhujaṁ janajanita<br/>
vyākuḷade bandanendoḍe<br/>
lōkadoḷinnenna dorege piriyarumoḷarē // ViVi.9.30 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu tanna besanane pārdu lalāṭataṭa ghaṭita mukuḷita karakamaḷanāgirda<br/>
mahā pratihārana mogamaṁ nōḍi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
baravēḻembudumañjanācaladavōl kaṇgoppi barpambujō<br/>
daranaṁ mellane nōḍi meyyalasidantentānumeḻdirdu kē<br/>
sari pīṭhāgradinappikoṇḍu poḍevaṭṭuccāsanāsīnanā<br/>
giravēḻdarphyamanittanantarame tāṁ kuḷḷirdu duryōdhanaṁ // ViVi.9.31 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu madhukaiṭabhārātiya mogamaṁ nōḍi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
saṁsāradoḷinnennavo<br/>
lēṁ saipaṁ paḍedaroḷare nīṁ bare peṟatēṁ<br/>
kaṁsārī yuṣmatpada<br/>
pāṁsugaḷindāṁpavitra gātranenādeṁ // ViVi.9.32 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 231]<br/>
banda baravāvudidu bisa<br/>
vandaṁ besanāvudāva besanaṁ besasal<br/>
bandir baravinoḷīgaḷa<br/>
gundaleyāytenagamīgaḷembudumāgaḷ // ViVi.9.33 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
ā sabheyoḷ hari kara vi<br/>
nyāsaṅgaḷ nuḍiyanaḍakuvantire nuḍidaṁ<br/>
pāsuṁ pokkuṁ paredu sa<br/>
bhāsadanaṁ toḷagi beḷage danta prabhegaḷ // ViVi.9.34 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
aya naya parākramōpā<br/>
śrayaṅgaḷaṁ śrīgaḍarpumāḍida ninniṁ<br/>
driya jayame kūḍe lōka<br/>
trayadiṁ pogaḻisidudintu piriyarumoḷarē // ViVi.9.35 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
unnatane āgiyuṁ nuḍi<br/>
nanniyanaḷavaṇmanaṟivu vinayamanādaṁ<br/>
mannaṇe guru janamaṁ neṟe<br/>
mannisidudu piriya siriyoḷēṁ sujanateyō // ViVi.9.36 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
kuvaḷaya bāndhavanesevane<br/>
kuvaḷayamaṁ beḷagi kuvaḷayaṁ poṟagene pāṁ<br/>
ḍavare poṟagāge ninagī<br/>
kuvaḷayapatiyemba pempoḍambaḍe nr̥patī // ViVi.9.37 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
manakatadindondorvara<br/>
ninisanagaldirdirinise nimagaṁ tamagaṁ<br/>
munisuṇṭe kāyda bennīr<br/>
mane suḍadembondu nuḍiyavōl kururājā // ViVi.9.38 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
poṅguva maleparamalegaḷa<br/>
ḍaṅgaṁkaṇmaleva maṇḍalaṅgaḷ pratyaṁ<br/>
taṅgaḷenaloḷave pāṇḍava<br/>
raṁ geḍegoḷe ninage kurukuḷāmbara bhānū // ViVi.9.39 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 232]<br/>
paṭṭada modaligarājige<br/>
jaṭṭigaravarendumāḷvamunnina nelanaṁ<br/>
koṭṭu baḻiyaṭṭu ninagoḍa<br/>
vuṭṭidarā doreyarāge tīraduduṇṭē // ViVi.9.40 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
munnina nelanaṁ kuḍugema<br/>
gennar dāyigaremennarantaltinta<br/>
ltennar karuṇisi dayeyiṁ<br/>
dinnittude sālgumembarembudanembar‌ // ViVi.9.41 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
kari kaḷabha pracaṇḍa mr̥garāja kiśōra kaṭhōra ghōra hūṁ<br/>
karaṇa bhayaṅkarāṭaviyoḷinnevaraṁ nelasirda sēde nīṁ<br/>
karuṇisidāgaḷalladavargāṟadu kemmage nāḍa callava<br/>
ttara nuḍigoḷḷadir‌ ninage pāṇḍavarappudanārumapparē // ViVi.9.42 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
ondumoḍambaḍuṁ poreyumillavargembudaneyde nambi nā<br/>
ḍaṁ dayegeydu nīṁ kuḍuvinaṁ peṟatē paḍemāto paḷḷira<br/>
lkendavargīvudoḷpu nile kañci negaḻteya vāraṇāsi kā<br/>
kandi kurusthaḷaṁ[vara vr̥kasthaḷa]membivanaydu bāḍamaṁ // ViVi.9.43 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
embuduṁ suyōdhanaṁ krōdhānalōddīpita hr̥dayanāgi<br/>
śauryamadāḍambaradoḷambarambaraṁ siḍildu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
tolagade gōvugāda kiṟiyandina gōvike ninna cittadoḷ<br/>
nelasidudakkumaggaḷada vaiṣṇava mōhame ninna meyyoḷa<br/>
ggalisidudakkumā jaḍadhi saṅgatiyiṁ jaḍabuddhi buddhiyaṁ<br/>
tolagisitakkumalladoḍe nīninitaṁ nuḍivai paḷāḷamaṁ // ViVi.9.44 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
paṟipaṭṭa pagevaraṁ neṟe<br/>
paṟipaḍalaṇamīyadavaranavargaḷa bāḻoḷ<br/>
niṟisal bagedai karamena<br/>
guṟadirkume ninna pēḻda dharma śravaṇaṁ // ViVi.9.45 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 233]<br/>
bhāgamanāsevaṭṭaḷipi bēḻpudu ninnaya kalta vidde nī<br/>
nāgaḷumaṇṇa bēḍidape sajjanadantenagekka bāgenō<br/>
ḍīgaḷiḷā latāṅgi puduvallaḷadentene munna nūla tō<br/>
ḍāgade keṭṭu pōdavaraniṁ maguḻduṁ niṟipantu beḷḷanē // ViVi.9.46 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
vijigīṣutvadoḷondi gōvuḷiganappaṁ matsyanāḷāgi vā<br/>
rijanābhaṁ hariyemba doḍḍivesaraṁ pottirda nīṁ mantriyā<br/>
ge jayōdyōgamanettikoṇḍu raṇadoḷ bhūbhāgamaṁ neṭṭano<br/>
ṭṭajeyindañjisikoḷḷadirpire samantā gaṇḍarī gaṇḍaraṁ // ViVi.9.47 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
pusiyene sāmamaṁ nuḍidu bhēdamanuṇṭoḍatāge māḍi chi<br/>
drisaloḷapokku mikkunegaḻdugra virōdhigaḷettameyde baṁ<br/>
cisi poṟagaṇge saydarene tāvoḷagaṁ tave tōḍi tindu ra<br/>
kkasiyara kaṇḍa kumbaḷada māḻkevolāgire māḍadirpirē // ViVi.9.48 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
nāmellamonde garuḍiyoḷōdida mānasarevemmaṁ nimmaḍi kemmane<br/>
baḻalisalvēḍa banda baṭṭeyine bijayaṅgeyyimene murāntakanantakanante<br/>
māmasakaṁ masagi duryōdhanananintendaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
sīteya dūsaṟindaḻida rāvaṇanantire nīnumīgaḷī<br/>
sīteya dūsaṟindaḻiyalāṭisidai ninagantu sīteyē<br/>
sīte kaḍaṅgi kāydu kaḍegaṇcidaḷappoḍe dhātraniṁ toda<br/>
ḷvātinoḷēnō pāṇḍavara keyyoḷe ninna nisēkamāgadē // ViVi.9.49 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
ārkaḍukeydu pāṇḍavaroḷāntiṟiyal nerevannarintidē<br/>
tarke bigurtapai nelananoppisi tappade bāḻvenennadī<br/>
yurkinoḷentu nindu seṇasal bage bandudu ninna meyyane<br/>
ttarkudidurki sāva bageyiṁ seṇasal bage bandudāgadē // ViVi.9.50 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
muḷiyisi barduṅkalādanu<br/>
moḷane yudhiṣṭhirananamaḷaraḷavembudu bhū<br/>
vaḷaya prasiddhamarinr̥pa<br/>
baḷaṅgaḷavariṟiye peḷaṟevembarumoḷarē // ViVi.9.51 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 234]<br/>
gajegoḷe bhīmasēnanidirāntu barduṅkuva vairi bhūbhuja<br/>
dhvajinigaḷilladalladeyumī yuvarājana nettaraṁ kuru<br/>
dhvajiniye nōḍe pīrdu bhavadūruyugaṅgaḷanājiraṅgadoḷ<br/>
gijigiji māḍalendavana pūṇdudu nikkuvamāgadirkumē // ViVi.9.52 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
adalladeyuṁ rājasūya vyatikaradoḷ digvijayaṁ geydu laṅkeya<br/>
vibhīṣaṇananonde divyāstradoḷeccu kappaṅgoṇḍa vikramārjunana vikramamumaṁ<br/>
kāpina dēvarendu poḻtumagalada nūṟu yōjanadaḷaviya khāṇḍavavanamana<br/>
nalaṅgūḍidarātikāḷānaḷanaḷavumuṁ javananavayavadoḷ geldu pārvarapiḷḷeya<br/>
pōda prāṇamaṁ tanda sāhasābharaṇana sāhasamumanindrakīlanagēndradoḷindrana<br/>
besadoḷ tapōvighātaṁ māḍalendu banda purandarana gaṇikeyara kaḍegaṇṇa<br/>
nōṭakkaṁ kāṭakkamaḷkada śaucāñjanēyana śaucamumaṁ dānavādhipanappa mūka<br/>
dānava sūkarananonde sūḻambinoḷeccukonda parākramadhavaḷana parākramamumaṁ<br/>
triṇētranoḷ kādi pāśupatāstramaṁ paḍeda kadanatriṇētrana gaṇḍagarvamu<br/>
manindralōkakke pōgi dēvēndrana pagevarappa nivātakavaca kāḷakēya pauḷōma<br/>
taḷatāḷukaremba daityaraṁ paḍalvaḍisida paḍemeccegaṇḍana gaṇḍumaṁ dēvēndra<br/>
noḷardhāsanamēṟida guṇārṇavana mahimeyumaṁ caḷukya kuḷatiḷakanappa<br/>
vijayādityaṅge gōvindarājaṁ muḷiye taḷarade peṟagikki kāda śaraṇāgata<br/>
jaḷanidhiya pempumaṁ gojjiganemba sakala cakravarti besase daṇḍuvanda mahā<br/>
sāmantaraṁ maraliṟidu gelda sāmanta cūḍāmaṇiya bīramumanativartiyāgi<br/>
mārmaleva cakravartiyaṁ kiḍisi tanna nambi banda baddega dēvaṅge sakaḷa sāmrājya<br/>
manōrantu māḍi niṟisidarikēsariya tōḷvalamumaṁ samadagaja ghaṭāṭō<br/>
pamberasu nelanadirevandu tāgida kakkalana tammanappa bappuvanaṅkakāṟa nanonde<br/>
madāndhagandhasindhuradoḷōḍisida vairigajaghaṭāvighaṭananadaṭumaṁ paracakraṁ<br/>
gaḷanañjisida parasainyabhairavana mēgillada ballāḷtanamumaṁ kaṇḍuṁ kēḷduṁ ninage<br/>
seṇasalentu bage bandapudu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
neṭṭane būtugoḷva teṟadiṁ daśakandharanāḍi pāḍi nā<br/>
ṇgeṭṭire koṇḍanallade baraṅgaḷanīśvaranalli pēḻimā<br/>
voṭṭajeyinde koṇḍanenutuṁ vijayaṁ nelakikki gaṇṭalaṁ<br/>
meṭṭade koṇḍanē harana pāśupatāstramanindrakīladoḷ // ViVi.9.53 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 235]<br/>
poṅgi kaḍaṅgi bīradoḷe bīguva ninnaṇugāḷe nōḍe ni<br/>
nnaṅganeyar tovalgoḷe bhayaṅgoḷe kōḍagagaṭṭugaṭṭi ci<br/>
trāṅgadanuyye ninnaneḍemāḍadasuṅgoḷe kādi tanda vī<br/>
raṅgarigaṅge nīṁ maledu nilvudu pāḻivalaṁ suyōdhanā // ViVi.9.54 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
guruvillā karṇanillā guruvina maganillā kr̥pācāryanillā<br/>
kururājā ninna tammandiroḷinibaroḷārilla gāṅgēyanillā<br/>
maruḷē gāṇḍīviyārendeṇikega[ḷe]vegandharvaruyvandu ninnaṁ<br/>
karuviṭṭantirdudillā neredakurubalaṁ tandavaṁ pārthanallā // ViVi.9.55 [mahāsragdhare]<br/>
</p>

<p>
bavaraṅgeyvamamōghamemba bageyiṁ nīmellamādaṁ raṇō<br/>
tsavadiṁ ninneye pōda gōgrahaṇadandēnādiraṁtāparā<br/>
bhavamaṁ ciḥ maṟedirdirappoḍamadēnēvōdudinnuṁ guṇā<br/>
rṇavaniṁ nāḷeye kēḷadirpire mahā gāṇḍīva nirghōṣamaṁ // ViVi.9.56 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
suriva saral naralva bhaṭarettamuruḷva daḻaṁ poraḷva siṁ<br/>
dhura ghaṭe barpa nettara kaḍal kuṇivaṭṭegaḷājiyoḷ bhayaṁ<br/>
karataramappinaṁ pagevarokkaloḷōvenalorvarilladaṁ<br/>
tire tave kolgumantumarikēsarigāntu barduṅkalakkumē // ViVi.9.57 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu kāḷa nīḷa mēghadantu masagi garjisuvasurakuḷaviḷayakētuge<br/>
phaṇikētu muḷidutaḷamaḷisi kaṇgāṇade—<br/>
</p>

<p>
eḻpōgu dūtanappana<br/>
beḻpana nuḍigēḷdu muḷiyalāgadu nīnuṁ<br/>
meḻpaṭṭu viduranembī<br/>
toḻpuṭṭiya maneya kūḻe nuḍiyise nuḍidai // ViVi.9.58 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 236]<br/>
ene viduranati kupitamananāgi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
kaḍu muḷidu ninna toḍegaḷa<br/>
nuḍiveḍeyoḷ bhīmasēnanānā padadoḷ<br/>
piḍiyalkendirdenidaṁ<br/>
piḍiyeṁ pōgendu sabheyoḷuḍidaṁ billaṁ // ViVi.9.59 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu viduraṁ vicchidura mananāgi billanuḍivuduṁ suyōdhanaṁ tanna<br/>
balada tōḷuḍidantāgi siggāgi bāḷaṁ kiḻtodaṟi manadoḷādēvadiṁ<br/>
dēvakīnandanana mēle vāyvuduṁ nañjina mēlevāyva noḷavinanturuḷtare<br/>
pāydu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
mūṟaḍi māḍidandu nelanellamanā baligāda rūpamaṁ<br/>
tōṟadanī jagattrayamanormeye nuṅguva kālarūpamaṁ<br/>
tōṟidanante raudratara rūpamanormeye viśvarūpamaṁ<br/>
tōṟidanirdaraṁ neṟeye mōhisi vaiṣṇavadiṁ murāntakaṁ // ViVi.9.60 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgaḷ dhr̥tarāṣṭraṁ bandu mukundanananēka stuti śata sahasraṅgaḷiṁ<br/>
stutiyisidoḍātaṅge varadanāgi divya dr̥ṣṭiyaṁ dayegeydu munninante<br/>
manuṣyadēhamaṁ keykoṇḍu trailōkyaguru gurutanūjana keyyaṁ piḍidara<br/>
maneyaṁ poṟamaṭṭu kapaṭa prapañcadindātanumaṁ tanage māḍi bīḍiṅge vandu<br/>
kuntigēkāntadoḷintendaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
guru kr̥pa śalya sindhusutarappoḍe nammaya pakṣamondidaṁ<br/>
gurusutanīgaḷemmoḷakhiḷāstraviśāradanappanuṁ gela<br/>
lkariyanumondibāradanumaṅkada karṇane bīramātaniṁ<br/>
durivaridattu cāgamavanindesedattu samasta dhātriyoḷ // ViVi.9.61 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
entene vajri vajra kavacakke nijōjvaḷa kuṇḍaḷakke ke<br/>
yyāntoḍe pāṇḍuputraranekāderevandugivaṁdalendinaṁ<br/>
mantaṇadinde bāriseyumendudanennade mīṟi koṭṭanō<br/>
rantu jasakke nōntu biḍe nērdoḍaloḷ toḍardā tanutramaṁ // ViVi.9.62 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 237]<br/>
baravaṁ bēḍidargīva dēvane valaṁ nāṇgeṭṭu bandennaniṁ<br/>
teredaṁ bardaroḷāne bardanenutuṁ nērvalli kennettaruṁ<br/>
biri kaṇḍaṅgaḷe bīḻaluṇme manadondaṇmiṭṭaḷaṁ poṇme vī<br/>
rarasakkāgaramāytu nōḍe kavacaṅgoṇḍandamā karṇanā // ViVi.9.63 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu sahaja kavaca ratna kuṇḍalaṅgaḷaṁ nettar panapana paniye<br/>
tidiyugivantugidu koṭṭudarke mecci dēvēndranātaṅgamōgha śaktiyanitta<br/>
nātanaṁ nānumenna balla māḻkeyiṁ bhēdisidappeṁnīmuṁ nimma coccila<br/>
maganappa sūryasūnuvaṁ sūrya dinadandu kaṇḍu kāryasiddhiyaṁ māḍi<br/>
bannimendu kontiyaṁ bīḻkoṇḍu parakeyaṁ kaikoṇḍu rathāṅgadharaṁ<br/>
rathamanēṟi karṇana maneya mundane bandu mēle biḻdemmaṁ kiṟidantaraṁ<br/>
kaḷipi maguḻve bā pōpamendu tannoḍane rathamanēṟisikoṇḍu pōgi<br/>
mundondeḍeyoḷ nindu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
bhēdisalende dal nuḍidarennadiroyyane kēḷa karṇa ni<br/>
nnādiyoḷabbe konti ninagammanaharpati pāṇḍunandanar<br/>
sōdarareyde maydunane nāṁ peṟatēṁ paḍemāto ninnadī<br/>
mēdini paṭṭamuṁ ninate nīnire matte peṟar narēndrarē // ViVi.9.64 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
gaṅgege keyyeḍeyendu<br/>
ttuṅgastani koṭṭu pōge sūtaṁ kaṇḍā<br/>
tmāṅganege rādhegittu ma<br/>
naṅgoḷe rādheyanenisi sūtajanādai // ViVi.9.65 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
ninnutpattiyaninteṁ<br/>
dennarumaṇamaṟiyaraṟivenāṁ sahadēvaṁ<br/>
pannagakētu dinēśaṁ<br/>
ninnambike kuntiyintivar‌ neṟe ballar // ViVi.9.66 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
duryōdhanaṁ ninnanētaṟoḷ nambidanendoḍe nīnuṁ tānumorme<br/>
gaṅgānadī tīradoḷ bēṇṭeyāḍuvalli tatsamīpada tāpasāśramadoḷ<br/>
[p. 238]<br/>
satyantaparemba divya jñānigaḷaṁ kaṇḍu poḍevaṭṭirvarumaṁ parasi ninagemunnamēṟal tarisidoḍe suyōdhananēvayisi ninnaṁ pōgalvēḻdu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
ānire nīmidēke dayegeydiro mīṅguligaṅge pēḻimeṁ<br/>
dā naranāthanaṁ tiḷipe tanmuni bhūbhujaneyde nambi kā<br/>
nīna samantu pāṭisuvenoyyane muḷḷoḷe muḷḷanendu tā<br/>
nī nayadinda perciporedaḻkaṟoḷandoḍanuṇḍanallanē // ViVi.9.67 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
eneyene bāṣpavāri puḷakamberasormeye poṇme munne nī<br/>
venagidanēke pēḻdironegaḻte pogaḻteyanāmpinaṁ suyō<br/>
dhananenagoḷḷikeyda kr̥tamaṁ peṟagikki negaḻte māse na<br/>
ṇpina nevadinde pāṇḍavaranānoḷavokkoḍe nīme pēsirē // ViVi.9.68 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
nettamanāḍi bhānumati sōltoḍe sōlamanīvudendu kā<br/>
ḍuttire[lambaṇaṁ paṟiye muttina]kēḍane nōḍi nōḍi ba<br/>
ḷkuttireyēvamilladivanāyvudo tappade pēḻimemba bhū<br/>
pōttamanaṁ bisuṭṭirade nimmoḷe pokkoḍe bēḍanallanē // ViVi.9.69 [utpalamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
embuduṁ karṇaṁ tanagentumoḍambaḍadudaṁ nirṇayamāgaṟidu<br/>
maguḻalvēḻdu nārāyaṇaṁ pōdanittalaṅgarājanumātmālayakke vandu<br/>
cintākrāntanāgi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
kurupatigilla daivabalamājige mēlmalegeyvarāgaḷuṁ<br/>
guru guruputra sindhusutarāḷdanumennane nacci perci muṁ<br/>
poredanidirci kāduvarumennaya sōdararentu nōḍi ko<br/>
kkarisade kolvenennoḍalanāṁ tavipeṁ raṇaraṅga bhūmiyoḷ // ViVi.9.70 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
aṟideṁ sōdararendu pāṇḍavaraninnentennaraṁ kolvena<br/>
ḻkaṟoḷennaṁ poredeyde nambida nr̥paṅgentājiyoḷ tappuveṁ<br/>
taṟisanduddhata vairi bhūpa baladoḍḍaḷḷāḍe lekkakke ta<br/>
ḷtiṟidennāḷdanināne muñce niṟipeṁ keykoṇḍu kaṭṭāyamaṁ // ViVi.9.71 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 239]<br/>
endu muntappa kajjamaṁ tannoḷe bagedavāryavīryaṁ sūrya<br/>
dinadandu mandākiniyaṁ mīyalendu bandu duryōdhananaṭṭida dēvasavaḷada<br/>
padineṇṭu kōṭi ponnumanoṭṭi beṭṭāge puñjisi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
sōrva vasudhāreyaṁ ke<br/>
ysārva nidhānamumaniḻisi tannīvaḷaviṁ<br/>
pārvaṅgamaḷipi bēḍida<br/>
pārvaṅgaṁ piridanittanaṅgamahīśaṁ // ViVi.9.72 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu cāgaṅgeydu jaganmaṅgaḷa gaṅgāvāriyoḷanivārita parākrama<br/>
naghamarṣaṇa pūrvakaṁ mindu kanakapātradoḷ tekkane tīvida kanakakamaḷaṅga<br/>
ḷindādityatējanādityaṅgarghyametti sūryajaṁ sūryamantraṅgaḷanōdi nīraṁ<br/>
sūsi triḥpradakṣiṇaṁ geyvāgaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
saṅgata taraṅgayuteyaṁ<br/>
maṅgaḷa lakṣaṇeyanandu bhōṅkane kaṇḍaṁ<br/>
gaṅgāṅganeyaṁ kāṇbavo<br/>
laṅganr̥paṁ munde ninda kontiyanāgaḷ // ViVi.9.73 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu kaṇḍu manadoḷādeṟakadiṁ sāṣṭāṅgameṟagi poḍevaṭṭa nija<br/>
nandanananaḻkaṟindappikoṇḍu paramāśīrvacanaṅgaḷiṁ parasi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
toredakucayugaḷavandaṁ<br/>
biriviḍe molevālanaḻkaṟindaṁ meyyaṁ<br/>
kurise surivaśrujalamu<br/>
bbarisi ponal ponalanaṭṭe jananutegāgaḷ // ViVi.9.74 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgaḷe maganaṁ pettavo<br/>
lāgi latālalite nosala kaṇbettavolaṁ<br/>
tāgaḍe rāgakkāgara<br/>
māge dinādhipa tanūjanosedirpinegaṁ // ViVi.9.75 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 240]<br/>
gaṅgādēviyuṁ divyamūrtiyaṁ keykoṇḍu bandu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
oppisideṁ keyyaḍeyeṁ<br/>
dappaisida ninna magananīgaḷe ninageṁ<br/>
dappaisi gaṅge pōpudu<br/>
moppuva nija bimbadoḷagaṇindaṁ dinapaṁ // ViVi.9.76 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
poṟamaṭṭu baral tannaḍi<br/>
geṟagida nija sutananaḻkaṟiṁ parasi manaṁ<br/>
maṟugi ravi nuḍidanennuma<br/>
nuṟade maruḷmagane harige kavacamanittai // ViVi.9.77 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
nuḍiyenidaṁ ninnambike<br/>
paḍemātēṁ konti hariya matadiṁ kāya<br/>
lkoḍarisi bandaḷ sutaraṁ<br/>
kuḍadir purigaṇeyanenitu lallaisidoḍaṁ // ViVi.9.78 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endaravinda priya sakha<br/>
nandambarataḷamanaḍarvuduṁ keymugidiṁ<br/>
tendaṁ kuntiyanabbēṁ<br/>
vandirpudadenage saypu barpantīgaḷ // ViVi.9.79 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
calamuṁ cāgamumaḷavuṁ<br/>
kalitanamuṁ kulamumīgaḷennaya meyyoḷ<br/>
nelasiduvu nimma karuṇā<br/>
baladiṁ nīvennanindu maganendudaṟiṁ // ViVi.9.80 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
paḍedar‌ tāyuṁ tandeyu<br/>
moḍalaṁ prāṇamumanavaravavu keyyeḍeyaṁ<br/>
kuḍuvudaridāyte nīmena<br/>
geḍe maḍagade besapa toḻtuvesanaṁ besasiṁ // ViVi.9.80 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
embudumambike magane ma<br/>
nambeḷaṟade nīnumitteyānuṁ petteṁ<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 241]<br/>
nambida ninnanujar ni<br/>
nnaṁbesakeye nīne nelananāḷvudu kandā // ViVi.9.81 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
ninagapparasaṁ duryō<br/>
dhananolavaṁ mundugeydubesakeyvare ni<br/>
nnanujareraḻdesegaṁ kisu<br/>
ṟinisāgadu magane nīnoḍambaḍavēḻkuṁ // ViVi.9.83 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
embudumadellamaṁ kēḷdu karṇaṁ muguḷnage nakku—<br/>
</p>

<p>
bhayamaṁ lōbhamumemba tammuteraḍuṁ pāpakke pakkāge pā<br/>
ḻiyanokkāḷdana geyda satkr̥tamumaṁ pintikki jōḷakke ta<br/>
ppiyumiṁ bāḻvude pūṇdu nilladikeyiṁ bāḻvantu vikhyāta kī<br/>
rtiyavōlīyoḍalabbe pēḻimenagēṁkalpāntarasthāyiyē // ViVi.9.84 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
mīṅguliganenāgiyumaṇa<br/>
māṁ guṇamane bisuṭenilla nimagaṁ maganā<br/>
daṅgenage bisuḍalakkume<br/>
nīṁ gaḷa pambalane bisuḍiminnenneḍeyoḷ // ViVi.9.85 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
embuduṁ konti bhōṅkanerdedeṟedu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
aṟideṁ neṭṭane beṭṭanintu nuḍivai nīṁ kanda pōginde ka<br/>
ṭṭaḻidattāgade sōmavaṁśamenagiṁ bāḻvāseyallitto bi<br/>
ṭṭuḻideṁ mattina makkaḷāseyumanāneṁdaḷgeśōkāgni poṁ<br/>
puḻivōguttire karṇanendaninitēṁ pēḻabbe cintāntaraṁ // ViVi.9.86 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
piḍiyeṁ purigaṇeyaṁ nara<br/>
neḍegoṁḍoḍamuḻida ninna makkaḷaninnē<br/>
rdoḍamaḻiyeṁ perjasamane<br/>
piḍidennane raṇadoḷaḻiveniradaḍiyettiṁ // ViVi.9.87 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 242]<br/>
endu kontiyaṁ visarjisi calada cāgada kulada nanniyanāvarjisi<br/>
rādhēyanoḷpiṅgādhēyamāgirdanitta puruṣōttamanuṁ katipaya prayāṇaṅgaḷiṁ<br/>
virāṭapura nikaṭavartiyappa divijāpagātaṭadupavanadoḷarinr̥pavanakkupadrava<br/>
kāriyāgi nelaṁ mūriviṭṭante biṭṭirdajātaśatruvanavanatōttamāṅganāgi<br/>
kaṇḍu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
himakr̥dvaṁśajarappa pāṇḍusutaraṁ keykoṇḍu ninnaydu bā<br/>
ḍamanittuṁ naḍapendu sāmamane muṁ muntiṭṭoḍātaṁ parā<br/>
kramamaṁ tōṟi siḍildu pāyvudumasuṅgoḷvannegaṁ viśva rū<br/>
pamanāṁ tōṟideniṁ kaḍaṅgi raṇadoḷ nīṁ tōṟu ninnārpumaṁ // ViVi.9.88 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
embannegaṁ duryōdhananaṭṭida dūtaṁ sañjayanembaṁ bandu sakala<br/>
sāmanta maṇimakuṭamarīci masr̥ṇita caraṇāravindanappa dharmanandananaṁ kaṇḍu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
aṭṭida nimma pergaḍe barduṅkidanembudanindrajālamaṁ<br/>
toṭṭane tōṟi bandu bardukāḍidaninnaḷipindavaṭṭuva<br/>
ṭṭaṭṭigaḷaṁ bisuḻpudemagaṁ tamagaṁ muḷisindamīgaḷa<br/>
ṭṭaṭṭigaḷappuvendidane dal nuḍidaṭṭidanemma bhūbhujaṁ // ViVi.9.89 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
baḷa sampannaranāsegeyge caturaṅgānīkamaṁ kūḍi ko<br/>
ḷguḷamaṁ gaṇḍumanappukeyge manamamballittu māḻkendumā<br/>
neḷeyaṁ kādidoḍalladīyenaṟidirkendā kurukṣētramaṁ<br/>
kaḷavēḻdaṭṭidanaṇmi sāyimuḻiyiṁ nimmondu bāḻvāseyaṁ // ViVi.9.90 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
embuduṁ vr̥kōdaraṁ muḷidāsphōṭisi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
visasana raṅgamappudenagaṁ tanagaṁ dore kāypumēvamuṁ<br/>
pasarisi parvi tannoḷamadennoḷamirdudu bhīmanendoḍā<br/>
pesarane kēḷdu sairisada ninnarasaṁ kaliyāgi nāḷe sai<br/>
risugume vairibhūpa rudhirārdra madīya gadābhighātamaṁ // ViVi.9.91 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
embuduṁ parākramadhavaḷanintendaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 243]<br/>
kaṟupuṁ kāypumanuṇṭumāḍi nelanaṁ duryōdhanaṁ tāgi ta<br/>
ḷtiṟidandallade kūḍanāji bharamuṁ sārcittadēnendu mu<br/>
nnaṟudiṅgaḷ jaṟucuttumirpude raṇakkārennarendīgaḷeṁ<br/>
taṟiyal barkume barke bandoḍaṟiyalkakkuṁ kurukṣētradoḷ // ViVi.9.92 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
embuduṁ yamanandananintendaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
eḷeyaṁ duryōdhanaṁ taḷtiṟiyade kuḍenendaṭṭi kādalkamīgaḷ<br/>
kaḷanaṁ pēḻdaṁ kurukṣētramanene taḍavinnāvudugrājiyoḷ dō<br/>
rvaḷadindaṁ tanna meccaṁ salisiye nelanaṁ koḷveniṁ taḷvenemmoḷ<br/>
kaḷa[na]ṁbēḍeyde kēḷdeṁ bageyanaṟiyalāytēḻimantende pēḻiṁ // ViVi.9.93 [mahāsragdhare]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endajātaśatru śatru pakṣa kṣayaṁ māḍuvudyōgamanettikoṇḍu<br/>
prayāṇabhēriyaṁ poysidāgaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
deseyaṁ potta madēbha rāji desegeṭṭōḍaltaguḷdattu sa<br/>
pta samudraṁ karegaṇmi tannavadhiyaṁ dāṇṭittajāṇḍaṁ siḍi<br/>
ldu siḍilpoydoḍedondutattiyavolāytembondu sandēhamaṁ<br/>
posataṁ bhū bhuvanakke māḍidudu tatsannāha bhērīravaṁ // ViVi.9.94 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
karigaḷ bhr̥ṅga kuḷākuḷīkr̥ta kaṭōpētaṅgaḷombattu sā<br/>
siramantondu gajakke nūṟu rathamantāsyandanakkondaṟoḷ<br/>
turagaṁ nūṟanituṁ turaṅga daḷamondondarke nūṟāḷ tagu<br/>
ḷdire ballar naḍe nōḍi kūḍe paḍedattakṣōhiṇī saṅkhyeyaṁ // ViVi.9.95 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu māḍida parisaṅkhyeyoḷondakkōhiṇī balamberasu tale<br/>
baḻivaḻiyendabhimanyuge kūsaṁ koṭṭa jaṭṭigaṁ virāṭaṁ śvētanuttaraṁ śaṅkhanemba<br/>
mūvar makkaḷuṁ śatānīka śatadyumna śatacandraṁ modalāgi pannorvar<br/>
tammandirumberasu nelanadire muṅgōḷoḷ naḍeye draupadiyakoṭṭa<br/>
naṇpumaṁ drōṇanoḷāda paribhavamumaṁ nenedondakṣōhiṇī balamberasu<br/>
[p. 244]<br/>
drupadaṁ dhr̥ṣṭadyumna śikhaṇḍi cēkitāna yudhāmanyūttamaujaḥ purukutsu<br/>
vicitrādigaḷappa tanna makkaḷverasu nelaṁ mūriviṭṭante balavakkadoḷ naḍeye<br/>
subhadreyakoṭṭa naṇpiṅganubalamāgi puṇḍarīkākṣana tammaṁ sātyaki vr̥ṣṇi<br/>
kāmbhōja kuḷatiḷakarappa yādavara kuladoḍaneyakṣōhiṇīpatināyakaṁ<br/>
bhūpatiyeḍavakkadoḷ naḍeye kēkaya viṣayādhīśvararappa kaikayarayvaru<br/>
mondakṣōhiṇī baladoḍane siḍilanuruḷi māḍidantu piṅgōḷoḷ naḍeye<br/>
pāṇḍyaṁ śrījayasōmakaroḍanondakṣōhiṇī balamberasu suttiṟidu baḷasi<br/>
bare dharaṇīndrana taṅgeyappakanakalategaṁ vikramārjunaṅgaṁ puṭṭida<br/>
maganiḷāvantanananta nāgarāja balamberasu nāgalōkame kiḻteḻdubarpante bare<br/>
hiḍimbegaṁ bhīmaṅgaṁ puṭṭida maga ghaṭōtkacanaṟuvatteṇṭu kōṭi rākṣasa<br/>
balamberasu bare sāmantacūḍāmaṇiya kr̥tōpakāramaṁ nenadaṅgada parṇanemba<br/>
gandharvaṁ sāmantacūḍāmaṇiya kr̥tōpakāramaṁ nenadaṅgadaparṇanemba<br/>
gandharvaṁ nālku kōṭi gandharva balamumaṟuvattu sāsira giḷiyabaṇṇada<br/>
kuduregaḷuṁ berasu gandharvalōkame kiḻteḻdu barpante bare mahā pracaṇḍaruṁ<br/>
pratāpigaḷumappapañcapāṇḍavarumaṅkadabhimanyuvuṁ kela keladoḷōlagi suttuṁ<br/>
bare kontiya māvanappa kontibhōjanuṁ sōmakaṁ berasondakṣōhiṇī<br/>
balamberasu bare mattaṁ prabhadraikabalamumaṅga vaṅga kaḷiṅga koṅga koṅkaṇa<br/>
golla kāmbhōja magadha saurāṣṭra varāṭa lāṭa karṇāṭa karahāṭa maḷaya māḷava<br/>
nēpāḷapārivapāriyātra barbara kōsaḷa kāśi kāśmīra kauśikāndhra draviḷa<br/>
gajamukhāśvamukhōṣṭramukha kharamukha mēṣamukha lambakarṇa hastikarṇāśva<br/>
karṇa turuṣka pravara nānādvīpa dēśādhīśvararuṁ pagegaṁ pāḻigaṁ paribhavakkaṁ<br/>
paḻavegaṁ pāguḍakkaṁ paḷabaddhakkaṁ vaivāhika sambandhakkaṁ maitrakkaṁ mēregaṁ<br/>
aṭṭaṭṭigaṁ svāmi bhr̥tya sambandhakkaṁ dōrvalakkaṁ maimegaṁ mōkṣakkaṁ mahā<br/>
samudradoḷ mahā nadigaḷ kūḍuvantēḻakṣōhiṇī balaṁ kūḍi naḍeye tanna<br/>
nālvar‌ tammandiroḍane maṅgaḷavasadanaṅgoṇḍu maṅgaḷa pradhānōcita vijaya<br/>
gajamanēṟi vidyōtamāgi dakṣiṇāvartamappa hōmāgniyaṁ balaṅgoṇḍu<br/>
balada kōḍa mēle keyyaṁ pēṟi mukhavikṣēpaṇaṅgeydu ghanāghana ninādadiṁ<br/>
br̥ṁhitaṅgeyva vijayagajamuṁ nelanaṁ pokkaḍaṅgida pagevaranaguḻdu<br/>
[p. 245]<br/>
kolvudanudāharisuvante dakṣiṇa caraṇadoḷ nelanaṁparaḍigambhīra ninādadiṁ<br/>
hēṣitaṅgeyva vijayahayamuṁ vijayana vijayamane sūcise—<br/>
</p>

<p>
esagittandanukūla mandapavanaṁ peṇdumbigaḷ muttutuṁ<br/>
musuṟuttuṁ bare bandudindravanadiṁ pūdandalambōdhi ga<br/>
rjisuvantādudu dēva dundubhi jaya prārambhamaṁ sāṟuvaṁ<br/>
tesedattaccariyappinaṁ jaya jaya dhvānaṁ digantaṅgaḷoḷ // ViVi.9.96 [maṅgaḷavr̥ttaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
ā prastāvadoḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
vātyādurdhara gandhasindhurakaṭasrōtassamudyanmada<br/>
vrātēndindira caṇḍa tāṇḍava kala svābhāvika śrēyasaḥ<br/>
kiñcākasmika pāṁsu pallava jaḷasyandī sadā sindhura<br/>
prāgēyaṁ priyagaḷḷabhūpati camū prasthānamācakṣatē // ViVi.9.97 [śārdūlavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
emba maṅgaḷapāṭhakara maṅgaḷa vr̥ttōccāraṇegaḷeseye dharma putraṁ<br/>
kurukṣētrābhimukhanādāgaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
dhvajamayamambaraṁ gajamayaṁ bhuvanaṁ praḷaya pracaṇḍa bhū<br/>
bhujamayamaṣṭadigvaḷayamaśvamayaṁ jagatītaḷaṁ ratha<br/>
vrajamayamuṁ padātimayamuṁ neṟeyādudukāḍu kōḍumār<br/>
trijagadoḷāmparī balamaninnenisittu caturbalārṇavaṁ // ViVi.9.98 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
eṇikegaḷumbamuṁ piridumāda padāti varūtha vāji vā<br/>
raṇa baladindamirmaḍise dhātriya biṇpenagendinandava<br/>
ltaṇakamidendu kaṇ tumuḻe perbeḍeyiṁ maṇi sūse bēsaṟiṁ<br/>
tiṇukidanānalummaḷisi śēṣanaśēṣa mahīvibhāgamaṁ // ViVi.9.99 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
ēṟida ponna paṇṇugeya perviḍi kaṭṭidirāge munde baṁ<br/>
dēṟida cennagannaḍiya cēṭike bīsuva kuñcameyde me<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 246]<br/>
ydōṟuva gāḍi kāñcanada daṇḍada sīguri nōḻpoḍārumaṁ<br/>
māṟe manōjanoḍḍenisidar naḍetanda narēndra kānteyar // ViVi.9.100 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu tiruviṁ barduṅkida<br/>
kantuvananegaṇegaḷantevōl naḍetandar‌<br/>
santasade ponna kaḷasada<br/>
dantada sivigegaḷanēṟi bhōgiyararebar // ViVi.9.101 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
naḍeye turagaṁ ponnāyōgaṅgaḷindamardaḻtiyiṁ<br/>
paḍeye neḻalaṁ cañcatpiñchātapatramekūḍe ta<br/>
mmoḍane bare bandettaṁ patteṇṭu dēseviḷāsadoḷ<br/>
toḍare caritaṁ bandar kaṇgoppiral vara bhōgiyar‌ // ViVi.9.102 [hariṇīplutaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
saḍahuḍanappa kaḻtekoḍesantasadiṁ peṟagēṟi barpa ka<br/>
nnaḍiviḍidāke cinnada savaṅgamapūrvada mocceyaṁ pava<br/>
ṇbaḍeda suvarṇa pārivada kuppasamoppe beḍaṅganāḷdu ka<br/>
ṇgeḍaṟade peṇḍavāsada viḷāsada sūḷeyaroppi tōṟidar // ViVi.9.103 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
naḍeyalbandiṟiyalke takka turaṅgaṁ bhōrendu barpondoḍaṁ<br/>
baḍu bandettisidondu sattige karaṁ meyvettumuyvāgamā<br/>
gaḍumārgaṁ kuḍutirpa kappurada bambaldambulaṁ rāgamaṁ<br/>
paḍegellaṁ paḍevannegaṁ naḍedarandettaṁ kela‌r nāyakar // ViVi.9.104 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
mattaṁ sasambhrama pracaḷita samada gaja ghaṭā ghaṇṭāravaṅgaḷindaṁ<br/>
turaṅgama hēṣitaṅgaḷindaṁ mahā sāmantara padira[pa]ṟegaḷindamagurvāge<br/>
naḍeva bīḍiṅge bīḍuviḍal nelanumolegalgaḷge beṭṭugaḷuṁ guḍiya gūṇṭakke<br/>
ballaḍavigaḷuṁ daṇḍigege vēṇu vanaṅgaḷumānegambakke permaraṅgaḷumā paḍege<br/>
neṟeyavenisi pāṇḍavarēḻakṣōhiṇī balamberasēḻuṁ samudraṅgaḷuṁ mēredappi<br/>
barpantire bandu kaḍitamikkidantirda samacaturaśraṁ nālvatteṇgāvudupari<br/>
pramāṇamenipa kurukṣētramaneydevandadaṟa paścima diśā bhāgadoḷ munne<br/>
paraśurāmanīlōkadoḷuḷḷarasumakkaḷḷellarumanirpattondusūḻvaraṁ pēḻe<br/>
[p. 247]<br/>
pesarilladante kondu tandeya pagegendalliye tandu nija niśita paraśudhāregaḷiṁ<br/>
nettar sūsi pāye kaḍidavara nettara dhāreyoḷ tīvi tanna tāyaṁ nīriḻipaluṁ<br/>
tānuṁ mindu tanna tandege nīrguḍalumendu māḍida śamanta pañcakaṅgaḷembaydu<br/>
permaḍugaḷa keladoḷeḍeyaṟidu bīḍaṁ biḍisi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
vīrakṣētramagurvigaṅkada kurukṣētraṁ balastharmahā<br/>
krūrārātigaḷennadōrvaladagurvindaṁ trilōkakke saṁ<br/>
hāraṁ māḍida bhairava prabhuvinondākāradiṁ vairi saṁ<br/>
hāraṁ māḍade māṇenendu harigaṁ keykoṇḍanutsāhamaṁ // ViVi.9.105 [śārdūlavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
idu vividha vibudha jana vinuta jina padāmbhōja<br/>
varaprasādōtpanna prasanna gambhīra vacana racana<br/>
catura kavitā guṇārṇava viracitamappa<br/>
vikramārjuna vijayadoḷ<br/>
navamāśvāsaṁ<br/>
</p>

<p>

paḍeyoḷ gaṇḍanumā molaṁ drupadanuṁpēroṭṭeyā matsyanuṁ<br/>

<p>
embuduṁ kumbhasambhavanintendaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>

rvaḷa cāturvaḷa tatsuhr̥dbaḷamaninnēgēḷdapai pāṇḍavar<br/>
baḷa sampannarudagra daivabaḷa sampannar maruḷmātani<br/>

</p>

<p>
embudumā mātaṁ manadēgoṇḍantegeyvenendanibarumaṁ visarjisi<br/>
niśāsamayadoḷ patteṇṭu keydīvigegaḷa beḷaginoḷaṁkatipaya parijana<br/>
[p. 249]<br/>
parivr̥tanāgi rājarājaṁ sindhujanaramanegevandu vāhanadindamiḻidu<br/>

mahā prasādamintirpenendu maṇimayahēmāsanadoḷ kuḷḷirdanaṁ nōḍi<br/>
kajjaṁ puṭṭidoḍemage baḻiyaṭṭadīpoḻtidāvudu manavāḻtegeḻtandeyeṁ doḍe<br/>
suyōdhananintendaṁ—<br/>

<p>
hari baladiṁ pāṇḍavaranu<br/>

<p>

<p>

<p>
koraloḷ kaṭṭida dēviyantiruradoḷ śrī toṭṭiloḷ toṭṭanaṁ<br/>

<p>
endu nuḍida tanna mommana nayada vinayada nuḍigaḷge karuṇisi<br/>
kuruvr̥ddhanintendaṁ—<br/>

<p>
[p. 250]<br/>
dhr̥tarāṣṭraṁ nuḍidārtane hari bharaṅgeydārtanē nīṁ pr̥thā<br/>

ṭutanaṁ kaigaḻivāytadappoḍe mahābhārāvatāraṁ raṇō<br/>

</p>

<p>

<p>
aṇiyaramodavida muḷisino<br/>
ḷaṇamuṟadavarendu raṇade jayisal nārā<br/>

<p>
ennane naccidananuvara<br/>

nennaya makkaḷoḷamenna mommakkaḷoḷaṁ // ViVi.10.12 [kandaṁ]<br/>

<p>
makkaḷa mommakkaḷa ratha<br/>
mekkeyineḍegoṇḍoḍavaranōvade raṇadoḷ<br/>

<p>
endu tannoḷ bageyuttirpinamatta duryōdhanaṁ sahasra<br/>

baḻiyanaṭṭi barisi maṇimaya pīṭhadoḷ kuḷḷirisi dēvāsura yuddhadoḷ<br/>

<p>

</p>

<p>
[p. 251]<br/>
tnaṅgaḷumaṁ puduṅgoḷisi poṅgaḷasaṅgaḷoḷirda puṇyatō<br/>
yaṅgaḷoḷaḻkaṟiṁ misisi kaṭṭidanā vibhu vīrapaṭṭamaṁ // ViVi.10.15 [utpalamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu paraśurāmananañjisida vīraṅge vīrapaṭṭamaṁ kaṭṭi pagevaranenna<br/>

<p>

<p>

ṇgeṭṭa mudupaṅge pagevara<br/>
niṭṭelvaṁ muṟivoḍenage paṭṭaṅgaṭṭā // ViVi.10.17 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
ādiyoḷavaraṁ piridoṁ<br/>
dādaradiṁ naḍapidajjarappudaṟindaṁ<br/>

<p>

</p>

<p>

<p>
piḍiyeṁ cakramanemba cakriyaniḷācakraṁ bhayaṅgoḷvinaṁ<br/>
piḍiyippeṁ karacakramaṁ nara rathaṁ tūḷdā kurukṣētradiṁ<br/>

<p>

<p>
keḍedaṁ padmajanāsanāmburuhadindāgaḷ surēndrācaḷaṁ<br/>

mr̥ḍanaṁ gauri samastamī tribhuvanaṁ paṅkēja patrāmbuvōl<br/>

<p>
antu moḻaguva bhērī ravadoḍane nelaṁ moḻageyuṁ taḷtettida vicitra<br/>

varṣasuriyeyuṁ hita purōhita jaya jaya dhvanigaḷoḍane hāhākrandana<br/>
dhvanigaḷanimittamākāśadoḷ negaḻeyuṁ kāduvenendu negaḻe nuḍida nuḍiyumaṁ<br/>
piḍida calamumaṁ bagedu seragaṁ beragumaṁ bageyade maṅgaḷābharaṇadoḷ<br/>
neṟeye keygeydu muttina māṇikada maṇḍanāyōgaṅgaḷoḷāyōgaṅgoṇḍu<br/>
banda madāndha gandhasindhuramappa paṭṭavardhanada beṅgavāydu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
nayamanayaṁ jayamenagapa<br/>
jayavidu yaśamayaśamembidaṁ bageyade ni<br/>
ścayisi kalahamane manadoḷ<br/>
bhayamaṟiyada kali suyōdhanaṁ poṟamaṭṭaṁ // ViVi.10.27 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu poṟamaṭṭu munde pariva dhavaḷacchatra cāmaraṅgaḷuṁ miḷirva<br/>
pāḷikētanaṅgaḷuṁ poyva pañcamahāśabdaṅgaḷuṁ tanage rājarāja śabdamananvarthaṁ<br/>
māḍe jayadratha jayatsēna sudakṣiṇa śalyaśakuni dhr̥ṣṭakētu nīḷa bhagadatta<br/>
śrutāyudha niyatāyudhācyutāyu[dhā]digaḷappa pannondakṣōhiṇīpatigaḷuṁ<br/>
gāṅgēya drōṇāśvatthāma kr̥pakr̥tavarma prabhr̥tigaḷuṁ karṇa vr̥ṣasēna<br/>
citrasēnaremba tande makkaḷ mūvaruṁ berasu bare bāhlika bhūriśravassō<br/>
madattaremba mūvarumananta balamberasu kūḍibareyavanti dēśādhīśvararappa<br/>
vindānuvindareṇbattunālsāsira madadāneverasu bandu kūḍe kaḷiṅgarājaṁ<br/>
kṣēmadhūrtiyuṁ bhīmasēnana keyyoḷ satta bakāsura jaṭāsurara makkaḷ<br/>
[p. 254]<br/>
catustriṁśatsahasra naktañcara parivr̥tahaḷambhūṣa musalāyudha kāḷa nīḷa<br/>
vidyunmālyādigaḷuṁ bandu kūḍe trigartādhīśaṁ suśarmanuṁ saṁsaptakar<br/>
padineṇṭu kōṭi rathaṁ berasu bandu kūḍe mattamanēka dēśādhīśvararuṁ bare<br/>
yuyutsu duśyāsana citrasēna dussaha dussaḷa vindānuvinda durdharṣaṇa<br/>
durmarṣaṇa dussparśana subāhu durmukha duṣkarṇa vikarṇa viviṁśati<br/>
sulōcana citrōpacitra nandōpananda citrāṅgada citrakuṇḍala jarāsandha<br/>
satyasandha suhasta dr̥ḍhahasta pramāthi dīrghabāhu mahābāhugaḷ modalāge<br/>
tanna nūrvar tammandiruṁ lakkaṇaṁ modalāge nūrvar makkaḷuṁ suttiṟidu<br/>
baḷasi bare viḷayakāḷa vātāhatiyiṁ jaḷanidhiye taḷarvante taḷardu kurukṣētrakke<br/>
mogasidāgaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
kari makaraṅgaḷaṁ kari ghaṭāvaḷiyabda kuḷaṅgaḷaṁ bhayaṁ<br/>
karataramāda perderegaḷaṁ haya santati matsya kōṭiyaṁ<br/>
sphurita niśāta hētiyuta sadbhaṭa kōṭi nirantaraṁ tira<br/>
skarisire pūrṇitārṇavamanottarisittu caturbalārṇavaṁ // ViVi.10.28 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
madavaddhanti varūtha vāji bhaṭa saṅghātaṅgaḷī lekkameṁ<br/>
budanāṁ niṭṭisalāṟenondanaṟiveṁ tatsainya pādōtthitaṁ<br/>
pudidettaṁ rajamambarasthaḷamumaṁ muṭṭittu taḷturvi pa<br/>
rvidoḍā munninateḷpugeṭṭu kesaṟāytākāśa gaṅgājalaṁ // ViVi.10.29 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
ravi kiraṇāḷigaḷ dhvaja paṭāḷiya tintiṇiyindamurcalā<br/>
ṟave ravi vājigaḷ negeda pāṁsugaḷiṁdesegeṭṭu pōgalā<br/>
ṟave ravi bimbamandeseyalāṟade pempina tiṇpanānta kau<br/>
rava baḷadantu mēre pavaṇembudaninnaṟivandamāvudō // ViVi.10.30 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
madavaddhanti madāmbudhāregaḷavandondondaṟoḷ kūḍe pa<br/>
ṇṇida jātyaśva rathāśva saṅkuḷa khalīnōdbhūta lālājalaṁ<br/>
kadaḍeḻdettamavuṅke bēṟe para bhāgaṁ bettu lōkakke sa<br/>
nnidamāgirduvu kaurava dhvajiniyoḷ kāḷindiyuṁ gaṅgeyuṁ // ViVi.10.31 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu duryōdhanaṁ tanna balada karighaṭegaḷa karṇa tāḷāhatiyiṁ<br/>
kulagirigaḷaḷḷāḍeyuṁ tanna balada padābhighātadoḷaṁ kulagirigaḷ jīṟeḻdu<br/>
[p. 255]<br/>
pāṟēḻeyuṁ tanna balada padōtthita rajame mahā samudraṅgaḷaṁ tekkane<br/>
tīveyuṁ niccavayaṇadiṁ bandu kurukṣētrada pūrva digbhāgadoḷ praḷayaṁ<br/>
mūriviṭṭante bīḍaṁ biṭṭu dharmaputranalliguḷūkanemba dūtananintendaṭṭidaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
maseyisuguḷḷa keydugaḷanarcisugānegaḷaṁ taguḷdu pū<br/>
jisuge viśuddhavājigaḷanājige jeṭṭigarāgi koḷḷivī<br/>
sisuge nirantaraṁ ravaḷi ghōṣisuginde kaḍaṅgi sārci bi<br/>
ṭṭusirade nilva kāraṇamadāvudo neṭṭane nāḷe kāḷegaṁ // ViVi.10.32 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endā dūtanāmāḻkeyoḷe bandu pēḻe kēḷdu yamanandana<br/>
nintendaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
page masedaṁdekeydu masedirduvu pūjisuvaṅkadānevā<br/>
jigaḷemagillajaṭṭigareennoḍavuṭṭidaralte nālkumā<br/>
negaḷivanāṁdalīraṇadoḷarcisi biṭṭapenēke māṇbenā<br/>
vagamidanintepēḻ neṟe[ye]nāḷeye kāḷegamante geyvamāṁ // ViVi.10.33 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endā dūtanaṁ visarjisi puṇḍarīkākṣaṅge baḻiyanaṭṭi barisi namma<br/>
paḍeyoḷārge vīrapaṭṭamaṁ kaṭṭuvaṁ pēḻimene—<br/>
</p>

<p>
mātaṅgāsura vairiyallipaḍedaṁ billaṁdhanurvidyegaṁ<br/>
tātaṅgaggaḷamārumalladaṟināśvētaṅgamantā nadī<br/>
jātaṅgaṁ dore yuddhamendaṟidu tacchvētaṅge bhūlōkavi<br/>
khyātaṅgaggaḷa vīrapaṭṭamanudāraṁ kaṭṭidaṁ dharmajaṁ // ViVi.10.34 [śārdūlavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu virāṭa nandananaṁ dharmanandanaṁ sēnānāyakanaṁ māḍe nāḷe<br/>
kāḷegamendu paḍevaḷar pōgi sāṟimembudumavar bīḍu vīḍugaḷgellaṁ<br/>
sāṟidāgaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 256]<br/>
page sugivannegaṁ maseva vīra bhaṭarkaḷa raudramappa ke<br/>
ydugaḷenagurvinadbhutadinurvidakeṅgiḍigaḷ‌ paḷañci to<br/>
ṭṭage koḷe pāydavōl poḷevasañjeya kempadu sāṇegoḍḍidi<br/>
ṭṭageyarajambolembinegamastamayakkiḻida divākaraṁ // ViVi.10.32 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgaḷubhaya balaṅgaḷoḷaṁ cāturyāmāvasāna ghaṭita gha[ṁ]ṭikā<br/>
dhvanigaḷuṁ sandhyāsamaya samudita śaṅkhadhvanigaḷuṁ pañcamahāśabdadhvani<br/>
gaḷumoḍanoḍane negaḻduvāgaḷeraḍuṁ bīḍugaḷoḷaṁ bhōrendārduravaḷi<br/>
ghōṣisi koḷḷivīsidāgaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
urimuṭṭidaraḷeyantaṁ<br/>
baramuridattajana padmaviṣṭaradesaḷaṁ<br/>
dare sīduvakhiḷa digdvira<br/>
da radaṅgaḷ karame karipugāṟiduvāgaḷ // ViVi.10.36 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu koḷḷivīsidimbaḻiyaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
dhr̥ta dhavaḷavasanarārā<br/>
dhita śivararcita samasta śastrar‌ nīrā<br/>
jita turagaroppidar kela<br/>
ratiratha samaratha mahārathārdharatharkaḷ // ViVi.10.37 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
uḍaluṁ tuḍaluṁ vastraṁ<br/>
tuḍugeyanāneyumanarthi santatigīyal<br/>
biḍuvonnumanāḷgaṭṭuva<br/>
toḍaroḷ toḍardirdararasu makkaḷ kelabar // ViVi.10.38 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
ā prastāvadoḷorvaṁ tanna dōrvaladagurvinoḷurvīpatiya<br/>
nintendaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
nāḷe virōdhi sādhana ghaṭāghaṭitāhavadalli ninna ka<br/>
ṭṭāḷire muñci tāgadoḍamaḷkuṟe tāgi virōdhi sainya bhū<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 257]<br/>
pāḷaranondepoyyadoḍamī tale pōdoḍamaṭṭeyaṭṭika<br/>
ṭṭāḷane muṭṭi taḷtiṟiyadirdoḍamañjidenāṁ mahīpatī // ViVi.10.39 [utpalamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu tanna manada poḍarpumaṁ kūrpumanuṇṭumāḍi nuḍidaṁ<br/>
mattorvaṁ tannanāḷdaṁ perci poredudarke karaṁ meyverci nuḍidaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
odavida ninnadondu daye mēṇ piridō negaḻdenna gaṇḍumā<br/>
dadaṭumaḷurkeyuṁ pirido sandeyamādapudintidilli tū<br/>
gidoḍaṟiyalke bāradadu kāraṇadiṁ ripu bhūpa danti daṁ<br/>
tada toleyoḷ parākramadinennane bhūpati tūgi tōṟenē // ViVi.10.40 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu tanna seraguṁ beragumillada kalitanamanaṟiye nuḍidaṁ matta<br/>
mondeḍeyoḷorva vīrabhaṭanudāra vīrarasa rasikanāgi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
kudureyanēṟidamberasu sauḷene vōgirepoydumeyde ka<br/>
ṭṭidiroḷe nūṅkidānegaḷa kōḍugaḷaṁbaḷevōge poydumāṁ<br/>
tadaṭaranondevoydumeraḍuṁ balamennane nōḍe takkine<br/>
nnadaṭamanenna vīramumanājiyoḷennarasaṅge tōṟuveṁ // ViVi.10.41 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endatirabhasa raṇavyasanamanātmīyaśāsanāyattaṁ māḍidaṁ mattorvana<br/>
tyugra maṇḍaḷāgramananugeydu vīragraha grastanāgi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
siḍiloḷe taḷtu pōrva siḍilantire bāḷoḷe bāḷ‌ paḷañci mā<br/>
rkiḍiviḍe nōḍalañji desedēvategaḷ peṟapiṅge tōḷa tīn<br/>
kiḍenalidonderaḻkudureyaṭṭeyumonderaḍāneyaṭṭeyuṁ<br/>
toḍardoḍanāḍetaḷtiṟiyadirdoḍe jōḷamanentu nīguveṁ // ViVi.10.42 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu nijabhuja vijayamanappukeydu nuḍidaṁ mattōrvanalliye—<br/>
</p>

<p>
suralōkaṁ dorekoḷvudondu parama śrī lakṣmiyuṁ barpudā<br/>
daradiṁ dēvanikāyadoḷ nerevudondutsāhamuṁ tanna me<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 258]<br/>
ysiri bhāgyaṁ neramappudonde raṇadoḷ geldājiyaṁtaḷtusaṁ<br/>
garadoḷ jōḷada pāḻiyaṁ nerapidaṁ gaṇḍaṁ peṟaṁ gaṇḍanē // ViVi.10.43 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[endu nuḍidaṁ]—<br/>
</p>

<p>
tave māṟānta balaṁ kaṟuttiṟidu tannāḷdaṁ karaṁ mecce ge<br/>
ldavanaṁ śrīvadhu pattuguṁ maḍidanaṁ dēvāṅganānīkamu<br/>
tsavadinduygumadentumimbusubhaṭaṅgintappudaṁ kaṇḍumaṁ<br/>
juvanēkañjuvanendu perci nuḍidaṁ mattorvanāsthānadoḷ // ViVi.10.44 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu nuḍideraḍuṁ balaṅgaḷuṁ tantamma vīramaṁ cāgamaṁ meṟedu<br/>
tamma keydugaḷanarcisi darbhaśayanaṁ māḍi pallaṁ sulidu śastrasaṅgraharāgi<br/>
palaruṁ vīrabhaṭar tammaṁ tāme paricchēdisirdaratta mattamorvaṁ tanna<br/>
nallaḷoḷintendanī poḻte poḻtu nāḷe dēvalōkada kanyakeyarōlagadoḷirpe<br/>
nendu nuḍiye nīnendantu pōgal‌ tīradu nāḷe maguḻdu bandennoḷ<br/>
nereveyendu pēḻe ninagaṟivuṇṭe endu kēḷiyennōlevāgya muṇṭendaḷ<br/>
mattamondeḍeyoḷorvaḷ darbhaśayanasthanāda nija prāṇēśvarana<br/>
paricchēdamanaṟidu tanna sāvaṁ paricchēdisi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
tāṁ gaḍa nāḷe pōgi divijāṅganeyoḷ toḍardirpanilli mā<br/>
ṇdāṁ gaḍamirpenantanitubeḷḷene munname pōgi nalmege<br/>
llaṅgoḷe dēvalōkadoḷadhīśananānidirgoḷvenōvo sa<br/>
ggaṅgaḷoḷirpa dēvaḍiti toḻtiroḷaḻtiyanāgalīvenē // ViVi.10.45 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu kaidavamillada nalmeyiṁ nālageya tudige tandu nuḍidaḷ<br/>
mattorvaḷ tannāṇmana dōrvaladagurvaṁ nacci—<br/>
</p>

<p>
jaḷadhiyoḷāda muttugaḷavēṁ posatāduve ninna tōḷa bā<br/>
ḷoḷe bala garvadiṁ tegedudagra virōdhi madēbhamastaka<br/>
sthaḷa jaḷarāśiyoḷ baḷeda nirmaḷa nirvraṇa vr̥ttamauktikā<br/>
vaḷiyane tarpudendu nuḍidaḻkaṟoḷāṟisidaḷ nijēśanaṁ // ViVi.10.46 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 259]<br/>
antubhaya balaṅgaḷoḷaṁ vīrajanajanitāḷāpaṅgaḷ negaḻe vikramārjuna<br/>
nanantanuṁ tānuṁ jalakkanire pallaṁ sulidagaṇya puṇya tīrthōdakaṅgaḷaṁ mindu<br/>
maṅgaḷavasadanaṅgoṇḍu sāmānya yajñaṅgeydu palavuṁ teṟada paṟegaḷeseye<br/>
nāndī mukhamaṁ nirvartisi śubha lakṣaṇa lakṣitanuṁ sannāha karmanirmitanuṁ<br/>
hastāyudha kuśaḷanuṁ bhadramananumappa vijaya gajamu manakṣayarathāśva kētana<br/>
śarāsana śaradhi vicitra tanutra vividhāstra śastraṅgaḷumaṁ gandha dhūpa<br/>
dīpādigaḷindarcisi poḍevaṭṭāgaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
beḷaguva soḍargaḷa beḷaguma<br/>
niḷisi taḻattaḻisi poḷeye tammaya beḷaga<br/>
ggaḷisi taḻataḻisi vidyu<br/>
dviḷasitamenisiduvu narana divyāstraṅgaḷ // ViVi.10.47 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
soḍarguḍiya kempinoḷ keṁ<br/>
piḍidire ripu nr̥pati balada śōṇita jaḷamaṁ<br/>
kuḍiyadeyuṁ dal munname<br/>
kuḍidantesedirduvariganastracayaṅgaḷ // ViVi.10.48 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antāyiruḷaṁ vijayaṁ vijayōdyōgadoḷ kaḷeye beḷagappa<br/>
jāvadoḷ bīḍuvīḍugaḷgellaṁ toḻaldēkirpirēḻiṁ paṇṇimene—<br/>
</p>

<p>
taṇḍade kīṟi sāṟuva palar paḍevaḷḷara mātugaḷ manaṁ<br/>
goṇḍiresannaṇanduḍuva paṇṇuva bāḻteyavandiraṁ maru<br/>
ḷgoṇḍavolūḷva baggisuva bēgadoḷā kaṭakaṅgaḷeyde ke<br/>
ykoṇḍuvu mandara kṣubhita dugdhapayōdhi gabhīranādamaṁ // ViVi.10.49 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
kr̥ta vividhāstra vīrabhaṭa kōṭi bhayaṅkaramāgebīsuvā<br/>
vutiya kaḷaṅka paṅkadoḷe percida kaḻtale tīvra śastra saṁ<br/>
hatigaḷa dīptiyiṁ bisugeyāgi karaṁ pogarvaṭṭagurvuma<br/>
dbhutamumanīye paṇṇiduvu pāṇḍava kaurava raudra sādhanaṁ // ViVi.10.50 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
anteraḍuṁ paḍegaḷuṁ paṇṇapaṇṇane paṇṇi kāḷegakke naḍeyaloḍarisi<br/>
dāgaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 260]<br/>
lōkaika cakṣu nava kama<br/>
lākara bāndhavananēka ditisuta samarā<br/>
nīka bhayaṅkaraneraḍuma<br/>
nīkaṅgaḷanaḍare nōḍuvantudayisidaṁ // ViVi.10.51 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgaḷēṟisidabisugegaḷumikkida lōhavakkaregaḷumurcida<br/>
mogavaḍaṅgaḷuṁ kaṭṭida paḻayigegaḷumoṭṭida mūvatteraḍāyudhaṅgaḷuṁ<br/>
beraseṟaṅkeverasida kulagirigaḷe taḷarvante taḷarva madāndha gandhasindhuraṅgaḷumaṁ<br/>
cakra cītkr̥ta nādadoḷ dikcakramumaṁcakraghātadoḷ dharācakra manākramisi<br/>
niśāta hēti garbhaṅgaḷumanēka prakāra kētana vājirājigaḷumāgidommaḷisinaḍeva rathaṅgaḷumaṁ kaṇṇuṁ khuramaṁ tōṟe pakkareyikki poḷeva ponna<br/>
paryāṇaṅgaḷumeseye ghōḷāylar‌ poḷeyise bisilguduregaḷ poḷevante<br/>
poḷeva kaḍuguduregaḷumaṁ miḍumiḍukanemiḍukuvasiḍilēḻgeyumaṁ<br/>
kōḷmasagida puliya piṇḍugaḷumananukarisi naḍevaṇiya sandaṇiyumaṁ kāḻtuṟu<br/>
masagidante masagida durdhara dhanurdhara balamumaṁ śvēta bhīṣmara pēḻdōje<br/>
yoḷeraḍuṁ paḍegaḷa paḍevaḷarkaḷ kurukṣētradoḷ citrisidantoḍḍi nindāgaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
jalaśayanōdarāntaradinī trijagaṁ poṟamaṭṭudīgaḷeṁ<br/>
buli sale tamma tamma śibiraṅgaḷinugra caturbalaṅgaḷaṁ<br/>
palavumanonde māḍi desegaḷ masuḷalnaḍetandarājigi<br/>
rvaladalarātināyakarumorbaranorbare gelva takkinoḷ // ViVi.10.52 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgaḷ kaurava balada sēnānāyakaṁ gāṅgēyanaḍḍamāge tannoḍḍida<br/>
makaravyūhada moneyoḷ suttiṟidettida ponna toḷapa paḻayigegaḷuṁmeṟevabeḷḷiya rathamumā rathadoḷoḍambaḍe pūḍida kuduregaḷuṁ jōlda purvanetti<br/>
kaṭṭida lalāṭa paṭṭadoḷiṭṭaḷamoppuva bīravaṭṭamumasadaḷameseye divyakavacamaṁ<br/>
toṭṭu paraśurāmaṁ bāḻgendu pracaṇḍa kōdaṇḍamaṁ koṇḍu pāṇḍava balamaṁ<br/>
mārkoṇḍu nindāgaḷ śvētanumā vyūhakke prativyūhavāgi sūcīvyūhama<br/>
noḍḍi kanakakavacālaṅkr̥ta śarīranumārūḍha samara rasanumupārūḍha<br/>
[p. 261]<br/>
kanakarathanumāgi kailāsavāsige poḍevaṭṭu billaṅkoṇḍu gaṅgāsutaṅgadiradidirci<br/>
nindāgaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
śvētana gaṅgājātana<br/>
mātane pārderaḍumoḍḍaṇaṁ kādalkeṁ<br/>
dī teṟadinoḍḍi ninduvu<br/>
bhūtaḷamaḷḷāḍe kesaṟa kaḍitada teṟadiṁ // ViVi.10.53 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgaḷ dharmaputraṁ puruṣōttamana mogamaṁ nōḍi kaurava<br/>
baladoḍḍaṇada nāyakarivarārendu besagoḷe makara mastakabhūmiyoḷ<br/>
yuddhasannaddhanāgi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
kembaṇṇada kuduregaḷoḷo<br/>
ḍambaḍe nija rajata rathamagurvurvareyaṁ<br/>
timbe kaḷaśadhvajaṁ miḷi<br/>
rdambaramaṁ baḷase nindanātaṁ drōṇaṁ // ViVi.10.54 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
ātana sāre kamaṇḍalu<br/>
kētanamambaramanaḍare caturaṅga balō<br/>
pētanati dhavaḷa rathanabhi<br/>
jātaṁ kṣatriyaranuṟada kali kr̥panātaṁ // ViVi.10.55 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
mattitta gāṅgēyana dakṣiṇōpāntadoḷ karganekargidasamada<br/>
gajaghaṭāṭōpada naḍuve—<br/>
</p>

<p>
saradada mugilane biḍadanu<br/>
karisuva dhavaḷāśvadindamesedoppuva lō<br/>
harathamadu puliya paḻayige<br/>
verasu taḻattaḻise nindanātaṁ śalyaṁ // ViVi.10.56 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
mattitta gaṅgāsutana vāmabhāgadoḷambara bhāgamaṁ kaṭṭi meḍaṟidantāgi<br/>
tanna rathadoḷoṭṭida keydugaḷa beḷage beḷagāge—<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 262]<br/>
kaṟe koraloḷ kaṇṇosaloḷ<br/>
peṟe makuṭadoḷugra dhanu karāgradoḷireya<br/>
ḷḷiṟiye harikētu nabhadoḷ<br/>
miṟuguva cembonna rathadanaśvatthāmaṁ // ViVi.10.57 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
ā rudrāvatārana keladoḷ kikkiṟigiṟida taḻeduṟugala naḍuve<br/>
ponnarathamanēṟi nindaṁ bhūriśravanātana keladoḷbāḷabaṭṭaṁtūntiṭṭante<br/>
sandaṇisi ninda gōpakumāraraṇiya naḍuve ponnarathamanēṟinindātanenna tammaṁ<br/>
kr̥tavarmanātana keladoḷondakṣōhiṇī balamberasu suttiṟidu kanaka daṇḍa<br/>
maṇḍita vicitrātapatraṅgaḷa naḍuve maṇimakuṭa marīcigaḷ poḷeye nānā<br/>
vāhanaṅgaḷanēṟi nindar jayatsēna kāmbhōja sudakṣiṇa daṇḍadhāra śatadaṇḍa<br/>
dhararavara keladoḷ nīḷa śrutāyudhaniyutāyudhācyutāyudharembavara<br/>
keladoḷnilebalada seṟekōloḷondakṣōhiṇī balamberasumayvattusāsira<br/>
madadāneverasu nindaṁ suyōdhananaṇuga maydunaṁ sindhudēśādhīśvaraṁ<br/>
jayadrathanātana kelaloḷ makara mastaka bhūmiyoḷ karaṭataṭagaḷita<br/>
madajaḷadhārāpūra pariplāvita sakaḷa bhūtaḷamappa nālku lakka bhadrahastiyuma<br/>
nondumāḍi ghaṭeya moneyoḷ diggajēndramenisida supratīka gajēndra<br/>
manēṟi nindātanindrana keḷeyaṁ bhagadattanātana keladoḷondu lakka kudureyu<br/>
maṟuvattu sāsira rathamu mondakṣōhiṇiya kālāḷverasu nindar sōmadatta<br/>
bāhlīkaravara keladoḷ dēvēndraṅge pagevarāgi vikramārjunana keyyoḷ satta<br/>
nivātakavaca kāḷakēya pauḷōma taḷatāḷukaremba daityar‌ vr̥ddha vairamaṁ nenedu<br/>
trigartādhīśa suśarma prabhr̥tigaḷuṁ saṁsaptakarumāgi puṭṭi mūrukōṭiyu<br/>
maṟuvattusāsira daitya pradhāna nāyakarumarjunanoḷ kāduva besanaṁ<br/>
duryōdhananoḷ bēḍi paḍedu padineṇṭu kōṭi rathamberasu bēṟoḍḍi<br/>
nindar‌ mattitta caturaṅgabaḷa jaḷanidhiya naḍuve kaḷiṅgarāja vaṅga koṅga<br/>
dēśādhīśvarareṇbattusāsira gajaghaṭegaḷuṁmūṟu lakka rathamumaṟuvattu kōṭi<br/>
padātiyuṁ berasu nindar mattaṁ kṣēmadhūrtiyuṁ bhīmasēnana keyyoḷ<br/>
satta bakāsura jaṭāsurana makkaḷaḷambhūṣa halāyudha musalāyudha kāḷa nīḷa<br/>
pramukha rūkṣarākṣasa balamberasu suttiṟidu baḷasiyu mire duśyāsanaṁ<br/>
[p. 263]<br/>
modalāge nūrvar tammandiruṁ lakkaṇaṁ modalāge nūrvar makkaḷumaṟu<br/>
vattusāsirarathamuṁ padineṇṭu sāsira madāndha gandhasindhuraṅgaḷuṁ berasu poyva<br/>
pañcamahāśabdaṅgaḷ kāḷa nīḷa jaḷandharaṅgaḷ moḻaguvante moḻage gaganataḷaṁ<br/>
taḷirtante poḷedu miḷirva pāḷi mahādhvajaṅgaḷuṁ gagana sindhu phēna paṭaḷa<br/>
śaṅkha saṅkāśa pāṇḍu chatracāmaraṅgaḷuṁ peṟavuṁ rājacihnaṁ gaḷumeseye—<br/>
</p>

<p>
kanaka girīndra rundra śikharasthita bāḷa dinēśa bimbamaṁ<br/>
neneyise tanna ponna rathadoḷ nelasirdu viḷāsadinde bhī<br/>
mana moneyaṁ vanīpakaranārayalaṭṭi yugānta vārdhi bhōṁ<br/>
kene taḷarvandadiṁ taḷaralaṭṭipanalte phaṇīndrakētanaṁ // ViVi.10.58 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
seṟekōl seṟekōliṁ pa<br/>
ttaṟugāvuda balada pavaṇananitinitendā<br/>
naṟiyeṁ dēvāsuraroḷa<br/>
maṟiyeṁ kaṇḍinitu balamanānavanipatī // ViVi.10.59 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu nāmuṁ namma balada nāyakaraneḍeyaṟidoḍḍuvamendu<br/>
drōṇana monegaṟuvattusāsira rathamberasu dhr̥ṣṭadyumnanumanaśvatthāmana monege<br/>
nālvattu sāsira rathamberasu śikhaṇḍiyumaṁ kr̥tavarmana monegondakṣōhiṇī<br/>
balaṁ berasu sātyakiyumaṁ duryōdhanana monegondu kōṭi rathamumondu<br/>
lakka bhadrahastiyuṁ berasu bhīmanumaṁ br̥hadbaḷana monege mūvattusāsira<br/>
rathamberasabhimanyuvumaṁ duśyāsanana monege nālvattu sāsira rathamberasu<br/>
nakulanumaṁ śakuniya monege nālvattu sāsira rathamberasu sahadēvanumaṁ kr̥pana<br/>
monegondakṣōhiṇī balamberasu kēkayarumaṁ sindhurājana monegondakṣō<br/>
hiṇī balamberasu drupadanumaṁ bhagadattana monegondakṣōhiṇī balamberasu<br/>
virāṭanumaṁ jaṭāsura bakāsurara makkaḷaḷambhūṣa haḷāyudha musaḷāyudha<br/>
kāḷa nīḷa naktañcarara monegondakṣōhiṇī balaṁ berasu ghaṭōtkacanumaṁ<br/>
vindanamonege padineṇṭu sāsira rathamumondulakka madadāneyumberasu<br/>
kontiyamāvanappa kontibhōjanumaṁ vindānuvindara monegaṟuvattu sāsira<br/>
rathamberasu nāgakumārananantabala samanvitaniḷāvantanumaṁ bhūriśravana monege<br/>
nālvattusāsira rathamuṁ nālvattusāsira madahastigaḷuṁ berasu madagajārūḍha<br/>
nuttaranumaṁ suyōdhanana makkaḷ lakkaṇaṁ modalāge nūrvara monegaṟuvattu<br/>
[p. 264]<br/>
sāsira rathamberasu suta sōmaka pramukharappa pañca pāṇḍavarumaṁ pēḻdu<br/>
kāmbhōja sudakṣiṇa daṇḍadhāraremba mūvarakṣōhiṇīpatigaḷa monege<br/>
mūṟukōṭi rathamberasu pāṇḍya śrījayasōmakaraṁ pēḻdu vīra puṣkara<br/>
pāriyātra barbara śabara nēpāḷa mahīpāḷara monegeraḍu kōṭi rathamberasu<br/>
haihayaraṁ pēḻdu nīḷananaṟuvattusāsira bhadrahastiverasu tanna cakra rakṣege pēḻdu<br/>
saṁsaptakara padineṇṭu kōṭi rathakkarikēsariya rathamanondane pēḻdu yudhiṣṭhiraṁ<br/>
śalyana monege neṟedunindu keyvīsuvā prastāvadoḷ ‘śūraṁ bhēdēna<br/>
yōjayēt’ emba nayamaṁ keykoṇḍu vinayamane mundiṭṭu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
baḷameraḍuṁ tannane miḷa<br/>
miḷa nōḍe narēndranonde rathadindasuhr̥<br/>
dbaḷamaniradeydi bhīṣmara<br/>
caḷaṇa yugakkeṟage ninage jayamakkendaṁ // ViVi.10.60 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu bhīṣmar tammamommanavinayakke mecci parase parakeyaṁ<br/>
keykoṇḍu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
guru kr̥pagurusutaśalyara |<br/>
caraṇaṅgaḷgeṟagi pōgi poḍevaḍuvudumā<br/>
daradindaṁ nalmeyoḷaṁ<br/>
parasi manaṅgoṇḍu nuḍidaravarā nr̥panaṁ // ViVi.10.61 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
ninna baravindavemma ma<br/>
nanninageṟagidudu jayamumemmī deseyiṁ<br/>
danninage sārge pōgene<br/>
mannisi gurujanamanāgaḷantakatanayaṁ // ViVi.10.62 [kandaṁ]<br/>

<p>
maguḻdu tannoḍḍaṇakke baruttuṁ duryōdhanana tammanappa yuyutsuvaṁ<br/>
kaṇḍu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 265]<br/>
pavanajaninde kauravakulaṁ paḍaliṭṭavolakkumādoḍi<br/>
nnavaravarārumillaṇame santati keṭṭapudilli kāvenī<br/>
bavaradoḷīgaḷānivananendu nr̥paṁ dayeyindamā yuyu<br/>
tsuvanoḍagoṇḍu bandanenitādoḍamēṁ prabhu pollakeygumē // ViVi.10.63 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antā yuyutsuvanoḍagoṇḍu bandu dharmaputranutsāhadoḷirpa<br/>
padadoḷ vikramārjunana manadoḷāda vyāmōhamaṁ kaḷeyalendu mukundaṁ<br/>
divyasvarūpamaṁ tōṟi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
adiradidirci taḷtiṟiyalī maledoḍḍida cāturaṅgameṁ<br/>
budu ninagoḍḍi nindudidanōvade kolvaḍe nīnumenna ka<br/>
jjadoḷesagendusaitajitanādiya vēdarahasyadoḷ niraṁ<br/>
tada[paricaryeyiṁ]neṟeye yōjisidaṁ kadanatriṇētranaṁ // ViVi.10.64 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgaḷ parasainyabhairavaṁ purāṇapuruṣanappa puruṣōttamaṅgeṟagi<br/>
poḍamaṭṭu ripupakṣakṣayakaramappa viśvakarma nirmitamāda tanna divyarathamaṁ<br/>
manōrathamberasurathāṅgadharanaṁ munnamēṟalvēḻdu mūṟu sūḻ balavandu<br/>
poḍamaṭṭu baḻiyaṁ tānēṟi vajrakavacamaṁ toṭṭu tavadoṇegaḷaneraḍuṁ<br/>
deseyoḷaṁ bigidu drōṇācāryaṅge manadoḷ namaskāraṅgeydu drōṇaṁ<br/>
bāḻgendu mahā pracaṇḍa gāṇḍīvamaṁ koṇḍēṟisi nīvi jēvoḍedu dēvadatta<br/>
śaṅkhamaṁ pūrisi saṁsaptakaroḍḍaṇadatta rathāṅgadharanaṁ rathamaṁ cōdisa<br/>
lvēḻdāgaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
kuḷaśaiḷēndraṅgaḷambhōnidhigaḷakhiḷa digdantigaḷ viśvadhātrī<br/>
vaḷayaṁ pātāḷamūlaṁ sakala bhuvanamondondaṟoḷkēṇigoṇḍu<br/>
ccaḷisal sūsal paḷañcal siḍidoḍedaḷaṟal pāṟi jīṟēḻalandu<br/>
mmaḷisuttattirdarāvaṁ hariganoḷidiraṁ mīṟi māṟāmpa gaṇḍaṁ // ViVi.10.65 [mahāsragdhare]<br/>
</p>

<p>
embannegaṁ praḷaya kāla jātōtpāta vāta nirghātadindamaḷḷāḍi<br/>
taḷḷaṅkaṅguṭṭuva jaḷanidhigaḷante mēredappal bagevubhaya sainyaṅgaḷaṁ kaṇḍatta<br/>
rājarājanumitta dharmarājanumoḍanoḍane keyvīsidāgaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 266]<br/>
pūrvāpara jaḷanidhigaḷa<br/>
gurvisuvinamondanondu tāguvavolagu<br/>
rvurvire parvi caturvala<br/>
mērvesadindandu bandu tāgittāgaḷ // ViVi.10.66 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
ghaṭeya daḻadulivu laya ghana<br/>
ghaṭegaḷa moḻagenise poṭṭagoḍedattu raṭa<br/>
tpaṭu paṭaha śaṅkha bhēriya<br/>
caṭuvaḷitadindaṭaḷa paṭaḷamambara paṭaḷaṁ // ViVi.10.67 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
kari turaga ratha padātiya<br/>
caraṇāsaṅghāta jāta rajamājasraṁ<br/>
neredambarakogeyal baḷa<br/>
bharadiṁ dhareyeḻdu pāṟuvantāytāgaḷ // ViVi.10.68 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
samara rasapriyaroḷ sa<br/>
ttvamumiḷeyoḷ rajamumodave raṇagaḻtaleyoḷ<br/>
tamamuṁ mige sattva raja<br/>
stamaṅgaḷuṁkāṇalāduveraḍuṁ paḍeyoḷ // ViVi.10.69 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
paḍeya poṟegagidu śēṣaṁ<br/>
peḍegaḷanuḍuguvudumeḷe bodillene biḻda<br/>
ttaḍigiḍe kūrmana bennaṁ<br/>
doḍedu siḍildoḍane nuccunūṟappinegaṁ // ViVi.10.70 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu nelanumākāśamondondaṟoḷ tāgida bēgadoḷambaraṁ baraṁ<br/>
negeda dhūḷiyoḷ deseyaṟiyadeyuṁ tamma balamaṁ mārvalamanaṟi<br/>
yadeyuṁ cāturvalaṅgaḷ modala samakaṭṭugeṭṭu taḍavarisi taṭṭu<br/>
poṭṭendeccumiṭṭumiṟidutaṟidu ghaṭṭiseyumāṅkegoṇḍu kiṟidu poḻtu<br/>
kāde kāde suriva bisunettara sariyoḷamambina sariyoḷamambiriviṭṭu pāyva<br/>
madagajaṅgaḷa madajaladoḷaṁ balada kaḷakaḷakke masagi deseyaṟiyadeyuṁ paṟiye<br/>
[p. 267]<br/>
ghaṭṭisida kīḷa ghaṭṭaṇeyoḷ poṭṭagoḍeda tāḷugegaḷa rudhirajaladoḷ berasi<br/>
padagempanāḷda jātyaśvada lāḷājaḷadoḷaṁ neladoḷogeva rajaṁ modalmūlaṁ<br/>
giḍeyuṁ tiṟidikkidante talegaḷpaṟiduruḷdoḍe permaraṅgaḷa pōḻgaḷoḷagaṇiṁ<br/>
damogeda kēsurigaḷa baḷagadantaṭṭegaḷindambarambaraṁ negedu pāṟuva nettara<br/>
suṭṭuregaḷindaṁ mēge negeda rajaṁ masuḷanāge deseyaṟidu tamma balamumaṁ<br/>
mārvalamumanaṟidu navarudhira jaḷacaḷatsēcanadoḷghaṭṭisi<br/>
sinduradoḷ nelagaṭṭisidantirda raṅga bhūmiyoḷeraḍuṁ paḍeya nāyakar<br/>
bilgāḷegaṅgāduvāgaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
piḍikey tīvida kūrgaṇe<br/>
maḍakālvaramaleva kacce niḍiyasiyoṟe ka<br/>
rpiḍida paṇegaṭṭu keypoḍe<br/>
beḍaṅganoḷakoḷe dhanurdharar peṇedeccar // ViVi.10.71 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
śarasandhānaṁ niṭṭisa<br/>
laridembinameraḍu balada kaḍuvillar bhō<br/>
rgaredise kūrgaṇeyoḷ paṁ<br/>
darikkidantāytu gagana maṇḍaḷamellaṁ // ViVi.10.72 [kandaṁ]<br/>

<p>
gaṟisannegeydu tegeneṟe<br/>
deṟagi paraṅkalisi parvi kūkiṟidise keṁ<br/>

<p>
antubhayabala dhanurdhara balaṅgaḷumaḻgi maḻgidāgaḷ—<br/>

<p>
toḷaguva bāḷ taḻattaḻipa kakkaḍe bumbhukadoḷ taguḷdu pa<br/>
jjaḷisuva pañcarāyudhamagurvisuvāvuti pūsidantiri<br/>
ṭṭaḷamamardirda māḷajige pakkareyikkidajāyilaṁ bhayaṁ<br/>

<p>

<p>
pasuge nelaṁ jalaṁ hayadoḍambaḍu vañcane kēṇamāsanaṁ<br/>

<p>

<p>

<p>

<p>
[p. 269]<br/>
anteraḍuṁ balada daḻaṅgaḷkōlāṭamāḍuvante kiṟidānuṁ bēgaṁ<br/>
taṭṭupoṭṭendu kōlkuṭṭi patteṇṭu sāsirakudureyaṭṭeyumēḻeṇṭu nettara<br/>
kaḍal kaḍalanaṭṭeyuṁ kādi basamaḻidu peṟapiṅgi nindāgaḷ praḷayaduriya<br/>
nuruḷi māḍidantānuṁ baḍavāgniyananuvisidantānuṁbaṟa siḍilakiḍigaḷa<br/>
baḷagamanoḷagumāḍidantānuṁ gondaṇisi sandaṇisi nindaṇiyaneraḍuṁ balada<br/>
kaḍitaleya nāyaka‌r keykoṇḍu baḷḷugeḍedekkevāṟu vāṟi palagevāḍigūḷisorki mārkoṇḍu kāde—<br/>
</p>

<p>
pusi nasu vañcane nōrpanu<br/>
vasidagalitu takkudakku page keybage ke<br/>
ykusuri nusuḷemba kēṇada<br/>
kusuriyanaṟidiṟidu meṟedu neṟeduṟadarebar // ViVi.10.81 [kandaṁ]<br/>
