<p>
baṟa siḍileṟapantire baṁ<br/>
deṟagidaraṁ taḷtu bāḷa kīḻmoneyiṁ ta<br/>
ḷtaṟadaṟidubbaramembiva<br/>
naṟidiṟidar peṇabaṇambegaḷ negevinegaṁ // ViVi.10.82 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
cārisi bāḷāgamamava<br/>
tāraṁ geydante kāladantakanane pō<br/>
ltāruttuṁ kavivadaṭara<br/>
nōrondōrondevoydu kondar palaraṁ // ViVi.10.83 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
bāḷvāḷgaḷa ghaṭṭaṇeyoḷ<br/>
baḷvaḷa baḷedogedu negeda kiḍigaḷa bamba<br/>
lgaḷverasu poḷedu negedudu<br/>
bāḷvoge[kāṟa mugil]baḷḷimiṁ[cinindu]ḷkuvavōl // ViVi.10.84 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 270]<br/>
tale neladoḷuruḷdoḍaṁ mē<br/>
ygaliyorvaṁ piḍidu taleyaniṭṭaṭṭeyoḷa<br/>
ggalisida muḷisiṁ māṭada<br/>
taleyiṭṭāḍuvavaninisu pōltanugeydaṁ // ViVi.10.85 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antaṇi maṇiyade seṇasi poṇardu kiṟidu poḻtu kādinindāgaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
māruta ghāta sañcaḷita kētu samūhamudagra cakra cī<br/>
tkāramudāra vīra bhaṭa siṁha nināda vimiśritōtkaṭa<br/>
jyāravamambarāntaramanaḷḷiṟidavvaḷipannegaṁ śarā<br/>
sāradagurvu parvi nile tāgiduvugra rathaṁ rathāḷiyoḷ // ViVi.10.86 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu tāgidāgaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
kudureya baṇṇadiṁ rathada tōrkeyinettida citrakētu vr̥ṁ<br/>
dada kuṟupindudagra ratha cōdaka cihnadinātanītaneṁ<br/>
budanaṟidorvarorvarane maccaradiṁ gaṟisannegeydidi<br/>
rcida padadoḷ patatrimayamembinitāytu samasta diktaṭaṁ // ViVi.10.87 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
paraśu śara nikaradiṁ ku<br/>
mmarigaḍidavoloḍane kaḍiyerathigaḷ rathadiṁ<br/>
dharegiḻidu viratharatiratha<br/>
rarebar mēlvāydu rathigaḷaṁ surigiṟidar // ViVi.10.88 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
tēraṁ pāyisi nōyisi<br/>
pāruvakuduregaḷanarebarerdeyuriyeccar‌<br/>
sārathiya rathiya talegaḷa<br/>
nōrondastradoḷe pāṟi jīṟēḻvinegaṁ // ViVi.10.89 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
nettara kesaṟoḷ gāliga<br/>
ḷettaṁ taḷarade jigiltu nile dharegiḻidā<br/>
rdetti pariyisidarēṁ me<br/>
yvettudo rathakalpamalli sūtar kelabar // ViVi.10.90 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 271]<br/>
antubhaya varūthiniya varūthaṅgaḷ mallāmalliyāge kāduvāgaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
uḍidirdaccaḻidīsu taḻgida nogaṁ jīṟeḻda cakraṁ siḍil<br/>
poḍedantormeye sūsi pāṟida maḍaṁ nurgāda kīl sāyakaṁ<br/>
naḍe nondeyde suruḷduruḷda turagaṁ surkirda sūtaṁ kaḍal<br/>
kaḍalaṁ muṭṭi teraḷva nettara ponal kaṇgoṇḍudugrājiyoḷ // ViVi.10.91 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu patteṇṭu nettara kaḍal kaḍalanaṭṭeyuṁ varūtha yūthaṅgaḷaḷki<br/>
meḷkidantāgaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
ikkida lōhavakkareyakarpugaḷiṁkavitarpa vindhya śai<br/>
lakkeṇeyāge jōdarisuvambina balsari tiṇṇamāgi ke<br/>
ymikku virōdhi sādhana ghaṭāḷiyanōḍisalāgaḷārdu bi<br/>
ṭṭikkidarugra sindhura ghaṭāvaḷiyaṁ muḷisiṁ niṣādigaḷ // ViVi.10.92 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
ādityaṁ masuḷvannegaṁdhvaja ghaṭāṭōpaṅgaḷinda layāṁ<br/>
bhōdaṅgaḷ kavivantevōl kavivuduṁ kālgāpu kālgāpinoḷ<br/>
jōdar jōdaroḷāneyāneyoḷagurvappannegaṁ kāde ka<br/>
ṇgādaṁ celvesedattu mūṟu neleyiṁ mādyadgajēndrāhavaṁ // ViVi.10.93 [śārdūlavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antā dantighaṭegaḷanārōhakar‌ tōṟikoṭṭondondarke<br/>
mogambugisi dāgaḷubhaya vyāḷadantivadhya kramaṅgaḷoḷ bhārgavar<br/>
surigiṟivantiṟiye sūsuva kennettar kaḻaldudirva sakkada sippugaḷuṁ siḍildu<br/>
jīṟēḻva kōḻkaḷumagurvaṁ paḍeye—<br/>
</p>

<p>
naḍuva saralge meyyoḷagaḍaṅguva saṅkuge diṅkugoḷva ka<br/>
kkaḍegidirurcuviṭṭigidirāneya kōḻkaḷa kōḷge nondu bā<br/>
yviḍadinisappoḍaṁpeḷaṟadaḷkade pāvinaliṭṭavōl poḍa<br/>
rpuḍugade biḻduvirda neleyiṁ kelavunmada gandhasindhuraṁ // ViVi.10.94 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 272]<br/>
pāṟuva pāṟumbaḷe koḷe<br/>
jīṟeḻdambarake tale siḍildoḍamā kā<br/>
ypāṟade haraṇaṁ geyduvu<br/>
jāṟallade jōdaraṭṭegaḷ kelavāgaḷ // ViVi.10.95 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
kaṇakene cakra tīvra hatiyiṁ tale pōdoḍe jōdaraṭṭe saṁ<br/>
daṇisidabandhadiṁ bisugeyoḷ nelasirdesedāḍe naṭṭa kū<br/>
rgaṇeverasirdakūrgaṇegaḷuccaḷisuttire suydupuṇṇatiṁ<br/>
thiṇigaḷinandagurvuverasāḍiduvonderaḍāneyaṭṭegaḷ // ViVi.10.96 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
anteraḍuṁ balada karighaṭegaḷondondaṟoḷ tāgi taṭṭiṟiye<br/>
bisunetta[ra]rbigaḷurvipāye pērurvigaḷverasu jājina parvataṅgaḷante<br/>
keḍedaḻgitaḻgidāgaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
ānireyēniṟivudu gaḍa<br/>
mī nālkuṁ balamidalte paribhavamenageṁ<br/>
dēnuṁ māṇade bhīmana<br/>
nūnabalaṁ bandu tāgidaṁ kurubaladoḷ // ViVi.10.97 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu kurubalada karighaṭegaḷaṁ nuṅguvante desedesege miḷirdu miḷḷisida<br/>
siṅgada paḻavigeyuṁ kurubalakke miḻtu palmorevante moredu pariva tanna<br/>
kisuvonna rathamuṁ bhayaṅkarākāramāge pagevara gaṇṭalanottuvantepauṇḍramemba<br/>
śaṅkhamanotti mundoḍḍidoḍḍellamanambinabambaloḷe paḍalvaḍisuttuṁ barpa<br/>
bhīmasēnaṅge duryōdhananadiradidirāntāgaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
entidirānteyante kaliyāgoḷasōradirendu bhīmanō<br/>
rante kanaldu tiṇṇamise pāyva saralgaḷaneydalīyadāṁ<br/>
tāntu nirantaraṁ taṟidu sūtananātana vājiyaṁ mahī<br/>
śaṁ tegedeccanacca bisunettara suṭṭure sūsuvannegaṁ // ViVi.10.98 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 273]<br/>
ise masagi bhīmanīra<br/>
yduśitāstradinuruḷe sūtanuḍiye rathaṁ kī<br/>
lise kudure muṟiye paḻavige<br/>
masakadinecceccanonde saraloḷ nosalaṁ // ViVi.10.99 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
paṭṭaṅgaṭṭida nosalaṁ<br/>
naṭṭa saralviḍidu nettarambiriviḍe ka<br/>
ṇgeṭṭirda nr̥pananaṅkada<br/>
kaṭṭāḷgaḷ kādu kaḷipeduryōdhananaṁ // ViVi.10.100 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgaḷ avananujarnūrvaruṁ bandu tannanorvanaṁ tāgidoḍa<br/>
nibarumaṁ viratharmāḍi bhāratamaninde sameyisuvenendu kōdaṇḍamaṁ bisuṭu<br/>
gadādaṇḍamaṁ bhujādaṇḍadoḷaḷavaḍisikoṇḍu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
kuru balamaṁ paḍalvaḍipa takkinoḷeytare barpa bīmanaṁ<br/>
bare baralīyadirdavaranāpadadoḷ peṟagikki gandhasiṁ<br/>
dhuraghaṭe nālku kōṭiverasāgaḍe bandu kaḷiṅgarājanāṁ<br/>
tire page keygevandu bardukāḍida balmuḷisiṁ vr̥kōdaraṁ // ViVi.10.101 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu kaḷiṅgarāja matta mātaṅga ghaṭegaḷa mēle muḷisaṁ kaḷevenendu<br/>
siṁhanādadinārdu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
gajeyaṁ bhōrene parvi bīsi kaḍupindeytandu māṟaunta sā<br/>
majasaṅghātamanondugoḷḷeraḍugoḷḷendurvi poyvondu po<br/>
ygejavaṅgundi siḍildu munnaḍiguruḷtarpannegaṁ bīḻe di<br/>
ggajamaṁ pōlva gajaṅgaḷaṁ palavumaṁ kondaṁ marunnandanaṁ // ViVi.10.102 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
baḍigoḷe bidu bibbara biri<br/>
doḍanuge posa muttu kōḍanūṟi madēbhaṁ<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 274]<br/>
keḍeduvu kolladirendira<br/>
daḍigeṟaguva teṟananinisananukarisuvinaṁ // ViVi.10.103 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu patteṇṭusāsiramāneyaṁ paḍalvaḍisiyuṁ sairisalāṟade—<br/>
</p>

<p>
piḍidondondaṟa gātramaṁ tiripikoṇḍondondaṟoḷ poydu me<br/>
lvaḍagappannegamettikoṇḍasagavoyvoyloḷ taḍamboydumu<br/>
ḷḷaḍaguṁ nettarumelvumella desegaṁ jīṟeḻdu pāṟēḻe ba<br/>
ldaḍigaṁ bīsiyumondu kōṭivaregaṁ kondaṁ madēbhaṅgaḷaṁ // ViVi.10.104 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
siḍilantormeye poyye poyda bharadindondāne tōl nettare<br/>
lvaḍagondondaṟoḷondumondade gadā nirghātadiṁ māyamā<br/>
doḍe pō tappidenendu palmoredagurvappannegaṁ mīseyaṁ<br/>
kaḍidaṁ tōḷvaladēḻge meccuvanitarkugrājiyoḷ bhīmanā // ViVi.10.105 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
dhvajamuṁ bisugeyumēṟi<br/>
rda jōdaruṁ berasu gajeyinari gaja ghaṭeyaṁ<br/>
gijigijiyāgire poydoḍe<br/>
gujugujugoṇḍārdaramararambara taḷadoḷ // ViVi.10.106 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu gāḷigoḍḍida ghana ghaṭeyante tanagoḍḍida kaḷiṅgarāja matta<br/>
mātaṅga ghaṭegaḷaṁ kaḻakuḻaṁ māḍidanannegamitta śalyana moneyoḷ dharmaputraṁ<br/>
kādi nālku kellambugaḷindātana varūtha sūta kētanaṅgaḷaṁ kaḍidu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
uramaṁ birivinamise ma<br/>
dra rājanaḷiyana parākramakkosedu mogaṁ<br/>
muriyade peṟatuṁ ratha[maṁ]<br/>
[tarisi kanaldaḍardu kadanakāgaḷe neṟedaṁ] // ViVi.10.107 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[muṟidu rathamaṁ]rathāśvama<br/>
nuṟade[raḍuṁ śarade]nālkaṟiṁ sūtananoṁ<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 275]<br/>
daṟikeya saraloḷ[māṇade]<br/>
taṟidaṁ paḻavigeyanēṁ kr̥tāstrano śalyaṁ // ViVi.10.108 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu virathanaṁ māḍi dharmaputranaṁ piḍiyaleytarpa madra rājanaṁ<br/>
pannirchāsiramāneverasu nr̥pana cakrarakṣakaṁ nīḷaneḍegoṇḍu tāgidāgaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
mr̥garāja nakhara bāṇā<br/>
ḷigaḷiṁ tegeneṟedu śalyanuṟadise biduvaṁ<br/>
mr̥garājaṅgaḷe pōḻvavo<br/>
lagalvinaṁ pōḻduvugra bāṇāvaḷigaḷ // ViVi.10.109 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antā dantighaṭeyaṁ paḍalvaḍisi nīḷanēṟidāneyumanūṟi<br/>
koṇḍeccāgaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
peṟagiḍuva dantiyaṁ kali<br/>
niṟisi calaṁ nelase tōṟikuḍuvudumāgaḷ<br/>
poṟamuyvuvaraṁ tegeneṟe<br/>
duṟadeccaṁ śalyanānta nīḷana taleyaṁ // ViVi.10.110 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu nīḷaṁ nīḷagiriya mēgaṇiṁ baṟasiḍil poḍeye keḍeva<br/>
mr̥garājanante hasti mastakadiṁ keḍevudumatta bhūriśravana moneyoḷ kāduttirdu<br/>
ttaraṁ nālvattu sāsiramāneverasarasanaṁ peṟagikki bandāntāgaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
nage pagevāḍi gōgrahaṇadoḷ poṟamāṟida bannamondu ne<br/>
ṭṭage manamaṁ paḷañcaleye māṇade śalyananandaśalyanaṁ<br/>
bagevavolēḷidaṁ bagedu dantiyanāgaḍe tōṟikoṭṭu to<br/>
ṭṭage rathamaṁ paḍalvaḍisi pūḻdanarātiyanastrakōṭiyiṁ // ViVi.10.111 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antuttaraṁ tanagaḷavumadaṭuṁ rājōttaramāge kādidoḍe śalyaṁ<br/>
virathanāgi siggāgi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 276]<br/>
tārakanaṁ guhaṁ muḷidu śaktiyināntiḍuvantarāti saṁ<br/>
hārakavappa visphurita śaktiyinātananiṭṭu khaḻgadiṁ<br/>
vāraṇamaṁ paḍalvaḍisi tāṁ peṟapiṅguvuduṁ balakke hā<br/>
hā ravamuṇme dantiverasājiyoḷuttaranaḻgitaḻgidaṁ // ViVi.10.112 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antuttaranaṁ javaṅge posatikkuvantikki basavaḻida śalyanaṁ kr̥tavarmaṁ<br/>
tanna rathamanēṟisikoṇḍu nindanannegamittalamarāpagāsutana moneyoḷ<br/>
bharaṅgeydu kāduva sēnānāyakaṁ śvētaṁ tanna tammanatītanādudaṁ kēḷdu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
praḷaya payōdhivōlaḷurdu peṅkuḷigoṇḍa madēbhavairivōl<br/>
keḷardu layāgnivōlaḷurdu madra mahīśananeyde tāge ba<br/>
ḷvaḷa baḷedattu śalyanoḷe kāḷegamīgaḷenuttumante ke<br/>
ykoḷalahikētu sindhutanayamberasāgaḍe bandu tāgidaṁ // ViVi.10.113 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
itta dharmaputranuṁ virāṭa dhr̥ṣṭadyumna śikhaṇḍi cēkitāna kēkaya sātyaki<br/>
nakuḷa sahadēva saubhadra pramukha nāyakarverasu raṇapaṭahaṅgaḷaṁ negaḻce kr̥pa<br/>
kr̥tavarma viviṁśati vikarṇa citrasēna sōmadatta bhagadatta bāhlīka bhūriśravaḥ<br/>
prabhr̥tigaḷ gaṟisannegaidu kāduvāgaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
naḍuva saral saralkoḷe suruḷva hayaṁ hayaduḷgaruḷgaḷoḷ<br/>
toḍarva bhaṭar bhaṭarkaḷoḷe toḻtuḻimāḻpa rathaṁ rathakke vā<br/>
ydaḍigiḍi meyvoṇarcuva mahāratharājiyoḷantagurvina<br/>
ccuḍidire kādi biccaḻisida‌r bisunettara suṭṭure sūsuvannegaṁ // ViVi.10.114 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
anteraḍuṁ paḍeya nāyakarorvarorvaroḷ talemaṭṭu kāduvāgaḷ<br/>
śvētaṁ tanna tammanaḻivinoḷāda muḷisinoḷ kaṇgāṇade śalyanaṁ muṭṭevandu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
muḷisinoḷeyde kempaḍarda kaṇgaḷinormeye nuṅguvantasuṁ<br/>
goḷe naḍe nōḍi māṇaduramaṁ biriyeccoḍe sūsi pāyvasr̥<br/>
gjaḷamavanugra kōpa śikhi taḷtaḷurvantevolāge śalyanā<br/>
gaḷe raṇadoḷ neṟaldoḍavanaṁ peṟagikki surāpagātmajaṁ // ViVi.10.115 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 277]<br/>
antu praḷayakāladandu mūḍuva pannirvarādityara tējamumaṁ<br/>
mahēśvara bhairavāḍambaramumaṁ yugānta kālāntakana masakamumaṁ<br/>
tannoḷaḷavaḍisikoṇḍu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
khara kiraṇa pracaṇḍa kiraṇāvaḷi lōkamaneyde parvuvaṁ<br/>
tire kaḍukeydu tanneraḍu keyyoḷamecca śarāḷigaḷ bhayaṁ<br/>
karataramāge bhū bhuvanamellamanormeye sutti mutti koṁ<br/>
ḍire desegāṇalāgadudalā raṇagaḻtale mandamādudō // ViVi.10.116 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
embinamambina bambaloḷaṁ jōḍāgi kōḍanūṟi keḍeda gajavrajaṅgaḷa<br/>
ḍoṇevugaḷindoṟetu pariva nettara kaḍalgaḷuṁ nettara kaḍalgaḷoḷ miḷirva<br/>
paḻavigegaḷ taledōṟe muḻuṅgida rathaṅgaḷuṁ rathaṅgaḷa gāligaḷgaḍḍamāgi<br/>
biḻdirda madahastigaḷuṁ madahasti mastakaṅgaḷanōsarisi rathamaṁ pariyisuva<br/>
rathacōdakaruṁ rathacōdakara biṭṭa bāy biṭṭantire biṭṭa tamma karuḷgaḷoḷ<br/>
tavetoḍardu kīḻaṁ karci diṇḍu maguḷdu keḍeva jātyaśvaṅgaḷuṁ jātyaśvaṅgaḷa<br/>
peṇada tintiṇiyoḷ toḍardeḍaputtumāḍuva subhaṭaraṭṭegaḷuṁ subhaṭaraṭṭe<br/>
gaḷaneḻbaṭṭi kuṭṭuva toṇḍu maruḷgaḷuṁ maruḷgaḷāṭamaṁ paḷapaḷanemeyikkade<br/>
nōḍi muguḷnage naguva vīra bhaṭara pandalegaḷumagurvumadbhuta bhayānaka<br/>
vīrabībhatsaraudrarasaṅgaḷaṁ puduṅgoḷisi gāṅgēyaṁ nāḍeyuṁ poḻtu kāde—<br/>
</p>

<p>
paṭṭaṅgaṭṭidiḷādhināthare payiñchāsirvaroḷḷānegaḷ<br/>
paṭṭaṅgaṭṭiduvondu lakka turagaṁ patteṇṭu lakkaṁ paḍa<br/>
lvaṭṭaḻkāḍiduvonde bilgene nadīputraṅge pēḻār calaṁ<br/>
baṭṭuṁ mārmaledambudoṭṭumuḻivar saṅgrāma raṅgāgradoḷ // ViVi.10.117 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
embannegaṁ śvētanumanavarata śarāsāradiṁ kurubalamellamanaredu<br/>
saṇṇisidante māḍi taveneraviyanenitaṁ kondoḍamēvandapudendu<br/>
gāṅgēyaṅgadiradidiraṁ mārkoṇḍu bilvoydu nindāgaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
śvētana billoḷirda madanāriya rūperdegoḷvuduṁ nadī<br/>
jātanudātta bhaktiyoḷe keymugidāgaḷidento nimma pe<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 278]<br/>
rmātina bīramīyeḍegevandude muppinoḷeyde lōka vi<br/>
khyātarirāgi keyduviḍivalliye kālviḍiyalke takkudē // ViVi.10.118 [utpalamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
enage raṇāgradoḷ poṇarvoḍaṅkada poṅkada sindhuputrano<br/>
rvane doreyendu nimmoḷe valaṁ taṟisandiṟiyalke pūṇdenā<br/>
nenagiṟivaḻtiyaṁ kiḍisi nimmaḷavaṁ peṟagikki nīmumiṁ<br/>
tiniterdegeṭṭiriṁ tuḻilasandaranārumanentu nambuvar // ViVi.10.119 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu tannaṁ nōye nuḍidoḍe sindhuputranintendaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
ninagēnendoḍamendudoppidapudantēkennaninnī śarā<br/>
sanadoḷ śūla kapāla pāṇi dayeyiṁ bandirdanuntānumiṁ<br/>
tinitaṁ nīṁ nuḍivannegaṁ taḍevenē trailōkyanāthaṁ kaṇā<br/>
vinamanmastakanādenaṇmuvoḍe nīnī dēvanaṁ tōṟuvai // ViVi.10.120 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
iṟivantu ninage manadoḷ<br/>
taṟisalavuṇṭappoḍelavo dēvēśananēṁ<br/>
seṟeviḍidetolagu dēvana<br/>
maṟeyaṁ baḻikaṟiyalakkumenagaṁ ninagaṁ // ViVi.10.121 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
embuduṁ śvētanintendaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
kāgevolintu bilge karamañjuvirañjalimā triṇētranaṁ<br/>
pō geḍegoṇḍu kāduvene kādenidaṁ haranittanendu nō<br/>
ḍāgaḍumaḻtiyiṁ piḍivenakkaṭa nimmanadirpuvalli cā<br/>
pāgamamēvudantenage bilvaramājiyoḷāmpa gaṇḍarār // ViVi.10.122 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
bisuṭeṁ billanadēvudendu kaḍupindīḍāḍi sūryaprabhā<br/>
prasaraṅgaḷ masuḷvannegaṁ poḷevudondaṁ śaktiyaṁ koṇḍagu<br/>
rvisi gāṅgēyananiṭṭaniṭṭoḍadanīraydastradindeccu khaṁ<br/>
ḍisi pērāḷ tiṟidikkidante taleyaṁ pōgeccanā śvētanā // ViVi.10.123 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 279]<br/>
śvētana bīramanupamā<br/>
tītamanī dharege negaḻe negaḻdudanidanāṁ<br/>
pātāḷakkaṟipuveneṁ<br/>
bī teṟadoḷe dinapanapara jalanidhigiḻidaṁ // ViVi.10.124 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgaḷeraḍuṁ paḍeya nāyakarapahāratūryaṅgaḷaṁ bājisi tamma tamma<br/>
bīḍugaḷge pōdarannegamitta saṁsaptaka balamanellamanonde rathadoḷāditya<br/>
nasuraranadirpuvantāṭandu vikramārjunanumarātikāḷānaḷanumatirathamathananuṁ<br/>
ripukuraṅga kaṇṭhīravanuṁ sāhasābharaṇanumammanagandhavāraṇanuṁ paḍemecce<br/>
gaṇḍanuṁ parasainyabhairavanumemba pesargaḷananvartha māḍi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
neredanurāgadiṁ paḍeya pāḍiya bīrara peṇḍiraḻkaṟiṁ<br/>
parasiyoṟaldusēsegaḷanikke murāriya pāñcajanya vi<br/>
sphurita ravaṁ jayōtsavada ghōṣaṇeyantire pokkanātma maṁ<br/>
diramanudāttacittanavanītaḷa pūjya guṇaṁ guṇārṇavaṁ // ViVi.10.125 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
idu vividha vibudha janavinuta jinapadāmbhōja<br/>
varaprasādōtpanna prasanna gambhīra vacana racana<br/>
catura kavitā guṇārṇava viracitamappa<br/>
vikramārjuna vijayadoḷ<br/>
daśamāśvāsaṁ<br/>
</p>

<p>
---------------------------------------------------------------------<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 280]<br/>
[ēkādaśāśvāsaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
śrīyuvatiyanā vīra<br/>
śrīyuvatige savatimāḻpeneṁdari nr̥paru<br/>
ḷḷāyaveraseḻedukoṇḍu dha<br/>
rāyuvatige negaḻda hariganorvane gaṇḍaṁ // ViVi.11.1 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
emba nija caritamaṁ pala<br/>
ruṁ baṇṇise kiviyanāntu kēḷuttumaḷuṁ<br/>
baṁ bīramenisi tanagidi<br/>
raṁ bandu kaḍaṅgi sattaraṁ pogaḻuttuṁ // ViVi.11.2 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu vikrānta tuṅganirpannegamittaleraḍuṁ paḍeya nāyakaraḻiye nonda<br/>
tammaṇugāḷgaḷa koṇḍāṭadānegaḷa naccina kuduregaḷa puṇgaḷanuḍiyalumōvaluṁ<br/>
mardubejjarumanaṭṭuttumikkida sannaṇaṅgaḷaṁ geldu kaṇakene pōgurci tamma<br/>
meyyoḷuḍidambugaḷumanelvaṁ naṭṭuḍida bāḷa kakkaḍeyuḍigaḷumanayaskāntamaṁ<br/>
tōṟi tegeyisuttuṁ vajramuṣṭiya poyloḷaṁ bāḷa kōḷoḷamuccaḷisida<br/>
kapāladōḍugaḷaṁ gaṅgegaṭṭuttuṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
unnata mastaka sthaḷadoḷambugaḷaḻduḍidirdoḍattami<br/>
ttanneṟe tandu baldaḍigariḻkuḻinoḷ kiḻe nondenennadaḥ<br/>
ennadaṇaṁ mogaṁ muriyadaḷkade bēnegaḷoḷ mogaṅgaḷaṁ<br/>
binnage māḍadirdaraḷavaccariyāge kelar mahārathar // ViVi.11.3 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
rasamosarvannegaṁ taguḷe pāḍuva gāṇara gēyamaḻkaṟaṁ<br/>
posayise sōṅkuvoldolisuvōpaḷa sōṅku podaḻdajādiyoḷ<br/>
masagida kampu kampanoḷakoṇḍalevondela[rembi]vandupā<br/>
ṟisuvuvudagra vīra bhaṭarāhava kēḷi pariśramaṅgaḷaṁ // ViVi.11.4 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 281]<br/>
āgaḷ dharmanandanaṁ mukundaṅge baḻiyanaṭṭi barisi namma<br/>
sēnānāyakanuttāyakanāgi gāṅgēyarindamaḻidaninnārge vīrapaṭṭamaṁ kaṭṭuvaṁ<br/>
pēḻimene—<br/>
</p>

<p>
bēḷveya koṇḍadoḷurcida<br/>
bāḷverasari balamanariyalendaṅkada ka<br/>
ṭṭāḷvīranati balaṁ nina<br/>
gāḷvesakendirdanalte dhr̥ṣṭadyumnaṁ // ViVi.11.5 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
embudumī kajjamenna manadoḷoḍambaṭṭa kajjamātane vīrapaṭṭakke<br/>
takkanendu dharmanandanaṁ drupadanandanaṅge baḻiyanaṭṭi barisi piridumosageverasu<br/>
tāne vīrapaṭṭamaṁ kaṭṭi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
ā samara mukhadoḷesevari<br/>
kēsariya virōdhi rudhira jalanidhivol saṁ<br/>
dhyāsamayameseye taḻataḻa<br/>
nēsaṟ mūḍuvudumoḍḍaṇakkeḻtandar‌ // ViVi.11.6 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antajātaśatru munname bandoḍḍi śatru bala jalanidhiyaḷḷāḍe viḷaya<br/>
kāḷāniḷane bīsuvante keyvīsidāgaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
caturaṅgaṁ caturaṅga sainyadoḷaḍu[rtuṁ]tiṟraneytandu tā<br/>
gi taḍaṁmeṭṭade kāde bāḷgaḷuḍigaḷjīṟeḻdumārtāgiśō<br/>
ṇita dhārāḷigaḷurci perci siḍiyal tēṅkal vimānaṅgaḷa<br/>
ḷki taguḷdāgaḷe mattamatta taḷardar dēvar nabhōbhāgadoḷ // ViVi.11.7 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgaḷeraḍuṁ paḍeya nāyakarondorvaroḷ tāgi kiḍiguṭṭidante<br/>
kāduvāgaḷabhimanyu ugra tējanappa magadha tanūjananondepāṟeyambinoḷ<br/>
keyya kūsanikkuvantikkuvuduṁ neppiṅge neppugoḷḷade māṇenembante bakāsurana<br/>
maganaḷambhūṣanarjunana maganiḷāvantananantaka lōkamaneydisuvuduṁ<br/>
ghaṭōtkacaniḷāvantana sāvaṁ kaṇḍu sairisadaḷambhūṣananeḻbaṭṭuvudu mavanaḷki<br/>
bhagadattanāneya maṟeyaṁ puguvudumaḷambhūṣanaṁ pintikki bhagadattaṁ<br/>
ghaṭōtkacanaṁ mārkoṇḍu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 282]<br/>
utkōpa dahanadoḍane pr̥<br/>
ṣatkaṅgaḷkōṭi gaṇitadinduṟuvinamā<br/>
rdutkaca ditijananuṟade gha<br/>
ṭōtkacanaṁ biḻdu mūrchevōpinameccaṁ // ViVi.11.8 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
annegaṁ vr̥kōdaraṁ caturdaśabhuvanaṅgaḷellamaṁ teraḷci tēraisi<br/>
nuṅguvantu masakadiṁ bhagadattanaṁ mārkoṇḍu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
isuvudumecca śāta śara santatiyaṁ bhagadattaneyde khaṁ<br/>
ḍisi rathamaṁ paḍalvaḍise maccaradiṁ gajegoṇḍu tāge mā<br/>
ṇisalamarāpagāsutanidircuvuduṁ rathamaḻge poydu śaṁ<br/>
kisadidirānta saindhavanumaṁ pavanātmajanōḍe kādidaṁ // ViVi.11.9 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu kāde sindhurājana bembaladoḷ kādalendu banda nūrvar<br/>
kauravaruṁ bhīmanoḷ tāge tāgida bēgadiṁ durdharṣaṇa durmarṣaṇa<br/>
dīrghabāhu mahābāhu citrōpacitra nandopananda‌r modalāge mūvattu<br/>
mūvaraṁ javaṅge birdanikkuvantikki mattinuḻidarumanuḻiyalīyade<br/>
baḻisandāgaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
modaliṭṭaṁ kolalendu kauravaraninnēkirpanārdurci mu<br/>
kkadivaṅgāṁkarameyde kūrpenivaruṁ sattapparindiṅge kā<br/>
vudanāṁ kāvenenutte bēṟe rathamaṁ bandēṟi pō pōgaleṁ<br/>
doduṟuttuṁ paritandu tāgitagardagaṅgāsutaṁ bhīmanaṁ // ViVi.11.10 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
annegamatta saṁsaptaka balamellamanaḷaṟe peḷaṟe kivuḻiduḻidu kolvalli<br/>
vikramārjunaṁ murāntakanoḷintendaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
praḷaya payōdhi nādamane pōltu raṇānaka rāvamīgaḷa<br/>
ggaḷamesedappudattakaṟevambina balsariyindamā diśā<br/>
vaḷi masuḷdintu nīḷdapudu pōgade kāduva gaṇḍarilla ni<br/>
nnaḷiyanumā vr̥kōdaranumalladarilla peṟar murāntakā // ViVi.11.11 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
guru guruputra śalya bhagadatta nadīsutaremba sanda bī<br/>
rare maṟuvakkamaṇṇanoḍanirvare kūsugaḷemba śaṅkeyuṁ<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 283]<br/>
piridenagīgaḷādapudu māṇade cōdisu bēgamattala<br/>
tta rathamanendu bhōrgareye bandanarātige miḻtu barpavōl // ViVi.11.12 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu nelanadire barpa vikramārjunana baraviṅge kurubalamella<br/>
mollanulidōḍi surāpagānandanana maṟeyaṁ pokkāgaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
eḍegoṇḍaṅkada śalya saindhava kr̥pa drōṇarkaḷuṁ sāyakaṁ<br/>
giḍe tannecca śarāḷigaḷ vilaya kālōlkaṅgaḷaṁ tāgidā<br/>
gaḍe tatsūta rathāśva kētana śaravrātaṅgaḷuṁ nurgi ka<br/>
ṇgiḍe bennaṭṭidanantu namma harigaṁ gaṇḍaṁ peṟar gaṇḍarē // ViVi.11.13 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antatiratha samaratha mahārathārdharatharkaḷanāne meṭṭida kuḷumpeya<br/>
nīrante dese desege kedaṟuvannameḻbaṭṭidāgaḷ sōlta tanna balamanaḷumbamāda<br/>
vikramārjunana bhujabalamumaṁ kaṇḍu kanaka tāḷadhvajaṅge pannagadhvajanintendaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
muḷiye binnapamajja dāyigaroḷ virōdhamanintu ba<br/>
ḷvaḷane māḻpudanandu nimmane nambi māḍidenintu gō<br/>
vaḷiganaṁ geḍegoṇḍu muṁ baḷedoṭṭa pēḍiye nimmaniṁ<br/>
tiḷisi madbalamellamaṁ kole nōḍutirpudu pāḻiyē // ViVi.11.14 [taraḷaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
mēḷadoḷentuṁ pō peṟa<br/>
rāḷaṁ chidrisuvevemba pāṇḍavaroḷ nīṁ<br/>
mēḷisi naṇpane bagedir<br/>
jōḷada pāḻiyumaninisu bageyiṁ nimmoḷ // ViVi.11.15 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
embuduṁ sindhutanūjanintendaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
trijagakkaṁ guru dēvanādi puruṣaṁ kēḷorvanorvaṁ ripu<br/>
dhvajinī dhvaṁsakanāgi sanda kaliyuṁ billāḷuminnendoḍeṁ<br/>
tu jagatkhyātaranēḷipai maṟevenē muṁ pūṇdudaṁ bil rathaṁ<br/>
dhvajamambembivaneyde sandhisu jasaṁ nilvannegaṁ kāduveṁ // ViVi.11.16 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
embudumanēka śarabharita śakaṭa sahasramanondumāḍi gāṅgēyana<br/>
peṟage nilisidāgaḷamarāpagānandananumamarēndranandananumorvarorvaraṁ<br/>
[p. 284]<br/>
gaṟisannegeydu kāduvāgaḷambara taḷadoḷellaṁ biḷiya mugilgaḷa caupaḷigegaḷoḷ<br/>
bandirda dēva vimānaṅgaḷumoḍanoḍane kalaṅke kula girigaḷuṁ dikkarigaḷu<br/>
moḍanoḍane tāgidante tāgidāgaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
upamātītada billa balme samasandondorvaroḷ parve pa<br/>
rvi paravyūha bhayaṅkaraṁ negedu pārdārdeccoḍambambana<br/>
ṭṭi paḷañcutte siḍilda tōragiḍiyindondondaṟoḷ bēvuduṁ<br/>
tripurambottisidante potti pogedattettaṁ viyanmaṇḍaḷaṁ // ViVi.11.17 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu brahmāṇḍamuriye kāde—<br/>
</p>

<p>
naḍapidanajjanendu vijayaṁ kaḍukeydisanenna maṁmanāṁ<br/>
naḍapidanendu sindhutanayaṁ kaḍukeydisanintu pāḍugā<br/>
doḍanoḍanirvaruṁ meṟeyalende śarāsana vidyeyiṁ paḍa<br/>
lvaḍisidarettamittamidiroḷ maledoḍḍida cāturaṅgamaṁ // ViVi.11.18 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu kiṟidu poḻtu keygādu kāde saritsutana suriva sarala<br/>
maḻeyoḷaḻida nija varūthiniya sāvuṁ nōvumēvamaṁ māḍe—<br/>
</p>

<p>
munideraḍambinoḷ rathamumaṁ padavillumaneyde pārdu ne<br/>
kkane kaḍidindra nandananaḷurkeyinārdoḍe divya sindhu naṁ<br/>
dananiradēṟi bēṟe rathamaṁ peṟatondu śarāsanakke me<br/>
llane niḍudōḷanuydu karamaccariyāge kaḍaṅgikādidaṁ // ViVi.11.19 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu tōḍuṁ bīḍuṁ kāṇalāgaderdegāya[lekka]yinembattu nālku lakka<br/>
baṇḍiyoḷ taṇḍa taṇḍade tīvidakāṇḍa praḷayānaḷa visphuliṅgōpamānaṅgaḷappa<br/>
niśita kāṇḍaṅgaḷindoḍḍida caturbalaṅgaḷa meyyoḷ rōma rōmandappade<br/>
naḍuvannameccu payiñchāsirvar makuṭabaddharumanondu lakka madadāneyumaṁ<br/>
mūṟu lakka rathamumanondu kōṭi turuṣka turaṅgaṅgaḷumaṁ padineṇṭu<br/>
kōṭi padātiyumanalasade pēsēḻe kondu paraśurāmanalli paḍeda<br/>
divyāstraṅgaḷanondanondu sūḻoḷe toṭṭu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
nuḍivaḷige narana rathamaṁ<br/>
paḍuveṇgāvuduvaraṁ siḍilvinamecca<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 285]<br/>
ccuḍiye bhujabalade hariyura<br/>
deḍeyaṁ biriyeccu meṟedanaḷavaṁ bhīṣmaṁ // ViVi.11.20 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
dēvāsuradoḷamindina<br/>
nōvaṁ nondaṟiyenuḻida keyduvinoḷivaṁ<br/>
sāvane seragaṁ bagedoḍe<br/>
sāvādapudendu cakri cakradoḷiṭṭaṁ // ViVi.11.21 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
iṭṭoḍe tanagasurāriya<br/>
koṭṭa mahā vaiṣṇavāstramaṁ gāṅgēyaṁ<br/>
toṭṭisuvudumeraḍuṁ kiḍi<br/>
guṭṭi siḍil siḍiyepōrduvambarataḷadoḷ // ViVi.11.22 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
pōrvudumiṁ peṟatambiṁ<br/>
tīrvude pageyendu pāśupatamaṁ piḍiyal<br/>
pārvudumarjunanāgaḷ<br/>
bērverasu kiḻalke bageye surareḍevokkar // ViVi.11.23 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
ā prastāvadoḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
ennumanasurāriya piḍi<br/>
vunnata karacakramendu bhīṣmaṁ taṟiguṁ<br/>
munnamaḍaṅguvenembavo<br/>
lannegamastācaḷasthanādaṁ dinapaṁ // ViVi.11.24 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgaḷeraḍuṁ paḍegaḷapahāra tūryaṅgaḷaṁ bājisimunnottidavēḷegaḷ<br/>
samudraṅgaḷaṁ puguvante tantamma bīḍugaḷaṁ pokkarāgaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
barisi manegasura vairiya<br/>
narasaṁ bhīṣmaṅge cakramintēke mogaṁ<br/>
diridudo nimmaṁ piḍidena<br/>
garidenalariduṇṭe dhuradoḷēnasurārī // ViVi.11.25 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 286]<br/>
besasene nuḍidaṁ muraneṁ<br/>
basurananenagāgi kādi bhīṣmaṁ piḍido<br/>
ppisidoḍe vaiṣṇava bāṇama<br/>
nosedittenadaṁ gelalkekeydugaḷoḷavē // ViVi.11.26 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
bhēdadoḷallade gelalari<br/>
dādaṁ surasindhusutananindiruḷoḷ nīṁ<br/>
bhēdisene nr̥patiyorvane<br/>
ādaradiṁ bandu sindhusutanaṁ kaṇḍaṁ // ViVi.11.27 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
kaṇḍu poḍevaṭṭu nayamerde<br/>
goṇḍire pati nuḍidanenage dēvar kaluṣaṁ<br/>
goṇḍāgaḷ kāvar kaṇe<br/>
goṇḍavolendemba mātinantāgiradē // ViVi.11.28 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
toṁmbaysāsirvar ni<br/>
mmambina bambaloḷe makuṭabaddhar‌ maḍidar<br/>
nambiṁ nambalimindiṁ<br/>
gombattu dinaṁ dalemma bennale nindir‌ // ViVi.11.29 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
cakriya cakradoḷaṁ toḍa<br/>
rdākramisidudecca nija patatri dalene ni<br/>
mmī krama kamalakkeṟagade<br/>
vakrisi bhūcakradoḷage bāḻvarumoḷarē // ViVi.11.30 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
sāve nimaticceyene poṇa<br/>
rdāvaṁ taḷtiṟidu gelvanemagadaṟiṁdaṁ<br/>
sāvu diṭaṁ nimmaḍi kole<br/>
sāvudu lēsalte sugativaḍeyalkakkuṁ // ViVi.11.31 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endoḍadellamaneyde kēḷdu karuṇārasahr̥dayanāgi mammana mogamaṁ<br/>
kūrmeyiṁ nōḍi kaṇṇa nīraṁ negapi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
jagadoḷavadhyanaṁgelale bāradadādoḍamēṁ śikhaṇḍi to<br/>
ṭṭage koḷe bandu munde nile sāvenagappudu nāḷinondu kā<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 287]<br/>
ḷegadoḷidaṁ naraṅgaṟipadī teṟadiṁ negaḻdeyde vīra la<br/>
kṣmige neleyāgu pōgene nr̥paṁ poḍevaṭṭu manōnurāgadiṁ // ViVi.11.32 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
bandu mandaradharaṅge tadvr̥ttāntamanellamanaṟipi niścinta mananāgi<br/>
pavaḍisidāgaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
cala caladāntu kāduva suyōdhana sādhanadoḍḍugaḷ kaḻa<br/>
ldalaṟi teraḷdu tūḷdu biṟutōḍe guṇārṇavanindamājiyoḷ<br/>
kolisi samasta dhātriyumanāḷipavendulivante pakkigaḷ<br/>
cilimiliyemba poḻtaṟoḷe banduṟadoḍḍidanantakātmajaṁ // ViVi.11.33 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgaḷ kurudhvajiniyumanēka śaṅkha kāhaḷa bhērī paṇava jhallarī mr̥daṅga<br/>
tūryaṅgaḷantakālāntaka vikaṭāṭṭahāsaṅgaḷembante moḻage maledu bandoḍḍi<br/>
nindāgaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
ubhaya baladarasugaḷ raṇa<br/>
rabhasaṅgaḷverasu muḷidu keyvīse laya<br/>
kṣubhita jalanidhi ninādama<br/>
nabhinayisidudogedu negeda samarārāvaṁ // ViVi.11.34 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
isuva dhanurdharariṁ pā<br/>
yisuva daḻaṅgaḷinagurvu parvuvinaṁ cō<br/>
disuva rathaṅgaḷineṇṭuṁ<br/>
dese masuḷvinamiṟiduvāgaḷubhaya balaṅgaḷ // ViVi.11.35 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
aḻidaḻgida kari ghaṭegaḷa<br/>
baḷagadinuccaḷisi moreva nettarateregaḷ<br/>
suḻisuḻidoḍavariduvu ka<br/>
lpaḻiyoḷ bhōrgaredu pariva toṟegaḷa teṟadiṁ // ViVi.11.36 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu cāturdantamondondaṟoḷōrante naḍuvagalvaraṁ kāduvuduṁ<br/>
nāvindinanuvaramananibarumondāgi bhīṣmaroḷ kāduvamendu samakaṭṭi<br/>
dharmaputraṁ kadanatriṇētranaṁ mundiṭṭu samasta balamberasu kāduva samakaṭṭaṁ<br/>
duryōdhananaṟidu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 288]<br/>
kurubalamembudī suranadījana tōḷvalamemba vajra paṁ<br/>
jaradoḷagirdu baḻdapudu pāṇḍava sainyamumindu bhīṣmaro<br/>
rvaroḷiradāntu kādalavaraṁ peṟagikki kaḍaṅgi kādi ni<br/>
ttarisuvenendu pāṇḍava balakkidiraṁ taṟisandu tāgidaṁ // ViVi.11.37 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu tāguvuduṁ sātyaki kr̥tavarmanoḷ yudhiṣṭhiraṁ śalyanoḷ<br/>
saubhadranaśvatthāmanoḷ sahadēvaṁ śakuniyoḷ nakulaṁ citrasēnanoḷ cēkitānaṁ<br/>
saindhavanoḷ ghaṭōtkacaṁ kr̥panoḷ bhīmasēnaṁ kauravanoḷ kaḷiṅgarājaṁ<br/>
pāñcāḷarājanoḷ atirathamathanaṁ drōṇācāryaroḷ avaravaroḷadira<br/>
dāntāgaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
naḍuviḍuvurcuvārdariva nērvapaḷañcuva pōrva bāṇadiṁ<br/>
duḍidu siḍildu sūsiyakaḻaldu baḻaldu saḍildu jōldu nē<br/>
lduḍida nogaṁ dhvajaṁ palage kīl kavaraccu turaṅgamaṁ rathaṁ<br/>
kiḍe kavarindagurvanoḷakoṇḍire taḷtiṟidar mahārathar // ViVi.11.38 [campakamāle]<br/>

<p>
antu kiḍiguṭṭidante taḷtiṟiye jagadēkamallaṅge mārmaleyalāṟade<br/>
kurubalamellamollanulidōḍi bhīṣmara maṟeyaṁ pokkāgaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
dhavaḷa hayaṁ dhavaḷa rathaṁ<br/>
dhavaḷōṣṇīṣaṁśaśāṅka saṅkāśa yaśō<br/>
dhavaḷita bhuvanaṁ tāgida<br/>
navayavadiṁ bandu dharmatanayana baladoḷ // ViVi.11.39 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu tāgida sindhunandanana kōpaśikhi śikhākaḷāpaṅgaḷoḷ<br/>
puḍupuḍanaḻgisāyalendu pāyva pataṅgaṅgaḷante sōmakaśrījaya pramukha<br/>
nāyakarondakṣōhiṇī balamberasu bharaṅgeydāntoḍe—<br/>
</p>

<p>
śarasandhānada bēgamambugaḷanaṁmbīmbante mēṇambinā<br/>
garamembantene pāyvarāti śara saṅghātaṅgaḷaṁ nurgi nē<br/>
rdaridaṭṭumbarigoṇḍu kūḍe kaḍidantā sainyamaṁ parvi gō<br/>
ḻmurigoṇḍurviduvā rasātaḷamumaṁ gāṅgēyanastrāḷigaḷ // ViVi.11.40 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>

<p>
[p. 289]<br/>
antu bhīṣmaṁ grīṣmakāladādityanante kāydantakāladantakanante keḷardu<br/>

makuṭabaddharaṁ kondāgaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
maṇimakuṭāḷigaḷverasuruḷda narēndra śiraṅgaḷoḷphaṇā<br/>
maṇigaḷa dīptigaḷ beḷage dhātriyanoyyane kaṇḍi māḍi kaṇ<br/>
taṇivinamandu nindiṟida koḷguḷanaṁ naḍe nōḻpahīndraroḷ<br/>
seṇasiduvendoḍēvogaḻvudērvesanaṁ surasindhu putranā // ViVi.11.41 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu sōmaka balamellamaṁ pēḻe pesarilladantu kondu śrī jaya<br/>

mallaṁ modalāge virāṭa virāṭaja drupada drupadaja cēkitāna yudhāmanyūtta<br/>
mōjassaubhadra ghaṭōtkaca bhīmasēna nakula sahadēva sātyaki pañcapāṇḍava<br/>
pramukha nāyakarellarumberasu dharmaputraṁ śikhaṇḍiyaṁ mundiṭṭukoṇḍu bandu<br/>

</p>

<p>
ambaramellamambinoḷe pūḻe mahībhujarettamecca ki<br/>
ttambugaḷettamavvaḷise māṇadavaṁ kaḍidikki tanna na<br/>
llambugaḷindamārdiradaḍurtise bhūbhujarellamalli bi<br/>
lluṁ beṟagāge bandu poṇardaṁ seragillade vikramārjunaṁ // ViVi.11.42 [utpalamālike]<br/>

<p>
antu poṇardāgaḷemma mammaṅgamemagamīgaḷanuvaraṁ dore<br/>
yāytendu paraśurāmana koṭṭa divyāstraṅgaḷanondanoṁdusūḻoḷe<br/>

</p>

<p>
jvaḷana patatriyaṁ kaḍidu vāruṇa patriyinaindra bāṇamaṁ<br/>
kaḷedu samīraṇāstradinidircida bhūbhujarellaraṁ bhayaṁ<br/>
goḷisi niśāta vajriśaradiṁ surarambaradoḷ taguḷdu bi<br/>
ccaḷise nadījanuccaḷise kādidanēṁ kaliyō guṇārṇavaṁ // ViVi.11.43 [campakamāle]<br/>

<p>
antamōghāstra dhanañjayaṁ tannamōghāstraṅgaḷaṁ kaḍidoḍe sāmānyāstraṁ<br/>
gaḷoḷ dharmaputraṅge tanna nuḍida nuḍivaḷiyaṁ nenedallaḷigāḷegaṅgāde—<br/>

<p>
[p. 290]<br/>
kaḍidanudagranāyakara sāyakamellamanā śikhaṇḍi po<br/>
kkaḍigiḍe bandu munde nileyuṁ mogamaṁ naḍe nōḍiyātanā<br/>
rdoḍanoḍaneccoḍecca moneyambugaḷaḻgiḍivōgeyuṁ manaṁ<br/>
giḍanavanāṅkegoḷḷanagiyaṁ sugiyaṁ sura sindhunandanaṁ // ViVi.11.44 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
idu raṇamennoḷāntiṟiva meygaliyuṁsamaraikamēruve<br/>
nnadaṭumaḷurkeyuṁ piridu pēḍigadentidirāmpenendaṇaṁ<br/>
bedaṟade naṭṭa kūrgaṇeya biṇpoṟeyinde baḻaldanurvi pe<br/>
rvidira siḍimbinoḷ pudidadondu kuḷācaḷadante sindhujaṁ // ViVi.11.45 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
tintiṇiyāge naṭṭa kaṇeyoḷ nela muṭṭade meyyoḷattami<br/>

ddhāntada śāsanaṁ bareda pottageyantamarāpagātmajaṁ // ViVi.11.46 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
naḍedudu bāḷakāladoḷe toṭṭenagaṅkada śaucavīgaḷō<br/>
gaḍipude muṭṭi nāṁ nelananēkadupeṇgaḍimendu meyyoḷa<br/>
ḻdiḍida vikarṇa kōṭiyoḷaṇaṁ nela muṭṭade nōḍe biḻdoḍaṁ<br/>
baḍisidanayya śauca guṇadunnatiyaṁ sura sindhunandanaṁ // ViVi.11.47 [campakamāle]<br/>

<p>
antu śarapañjaradoḷoṟagiyumoḍaliṁ pattuviṭṭu pōpa jīvamaṁ<br/>
pōgalīyade svacchandamiḻtuvappudaṟinduttarāyaṇaṁ barpanna mirisida<br/>
nantumāgaḷ kurubalamellaṁ kurukuḷavanasiṁhaṁ śarapañjaradoḷoṟagida<br/>
ninnemmaṁ kāvarārendollanulidōḍi bīḍaṁ pokkāgaḷ dharmaputraṁ nijānuja<br/>
sahitaṁ bandu balagoṇḍu kāla mēle kavidu paṭṭu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
karuṇadinemmaṁtāyvōl<br/>
taruvaligaḷaneyde naḍapidajjar nīmiṁ<br/>
tireyuṁ nōḍidevēnema<br/>
gara[sike]yō pēḻimendu śōkaṅgeydar // ViVi.11.48 [kandaṁ]<br/>

<p>
[p. 291]<br/>
antu śōkaṅgeydoḍe nīmantenalvēḍa kṣatriyadharmamintadarkaḻalvēḍa<br/>

<p>
iṟivudanānta mārvalamaninnegamaccariyāge tāgi ta<br/>
ḷtiṟidiridondavasthe nimagennaya karmadinādudendoḍiṁ<br/>
maṟevudu kanda pāṇḍavara vairamanennoḍavōke kōpamuṁ<br/>
kaṟupumoḍambaḍēvudadaninnumoḍambaḍu sandhimāḍuveṁ // ViVi.11.49 [campakamāle]<br/>

<p>
embuduṁ duryōdhananintendaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
adaṭinaḷurkeyaṁ baladaḷurkeyumaṁ geḍegoṇḍu nīmidā<br/>
vudu paḍemātanintu nuḍidir‌ puduvāḻkeyoḷenna baḷkida<br/>
ḷkida bagegaṇḍirē magane nīṁ pageyaṁ taṟidoṭṭu neṭṭane<br/>
nnade bagegeṭṭu dāyigaroḷiṁ maguḻduṁ puduvāḻvudembirē // ViVi.11.50 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
embudumillindaṁ mēlāda kajjamaṁ nīne balle bīḍiṅge<br/>
bijayaṅgeyyimene poḍevaṭṭu suyōdhanaṁ pōdanāgaḷ—<br/>

<p>
nereda virōdhi nāyakaranāhavadoḷ taṟidoṭṭalondido<br/>
ḍḍuruḷvinamā guṇārṇavanaḍurtiṟidalli siḍilda nettaroḷ<br/>
poredu nirantaraṁ polasu nāṟuva meyyane karcalendu ce<br/>
ccaramaparāmburāśigiḻivantiḻidaṁ kamaḷaikabāndhavaṁ // ViVi.11.51 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgaḷ duryōdhananātmīya sēnānāyakanappa gāṅgēyaṁ bidira<br/>
siḍimbina podaṟoḷage maṟedoṟagida mr̥garājanante śaraśayanadoḷoṟagidaṁ<br/>
kadanatriṇētrananentu gelvenendu cintisi mantraśāleyaṁ pokku karṇa drōṇa<br/>
kr̥pa kr̥tavarmāśvatthāma śalya śakuni saindhava bhūriśravaḥ prabhr̥tigaḷgellaṁ<br/>
baḻiyanaṭṭi barisi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
āytēsādhisikoṇḍu pāṇḍusutaraṁ naṇpiṅge bennittu dal<br/>
saytāytajjana mātu namma paḍeyaṁ kāvannarinnāro su<br/>
ṣṭhītaṁkāvoḍe karṇanakkumadaṟiṁ nāmellamātaṅge ni<br/>
rdvaitaṁ bīrada bīravaṭṭamanidaṁ nirvyājadiṁ kaṭṭuvaṁ // ViVi.11.52 [śārdūlavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 292]<br/>
embuduṁ karṇanintendaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
surasindhūdbhavaniṁ baḻikke peṟarār sēnādhipatyakketa<br/>
kkare lōkaikadhanurdharaṁ kaḷaśajaṁ takkaṁ nadīnandanaṁ<br/>
ge raṇakkāṁ neramādenappoḍinitēkādappudī poḻte po<br/>
ḻtiravēḍīvudu bīravaṭṭamanadaṁ drōṇaṅge nīṁ bhūpatī // ViVi.11.53 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu bhīṣmādanantaraṁ drōṇayembudu parāśara vacanamene karṇana<br/>
nuḍigoḍambaṭṭu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
visasana raṅgakkānire<br/>
besagoḷvude peṟaranendu jaya paṭahaṅgaḷ<br/>
desedesegesevinegaṁ ka<br/>
ṭṭisikoṇḍaṁ bīravaṭṭamaṁ kaḷaśabhavaṁ // ViVi.11.54 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu kumbhasambhavananēka śātakumbha kumbhasambhr̥ta maṅgaḷa gaṅgā<br/>
jalaṅgaḷiṁ pavitrīkr̥ta gātranāgi kaurava baḷāgragaṇyanāgirdanitta tadvr̥ttānta<br/>
manellamanajātaśatru kēḷdu janārdananoḍane ripubaḷa mardanōpāyamaṁ<br/>
samakaṭṭutirpannegaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
adaṭaṁ sindhutanūbhavaṁ vijayanoḷ mārkoṇḍaṇaṁ kādalā<br/>
ṟade bembiḻdoḍe kādalendu besanaṁ pūṇdaṁ gaḍaṁ drōṇanaṁ<br/>
taduvaṁ nōḍuvenendu kaṇ taṇivinaṁ nōḍalke barpante baṁ<br/>
dudayādrīndramanēṟe bhānu poṟamaṭṭoḍḍittanīkārṇavaṁ // ViVi.11.55 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgaḷ pāṇḍava balada sēnānāyakaṁ dhr̥ṣṭadyumnanoḍḍida vajravyūhakke<br/>
padmavyūhamanoḍḍi tadvyūhada monege vandu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
śōṇāśvaṅgaśaḷ rajata rathamaṁ poḍe kumbhadhvajaṁ gī<br/>
rvāṇāvāsambaramaḍare māḻoḍḍudal sāladennī<br/>
bāṇāvāsakkenutumaḷavaṁ bīṟutuṁ bilge jāṇaṁ<br/>
drōṇaṁ nindaṁ masagi tiruputtondu kūrambanāgaḷ // ViVi.11.56 [mandākrāntaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
ā sakaḷa dharādhīśara<br/>
bīsuva kuñcamane pārdu bīsaloḍaṁ ke<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 293]<br/>
yvīsaloḍamaṟidu tāgidu<br/>
vāsukaraṁ berasu taḍeyadubhaya balaṅgaḷ // ViVi.11.57 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu cāturdantamondondaṟoḷ tāgi taḷtiṟivalli talegaḷ paṟiye<br/>
barigaḷ muṟiye toḍegaḷuḍiye puṇgaḷ suliye—<br/>
</p>

<p>
oḍane nabhambaraṁ siḍilva pandale sūsuva kaṇḍadiṇḍegaḷ<br/>
toḍare teraḷda nettara kaḍal neṇadoḷgesaṟoḷ jigiltagu<br/>
rvaḍare nirantaraṁ poḷeva bāḷuḍi suyva nava vraṇaṅgaḷoḷ<br/>
poḍare podaḻdudadbhuta bhayānakamāhava raṅgabhūmiyoḷ // ViVi.11.58 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgaḷeraḍuṁ balada sēnānāyakarondorvaroḷ kāduvāgaḷ<br/>
kumbhasambhavaṁ dharmaputrana moneyoḷ bharaṅgeydu kāduvāgaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
dhvajamaṁ khaṇḍisi pūṇdubāṇadoḷe dhr̥ṣṭadyumnanaṁ neṭṭano<br/>
ṭṭajeyiṁ tūḷdi śikhaṇḍiyaṁ drupadanaṁ kāypindamēsāḍi mi<br/>
kku javaṁ kolvavolātaniṁ kiṟiyaraṁ pannorvaraṁ kondu ma<br/>
tsyajanaṁ māṇade kondanonde śaradiṁ niśyaṅkanaṁ śaṅkanaṁ // ViVi.11.59 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgaḷ sālvala dēśadarasaṁ cēkitsaṁ praḷaya kālada mēgha ghaṭegaḷenisu<br/>
vanēkānēkapa ghaṭegaḷverasarasanaṁ peṟagikkibandu tāgidāgaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
ōronde pāreyambino<br/>
ḷōronde gajēndramuruḷe tege neṟedecce<br/>
ccōraṇadoḷ cēkitsana<br/>
nārumagurvise ghaṭōdbhavaṁ taṟidārdaṁ // ViVi.11.60 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu pāṇḍava balamellamanallakallōlaṁ māḍi kaḷaśakētananajāta<br/>
śatruvaṁ piḍiyaleytarpāgaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
kādal saṁsaptakarkaḷ karedoḍavara bennaṁ taguḷdāda kāypiṁ<br/>
kāduttirpātanantā kaḷakaḷamanadaṁ kēḷdu bhōrendu bande<br/>
ccā divyāstraṅgaḷiṁ tammovajarugiye tammaṇṇanaṁ śauryadindaṁ<br/>
kādaṁ muṁbijjanaṁkādariganuḻidaraṁ kāvudēṁ cōdyamāytē // ViVi.11.61 [sragdhare]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 294]<br/>
āgaḷ mārtāṇḍaṁ pracaṇḍamārtāṇḍana śara nikara sphurita kiraṇaṅgaḷ<br/>
kaviye tanna kiraṇaṅgaḷ masuḷdaparajaḷanidhigiḻidanāgaḷeraḍuṁ paḍegaḷapahāra<br/>
tūryaṅgaḷaṁ bājisidāgaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
paḍegaḷeraḍuṁ bīḍiṅgettaṁ teraḷdu negaḻteyaṁ<br/>
paḍedaḻidaraṁ meccuttutsāhadiṁ pogaḻuttumo<br/>
ḷpaḍare nuḍiyuttantirdādityanandudayādriya<br/>
ttaḍare poṟamaṭṭāgaḷ bandoḍḍi ninduvu kōpadiṁ // ViVi.11.62 [hariṇīplutaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antoḍḍi ninda cātu<br/>
rdantaṁ keyvīsuvannegaṁ sairisadō<br/>
rante peṇediṟiduvante di<br/>
gantāntamaneydi pariye nettara toṟegaḷ // ViVi.11.63 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
aḻgida bilvaḍe māṇade<br/>
taḻgida rathameydebagidapuṇgaḷa poṟeyiṁ<br/>
moḻgida kari ghaṭe javanaḍu<br/>
vaḻgeyananukarise vīra bhaṭa raṇaraṅgaṁ // ViVi.11.64 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgaḷ dhr̥ṣṭakētu vr̥ṣasēnanoḷ sātyaki bhagadattanoḷ drupada<br/>
dhr̥ṣṭadyumnarirvaruṁ drōṇācāryanoḷ prativindhyaṁ saubalanoḷ<br/>
ghaṭōtkacaṁ karṇanoḷ peṇedu kāde—<br/>
</p>

<p>
posa maseyambugaḷ desegaḷaṁ masuḷvannegameydepāye pā<br/>
yisuva rathaṅgaḷā rathada kīlmuṟidāgaḷe keyyanalli kō<br/>
desaguva sūtarambu koḷe sūtaruruḷdumiḷātaḷakke pā<br/>
ydasiyeḷe tāgi taḷtiṟiva niccaṭaroppidārājiraṅgadoḷ // ViVi.11.65 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgaḷ kaḷiṅgarājana gajaghaṭegaḷanitumondāgi bhīmasēnana rathamaṁ<br/>
viḷaya kāḷa jaḷadharaṅgaḷellamondāgi kulagiriyaṁ muttuvante sutti<br/>
muttidāgaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
rathadiṁ dhātrige pāydu koṇḍu gadeyaṁ keysārdudasmanmanō<br/>
rathamindendu kaḍaṅgi māṇade siḍil poyvantevōl poyvuduṁ<br/>
rathayūtha dhvaja śastraśaṅkha[puṭa]doḷ ghaṇṭāsamētaṁ mahā<br/>
rathanindaṁ kuḷaśaiḷadante karigaḷ bīḻtanduvugrājiyoḷ // ViVi.11.66 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 295]<br/>
madavaddantigaḷaṁ kaṟuttasagavoylpoydājiyoḷ bhīmanā<br/>
rdodedīḍāḍidoḍattajāṇḍa taṭamaṁtāpannegaṁ pāṟi tā<br/>
ṟida pērāneyoḍalgaḷabhrataḷadoḷ silkirduvōrondu mā<br/>
ṇade bīḻtarpuvu beṭṭu bīḻva teṟadindinnuṁ kurukṣētradoḷ // ViVi.11.67 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
toḍare taḍaṅgāl poydoḍe<br/>
keḍeduṁ tividoḍe suruḷdu mōdidoḍirade<br/>
lvaḍagāgi maḍidu biḻduvu<br/>
gaḍaṇade karighaṭegaḷēṁ balasthano bhīmaṁ // ViVi.11.68 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antalli padinālsāsira madadāneyumaṁkaḷiṅganāyakaṁ bhānudattaṁ<br/>
modalāge nūrvararasumakkaḷumaṁ kondoḍe kaurava balamellamollanu<br/>
lidōḍi bhagadattanāneya maṟeyaṁ pokkāgaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
negaḻdeṁ dēvēndranairāvatada keḷeyanennēṟidīyāneyuṁ dal<br/>
digibhaṁ duryōdhanaṁ naccidanenagidiraṁ bhīmaneḻtandanīgaḷ<br/>
mugilaṁ muṭṭittu sandennaḷavumadaṭuvendārdu dōrdarpayuktaṁ<br/>
bhagadattaṁ supratīkadvipamanupacitōtsāhadiṁ tōṟikoṭṭaṁ // ViVi.11.69 [mahāsragdhare]<br/>
</p>

<p>
mada kariya pariva bharadiṁ<br/>
dadirdoḍe nelanoḍḍi ninda caduraṅgamumo<br/>
rmodale naḍugidudu kūḍida<br/>
caduraṅgada maṇeyanalgidantappinegaṁ // ViVi.11.70 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgaḷasuranuyda nelananādi varāhanaṟasalendu sakaḷa jaḷacarakaḷita<br/>
jaḷanidhigaḷaṁ kalaṅkuvante pāṇḍava baḷa jaḷanidhiyanaḷikuḷa jhēṅkāra mukharita<br/>
viśāla karaṭa taṭamā diśāgajēndraṁ kalaṅke—<br/>
</p>

<p>
taḷardudu karṇatāḷa pavanāhatiyiṁ jaḷarāśi keyya ba<br/>
ḷvaḷikege diggajaṁ deseyinatta teraḷduvu kāypiniṁ diśā<br/>
vaḷiverasambaraṁ pogedu pottidudāda madāmbuviṁ jagaṁ<br/>
jaḷadhivolāytadaṁ neṟeye baṇṇiparār gaḷa supratīkamaṁ // ViVi.11.71 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 296]<br/>
kara nakha danta ghātadinuruḷva caturbaladiṁ teraḷva ne<br/>
ttara kaḍalā kaḍalvaregameyde mahā makaraṁ samudradoḷ<br/>
parivavolintagurvuverasā bhagadattana kāloḷantadēṁ<br/>
paridudo supratīka gajamaccariyappinamāji raṅgadoḷ // ViVi.11.72 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu parida bīdigaḷoḷellaṁ nettara toṟegaḷ pariye keṇḍada toṟe<br/>
[yante]parida supratīkaṁkeyya kāla kōḍēṟinoḷ balamanellaṁ javanejivuḷiduḻivante toḻtuḻiduḻidu padinālsāsira madāndha gandhasindhuraṅgaḷu<br/>
manondu lakkarathamumanaredusaṇṇisidante māḍidāgaḷ gajāsuranoḷāsuraṁ<br/>
berasu tāguvandhakārātiyante bhīmasēnaṁ bandu poṇare—<br/>
</p>

<p>
tolagidu supratīka gajamāṁ bhagadattanenilli ninna tō<br/>
ḷvalada poḍarpu salladele sāyade pōgene kēḷdu bhīmanāṁ<br/>
toleyadirurkinoḷ nuḍiveyī kari sūkariyalte patti gaṁ<br/>
ṭalanoḍeyotti kondapenidaltidaṟammanumennanāmpudē // ViVi.11.73 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu nārācaṅgaḷiṁ tōḍuṁ bīḍuṁ kāṇalāgadantu supratīka kariyemba<br/>
giriya mēle bhīmanemba kālamēghaṁ sarala sariyaṁ suriye—<br/>
</p>

<p>
siḍileṟapandadindeṟagi dikkari tanna varūthamaṁ paḍa<br/>
lvaḍise marutsutaṁ muḷidu maccaradiṁ gajegoṇḍu suttugoṁ<br/>
ḍaḍigiḍe nurgipoydu peṟapiṅguvuduṁ kari nondu kōpadiṁ<br/>
piḍideṟagittu bhīmananagurvisi pāṇḍava sainyamaḷkuṟal // ViVi.11.74 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
anteṟagidoḍe kōḍakeyya kāleḍegaḷoḷbiṇpumaṁ[peṇe]vanda<br/>
diṁdērduḍokkaraṅgoṇḍu kurukṣētradindatta panneraḍu yōjanambara<br/>
mottuvuduṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
kariyuṁ kuru bhūmiya naḍu<br/>
varegaṁ pavanajananotte tōḷvalamāgaḷ<br/>
sari sariyādudu taddi<br/>
kkarigaṁ bhīmaṅgamugra saṅgara dhareyoḷ // ViVi.11.75 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 297]<br/>
annegamitta saṁsaptakabalamellamanaḷaṟe peḷaṟekivuḻeduḻidu kolva<br/>
vikrāntatuṁgaṁ cakriyanintendaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
paridudu supratīkagajamēṟidavaṁ bhagadattanā mada<br/>
dviradamanāṅkegoṇḍu peṇevaṁ pavanātmajanīgaḷāhavaṁ<br/>
piridudalatta pōpamene tadrathamaṁ hari vāyuvēgadiṁ<br/>
pariyise tāgidaṁ hariganaṅkada poṅkada supratīkamaṁ // ViVi.11.76 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu tāgi mr̥garāja nakhara mārgaṇaṅgaḷoḷaṁ kūrmanakhāstraṅgaḷoḷa<br/>
māneyumaṁ bhagadattanumaṁ pūḻdoḍe bhagadattaṁ muḷidubhūdattamappa<br/>
divyāṅkuśamaṁ koṇḍu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
iḍuvudumadu vilayāgniya<br/>
kiḍigaḷanuguḻuttumeydevarpudumidiraṁ<br/>
naḍedajaranuradināntoḍe<br/>
tuḍugevolesedirdudaṅkuśaṁ kandharadoḷ // ViVi.11.77 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgaḷ vikrāntatuṅgaṁ cōdyambaṭṭidēnendu besagoḷe—<br/>
</p>

<p>
idu peṟataltu bhūtalamanāṁ taralādi varāhanādenaṁ<br/>
dadaṟa viṣāṇamaṁ baḻiyamā vasudhāṅganegittēnītanā<br/>
sudatiyapautranāke kuḍe bandudivaṅgenagalladānalā<br/>
gadudaṟinānteniṁ taṟivudī kari kandharamaṁ guṇārṇavā // ViVi.11.78 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
embudumonde divyaśaradiṁ śiramaṁ paṟiyeccoḍātano<br/>
ttambadināntoḍāṁ baṟide tappidenendu kirīṭi tanna bi<br/>
llaṁ bisuṭirdoḍacyutanidētarinākulamirdenōḍideṁ<br/>
tembudumeccananteraḍu keygaḷumaṁ muḷisiṁ guṇārṇavaṁ // ViVi.11.79 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
eccavana taleyumaṁ paṟi<br/>
yeccoḍe dikkariya taleyumātana taleyuṁ<br/>
paccikkidante keygaḷu<br/>
maccariyappinegamoḍanuruḷduvu dhareyoḷ // ViVi.11.80 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 298]<br/>
ittarigaṅgamitra jayamappudumattamararkaḷārdu sū<br/>
suttire puṣpavr̥ṣṭigaḷanōgaravūgaḷa baṇḍaneyde pī<br/>
ruttoḍavanduvindra vanadiṁ maṟidumbigaḷindra nīlamaṁ<br/>
muttumanōḷiyōḷiyoḷe kōdeḻalikkida māleyantevōl // ViVi.11.81 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
dharaṇī sutanaḻidaṁ di<br/>
kkari keḍedudu nara śaraṅgaḷiṁ bhuvanamumi<br/>
nnuriyadiradānaḍaṅguve<br/>
niradembavolarkanapara jaḷanidhigiḻidaṁ // ViVi.11.82 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgaḷeraḍuṁ paḍegaḷapahāra tūryaṅgaḷaṁ bājisi tantamma bīḍugaḷge<br/>
pōpuduṁ suyōdhanaṁ bhagadattana sāviṅgaḻaldu toṭṭa sannaṇamanappoḍaṁ<br/>
kaḷeyadeyumaramanege pōgade kumbhasambhavanalligevandu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
masakaṅgundada supratīka gajamaṁ dhātrīsutaṁ kīṟi cō<br/>
disi bhīmaṁ gele muṭṭevandu hariyuṁ tānuṁ bharaṅgeydu ta<br/>
nnesakaṁ gāyadadharmayuddhade naraṁ kolvalli kaṇḍintupē<br/>
kṣisi nīmuṁ naḍe nōḍutirdirene mattinnāranāṁ nambuveṁ // ViVi.11.83 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu nuḍida pannagadhvajana nuḍige kārmukācāryanintendaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
enagaltārgamasādhyanalte vijayaṁ nīnātanaṁ gelva mā<br/>
tanamōghaṁ bisuḍinde nāḷe vijayaṁ mārkoḷḷadandurki po<br/>
kkananāntorvananikkuveṁ kadanadoḷ mēṇ kaṭṭuveṁ dharma naṁ<br/>
dananaṁ nīnidanintu nambu bageyalvēḍannanaṁbhūpatī // ViVi.11.84 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
embudumāninitaṁ nimmapūṇisale bandenendu poḍemaṭṭu<br/>
bīḻkoṇḍu pōgi saṁsaptakarkaḷge baḻiyanaṭṭi barisi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
arigananāmpa gaṇḍumadaṭuṁ nimagāvagamādudāhavā<br/>
jiradoḷadarke nāḷe naranaṁ tegeduyvudu dharmaputranaṁ<br/>
guru piḍidappanendavaranāgaḷe pūṇisi pōgavēḻdu ma<br/>
ccaradoḷe māṇadoḍḍidanasuṅgoḷekakkara sañje sañjeyoḷ // ViVi.11.85 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 299]<br/>
āgaḷ pāṇḍava patākiniyumirade poṟamaṭṭardhacandravyūhamanoḍḍi<br/>
nile saṁsaptakar‌ tamage miḻtugarevante vikramārjunanaṁ kareduydaritta—<br/>
</p>

<p>
aṟipidaṁ guru bhārgavanintīyoḍdanidaṁ gelalāvanuṁ<br/>
neṟeyanurkinaḷurkeyinorvaṁ pokkoḍe pokkanemattaṇaṁ<br/>
poṟamaḍaṁtaṟidoṭṭuvenantā pāṇḍava sainyamanendu bi<br/>
lleṟeyanoḍḍidanaṅkada cakravyūhamanāhava raṅgadoḷ // ViVi.11.86 [anavadyaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antoḍḍida cakravyūhada naḍuveḍeyaṟidu kaḷiṅga rājana karighaṭegaḷumaṁ<br/>
karṇa śalya śakuni kr̥pa kr̥tavarma bhūriśravōśvatthāma duryōdhana vr̥ṣasēna<br/>
lakkaṇādigaḷappatiratha mahāratha samarathārdharatharkaḷanirisi mattamavara<br/>
baḷasiyumanēka sāmajabalamberasu jayatsēna sudakṣiṇa kāmbhōjādi nāyakara<br/>
nirisi mattamavara keladoḷeḍeyaṟidu bakāsura jaṭāsurara makkaḷappaḷambhūṣaṇa<br/>
haḷāyudha musaḷāyudha kāḷa nīḷa rūkṣa rākṣasa balamanirisi mattamavara<br/>
keladoḷivargivar pāsaṭiyāgirpudendu ninda neleyoḷ taḷarade nilvantāgirisi<br/>
guheya bāgiloḷ siṁhamirpandadiṁ bhāradvājaṁ sindhurājamberasu<br/>
cakravyūhada bāgiloḷ neṟedu meṟedu nindāgaḷ dharmaputranēgeyva<br/>
teṟanumanaṟiyadabhimanyuvaṁ karedintendaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
idu cakravyūhamī vyūhamanoḍevadaṭaṁ pārthanantātanuṁ geṁ<br/>
ṭidanemmī nālvaruṁ bhēdisalaṟiyevidaṁ kanda nīṁ ballapēḻeṁ<br/>
budumānemmayyanalkēḷdaṟivenidanidēnayya cintāntaraṁ po<br/>
kkidanīgaḷ vanya gandhadviradame koḷanaṁ pokkavōl kādi tōrpeṁ // ViVi.11.87 [mahāsragdhare]<br/>
</p>

<p>
analana koṭṭa gāṇḍivada tēra murāriya meccadēva dē<br/>
vana dayegeyda sāyakada bembaladoḷ kaliyendu kemmana<br/>
mmananadaṭaḻgutirpiravidēṁpageyoḍḍu gelalkaḷumbameṁ<br/>
banituvaraṁ manakke nimagattaḷagaṁ bare matte māṇbenē // ViVi.11.88 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 300]<br/>
neṟedu caturvalamberasu banduṟadoḍḍida gaṇḍarārume<br/>
nnaṟiyada gaṇḍarē negeda nettara suṭṭure kaṇḍadiṇḍegaḷ<br/>
paṟidu nabhambaraṁ paredu parvi layāgni śikhākaḷāpamaṁ<br/>
maṟeyise tāgi taḷtiṟiyadannegamentu naraṅgevuṭṭideṁ // ViVi.11.89 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
embuduṁ yamanandananintendaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
anuvaradalli taḷtu pageyaṁ tave kondoḍamāntarāti sā<br/>
dhanadoḷagaḻgi taḻgidoḍamennaya santatigāgisirda ni<br/>
nnane mada danti danta musalāhatigaṁ karavāḷa bāygamaṁ<br/>
bina monegaṁ mahārathara tintiṇigaṁ piḍidentu nūṅkuveṁ // ViVi.11.90 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
magane padinālku varuṣada<br/>
maganai ninnannanorvanaṁ pagevaḍeyo<br/>
ḍḍugaḷanoḍeyalkevēḻderde<br/>
dhagamene sairisuvupāyamāvudu kaṟuvē // ViVi.11.91 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endoḍā mātaṁ mārkoṇḍabhimanyuvintendaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
kramamaṁ keykoḷalendu puṭṭi raṇadoḷ sāvannegaṁ māṇdoḍa<br/>
kramamakkuṁ kramamakkumē kramamanānēgeydapeṁ vikramaṁ<br/>
kramamāṁ vikramadātaneṁkramada mātantirke māṇdirdoḍāṁ<br/>
kramakendirdene biṭṭoḍaṁ biḍadoḍaṁ bīḻkoṇḍeniṁ māṇbenē // ViVi.11.92 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu tannēṟida kanaka rathamaṁ tanna manadannanappa jayanemba sārathiyaṁ<br/>
cōdisendāgaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
eṟaguva baṭṭinambugaḷa balsari kumbhajanaṁ maraḷcepā<br/>
ydaṟikeya pāreyambugaḷa tandalagurvisi sindhurājanaṁ<br/>
maṟugise bāgiloḷ musuṟi ninda ghaṭāvaḷiyaṁ teraḷci ta<br/>
ttaṟadaṟidotti pokkanabhimanyu virōdhi baḷāmbu rāśiyaṁ // ViVi.11.93 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu pokku virōdhi sainyamaṁ māri pokkante peṇamayaṁ māḍi<br/>
tūrikoṇḍa jōḷadantire paḍalvaḍisidāgaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
oṇagidudondu pervidira pervodaṟiṁ moredurvuvāśuśu<br/>
kṣaṇiyavolānta khaḻga nivahakke rathakke daḻakke matta vā<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 301]<br/>
raṇa nivahakke takkinabhimanyuva kūrgaṇe pāydu nuṅgaluṁ<br/>
ṭoṇeyalumurci mukkalumidēṁ neṟe kaltuvo yuddharaṅgadoḷ // ViVi.11.94 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antidirānta mārpaḍeyellamaṁ javana paḍege paḍigaccikkuvantikkininda<br/>
naranandananaṁ kaṇḍu vikramakkaṁ kramakkaṁ puruḍisuva suyōdhanana makkaḷ lakkaṇaṁ<br/>
modalāge nūrvarumondāge bandu tāgidāgaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
sūḻaisecceccu billaṁ rathada kudureyaṁ sūtanaṁ khaṇḍisuttā<br/>
ṟēḻeṇṭombattu pattembaṟikeya saralindūṟikoṇḍāva meyyuṁ<br/>
pāḻembantāge pārdārduṟadise muḷisiṁ nūrvaruṁ ponnatāḻgaḷ<br/>
sūṟoḷ bīḻvante biḻdar makuṭa maṇigaṇadyōtisārar kumārar // ViVi.11.95 [sragdhare]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgaḷ suyōdhanana makkaḷa sāvaṁ kaṇḍu tammaṇṇana mogamanāva<br/>
mogadoḷ nōḻpenendu duśyāsanaṁ bandu tāgidāgaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
onde saralindamavanerde<br/>
yaṁ dokkane tiṇṇameccu kolalollanesaṁ<br/>
krandananandana tanayaṁ<br/>
tandeya pūṇkeyane nenedu duśyāsananaṁ // ViVi.11.96 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgaḷ kānīna sūnu vr̥ṣasēnanēnuṁmāṇade kāduttirdanannegamitta<br/>
naranandanana baḻivaḻiyaṁ taguḷdu gaḻevaḻiya pāvinante cakravyūhamaṁ<br/>
pugalendu barpa drupada virāṭa dhr̥ṣṭadyumna bhīmasēna sahadēva nakula yudhiṣṭhira<br/>
ghaṭōtkacādigaḷoḍane mallāmalliyāgi kāduva kumbhasambhavanallige<br/>
duryōdhanaṁ bandu namma balamellamabhimanyuvinambina moneyoḷ tūḷdu<br/>
teraḷdōḍidappudu nimagalli kāḷegamati bharamēgeyvamene sindhurājanindinanu<br/>
varakīyeḍeyoḷenitādoḍamīśvara varaprasādadoḷāne sālvenendintendaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
uṟadidirāntu ninda ripu sainyamanāhava raṅgadalli ta<br/>
ttaṟadaṟidikkalāṁ neṟeveninniravēḍoḍagoṇḍu pōgu ni<br/>
nnaṟikeya kumbhasambhavananendoḍe pāṇḍava sainyamaṁ kaṟu<br/>
ttiṟivanitondaḷurke ninagētaṟoḷādudo pēḻ jayadrathā // ViVi.11.97 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 302]<br/>
ene jayadrathanintendaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
naranoḷ munnagapaṭṭudondaḻaloḷāṁ kaiḷāsa śaiḷēśanaṁ<br/>
piriduṁ bhaktiyoḷarcisuttumire taddēvādhipaṁ meccideṁ<br/>
naranorvaṁ poṟagāgalondu divasaṁ kauntēyaraṁ kādi gel<br/>
nirutaṁ nīnene pettenāṁ baramanadrīndrātmajādhīśanoḷ // ViVi.11.98 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
enda sindhurājana nuḍige rājādhirājaneraḍu muyvumaṁ nōḍi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
ninnane nacci pāṇḍavaroḷāntiṟiyal taṟisandu pūṇdenāṁ<br/>
ninna śarāḷigaḷgagidu ninduvu pāṇḍava sainyamendoḍiṁ<br/>
ninna bhujapratāpadaḷavārgamasādhyamāytadēṁ<br/>
ninnaḷavindaminnenage sārdudarāti jayaṁ jayadrathā // ViVi.11.99 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu pogaḻdu sindhurājananiralvēḻdu kumbhasambhavanuṁ tānu<br/>
mabhimanyuvina saṅgrāma raṅgamaneyde vandu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
uḍida rathaṅgaḷiṭṭeḍegaḷoḷ makuṭaṅgaḷa ratnadīptigaḷ<br/>
poḍarvinamaḻgi taḻgida nijātmajaraṁ naḍe nōḍi kaṇṇa nī<br/>
roḍanoḍanurcipāye muḷisindadanoyyane tāḷdi kāypinoḷ<br/>
kaḍagi jagaṁṅgaḷaṁ noṇedu nuṅgalumāṭisidaṁ suyōdhanaṁ // ViVi.11.100 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgaḷ drōṇa drōṇaputra kr̥pa kr̥tavarma karṇa śalya śakuni duśyāsana<br/>
vr̥ṣasēnādigaḷāḷdana muḷida mogamanaṟidu dharmayuddhamaṁ bisuṭu<br/>
naranandanana rathamaṁ suttimuttikoṇḍu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
tēraṁ kudureyanesaguva<br/>
sārathiyaṁ billanadaṟa goṇeyumanuṟadā<br/>
rdōrorvarondaneccoḍe<br/>
bīraṁ gadegoṇḍu bīraraṁ beṅkoṇḍaṁ // ViVi.11.101 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
beṅkoḷe kaḷiṅga rājana<br/>
nūṅkida karighaṭeyanuḍiye baḍi baḍidettaṁ<br/>
kiṅkoḻemāḻpudumuṟade<br/>
ccaṁ karṇaṁ niśita śaradineraḍuṁ karamaṁ // ViVi.11.102 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 303]<br/>
karameraḍuṁ paṟivudumā<br/>
karadindaṁ tanna kunnageyyoḷe koṇḍu<br/>
ddhura ratha cakradiniṭṭaṁ<br/>
tiripi narapriya tanūjanakṣōhiṇiyaṁ // ViVi.11.103 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgaḷ duśyāsanana magaṁ gadāyudhanaḻiye nonda siṅgada mēle<br/>
beragaṟiyada beḷḷāḷ pāyvante kiḻta bāḷverasu pāyvuduṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
sphurita kr̥pāṇa pāṇigidiraṁ naḍedaḷkuṟe toṭṭu vāydu ḍo<br/>
kkaradoḷe mikka dikkariyanikkuvavōl nelakikki patti ka<br/>
ttarigoḷe kāydu kaṇtumuḻdusir kusidantakanantameyde mey<br/>
paravaśavāge jōldanabhimanyu bhayaṅkara raṅgabhūmiyoḷ // ViVi.11.104 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
anitaṇmi satta naranaṁ<br/>
danaṅge kaṇ sōltu bageyadamarēndranani<br/>
nnenage tanagemba dēvāṁ<br/>
ganeyara kaḷakaḷame piridumāytambaradoḷ // ViVi.11.105 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
abhimanyu maraṇa vārtā<br/>
prabhūta śōkāgni dharmatanayananiradaṁ<br/>
dabhibhavisi tannanaḷurdaṁ |<br/>
te bhāskaraṁ keṅkamādanastācaladoḷ // ViVi.11.106 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu nijatanūjana maraṇa śravaṇāśani ghātadiṁ kuḷaśailaṁ keḍevante<br/>
keḍedu mūrchāgatanāda dharmaputranaṁ bhīmasēna nakuḷa sahadēva sātyaki drupada<br/>
virāṭādigaḷapahatakadana‌r mundiṭṭoḍagoṇḍu bīḍiṅge pōdarāgaḷ<br/>
dharmaputrana śōkamanāṟisalendu kr̥ṣṇadvaipāyanaṁ bandu saṁsāra<br/>
sthitiyanaṟiyadavarante nīnintu śōkākrāntanādoḍe—<br/>
</p>

<p>
enitidirāntarāti balamantanitaṁ tave kondutatsuyō<br/>
dhana sutarenna bāṇa gaṇadiṁ tavadirdaro yuddhadāḷge rō<br/>
danamenagāvudayyanenagēkeyo śōkipanendu dharmanaṁ<br/>
dana naranandanaṁ ninage saggadoḷēnabhimanyu nōyanē // ViVi.11.107 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 304]<br/>
jñānamayanāgi saṁsā<br/>
rānityateyaṁ jalakkanāgaṟidirda<br/>
jñāniyavōlnīnuṁ śō<br/>
kānalasantapta cittanappudu doreyē // ViVi.11.108 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu ṣōḍaśa rājōpākhyānamanaṟipi dharmaputrana śōkamanāṟe<br/>
nuḍidu pārāśara munīndraṁ pōdanittal—<br/>
</p>

<p>
aḻidudu mattanūja śatamājiyoḷittabhimanyuvorvana<br/>
ttaḻidanidāvagellamenagaṁkaliyādano pūṇda gaṇḍavā<br/>
taḻiyade gaṇḍanintaḻivudīyaḻivinnenagāji raṅgadoḷ<br/>
gaḻiyisugembidaṁ nuḍiyutuṁ ghaṭasambhavanoḷ suyōdhanaṁ // ViVi.11.109 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu bīḍiṅge pōdanannegamitta saṁsaptaka baḷajaḷanidhiyaṁ baḍabānaḷana<br/>
ḷurvantaḷurdu nija vijaya kaṭakakke vijayaṁ baravare—<br/>
</p>

<p>
hari nijayōgadindaṟidu tannaḷiyaṁ layamādudaṁ bhayaṁ<br/>
kara kapi kētanaṅgaṟipalollade bandu śamanta pañcakaṁ<br/>
baramiḻidalli saṅgara pariśramamaṁ kaḷeyendu maydunaṁ<br/>
berasu jaḷāvagāhadoḷirutte mahā kapaṭa prapañcadiṁ // ViVi.11.110 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
jaḷamantra mantritāśaya<br/>
jaḷadoḷ naraninisu muḻuge nija sutanasuhr̥<br/>
dbaḷa jaḷanidhiyoḷ phalguṇa<br/>
muḻugidanembidane nuḍidu hari muḻuguvuduṁ // ViVi.11.111 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
bhōṅkane kēḷderda kadaḍi ka<br/>
laṅkida bageverasu negedu nālkuṁ deseyaṁ<br/>
śaṅkākuḷitaṁ nōḍi ma<br/>
naṁkoḷukene muḻuginegeda hariyaṁ nuḍidaṁ // ViVi.11.112 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
ākāśa vacanamidu suta<br/>
śōkamanenagaṟipidappudasmattanayaṁ<br/>
gēkendaṟiyeṁ maraṇama<br/>
dā kurupatiyindamādudāgalevēḻkuṁ // ViVi.11.113 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 305]<br/>
indina cakravyūhama<br/>
nāṁ dalaṇaṁ meccalāṟenenutuṁ rathamaṁ<br/>
bandēṟi magana manakata<br/>
monduttaramerdeyanaleya naranintendaṁ // ViVi.11.114 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
kadanadināṁ bare niccalu<br/>
midirvandu koralge vāydu bāyvāyoḷalaṁ<br/>
pidirgoḷe tambulamaṁ ko<br/>
ḷḷade māṇdī magana taḍavidēnasurārī // ViVi.11.115 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
enuttuṁ bīḍaneyde vandu śōkasāgaradoḷ muḻugāḍuva<br/>
parijanamuṁ tanna mogava nōḍal nāṇci taleyaṁ bāgi nalanaṁ bareyuttu<br/>
mirda vīrabhaṭarumaṁ kaṇḍu magana sāvaṁ niścayisi rājamandiramaṁ pokku<br/>
rathadindamiḻidu dharmaputraṅgaṁ vāyuputraṅgaṁ poḍevaṭṭu kuḷḷirpudumavar<br/>
taleyaṁ bāgi nelanaṁ bareyuttumire kirīṭi kaṇḍidēnendu besagoḷe<br/>
dharmaputranintendaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
guru cakravyūhamaṁ paṇṇidoḍe pugalidaṁ ballarārendoḍiṁ nā<br/>
nire mattār ballarendorvane ripu baḷa vārāśiyaṁ pokku mikkāṁ<br/>
taranāṭandikki duryōdhanana tanayaraṁ nūrvaraṁ kondu tatsaṁ<br/>
garadoḷ kādemmanintāntiṟidu nijasutaṁ dēvalōkakke sandaṁ // ViVi.11.116 [mahāsragdhare]<br/>
</p>

<p>
baramaṁ bāḷa śaśāṅkamauḷi kuḍe pettondurkinindōvadāṁ<br/>
tu raṇōtsāhadinemmanorvane bharaṅgeydatta duryōdhanaṁ<br/>
berasā drōṇananaṭṭi sindhu viṣayādhīśaṁ podaḻdondu ma<br/>
ccaradiṁ ninna tanūjanaṁ kolisidaṁ mattāntavar kolvarē // ViVi.11.117 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
embuduṁ pracaṇḍa kōpa pāvaka praśamita śōkarasanumunnata lalāṭa<br/>
taṭa ghaṭita bhīṣaṇa bhrukuṭiyuṁ kalpānta dinakara durnirīkṣanumutpāta<br/>
mārutanante sakala bhūbhr̥tkampakāriyuṁ vindhyācaḷadante vardhamānōtsēdhanumandhakārātiyante bhairavākāranumāgi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
raseyiṁ bhūtaḷadiṁ kuḷādri kuḷadiṁ digdantiyiṁ vārdhiyiṁ<br/>
deseyindāgasadindajāṇḍa taṭadindattelli pokkirdumiṁ<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 306]<br/>
misukal tīrgume vairigenna sutanaṁ kondirdudaṁ kēḷdu sai<br/>
risi māṇdirdapeninnumendoḍidanāṁ pēḻētaṟoḷ nīguveṁ // ViVi.11.118 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
baḷeda suta śōkadindī<br/>
gaḷe surigumesuriyavā jayadrathana citā<br/>
naḷanindamogeda pogegaḷ<br/>
koḷe surivoḍe surivuvenna nayana jalaṅgaḷ // ViVi.11.119 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
bisajabhavanakke mr̥ḍana<br/>
kkasurāntakanakke kāvoḍaṁ nāḷinoḷa<br/>
rvisekondu sindhu rājana<br/>
basiṟaṁ pōḻdenna magananāṁ tegeyadireṁ // ViVi.11.120 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
kondenna magananiṁ bhaya<br/>
dindaṁ rasevokkumajana guṇḍigevokkuṁ<br/>
mandaradharanīporkuḻa<br/>
pondāvarevokku mēṇavaṁ bardukuvanē // ViVi.11.121 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
paḍe paḍemeccegaṇḍanene sandarikēsariyembagurvu nē<br/>
rpaḍe negaḻdānaṇaṁseḍedu māṇbene nāḷe dinēśanastada<br/>
ttuḍugada munna saindhavanagurvise kolladoḍēno gāṇḍīvaṁ<br/>
biḍidane ciḥ tovalviḍidenallene vairige yuddharaṅgadoḷ // ViVi.11.122 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu nr̥pa paramātmaṁ kr̥tapratijñanādudaṁ saindhavana sajjanaṁ dujjōda<br/>
nana taṅge duśyaḷe kēḷdu malamala maṟugi tammaṇṇanallige vandu kālamēle<br/>
kavidu paṭṭu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
tanna sutanaḻiyalaḻiyal<br/>
ninnaya maydunananarjunaṁ pūṇdanada<br/>
rkānnaḍugi bandeninnī<br/>
nennōleya kaḍagadaḻivanēṁ nōḍidapā // ViVi.11.123 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
embuduṁ suyōdhanaṁ muguḷnage nakkintendaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 307]<br/>
maruḷakkamagana śōkadi<br/>
nuruḷduṁ pūṇdavana pūṇke duśyāsananoḷ<br/>
karatanadindennoḷamā<br/>
marutsutaṁ pūṇdu pūṇkeyantevolakkuṁ // ViVi.11.124 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
kr̥ta vividhāstraśastrayamaputra marutsutayajñasēnaru<br/>
ddhata baḷaretti kādi sugidōḍidarallarekāvarī viviṁ<br/>
śati kr̥pa karṇa śalya kaḷaśōdbhava tatpriya putrarendoḍa<br/>
pratirathanaṁ jayadrathananājiyoḷeytare varṣa gaṇḍarār // ViVi.11.125 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
endu duśyaḷeyanoḍagoṇḍu kumbhasambhavanallige vandintendaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
suta śōkōdrēkadiṁ saindhavananaḻivenendarjunaṁ pūṇdanintī<br/>
sati bandaḷ kāvudātmānujeya kaḍagamaṁ nīme mārkoḷvoḍār tā<br/>
vitarar muṭṭal samarthar kadanadoḷene gelvāseyantirke sindhu<br/>
kṣitipaṁ tānēnanādaṁ raṇadoḷadane pōgānumappeṁ narēndrā // ViVi.11.126 [mahāsragdhare]<br/>
</p>

<p>
bijayaṅgeyyene pōpuduṁ nr̥panadaṁ dharmātmajaṁ kēḷdu pē<br/>
ḻdajitaṅgā hari pēḻdudondu nayadindā rātriyoḷ pōgi kuṁ<br/>
bhajanaṁ kaṇḍu vinamranāgi nuḍidaṁ nīmintu keykoṇḍu kā<br/>
de jagatpūjita beṭṭanādoḍemagiṁ bāḻvāseyāvāseyō // ViVi.11.127 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
nimmaḷavanaṟidu munname<br/>
nimma prārthisidemīgaḷaduvaṁ maṟedir<br/>
nimmaya dharmada makkaḷe<br/>
vemmaṁ kaḍegaṇisi nimage negaḻvudu doreyē // ViVi.11.128 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
ene guru karuṇā rasamadu<br/>
manadiṁ poṟapoṇme ninage jayamakkumanaṁ<br/>
tana pēḻda teṟade negaḻene<br/>
vinayade bīḻkoṇḍu nr̥pati bīḍaṁ pokkaṁ // ViVi.11.129 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 308]<br/>
āgaḷārūḍhasarvajñaṁ pratijñārūḍhanāgi gaṅgānadī taraṅgōpamāna<br/>
dukūlāmbara paridhānanumāgi dhavaḷa śayyātaḷadoḷ maṟedoṟagida[na]mō<br/>
ghāstra dhanañjayanaṁ puṇḍarīkākṣaṁ nōḍi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
aridu kolalke saindhavananājiyoḷītana pūṇda pūṇkeyuṁ<br/>
piridavanugra pāśupata bāṇadinallade sāyanantadaṁ<br/>
haranosedittumēnaduṟa muṣṭiyanīyane bēḍavēḻpudā<br/>
daradadanendu cakri śivanallige koṇḍogedaṁ kirīṭiyaṁ // ViVi.11.130 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu manaḥpavanavēgadiṁ kailāsa śaiḷamaneydi kadanatriṇētranaṁ triṇētrana<br/>
mundiḻipuvudumabhavaṁ tanna pādapadmaṅgaḷgeṟagidatirathamathananumaṁ<br/>
madhumathananumanamr̥ta dr̥ṣṭiyiṁ nōḍi pāśupatada muṣṭiyaṁ bēḍalendu<br/>
bandudaṁ tanna divya jñānadindamaṟidu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
apagata kapaṭade naṭanada<br/>
nupadēśaṅgeydu parasi pōgene poḍema<br/>
ṭṭu pasādameṁdaharigana<br/>
nupēndranā darbhaśayana taḷakiḻipuvuduṁ // ViVi.11.131 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antudāramahēśvaranīśvara varaprasādanamellaṁ tanage nenasāgeyuṁ<br/>
kanasinandamāgi tōṟe maṅgaḷa pāṭhaka ravaṅgaḷoḷ bhōṅkaneḻcattanannegaṁ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
tanna sutanaḻaloḷarjuna<br/>
nennudayamaneyde pārdu pagevara bēroḷ<br/>
bennīraneṟeyadiranada<br/>
nānnōḍuvenemba teṟadininanudayisidaṁ // ViVi.11.132 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgaḷubhaya sainyāmburāśigaḷamburāśigaḷ neleyiṁ taḷarvante taḷare<br/>
kaḷaśa sambhavanandinanuvaradoḷ tannaṁ paricchēdisi kanaka kaḷaśa sambhr̥ta maṅgaḷa<br/>
jaḷaṅgaḷaṁ mindu dhavaḷa vasana dukūlāmbara maṅgaḷa vibhūṣaṇanuṁ nirvartita<br/>
sandhyōpāsananuṁ parisamāpta japanumarcita śitikaṇṭhanumāhuti<br/>
hutāgnihōtranuṁ pūjita dharāmaranuṁnīrājita rathaturaganumāgi rajata<br/>
rathamanēṟi saṅgrāma bhūmiyaneydevandu sāmantacūḍāmaṇiyaninisu<br/>
mārkoṇḍu nilvoḍaṁ sindhurājanaṁ kāvoḍamanēka vyūha racaneyoḷallade<br/>
[p. 309]<br/>
gelal bāradendu cakravyūhamanidiroḷoḍḍi sakaḷa sāmanta cakramaniralvēḻdallige<br/>
nālkuṁ yōjanada padumavyūhadoḷaṅgarāja śalya vr̥ṣasēna kr̥pa<br/>
kr̥tavarmāśvatthāmaraṁ duryōdhanaṁ berasirisi mattitta nālku yōjanada śakaṭa<br/>
vyūhada bāgiloḷ bāhlīka sōmadatta vindānuvindaroḍane saṁsaptakaranirisi<br/>
śakaṭa vyūhada peṟage nālku yōjanadoḷardhacandra vyūhadoḷadhika balarappa<br/>
saubala duśyāsanādi pradhāna vīrabhaṭa kōṭiya naḍuve sindhurājananirisi modala<br/>
cakravyūhada bāgiloḷ śarāsanācāryaṁ nindanitta pāṇḍava balamellamuṁ<br/>
vikramārjunanuṁ vajrapañjaradantabhēdyamappa vajravyūhamanoḍḍi dharmarāja<br/>
noḍane bhīma nakuḷa sahadēva sātyaki dhr̥ṣṭadyumna ghaṭōtkaca pramukha nāyakaraṁ<br/>
pēḻdu drupada virāṭa śikhaṇḍi yudhāmanyūttamaujaḥ kaikaya pradhāna nāyakaraṁ<br/>
tannoḍane kūḍikoṇḍu nijāgrajanaṁ bīḻkoṇḍu nija rathamaṁ rathāṅgadharanaṁ<br/>
munnamēṟalvēḻdu mūṟu sūḻbalavandu poḍemaṭṭu rathamanēṟi<br/>
vajrakavacamaṁ toṭṭu tavadoṇegaḷanamare bigidu gāṇḍīvamanēṟisi nīvi<br/>
jēvoḍedāgaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
bhavaṁ bhavanagōtradindajanajāṇḍadiṁ bhānu bhā<br/>
nu vīdhiyiniḷātaḷaṁ taḷadineyde kiḻteḻdu tū<br/>
ḷvavārya bhuja vīryamaṁ neṟeye tōrpinaṁ kumbha saṁ<br/>
bhavaṁ maraletāgidaṁ ripukuraṅgakaṇṭhīravaṁ // ViVi.11.133 [pr̥thvi]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu tāgi cakravyūhada bāgiloḷ tannaṁ pugalīyadaḍḍamāgininda<br/>
kārmukācāryananuṟe seṟegeyyade vinayāstramaneccu vinayamane mundiṭṭu<br/>
balavandu poḍamaṭṭu pōgevōge—<br/>
</p>

<p>
kamanīyaṁ balavandu pōpananelē pōpōgadir pōgadir<br/>
samarakkennoḍanañji pōdeyenalinteṁdaṁnaraṁ drōṇaraṁ<br/>
nimagānañjuvudenna bālatanadindandādudindādudē<br/>
nimagānañjadoḍañjisal neṟevenē trailōkyamaṁ yuddhadoḷ // ViVi.11.134 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu vinayamane nuḍida vikramārjunanaṁ guruvanēkāśīrva<br/>
vacanaṅgaḷiṁ parasuvuduṁ padumanābhana cōdisuva ratha vēgadiṁ padma<br/>
vyūhamaneydevandu suyōdhanana sādhanadoḷ tāgidāgaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 310]<br/>
posamaseyambu kāra maḻevōl kaṟeyuttire nērdu sīḷdu khaṁ<br/>
ḍisi kaḍidoṭṭi suṭṭanitumaṁ nija mārgaṇa kōṭiyindagu<br/>
rvise tegedeccu tanna moneyambugaḷiṁ caturaṅgameyde kī<br/>
lise paḍe citradonde paḍeyantevolāytakaḷaṅka rāmaniṁ // ViVi.11.135 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
aḍi toḍe porkuḻuṁ tegale kai kaṇakāl koralembivuṁ beral<br/>
naḍuvura ben basiṟ toḷaku karcaremuyvu musumbu mūgu pe<br/>
rdoḍe kaṭi muṁmaḍaṁ paraḍu sandi nosal paṇe kaṇ kadampiveṁ<br/>
beḍeyane naṭṭuvurcidavu nērduvu sīḷduvu pārthanambugaḷ // ViVi.11.136 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu māṟānta mārpaḍeyellamaṁ javanokkalikki tannoḷ pōgade<br/>
peṇeda bāhlīka sōmadatta bhūriśravaranāne meṭṭida kuḷumpeya nīrante dese<br/>
desege sūsuvannegameḻbaṭṭi kāmbhōja sudakṣiṇa jayatsēnarembareytare<br/>
mūvarakṣōhiṇī patigaḷverasu nālsāsirvar makuṭa vardhanaraṁ kondu<br/>
śalyanuramaṁ biriyeccu kr̥paraṁ viratharmāḍi naḍuvagaliḻivinaṁ kādi baḻaldu<br/>
kuduregaḷaṁ nīroḷikkalendu dēvakhātavemba maḍuviṅge barpudumitta<br/>
duryōdhanaṁ drōṇarallige vandu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
aḻidudu cāturaṅga balamaḷkuṟadānta mahāratharkaḷuṁ<br/>
kaḻakuḻamādudoḍḍaṇamaṇaṁ taledōṟale gaṇḍarilla to<br/>
ttaḻaduḻidappaninninisu bēgade saindhavanaṁ negaḻteyaṁ<br/>
gaḻiyisikoḷvoḍinninisu nindiṟiyiṁ taṟisandu pārthanoḷ // ViVi.11.137 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
embuduṁ drōṇācāryaṁ muguḷnage nakku vikramārjunananiḷisi nuḍiva<br/>
ninneṇagōṇaṅgaḷumekkasakkatanaṅgaḷumettamōduvu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
ninagarasāḷtanaṁ nuḍiva bīrara bīradaḷurke vikramā<br/>
rjunanoḷadēke salladenagātanasādhyanavadhyanānumī<br/>
moreyoḷe nindu kādidapenannegamenna varūtha sūta kē<br/>
tana kavacaṅgaḷiṁ neṟedu taḷtiṟi nīṁ jagadēkamallanoḷ // ViVi.11.138 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
embuduṁ suyōdhananēnādoḍēnādudenna pageya nānē<br/>
kolvenendabhēdya kavacamaṁ toṭṭu divyaśarāsana śaraṅgaḷaṁ koṇḍukaḷaśakētana<br/>
varūthanāgi pōgi—<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 311]<br/>
taḍeyade rājarājanidiraṁ bare bhōrgaredeccoḍambugaḷ<br/>
naḍade siḍilvuduṁ karataḷvadvayamaṁ biriyeccu keyduvaṁ<br/>
piḍivadaṭellamaṁ kiḍisi tāṁ kolalollanebhīmanātanaṁ<br/>
maḍipuvenenda pūṇke pusiyādapudendamarēndranandanaṁ // ViVi.11.139 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
annegamitta dharmaputranamōghāstra dhanañjayanaṁ keykoḷalaṭṭi<br/>
doḍe kaurava baḷa jaḷanidhiya naḍuvanuttarisibarpa sātyakiyaṁbhūriśrava<br/>
neḍegoṇḍāntu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
pōgadirendu mūdalise sātyaki tīvra śarāḷiyindagu<br/>
rvāge varūthamaṁ kaḍidoḍurcida bāḷvarasātaneydevaṁ<br/>
dāgaḷidirce tānumasiyaṁ seragillade kiḻtu pāydu bhū<br/>
bhāga nabhōvibhāgavaramaḷkuṟe taḷtiṟidar‌ virōdhigaḷ // ViVi.11.140 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antirvarumōrorvaroḷ bīramumaṁ biṅkamumaṁ meṟedu<br/>
dāsavaṇadaṇḍeyaṁ tōradiṇḍeyāḍidante dese desege kedaṟida kaṇḍadiṇḍegaḷuṁ<br/>
nāraṅga sakaḷavaṭṭeyapaḻayigegaḷante nabhakke miḷirdu miḷḷisi pāṟuva nettara<br/>
suṭṭuregaḷumatibhayaṅkarākāramāge kādi basavaḻida sātyakiyaṁ bhūriśravana<br/>
śramadoḷ nelakikki gaṇṭalaṁ meṭṭi taleyanarivāgaḷ sātyaki bhūmi yuddha<br/>
pravīṇanappudaṟindātana bāḷa bāyoḷ cakrākr̥tiyoḷ taleyaṁ tiruputtu<br/>
mirdāgaḷadaṁmurāntakaṁ kaṇḍu vidviṣṭa vidrāvaṇaṅge tōṟidoḍe—<br/>
</p>

<p>
naraneccoḍe paṟidu karaṁ<br/>
karavāḷoḍanamare kāsi beccante vasuṁ<br/>
dhareyoḷ biḻdirdudadēṁ<br/>
tiravō pūṇisida muṣṭi bhūriśravanā // ViVi.11.141 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgaḷ sātyaki muḷisinol kaṇgāṇade bhūriśravana taleyanaridu<br/>
tannēṟiṅge tāne siggāgi pōdanannegaṁ yamanandanana besadoḷ phalguṇanaṁ<br/>
keykoḷal barpa marunnandanaṅgā drōṇaraḍḍaṁ bandoḍe guruge<br/>
gurudakṣiṇeguḍuvantavara rathamaṁ śata cūrṇaṁ māḍi kaḷiṅgarāja gaja ghaṭegaḷa<br/>
nauṅki sorkuttuṁ bare duśyāsanādigaḷadiradidiraṁ bandāntoḍe—<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 312]<br/>
niḍuvage saipininde dorekoṇḍudivar gajegoṇḍenappoḍī<br/>
gaḍe paredappareccu tave kolvenivandiranendu naccina<br/>
ccuḍivinameccoḍecceḍeyineccaruṇāmbu kalaṅki pāye mu<br/>
nnaḍiyoḷuraḷdarandhanr̥panandanarandu maruttanūjanā // ViVi.11.142 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu durmukha durmada durdharṣaṇa‌r modalāge mūvattu<br/>
mūvaraṁ kondu duśyāsananaṁ virathanaṁ māḍi duryōdhanananonde niśita<br/>
viśikha hatiyiṁ suruḷduruḷvinameccu mūrchāgatanaṁ māḍi siṁhanādadinārdu<br/>
muṭṭevarpāgaḷāḷdana sāvaṁ nōḍalāṟade—<br/>
</p>

<p>
eḍegoṇḍaṅkada karṇaneydevare divyāstraṅgaḷindaṁ siḍil<br/>
poḍevantappinameccudagra rathamaṁ muyyēḻu sūḻ kōpadiṁ<br/>
kaḍiyal sārdoḍaḻaldu sūtasutanondugrēṣuviṁ tiṇṇame<br/>
ccoḍanārdaṁ nasu mūrchevōgi rathadoḷ bhīma naralvannegaṁ // ViVi.11.143 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu mūrchāgatanāda bhīmana koraloḷ billaṁ kōdu mēgillade<br/>
tegedu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
tāṁ gaḍamennāḷdana toḍe<br/>
yaṁ gaḍaminnuḍivanennoḷaṁ kāduvaneṁ<br/>
daṅgapati nuḍidu kollade<br/>
tāṅgidanambikege nuḍida nuḍi nile manadoḷ // ViVi.11.144 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
annegamitta cāṇūrāri jarāsandhāriya munnegedu baḻikkaḍaṅgida<br/>
siṁhanādakke manaḥkṣatambaṭṭu sātyakiyanārayalaṭṭidoḍātaṁ bandacētananāgi<br/>
biḻdirda vr̥kōdaranaṁ tanna rathamanēṟisikoṇḍu kūḍe vandanannegaṁ<br/>
duryōdhanaṁ karṇamberasu saindhavana moneyoḷātanaṁ peṟagikki munde<br/>
nindāgaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
dinakaranasta mastakamanāsevaḍal bagedappanēke ke<br/>
mmane taḍevai jayadrathananikkuḻidāroḷamiṁ toḍaṅkavē<br/>
ḍenutumajaṁ marujjavade cōdise pārthana dēvadatta ni<br/>
svanadoḷe tīvi poṭṭanoḍavantevolādudajāṇḍa maṇḍaḷaṁ // ViVi.11.145 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
caṭuḷita cakranēmi parivartana ghaṭṭana ghāta nirbhara<br/>
sphuṭita dharātaḷaṁ vijayanugra rathaṁ paridattu dal ghaṭā<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 313]<br/>
ghaṭita haṭadvirōdhi rudhiraplava lampaṭa saṅkaṭōtkaṭaṁ<br/>
kaṭakaṭaghāta nāka taṭasaṅkaṭa saṅgara raṅgabhūmiyoḷ // ViVi.11.146 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
āgaḷ kurudhvajinige bhayajvaramuṁ mahēśvarajvaramuṁ bare barpudāra<br/>
mahēśvarana rathada baravaṁ kaṇḍu karṇa śalya śakuni śāradvata kr̥tavarma<br/>
duryōdhana duśyāsanar modalādatiratha samaratha mahārathārdharatharoṁ<br/>
devindeyalladondorvaroḷ sandhisi gondaṇisi nindāgaḷ—<br/>
</p>

<p>
śaradoḷagurci pōpa poḷapiṅgoḷagāgi taguḷdudondu be<br/>
ḷsarigeṇeyādudīyeṟaguvambina balsariyembinaṁniraṁ<br/>
taradoḷe pāyda kūrgaṇegaḷaṁ taṟidoṭṭi teraḷci toḷdikoṁ<br/>
ḍaredu maguḻci saṇṇisidanānta caturvalamaṁ guṇārṇavaṁ // ViVi.11.147 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
kaligaṁ ballāḷgamambettideniduve padaṁ mārkoḷal sindhurājaṁ<br/>
gelalendāṁ bandeniṁ kondapane neredu nindānimendāntaraṁ mū<br/>
dalisutteccaṁ pracaṇḍa praḷaya ghana ghaṭāravadindārdu bāṇā<br/>
valiyindaṁ pūḻe rōdō vivaramanodavittondu ghōrāndhakāraṁ // ViVi.11.148 [mahāsragdhare]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antamōghāstra dhanañjayanecca śara saṅghātadinogeda raṇagaḻtaleye<br/>
molagaḻtaleyaṁ māḍe nēsaṟ paṭṭattu vijayaṁ sōltanendu kaurava<br/>
balamārdoḍe—<br/>
</p>

<p>
jvaḷadanaḷāstradindamise kaḻtale tūḷdu teraḷdudāgaḷu<br/>
mmaḷisi mahārathar peḷaṟe saindhavanennaḷaviṅgamenna dō<br/>
rvaḷadaḷaviṅgamiṁ seḍediral doreyaltenagendu bandasuṁ<br/>
goḷe poṇardaṁ surar‌ pogaḻe tannaḷavaṁ jagadēkamallanoḷ // ViVi.11.149 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antatiratha mathanana rathakkadiradidiraṁ tanna rathamaṁ pariyisi jayadrathaṁ<br/>
muṭṭevandu—<br/>
</p>

<p>
ninne poraḷci ninna maganaṁ seragillade kondenindumiṁ<br/>
tinnegamirpudaṁ bhayadinirdene ninnane pārutirdeneṁ<br/>
dunnata śauryadindajitanaṁ naranaṁ munideccanēḻumeṁ<br/>
ṭunniśitāstradindadaṭadēṁ dorevettudo sindhurājanā // ViVi.11.150 [utpalamālike]<br/>
</p>

<p>
[p. 314]<br/>
anteccu kiccuṁ kiḍiyumāgi percidummaccaradindaccariyāgekāde—<br/>
</p>

<p>
entasmatputranaṁ saṅgaradoḷaḻideyinnante nil‌ śakti cātu<br/>
rdantaṅgaḷ ninnanāṁ kolveḍeyoḷelavo pēḻ kāvuvē kāyavaṇmeṁ<br/>
dantāntecceccu sūta dhvaja haya ratha saṅghātamaṁ nurge lōka<br/>
kkantaṁ māḻpantakambōl gadeviḍiduṟadeytarpanaṁ kaṇḍanantaṁ // ViVi.11.151 [sragdhare]<br/>
</p>

<p>
tuḍu pāśupatamanene nara<br/>
neḍemaḍagade tuḍe diśāḷi naḍugidudu suru<br/>
ḷduḍugidudu viyattaḷameḷe |<br/>
piḍugidudu kalaṅki kadaḍidudu śivana manaṁ // ViVi.11.152 [kandaṁ]<br/>
</p>

<p>
suḻiyoḷagirdu beṭṭu poṟapoṇmuvinaṁ lavaṇāmburāśi ku<br/>
kkuḻagudivalli kūḻgudiye mēge siḍildaguḷante kūḍe ta<br/>
ttaḻagudiyuttumirpa kudiyoḷ siḍidalliya muttugaḷ chaḻil<br/>
chaḻilene koṇḍuvormodale rudra surēndra vimānapaṅtkiyaṁ // ViVi.11.153 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
antu samudra kṣōbhamuṁ trailōkya kṣōbhamumoḍanoḍanāge—<br/>
</p>

<p>
tegeneṟedūṟikoṇḍise śiraṁ paridatta viyattaḷambaraṁ<br/>
negedoḍe rāhu bāydeṟedu nuṅgale bandapudemba śaṅkeyiṁ<br/>
dagidu dinēśanasta giriyaṁ maṟegoṇḍanamōghamemba mā<br/>
tugaḷa negaḻteyaṁ paḍedanāhavadoḷ parasainyabhairavaṁ // ViVi.11.154 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
biridalarōḷi saggada madāḷigaḷaṁ geḍegoṇḍu dēva suṁ<br/>
dariyara keygaḷindamuge tumburu nāradarondu gēyadiṁ<br/>
caramerdeyaṁ paḷañcaleye vīralatāṅgiyasōṅku meyyoḷaṁ<br/>
kurise nirākuḷaṁ kaḷedanāji pariśramamaṁ guṇārṇavaṁ // ViVi.11.155 [campakamāle]<br/>
</p>

<p>
idu vividha vibudha janavinuta jinapadāmbhōja<br/>
varaprasādōtpanna prasanna gambhīra vacana racana<br/>
catura kavitā guṇārṇava viracitamappa<br/>
vikramārjuna vijayadoḷ<br/>
ēkādaśāśvāsaṁ<br/>
</p>
